Miss Nimwiza yavuze ko hari imishinga iri gutegurwa yo gukorana hagati y'impande zombi """" izaba ari myiza """" Abanyarwanda bazagenda bamenya mu minsi iri imbere .
Bwiza Jolie mu bagore n'abakobwa bari guhatana muri Mrs Washington America .
Intego y'iri rushanwa ni ukongerera ubushobozi abagore kugira ngo bazane impinduka aho batuye .
Abatsinze bamara umwaka bahabwa amahugurwa , bagaragara mu biganiro bitandukanye bakanahuzwa n'abafatanyabikorwa .
Gutsinda muri iri rushanwa bitanga amahirwe yo guhatana mu yandi marushanwa arimo Mrs . America na Mrs . World Competitions .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Bwiza Jolie yavuze ko yitabiriye iri rushanwa nyuma yo kutabona amahirwe yo kwitabira Miss Washington America ivamo uhagararira Washington muri """" Miss America . """"
Yavuze ko kubura amahirwe yo kwitabira Miss Washington byatewe n'uko atarabona ubwenegihugu bwa Amerika .
Ati """" Nifuzaga kwitabira irushanwa rya Miss Washington , ariko bo basaba kuba ufite ubwenegihugu !
Njye rero nubwo mfite ibyangombwa byo kuba hano nkaba nabwo narabusabye ariko sindabubona .
Bahise bangira inama yo kwitabira Mrs Washington . """"
Uyu mukobwa witabiriye iri rushanwa ahagarariye Umujyi atuyemo wa Tacoma , ahatanye n'abandi 12 .
Muri 13 bahatanira ikamba rya Mrs Washington America , batatu bonyine barimo na Bwiza nibo bakiri abakobwa , mu gihe icumi bo ari abagore .
Uyu mukobwa avuga ko aramutse atsinze iri rushanwa , yaba abonye irindi jwi ryamufasha kugira inama abimukira bajya gutura muri Amerika kudatwarwa n'ibintu binyuranye ngo batakaze intego zabo mu buzima .
Ati """" Hari abantu benshi baza hano , bagahura n'ibibazo cyangwa n'ibintu bitandukanye bituma batakaza intego zabo mu buzima , Ugasanga kuba barabashije kuza inaha ntacyo bibamariye !
Ndamutse ntsinze naba mbonye ijwi ryo kujtya mbaganiriza . """"
Bwiza Jolie asanzwe ari umunyamideri utuye i Washington muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , akaba n'umunyeshuri wo muri kaminuza aho ageze mu mwaka wa gatatu yiga """" Political Scinces . """"
Uyu mukobwa wavukiye muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo ariko agakurira mu Rwanda , yahavuye mu 2016 yerekeza muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Umunyamakuru M Irene yahagaritse gufasha Vestine na Dorcas yinjije mu muziki .
Mu itangazo ryagiye hanze rigaragaza ko MIE yahisemo gutandukana n'aba bahanzi ku mpamvu zitaramenyekana .
Rigira riti """" Nyuma yo gusesengura imikoranire ya MIE na Vestine na Dorcas , MIE yifuje kubwira abakunzi bayo ndetse n'umuryango mugari wa muzika ko guhera tariki 7 Nyakanga yahagaritse ibikorwa yakoranaga n'aba bahanzikazi ku mpamvu muzamenyeshwa mu minsi iri imbere . """"
Batandukanye nyuma y'aho uyu munyamakuru ari we wabazanye mu muziki bagakorana indirimbo zirimo """" Nahawe Ijambo , """" """" Papa """" ndetse na """" Adonai """" baherukaga gushyira hanze .

Batangiye kuririmba ku giti cyabo mu 2018 ariko ubu ni bwo babashije gushyira hanze indirimbo yabo ya mbere .

Muri iyi minsi abanyamuziki badukanye umuco wo guhimba ibinyoma bikomeye , mu rwego rwo gushitura abakunzi babo mbere y'uko basohora indirimbo .
Lava Lava wo muri Tanzania na we aherutse kuyoboka uyu mujyo .
Yahimbye ikinyoma ko yabengewe kuri radiyo , nyamara agamije gushitura abantu ngo bitege indirimbo ye nshya .
Mu minsi ishize ubwo umuhanzikazi Lulu wo muri Tanzania yari kuri Wasafi FM , mu buryo bugaragara nk'ubuteguye , Lava Lava bari bambaye imyenda isa , yamwinjiranye mu kiganiro azanye igipfunyika cy'indabyo , aherekejwe n'itsinda ry'abafata amashusho n'amafoto amupfukama imbere amusaba kumubabarira .
Uyu muhanzikazi yiyamye Lava Lava amubwira ko atabishaka , ati """" Sitaki """" cyangwa se """" Simbishaka . """"
Nyuma yo kubona ko abenzwe , Lava Lava wari wigize nk'uri mu rukundo rukomeye , yanze guhaguruka ahubwo akomeza gufata amaguru Lulu yikuruza hasi amusaba ko yamubabarira .
Lulu na we ntiyahwemye kwiyama Lava Lava , amusunika cyane amusaba kumureka , undi na we ariko yanga kuva ku izima .
Nyuma yo kubona ko bigenze nabi , Lulu yemeye gufata izi ndabyo ariko yarakaye cyane .
Bimwe mu binyamakuru bitandukanye byo mu karere byari byanditse inkuru y'uko Lava Lava yabengewe muri studio za radiyo nyamara we ku rundi ruhande yari azi ibyo yakoze .
Nyuma y'iminsi mike ibi bisa n'ikinamico bibaye , Lava Lava yahise asohora indirimbo yise """" Nikomeshe . """"

Imishinga yihariye Dorcas & Vestine na Gisubizo Ministries binjiranye muri """" Rwanda Gospel Stars Live . """"
Irushanwa ryiswe """" Rwanda Gospel Stars Live """" ryahurijwemo abahanzi 15 bari ku ruhembe rw'abafite igikundiro mu muziki uhimbaza Imana , bahataniye igihembo cya miliyoni zirindwi z'amafaranga y'u Rwanda .
Mu mabwiriza agenga iri rushanwa harimo ko abatoranyirijwe kuryitabira bagomba kumurika imishinga yabo .
Gisubizo Ministries iri mu matsinda afite ibigwi mu muziki uhimbaza Imana yavuze ko umushinga wayo ari ugufasha abana baturuka mu miryango itishoboye binyuze mu kubigisha ijambo ry'Imana no kubafasha kwihangira imirimo .
Nkomezi Alexis wari uhagarariye Gisubizo Ministries yavuze ko ari ibikorwa itsinda risanzwe rikora ariko mu gihe baba babonye andi maboko babyagura bikagenda neza kurushaho .
Gisubizo Ministries yamenyekanye cyane mu ndirimbo zirimo """" Amfitiye byinshi , """" """" Mana uriho , """" """" Ndaguhetse ku Mugongo , """" """" Narababariwe """" n'izindi .
Ni umuryango ukora ivugabutumwa rinyuze mu ndirimbo mu bihugu binyuranye ku Isi ndetse mu bihe bitandukanye ryegukanye ibihembo byinshi mu muziki uhimbaza Imana .
Dorcas na Vestine baturuka mu Majyaruguru y'u Rwanda ubwo baganirizaga itangazamakuru iby'umushinga wabo , bavuze ko bashaka kubaka studio igezweho ikaba n'ikigo cyo kwigishirizamo urubyiruko umuziki .
Ni igitekerezo aba bana bavuga ko bakuye ku kuntu bakoze umuziki baturuka mu Ntara y'Amajyaruguru ariko badafite studio hafi , byatumye bashaka gufungura iyabo yajya inafasha abandi bafite impano ntibavunike nkuko bo bavunitse .
Bagize bati """" Twe twavaga i Musanze tuje gukora umuziki mu Mujyi wa Kigali , ni ibintu bituvuna cyane , rero abantu badushyigikiye tugatsindira ariya mafaranga byadufasha gukora ikigo cyigisha umuziki kirimo na studio byajya bifasha n'abandi banyempano . """"
Dorcas na Vestine bari mu bahanzikazi bashya bahanzwe amaso mu muziki uhimbaza Imana .
Iri tsinda ry'abavandimwe ryamenyekanye mu ndirimbo """" Nahawe ijambo """" . """"
Aba bana basengera muri ADEPR ndetse baririmba by'umwihariko muri Korali Goshen y'i Musanze .
Abakunzi b'umuziki wo kuramya no guhimbaza Imana , yaba abo mu Rwanda no hanze yarwo bakomeje gushyigikira abahanzi bakunda binyuze mu mushinga """" Rwanda Gospel Stars live . """"
Byitezwe ko tariki 30 Nzeri 2021 umuhanzi uzahiga abandi kugira umushinga mwiza no gushyigikirwa cyane , azashyikirizwa miliyoni zirindwi z'amafaranga y'u Rwanda ziyongera ku yo yagiye ahabwa mu gushyigikira umushinga we .
Izi miliyoni zirahatanirwa n'abahanzi barimo Serge Iyamuremye , Israel Mbonyi , Aline Gahongayire , Tonzi , Gaby Kamanzi , Rata Jah Naychah , James na Daniella , Gisubizo Ministries , MD , Dorcas & Vestine , Chorale Christus Regnat , Gisele Precious , True Promises Ministries , Aimee Frank Nitezeho na Aneth Murava .
Abahanzi batangiye gukangurira abakunzi babo kubaha inkunga yo gushyira mu ngiro imishinga yabo , binyuze mu bitaramo binyura kuri Televiziyo y'u Rwanda .
Buri wese wifuza gushyigikira umuhanzi akunda muri 15 bamaze gutangazwa , arasabwa kujya muri telefone ye umurongo yaba akoresha wose , agakanda * 544 * 300 * nimero y'umuhanzi ashyigikiye hanyuma agashyiraho # cyangwa .
Nta giciro cyashyizweho , buri wese yitanga uko yifite mu rwego rwo gushyigikira umuhanzi akunda .
Britney Spears agiye guhagarika umuziki burundu .
Yabitangaje mu ibaruwa yabonywe bwa mbere n'ikinyamakuru Deadline aho yanditse agaragaza ko atakomeza kuba umujyanama [ manager ] w'uyu muhanzikazi kandi ateganya kuva mu muziki mu minsi iri imbere .
Ati """" Hari hashize umwaka n'igice kuva ubwo Britney nanjye twavuganaga akambwira ko ashaka gufata ikiruhuko .
Uyu munsi namenye ko Britney ateganya kureka umuziki burundu mu buryo bweruye .
Nari nahawe akazi ku busabe bwe ngomba kumufasha mu by'umuziki ndetse no kumushyigikira mu rugendo muri muzika . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko atakomeza kumubera umujyanama kandi yararetse umuziki , ati """" Ndetse nka manager we mu muziki , nizera ko biri mu nyungu ze kuba nareka inshingano zanjye kuko zitagikenewe .
Mwakire iyi baruwa nko kwegura kwanjye ku mugaragaro . """"
Iyi baruwa yanayigeneye abarimo se w'uyu muhanzikazi , Jamie Spears , uri mu bakurikirana imitungo ye n'umunyamategeko w'uyu muhanzikazi Jodi Montgomery .
Rudolph ntiyigeze agaragara mu bacunga ibintu byose bya Britney birimo no kumenya ubuzima bwe bwa buri munsi uko yitwara [ Conservatorship ] , ibintu uyu muhanzikazi aheruka kuvuga mu rukiko ko atagikeneye ndetse akanavuga ko abifata nko kumuhohotera , ahubwo yari umujyanama mu by'umuziki gusa .
Rudolph yakoranye na Spears guhera mu 1995 ndetse anamufasha mu muziki ku buryo yabaye icyamamare kurusha uko bahuye ameze .
Uyu mugabo yanafashije abandi bahanzi barimo itsinda rya Aerosmith , Miley Cyrus , Justin Timberlake , Backstreet Boys , 98 Degrees , O - Town , will . i . am , Toni Braxton , Nicole Scherzinger , Swizz Beatz na Kim Petras .
Muri Gicurasi 2019 , Britney Spears , yahagaritse kongera kuririmbira ku rubyiniro mu bitaramo ndetse icyo gihe hari amakuru yavugaga ko bishobora kuba bitazongera kubaho ukundi .
Yari afite ibitaramo muri Gashyantare ariko ntiyabyitabira kubera impamvu yavuze ko zirimo n'iz'uburwayi .
Hagati ya 2007 na 2008 , Britney Spears yafashwe n'uburwayi bwo kwigunga no guhuzagurika mu bwonko bwatumye se aba umwe mu bakurikirana ubuzima bwe bwa buri munsi , akanamufasha gucunga umutungo we .
Amaze iminsi mu manza aburana na we ku bijyanye no kongera gusubirana uburenganzira ku gucunga imitungo ye .
Sosiyete ya Bessemer Trust yari isanzwe ireberera inyungu mu bijyanye n'imitungo uyu mukobwa ifatanyije na se iheruka gusohora itangazo igaragaza ko itagishaka kumukurikiranira imitungo ndetse umucamanza wa Los Angeles ahita abibemerera .
Britney Spears afite imyaka 39 , ni umwe mu bahanzi b'ibihangange ku Isi mu njyana ya Pop .
Ubuhamya bw'ababanye na Mukeshabatware uheruka kwitaba Imana .
Ni mu muhango wo gusezera uyu musaza wabaye kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki 6 Nyakanga mu rugo iwe ku Gisozi ahari hateraniye abantu bake barimo bamwe mu bo basenganaga n'abandi bakinanye amakinamico .
Mu buhamya bwinshi bwatanzwe , benshi bagaragaje ko Mukeshabatware yari umuntu ugira umutima wo gufasha , agakunda Imana n'abantu kandi akitanga cyane mu byo akora .
Pasiteri Hirali wabanye nawe cyane , yavuze ku rugendo rwo gukizwa rwe anakomoza ku kuba we n'umugore we baraviriye mu mubiri ku itariki imwe .
Ati """" Nk'umuntu wamusuye atarakizwa .
Bari batuye ku Muhima hariya imbere y'ibagiro .
Dusengerayo .
Twamenyanye bivuye kuri madamu nawe witabye Imana kuri 30 Ugushyingo 2007 .
Iyo tariki ni imwe bagiye bitabiraho Imana byatumye njya musura , ariko byasabaga kwitonda iyo hazagamo ijambo ry'Imana . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko kugira ngo akizwe byafashe igihe kinini cyane ko yari umuntu utarapfaga kwemera ikintu , ahubwo buri cyose yabanzaga kukibazaho ibibazo byinshi .
Ati """" Kumuganiriza byasabaga ubwenge bwinshi .
Akantu kose akabaza .
Byansabaga urugendo rurerure .
Nyuma twaje guhuza tukajya tuganira ijambo ry'Imana . """"
"""" Naje kwiyiriza iminsi itatu musengera , nsengera madamu waje kwitaba Imana ndetse no gusengera itorero .
Numvise ijwi rimbwira ko azabona ijuru .
Hari umwana witwa Lambert yari arwaye ahiga umuhigo ko nakira azakorera Imana , abonye bibaye ahita ayiyegurira . """"
Nsanzurwimo Anastase wasenganye na Mukeshabatware yavuze ko yabatijwe ku wa 19 Ukuboza mu 1998 , mu myaka 23 yamaze akijijwe akagaragaza urukundo mu murimo w'Imana no mu bantu .
Ati """" Amaze gukizwa yashyigikiye agakiza .
Yakundaga gusenga n'amateraniro cyane cyane aya nibature adashoborwa na benshi .
Byamuviriyemo umusaruro kuko yagize iherezo ryiza .
Icya kabiri ni ukugaragariza Imana urukundo .
Yari afite indangagaciro yo gukunda abantu bose .
Akabakunda , akabashyigikira [ . . . ] yagize iherezo ryiza . """"
Umukobwa wa Mukeshabatware witwa Bonne Marie Ntakwasa yavuze ko se yagiraga umuhate cyane mu kazi ndetse bigatuma agenda ahabwa amashimwe atandukanye kubera ubwitange bwe .
Yavuze ko ibyo se asize ari indorerwamo we n'abandi benshi bazajya bamureberamo .
Ati """" Ibikorwa yakoze n'indorerwamo twese twamureberaho .
Yari umukirisito ukunda umurimo w'Imana akanakunda kuririmba cyane no gucuranga ndetse n'ubwo nta korali yabayemo yagiye atera inkunga abaririmbyi benshi . """"
"""" We n'umufasha we baranzwe no gukunda Imana no kwitangira umurimo w'Imana .
Yarangwaga no kutagira uburyarya ndetse n'urukundo rwinshi .
Tuzamwibukira ku gukunda imfubyi n'abapfakazi agafasha abatishoboye abarihira amashuri ndetse akanabishyura ubwisungane mu kwivuza . """"
Perezida wa Korali Rehoboth yagiye aba hafi yavuze ko ashima Imana ko uyu musaza yamuhaye iherezo ryiza .
Murizaboro Marie Antoinette bakoranye akina ikinamico yavuze ko bigoye kubona icyo yavuga kuri Mukeshabatware kubera ibigwi bye gusa yemeza ko abo bakoranye yababereye inkingi ikomeye .
Ati """" Twe ababanye nawe tugatangirana nawe mu Indamutsa no muri Musekeweya yatubereye inkingi ikomeye , tuzajya tumwibukira kuri byinshi . """"
"""" Yari afite urukundo mu murimo no kuri twebwe .
Ikintu tuzahora tumwibukiraho ni ukwitanga .
Yabaga anafite intege nke ntabigaragaze .
Ndahamya ko mu ijuru bamwakiriye . """"
Mukeshabatware yitabye Imana ku wa 30 Kamena 2021 , aguye mu bitaro byitiwe Umwami Faisal .
Uyu mugabo wari mu bazwi cyane mu myidagaduro yo mu Rwanda yamenyekanye nka Mbirikanyi , Rutaganira muri """" Musekeweya """" n'andi mazina mu makinamico atandukanye yagiye akina ndetse agakundwa bihambaye n'abatari bake .
Kuri uyu wa Kabiri tariki 6 Nyakanga 2021 nibwo habaye umuhango wo guherekeza mu cyubahiro Mukeshabatware .
Umuhango wo guherekeza mu cyubahiro Mukeshabatware , watangiriye kwa muganga ubwo abo mu muryango we bajyaga gufata umurambo mu bitaro byitiriwe Umwami Faisal .

Umuryango wa Nyakwigendera wabanje gufata umwanya muto wo kumusezera mu cyubahiro , mbere y'uko inshuti n'abandi batumiwe muri uyu muhango bamusezeraga bwa nyuma .
Mukeshabatware yitabye Imana ku wa 30 Kamena 2021 , aguye mu bitaro byitiwe Umwami Faisal .
Uyu mugabo wari mu bazwi cyane mu myidagaduro yo mu Rwanda yamenyekanye nka Mbirikanyi , Rusisibiranya n'andi mazina mu makinamico atandukanye yagiye akina ndetse agakundwa bihambaye n'abatari bake .
Mukeshabatware yavukiye i Nyaruguru mu 1950 ku ngoma y'Umwami Rudahigwa .
Yasoje amashuri abanza mu 1965 atsinze ikizamini ahabwa amahirwe yo kujya kwiga muri St André .
Akirangiza Icyiciro rusange cy'amashuri yisumbuye yabaye umwarimu mu karere k'iwabo icyakora ntiyahamara igihe kuko mu 1970 yahise yinjira mu gisirikare .
Yigeze kubwira IGIHE ati """" Nyuma y'uko Inyenzi ziteye muri Nshiri bahise batujyana mu gisirikare ku ngufu njya muri ESO ( Ecole des Sous Officiers ) kwiga , sinahatinze kuko namazemo amezi atatu nkora ikizamini cyo kwandika mu binyamakuru mba ndagitsinze mpita njya mu Bubiligi . """"
Mukeshabatware avuga ko mu Bubiligi yahamaze umwaka umwe n'amezi atandatu .
Ati """" Mvuyeyo ndi mu batangije icapiro rya gisirikare . """"
Mu icapiro rya gisirikare yahakoraga yarahawe ipeti rya Kaporali .
Mukeshabatware avuga ko mu 1973 ari umwe mu bacapye amafoto y'uwari Perezida Habyarimana ubwo yari amaze guhirika ubutegetsi bwa Kayibanda .
Igisirikare Mukeshabatware yagikoreye imyaka umunani aza kukivamo agaye umushahara muto bahabwaga icyo gihe .
Yahawe akazi kenshi iwabo ariko kuko yari akeneye akaruhuko agenda akanga , icyakora abo biganye mu Bubiligi bakoraga mu icapiro rya ORINFOR mu 1979 basabye ubuyobozi ko bwamutumaho akaza kubafasha .
Yatangiye mu icapiro rya ORINFOR mu 1980 .
Mu 1982 Mukeshabatware yinjiye mu itsinda ryakinaga amakinamico ya ORINFOR ryaje guhabwa izina rya Indamutsa .

Urujijo ku bukwe bwa Ykee Benda n'umuhanzikazi Lydia Jazmine .
Mu Cyumweru gishize nibwo iyi nkuru yatangiye kuvugwa cyane nyuma y'uko aba bahanzi bashyize hanze amafoto agaragaza Lydia Jazmine yagiye kwerekana iwabo Ykee Benda .
Ni igikorwa cyasamiwe hejuru n'itangazamakuru ryo muri Uganda bamwe bahamya ko aba bahanzi bakoze ubukwe , mu gihe ku rundi ruhande hari abavuga ko ari ugushaka gusasira indirimbo baba bateganya gusohora mu minsi iri imbere .
Mu gihe bari bakibaza kuri ibi bibazo , aba bahanzi bongeye kuzamura impaka ku mbuga nkoranyambaga no mu itangazamakuru ryo muri Uganda ubwo basohoraga amafoto y'imihango yo gusaba no gukwa .
Icyakora nubwo hari abahamya ko aba bahanzi baba barakoze ubukwe , ku rundi ruhande hari abahamya ko ari umupango wabo wo gushaka kumenyekanisha indirimbo izasohoka mu minsi iri imbere .
Byinshi mu binyamakuru bihakana amakuru yo gukundana kw'aba bahanzi , bishingira ku kuba atari abantu basanzwe ari inshuti .
Ykee Benda na Lydia Jazmine basanzwe ari abahanzi bakomeye muri Uganda , ariko bose bahurije ku kuba ababyeyi babo bafite inkomoko mu Rwanda , byanatumye ubwo bifotozaga amafoto yo gusaba no gukwa bari bakenyeye Kinyarwanda .
Lion Gaga yashyize hanze amashusho ya """" Intare """" yanditse akomoye ku bwitange bw'Inkotanyi
Ku wa 4 Nyakanga u Rwanda rwizihiza umunsi wo Kwibohora , aho hongera kwibukwa no guha icyubahiro abitanze bose kugira ngo igihugu Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 ihagarikwe .
Ibikorwa byakoze na FPR Inkotanyi yagize uruhare rukomeye mu kubohora igihugu byagiye bikora benshi ku mutima ndetse bigatuma abahanzi bamwe bahanga bazirahira .
Lion Gaga ari muri abo ndetse afite iyo yise """" Intare . """"
Yabwiye IGIHE ko ubutumwa yayikoze ashaka gushimira """" Inkotanyi """" no kwerekana ubwitange bwazo .
Ati """" Nayikoze nshaka kwerekana ko ubutwari bw'ababohoye igihugu batweretse bwatubereye umurage . """"
Avuga ko akenshi iyo agiye hanze y'u Rwanda abona ko igihugu cy'u Rwanda kimaze kwiyubaka no kugera ku rundi rwego ugereranyije n'ahandi yagiye agera .
Muri iyi ndirimbo ya Gaga hari aho aririmba ati """" Turi Intare duhagaze bwuma , turi Intare turi intavogerwa turakomeye .
Twe turi ruti , turi rutikura , turakomeye [ . . . ] """"
Lion Gaga yakoze indirimbo zitandukanye zirimo """" Rekura amazi , """" """" Uhoraho , """" """" Ba intwari """" n'izindi nyinshi .
Lion Gaga ubusanzwe witwa Gaga Jean Bosco afite izindi ndirimbo zikoze mu njyana ya Reggae ndetse afite album yuzuye .
Uyu musore w'imyaka 33 , yatangiye umuziki mu 2012 .
Mu buryo bw'amajwi iyi ndirimbo ye nshya yakozwe na Bob Pro muri The Sounds naho amashusho yakozwe na Eliel Sando .
Muri aya mashusho yakoresheje imyenda ya mukotanyi nk'imyenda yibutsa ishusho y'inkotanyi zihagarika Jenoside .
Ni umwana bareranywe !
Ndanda yambitse impeta umukobwa bagiye kurushinga .
Nizeyimana wirinze gutangaza amazina y'umukobwa bitegura kurushinga , aganira na IGIHE yahamije ko ari umwe mu bo babyirukanye .
Ati """" Ni umwe mu rungano twabyirukanye ku Gisozi aho nakuriye , twakundanye kuva cyera ahubwo ni kumwe igihe kiba kitaragera ngo usobanukirwe uwawe . """"
Bitewe n'ingamba zikomeye zo kwirinda Covid - 19 u Rwanda rurimo , Nizeyimana yavuze ko atahita avuga gahunda ihamye y'ubukwe bwe .
Nizeyimana Alphonse Ndanda uherutse gusezera umupira yabaye umunyezamu wakinnye mu makipe akomeye nka Rayon Sports , Mukura VS , AS Kigali n'izindi .
Mu minsi ishize nibwo hatangiye kwamamazwa film """" Intandaro y'Ikibi """" yakinnyemo , icyakora avuga ko atari ibintu agiye kugira umwuga ahubwo yayikinnyemo ashyigikira inshuti ye .
Britney Spears mu ntambara ikomeye imuganisha ku kwigenga .
Aheruka kubwira urukiko byinshi bijyanye n'ihohoterwa yakorewe ndetse anatunga agatoki se James """" Jamie """" Parnell Spears ufite uburenganzira bwo kumugenzurira imitungo no kumukurikirana mu muziki ko yagiye amufata nabi , bigatuma ahura n'ihungabana .
The New Yorker yatangaje ko nyina w'uyu muhanzikazi witwa Lynne Spears , kubera ibibazo umukobwa we yagiye anyuramo yagiye agira ibyiyumviro bitandukanye .
Ati """" Nagiye ngira ibyiyumviro bivanze kuri buri kimwe .
Ntabwo nzi icyo gutekereza .
Ni umubabaro mwinshi n'impungenge nyinshi . """"
Yanavuze ko umukobwa we mbere ho umunsi umwe ngo yumvikane mu rukiko atanga ubuhamya , yabanje guhamagara Polisi akishinganisha avuga ko akorerwa ihohoterwa mu kumugenzurira imitungo n'ibindi bijyanye n'ubuzima bwe .
Se wa Britney aheruka guhakana ibyo umukobwa amushinja birimo no kuba yaranze ko abyarana n'umusore bakundana .
Nyamara mu minsi ishize sosiyete ya Bessemer Trust yari isanzwe ireberera inyungu mu bijyanye n'imitungo uyu mukobwa ifatanyije na se iheruka gusohora itangazo igaragaza ko itagishaka kumukurikiranira imitungo ndetse umucamanza wa Los Angeles ahita abibemerera .
Mu nyandiko People yabonye yandikiye urukiko , iyi sosiyete yavuze ko nyuma y'ubuhamya bwa Britney yahisemo kuba ivuye mu bamureberera inyungu .
Muri Mata uyu mwaka Britney yari yasabye ko yazaburanira mu ruhame ndetse ku wa 23 Kamena biza kuba aho yatanze ubuhamya bwababaje benshi bakavuga ko akwiriye guhabwa ubwigenge .
Nyuma yaho iyi sosiyete ikuyemo akayo , se wa Britney niwe usigaye areberera inyungu umukobwa we ariko bitegerejwe ko hari icyo urukiko ruzanzura mu gihe kiri imbere .
Kuva Britney yatanga ubuhamya bwe mu rukiko , abantu batandukanye barimo ibyamamare bagaragaje ko ibyo yakorewe bidakwiriye cyane cyane ubwo yavugaga ko se amugenzura kugeza aho yamubujije kubyarana n'umukunzi we .
Nka Justin Timberlake yaranditse ati """" Nyuma y'ibintu byose twabonye tugomba gushyigikira Britney kuri iyi nshuro .
Twirengagije ahahise hacu ibyiza cyangwa se ibibi ndetse tukirengagiza uko igihe gishize kingana .
Ibiri kumubaho ntabwo bikwiye .
Nta mugore ukwiriye kubuzwa uburenganzira ku mubiri we .
Nta muntu ukwiriye kubuzwa uburenganzira kugeza aho yaka uburenganzira kuri buri kintu yakoreye cyane . """"
Abandi barimo Mariah Carey , Rose McGowan , Missy Elliott , Meghan McCain , Brandy , Khloé Kardashian , Halsey n'abandi benshi bagaragaje ko Britney Spears akwiriye kwigenga .
Britney byatangiye agenzurwa na se by'igihe gito nyuma yo kugaragaza ko yaba yaragize ibibazo byo mu mutwe mu 2007 .
Kuva mu 2008 kugeza mu 2019 se niwe wakurikiranaga ibikorwa bye byose birimo gufata imyanzuro itandukanye mu buzima , gusurwa no gusura , ibijyanye n'amasezerano ashobora gukora n'ibindi .
Muri Nzeri 2019 yasimbuwe by'agateganyo na Jodi Montgomery kubera ibibazo by'ubuzima ariko muri Mutarama 2020 James """" Jamie """" Parnell Spears arongera asubirana umwanya we .
Ubusanzwe se wa Britney yafatanyaga na sosiyete ya Bessemer Trust mu kumureberera inyungu none yakuyemo akayo .
Don Cheadle yarushinze na Bridgid Coulter nyuma y'imyaka 28 bakundana .
Cheadle w'imyaka 56 mu kiganiro aheruka kugirana na """" The Ellen DeGeneres Show """" yabwiye Wanda Sykes wari ukiyoboye ko we na Bridgid Coulter ufite imyaka 52 bari bamaze igihe kinini bakundana , bafashe icyemezo cyo kurushinga .
Sykes yavuze ko Cheadle ko yamubwiye ko yarushinze umwaka ushize agatungurwa .
Ati """" Waranyandikiye mu ntangiro z'umwaka umbwira ko warushinze .
Naravugaga nti igihe cy'icyorezo gitumye Don na Bridgid barushinga . """"
Cheadle mu kumusubiza yagize ati """" Yego .
Ndabumva cyane ko twari tumaranye imyaka 28 dukundana mbere yo kurushinga .
Ntabwo nakurenganya . """"
Aba bombi bakundanye guhera mu 1992 .
Bafitanye abana babiri b'abakobwa barimo uwitwa Ayana ndetse na Imani .
Don Cheadle ni umwe mu bakomeye muri sinema ya Hollywood .
Yamamaye muri filime zitandukanye zirimo Hamburger Hill , Colors , Blue Dress , Captain America : Civil War , Avengers : Infinity War , Captain Marvel n'izindi nyinshi .
By'umwihariko bamwe mu banyarwanda bamumenye ubwo yakinaga muri filime """" Hotel Rwanda """" irata ubutwari mpimbano bwa Paul Rusesabagina .
Mico The Best yambitse impeta umukunzi we ; Reba amafoto y'uburanga bwe .
Ku mugoroba wo kuri Cyumweru tariki 4 Nyakanga 2021 nibwo uyu muhango wabaye mu ibanga rikomeye , nta inshuti z'uyu muhanzi zari zihari kuko imihuro y'abantu benshi ibujijwe muri iki gihe .
Amakuru IGIHE ifite ni uko aba bombi bemeranyije kurushinga nyuma y'iminsi mike uyu mukobwa yerekanye Mico The Best iwabo , umuhango nawo wagizwe ibanga .
Uyu mukobwa bagiye kubana , twamenye ko yitwa Clarisse .
Ntabwo azwi cyane mu myidagaduro yo mu Rwanda gusa yigeze kujya amurika imideli nubwo byamaze igihe gito .

Reba filime ya Bad Rama uyu mukobwa agaragaramo .
Bashimye ibyagezweho biyemeza kubisigasira : Ubutumwa bw'ibyamamare ku munsi wo # Kwibohora27 .
Kuri iyi nshuro u Rwanda rwizihiza uyu munsi ku nshuro ya 27 Abanyarwanda mu nzego zitandukanye bishimira ibyiza igihugu cyagezeho nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Uyu munsi abantu batandukanye bagaragaza imbamutima zabo , bamwe mu byamamare baganiriye na IGIHE bagaragaje ko bishimiye aho u Rwanda rugeze kandi biteguye gukomeza kurwubaka .
Mu butumwa bwabo bikije ku gushima ingabo zitangiye kubohora igihugu no kugiteza imbere .
Nyampinga w'Umurage 2021 , Ishimwe Sonia , yifurije Abanyarwanda umunsi mwiza wo Kwibohora abibutsa ko bakwiye guharanira kwiyubaka .
Ati """" Imyaka 27 irashize u Rwanda rubohowe .
Turazirikana umunsi twaharuriwe inzira nshya ubwo Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yahagarikwaga .
Abatubohoye bari bazi neza ko kwibohora ariryo pfundo ry'ibyishimo , natwe biduha inshingano zo gukomeza gukora . """"
Umuhanzi akaba n'umwanditsi w'indirimbo , Semivumbi Daniel [ Danny Vumbi ] , yavuze ko ukwibohora nyakuri Abanyarwanda bakwiriye ari ukugena inzira nziza abato bazanyuramo .
Ati """" Ubutumwa nagenera Abanyarwanda ni uko kwibohora by'ukuri ari ugutegura inzira abato bazanyuramo mu bihe bizaza hagamijwe kudasubira inyuma ku ntambwe imaze guterwa .
Twese duharanire uburenganzira bukwiriye umunyagihugu mu gihugu cye duteza imbere u Rwanda rwacu . """"
Umukinnyi wa Filime , Niyitegeka Gratien uzwi nka Seburikoko , yasabye Abanyarwanda gufatanyiriza hamwe mu guhangana n'icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyugarije Isi n'u Rwanda .
Ati """" Mu gihe twizihiza Umunsi wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 ni ingenzi kuzirikana ko igihugu cyugarijwe n'icyorezo cya Covid - 19 . """"
"""" Turwane urugamba rwo kurengera ubuzima bwacu n'ubw'abandi .
Dukurikize , tunakangurira abandi kubahiriza ingamba zo kurwanya Covid - 19 .
Niryo shimwe rikwiye guhabwa Intwari zarwaniye igihugu muri iki gihe . """"
Urubyiruko rwasabwe kudakerensa amahirwe rwahawe
Nyampinga w'u Rwanda mu 2009 , Bahati Grace , yasabye urubyiruko aho ruri ku Isi hose guharanira icyateza imbere igihugu cyabo .
Yagize ati """" Ndifuriza buri Munyarwanda wese umunsi mwiza wo Kwibohora ku nshuro ya 27 . """"
"""" Ndakangurira buri wese aho ari hose ku Isi , cyane cyane urubyiruko dore ko ari rwo mbaraga z'igihugu , kwirinda icyadusubiza inyuma icyo ari cyo cyose .
Duharanire kubaho neza twirinda gushyira imbere inyungu zacu , ahubwo dushaka icyateza imbere igihugu cyatwibarutse . """"
Umuraperi Abayizera Grace wamamaye nka Young Grace , yashimiye Inkotanyi ubutwari zagize bwo kubohora u Rwanda , asaba urubyiruko kurinda ibyagezweho .
Ati """" Turashimira Ingabo z'Igihugu ku butwari n'ubwitange zagize mu rugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda n'Abanyarwanda .
Ndasaba urubyiruko gusigasira ibyagezweho no guharanira gukomeza kwigira . """"
Ikinyarwanda cyasabiwe umwihariko ku Banyarwanda baba hanze
Umuhanzikazi Teta Diana yifurije Abanyarwanda umunsi mwiza wo kwibohora ndetse asaba abatazi ikinyarwanda kucyiga kuko ari ikirango cyabo .
Ati """" Ndifuriza Abanyarwanda aho bari hose Umunsi mwiza wo Kwibohora .
Dufite igihugu cyiza , giteye ishema kurata no mu mahanga . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko """" abatazi Ikinyarwanda bacyige , ni wo musingi w'ibindi byinshi twifuza kubaka imbere . """"
Umukinnyi wa Filime , Uwihoreye Jean Bosco Moustapha [ Ndimbati ] , yagarutse ku butwari bwaranze Inkotanyi ndetse asaba Abanyarwanda kurinda ibyagezweho .
Ati """" Kwibohora ni umunsi ukomeye cyane kuko hari ababohoye igihugu ku bw'ubwitange !
Buri Munyarwanda akwiye kubiha agaciro , akumva ko ari ikintu gikomeye . """"
"""" Abanyarwanda bareke dusigasire ibyagezweho kugira ngo Kwibohora kwacu kutazasubira inyuma .
Dukwiye kubiraga abana n'abuzukuru bacu kugira ngo bazature mu gihugu cyiza . """"
Umukinnyi wa Filime , Mugisha Clapton , wamamaye nka Kibonge yasabye Abanyarwanda gukomeza kurinda no gusigasira ibyagezweho .
Ati """" Ndasaba Abanyarwanda gukomeza gukunda igihugu , kugikorera no kukirwanira ishyaka kuko cyaduhaye ijambo . Twaribohoye .
Hanyuma natwe dusigasire ibyagezweho dukomeza gukorera u Rwanda rwacu . """"
Umuhanzi Emmy ukorera umuziki we muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika , yibukije Abanyarwanda ko kwibohora ari igihe cyiza cyo gusubiza amaso inyuma no gukomeza iterambere .
Yagize ati """" Kwibohora ni igihe cyiza cyo gusubiza amaso inyuma tukibuka aho igihugu cyavuye naho kigeze ubu , kugira ngo bidutere imbaraga zo kwiyubaka no kubaka ejo hacu hazaza heza . """"
Bagaragaje ko """" umugore """" ari uw'agaciro mu iterambere ry'igihugu
Umuhanzikazi Uwayezu Ariel uzwi nka Ariel Wayz , yavuze ko anyuzwe n'uburyo u Rwanda rwiyubatse cyane rugaha ijambo umugore .
Yagize ati """" Kwibohora27 kuri njye bisobanuye kwibuka ibitambo byose byatanze ngo igihugu cyacu kibe kiri aho kiri ubu , ibi bintera umurava wo kugira umusanzu ntanga mu kubaka ejo hazaza h'igihugu cyanjye . """"
"""" Nk'umukobwa ukiri muto ni iby'agaciro gakomeye kuba mu gihugu aho umugore yahawe ijambo , nishimiye kuba mu gihugu aho abaturage bafite uburenganzira bungana .
Nshimishijwe no kuba mu Rwanda rwibohoye . """"
Nyampinga w'u Rwanda wa 2016 , Mutesi Jolly , yatanze u Rwanda imyato asaba urubyiruko kurinda ibyo igihugu kimaze kugeraho .
Ati """" U Rwanda rurishimira ibyiza rwagezeho , igihugu gitekanye muri Afurika , igihugu gifite umwanya wa kabiri mu biri ku isonga muri Afurika , kiri ku mwanya wa kabiri mu koroshya ishoramari muri Afurika , kiri ku mwanya wa cyenda mu guha ijambo umugore . """"
"""" Igihugu kiri mu bifite ubuyobozi bwiza ku Isi , igihugu cya karindwi ku Isi mu gucunga umutekano wo kuri internet muri Afurika , igihugu cyiza cyiyubatse kandi gikataje mu iterambere . """"
Yakomeje asaba urubyiruko kurinda ibyagezweho no gutanga umusanzu warwo mu iterambere ry'u Rwanda .
Rita Kagaju yasohoye album ye ya mbere yahurijemo abahanzi bakomeye .
Iyi album uyu mukobwa yayise """" Sweet Thunder """" igizwe n'indirimbo 18 .
Izi ndirimbo zirimo iyitwa """" Intro , """" """" Mean It , """" """" Have """" , """" Always """" yahuriyemo na Jali , """" Ndeka , """" """" Loving """" yakoranye na Mazimpaka Prime , """" Good Times """" yakoranye na Andy Bumuntu & Kevin Skaa , """" X """" na """" Ok
"""" yakoranye na Kivumbi King , """" Hey , """" """" Done and Through """" yakoranye na Angel Mutoni na """" Try """" ye na B - Threy .
Hari kandi """" Better """" yakoranye na Kenny Sol , """" Ne T'inquiète Pas """" , """" Close , """" """" Grateful """" yakoranye na Jumper Keellu , """" I'll Be Here """" ndetse na """" You """" ye na Mike Kayihura basubiyemo mu buryo bwa Acoustic .
Izi ndirimbo ziri kuboneka ubu ku mbuga zicururizwaho nka Spotify , iTunes , YouTube n'izindi .
Rita Kagaju yabwiye IGIHE ko iyi album yahisemo kuyita """" Sweet thunder """" ashaka kugaragaza ishusho ye nk'umuhanzikazi ariko ashaka no kugaraga inkuru 16 ziyiriho .
Avuga ko ari itangiriro z'ibyo yifuzaga .
Ati """" Iyi album ni itangiriro ry'ibyo nifuza gukora mu muziki munyarwanda .
Ni intambwe yanjye ya mbere kandi nashakaga gukora umuziki utandukanye n'usanzwe uzwi mu Rwanda .
Indirimbo zose ziriho zirihariye .
Ndabararikira Kumva imvange y'Ikinyarwanda n'izindi nganzo mvamahanga kuko ni kimwe mu bintu nagerageje gukora kuri Iyi album . """"
Yavuze ko amasomo yagiyemo muri Amerika umwaka ushize atazabangamira ibikorwa bye bya muzika .
Ateganya kugaruka mu Rwanda mu mpera z'uyu mwaka .
Indirimbo zirimo """" No offense , """" """" Send flowers , """" """" Gukunda , """" na """" Jamaa """" zamenyekanye cyane z'uyu mukobwa ntabwo ziri kuri iyi album , kuko igizwe n'izindi nshya .
Ange Rita Kagaju afite ubuhanga mu kuririmba n'umwihariko wo kuba abasha kubijyanisha no kucuranga gitari , bidasanzwe ku bakobwa benshi mu Rwanda .
Ni umukobwa w'imyaka 21 , uvuka mu Karere ka Rwamagana mu Ntara y'Iburasirazuba .
Avuka mu bana icyenda akaba ari uwa karindwi .
Yatangiye kuririmba mu 2015 yiga mu wa Gatatu w'amashuri yisumbuye .
Yasoje amashuri yisumbuye mu 2018 mu ishami ry'Imibare , Ubugenge n'Ubumenyi bw'Isi mu ishuri rya Rwamagana Lutheran School .
Ushaka kumva indirimbo ziri kuri iyi album wakanda hano :
Mu myambaro y'amabara ya gisirikare , abarimo ibyamamare basuye ahatangirijwe urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda .
Mu rwego rwo guhugura Abanyarwanda by'umwihariko urubyiruko , ku mateka yaranze urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda , Sosiyete itembereza ba Mukerarugendo , """" MB Simba Safaris Rwanda LTD , """" yateguye urugendoshuri rwibanze kuri aya mateka .
Ni urugendo rwitabiriwe n'abantu batandukanye biganjemo abafite amazina akomeye mu myidagaduro y'u Rwanda .
Bamwe mu bazwi bifatanyije n'urundi rubyiruko muri uru rugendo harimo ; Muyoboke Alex , David Bayingana , Ntalindwa Diogene benshi bazi nka Atome , Kirenga Saphina uzwi muri sinema nyarwanda , Umuhanzi Cyusa Ibrahim n'abandi batandukanye .
Mu gutangira uru rugendo , abarwitabiriye wabonaga bagaragaza amatsiko adasanzwe yo kumenya uko urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu rwatangiye , icyakora rwagiye kurangira buri wese afite amatsiko y'igice cya kabiri cyarwo kizaba mu Ukwakira 2021 .
Iby'uru rugendo ntabwo byari ibintu byoroshye bitewe n'ibihe Igihugu kirimo byo kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Covid - 19 .
Muyoboke Alex uri mu bateguye uru rugendo , yabwiye IGIHE ko bafite ibyishimo by'uko ibyo batekereje byagezweho , anashimira buri rwego rwababaye hafi .
Ati """" Si ibintu byari byoroshye ariko turashimira inzego zose zagize uruhare mu kugira ngo iki gikorwa gikunde .
Uyu munsi twasuye igice cya mbere cy'Urugamba rwo kwibohora , ubutaha tuzagenda twihugura no ku bindi bice . """"
Igice cya mbere cy'ahabereye urugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu , uru rubyiruko rwasuye ni ku mupaka wa Kagitumba utandukanya u Rwanda na Uganda .
Muri aka gace hagaragara amateka y'uburyo Ingabo za RPA zatangije urugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu ariko zikagorwa cyane no kubura abari abayobozi babo ba mbere kubera imiterere y'aho hantu .
Igihe ingabo za RPA zageraga i Kagitumba tariki ya 1 Ukwakira 1990 , Maj . Gen . Fred Rwigema wari uyoboye urugamba , yasobanuye mu magambo make impamvu yarwo , avuga ko mu mateka y'u Rwanda ubuyobozi bubi ari bwo bwazanye amacakubiri n'ibindi bibazo byose byayogoje igihugu , kandi ko nta wundi wabibohora Abanyarwanda , uretse
Abanyarwanda bakunda igihugu .
Iki gihe yasabye abarwanyi bari umwe kwiyambura inyenyeri za gisirikare bari bavanye muri Uganda bazita mu mazi , abizeza ko izo bazakorera muri urwo rugamba arizo zizaba ari izabo .
Yahise atanga amabwiriza y'uburyo urugamba rugiye kugenda ubundi aha amahirwe uwumva atiteguye ko yakwisubirira muri Uganda .
Nyuma y'umunsi umwe urugamba rutangiye , ku wa 2 Ukwakira 1990 Maj . Gen . Rwigema yahise agwa ku rugamba i Kagitumba ho mu Karere ka Nyagatare arashwe n'imodoka yari itwaye ingabo za Leta zasakiranye n'iza RPA .
Nyuma y'urupfu rwa Rwigema , Maj Gen Paul Kagame yahise ava muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe z'Amerika ( USA ) aho yari yaragiye kwiga , maze akomeza kuyobora urugamba rwo kubohora u Rwanda .
Aka gace uru rubyiruko rwasuye kabitse kandi amateka y'abandi basirikare bari bakomeye muri RPA batahiriwe n'iminsi ya mbere y'urugamba barimo Major Peter Bayingana na Major Chris Bunyenyezi .
Nyuma yo gucengerwa n'amateka y'Igihugu cyabo , uru rubyiruko rwakomereje urugendo rwabo ku nkengero z'Ikiyaga cya Muhazi ( Muhazi beach resort ) , aho bataramiye mu ndirimbo zo kwibohora .
Bacurangirwaga na DJ Diallo ndetse na Dj Rugamba umuziki bumvaga bifashishije ama Ecouteurs , ibimenyerewe nka Silent Disco .
Usibye aba bavangaga imiziki na David Bayingana wari umushyushyarugamba , Cyusa Ibrahim nawe yasusurukije abarenga 60 bitabiriye uru rugendo .
Urugamba rwo kubohora Igihugu rwamaze imyaka irenga ine kuko rwarangiye tariki 4 Nyakanga 1994 ubwo ingabo zari iza RPA zabohoraga u Rwanda zikanahagarika Jenoside yakorerwaga Abatutsi .
Quentin Terantino ari kurebana ay'ingwe n'umukobwa wa Bruce Lee umushinja gushinyagura .
Iyi filime imaze imyaka ibiri igiye hanze ntabwo yavuzweho rumwe ikijya hanze kubera igice kirimo kigaragaza Brad Pitt ukina ari Cliff Booth akubita Mike Moh ukina ari Bruce Lee .
Benshi babifashe nko gutesha agaciro no gushinyagurira uyu mugabo wabaye igihangange muri sinema ziganjemo izirimo imikino njya rugamba .
Yitabye Imana mu 1973 .
Bamwe mu batarashimishijwe no kugaragazwa kwa Bruce Lee gutya muri iyi filime harimo n'umukobwa we Shannon Lee , wabifashe nko kubahuka no gushinyagurira se .
Aka gace katumye mu Bushinwa banga iyi filime ndetse bifuza ko gakurwamo .
Ariko Tarantino wayoboye iyi filime yanze ko gakurwamo avuga ko n'ubundi mu buzima busanzwe Bruce Lee yari """" umuntu w'ibikabyo ukunda kwishyira hejuru . """"
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na """" The Joe Rogan Experience """" ubwo yamamazaga agatabo gashamikiye kuri iyi filime , Quentin Terantino yavuze ko yumva koko umukobwa wa Bruce Lee ko afite ishingiro ariko akihaniza abandi bamugizeho ikibazo .
Ati """" Nshobora kubyumva impamvu umukobwa we afite ikibazo .
Ni umubyeyi we .
Nabyumva pe . """"
Agatabo kiswe """" Hollywood """" gashamikiye kuri iyi filime igaragaza Bruce Lee akubitwa na Cliff Booth yiswe """" """" Once Upon a Time . . . in Hollywood """" kagiye hanze ku wa 29 Kamena 2021 .
Safi Madiba yasohoye indirimbo """" Remember me """" yifashishijemo umunyamideri wo muri Eritrea .
Uyu muhanzi nubwo atifuje kuvuga amafaranga byamutwaye kugira ngo uyu munyamideri yemere kujya mu mashusho y'indirimbo ye , yavuze ko bitari ibintu byoroshye cyane ko asanzwe ari umukobwa uzwi iwabo wagize umwuga ibijyanye no kumurika imideri .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE ubwo yari akimara gusohora iyi ndirimbo , Safi Madiba yagize ati """" Ubusanzwe yitwa Febuven Temesghen , iwabo bamuzi nk'umunyamideri ukomeye , ninayo mpamvu nanjye namwiyambaje mu gufata amashusho y'indirimbo yanjye . """"
Avuga ku ndirimbo ye nshya , Safi Madiba yagize ati """" Iyi ndirimbo yanjye nshya rero ni impano nageneye abakunzi banjye muri ibi bihe by'impeshyi , ndabizi ko muri ibi bihe baba bashaka umuziki mushya kandi mwiza , ni muri urwo rwego nabatekerejeho . """"
Safi Madiba yanavuze kandi ko yishimiye kongera gusohora indirimbo nyuma y'iminsi ahugiye mu bikorwa bya """" Nukuri Music """" sosiyete yashinze ifasha abahanzi bakizamuka .
Ati """" Mu minsi ishize nari ndi kwita cyane kuri Nukuri Music , hari ibyo nari mpugiyemo ariko ubu bimaze kujya ku murongo ninayo mpamvu navuze ngo reka nsohore indirimbo yanjye nshya . """"
Kugeza ubu uyu muhanzi yamaze kwemeranya imikoranire na """" Darcy Muhoza """" nawe utuye muri Canada , uyu akaba aherutse gusohora indirimbo yitwa """" Too fun . """"
Iyi ndirimbo nshya ya Safi Madiba yakozwe mu buryo bw'amajwi na Element , mu gihe amashusho yayo yo yatunganyijwe n'umusore witwa Lievain Rucyaha .
Amasomo Kenny Sol yigiye kuri Bruce Melodie mu mwaka bamaranye .
Mu masaha make ashize , Kenny Sol yasohoye """" Haso """" indirimbo ye ya mbere nyuma yo gutandukana na Bruce Melodie ikanaba iya nyuma bakoranye .
Nubwo batandukanye ariko nanone ku rundi ruhande Kenny Sol yavuze ko hari byinshi yigiye kuri Bruce Melodie .
Mu byo yamwigiyeho , Kenny Sol yabwiye IGIHE ko harimo gukunda umurimo no guharanira kwigira abandi bakaza bakunganira .
Ati """" Bruce Melodie akunda ibyo akora , akunda akazi ke !
Wenda reka nguhe urugero mu minsi ishize ubwo hadukaga Covid - 19 nta bitaramo bigoye gukora amashusho y'indirimbo , niwe watweretse twese ko ari ibintu bishoboka ! """"
Yakomeje avuga ko hari imapanuro Bruce Melodie yigeze kumuha nubu zikimufashije , ati """" Hari umunsi yigeze kumbwira ko umuntu wa mbere ugomba gukunda ibyo akora ari njyewe ubwanjye , abandi bakaza ari ukunyunganira ! """"
"""" Murabizi ibintu byagiye bimubaho , kenshi yakundaga kumbwira ko iyo aba umuntu ucika intege aba yarabiretse ariko kutazicika ni byo byamugize uwo ari we ! """"
Nubwo ari byinshi yigiye kuri Bruce Melodie , Kenny Sol ahamya ko mu mwaka yamaranye n'uyu muhanzi ibi ari bimwe mu by'ingenzi yahamya ko yamukuyeho .
Kenny Sol akomoza ku kuntu yakiriye gutandukana na Bruce Melodie bari bamaze umwaka bakorana ndetse akaba n'umuhanzi yakuze arota kuzakorana nawe .
Kenny Sol yavuze ko nubwo yatandukanye na Bruce Melodie ariko nta gikuba cyacitse kuko ari ibintu baganiriye mbere yuko biba .
Ati """" Buriya Bruce Melodie yagiye kubitangaza tumaze igihe twarabiganiriye ndetse twaranabifasheho umwanzuro !
Nta cyantunguye ndetse nta n'icyambabaje , ni amasezerano yari arangiye kandi yatwerekaga impamvu zikomeye zitatuma dukomezanya ahubwo ko buri wese yaba yirwarije . """"
Kenny Sol yavuze ko atababajwe no gutandukana na Bruce Melodie , ahubwo ngo yishimiye igihe bamaranye n'ibyo babashije gukorana .
Ati """" Sinavuga ko byambabaje , ni urugendo nyine , buri kintu kigira iherezo narabyakiriye !
Gusa nishimira igihe twamaranye , nigeze kuvuga ko inzozi zanjye zari ugukorana nawe indirimbo kandi byarabaye n'ubu iracyakunzwe .
Ndamushimira cyane kandi ndabizi ko ninongera kumukenera azanyumva . """"
Uyu muhanzi yahishuye ko kugeza ubu ari kwikorana umuziki bityo ko igihe haboneka umuntu wifuza ko bakorana nta kabuza ari ibintu baganira .
Ikiganiro na Kenny Sol
Uko Safi Madiba yafashe icyemezo cyo gukura Ama G The Black mu ndirimbo """" Caguwa """"
Icyemezo cyo gukurwa muri iyi ndirimbo Ama G The Black agifata nk'ubuhemu yakorewe na Safi Madiba bari bamaze iminsi bacuditse bikomeye .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Ama G The Black abajijwe uko yisanze atari muri iyi ndirimbo , yasobanuye uko yayitakajeho imbaraga ariko akaza kuyikurwamo .
Yagize ati """" Safi Madiba twaraye ijoro turi kuyandika muri Bridge Record .
Naherutse tuyandika nongera kubona bari kuyifatira amashusho i Gikondo . """"
Icyo gihe uyu muraperi avuga ko yahamagaye Safi Madiba bari inshuti byihariye muri Urban Boys , amubaza impamvu yamusimbuje Jay Polly mu ndirimbo """" Caguwa """" batanamumenyesheje .
Safi Madiba ngo ntabwo yigeze ahisha uyu muraperi ukuri , yamubwiye ko bahisemo kumukuramo kuko bari bamaze gukorana indirimbo nyinshi .
Ati """" Safi Madiba yarambwiye ngo abantu bari batangiye gutekereza ko twakoze itsinda bituma bankuramo . """"
"""" Caguwa """" ni indirimbo ya Urban Boys na Jay Polly , yafashije iri tsinda ryari mu bahanzi bari bagezweho mu myaka ya 2014 gukomeza kwigarurira igikundiro cy'abakunzi b'umuziki .
Nyuma yo gukora iyi ndirimbo yamenyekanye bikomeye , yaba Urban Boys na Jay Polly batumiwe mu gitaramo gikomeye bakoreye mu Bubiligi .
Ama G The Black yakomoje kuri iyi ndirimbo nyuma yo gusohora inshya yitwa """" Inkebebe """" yanditse abitewe n'agahinda k'ubuhemu yagiye akorerwa .
Angelina Jolie na The Weeknd bafotowe basohokanye byibazwaho .
Aba bombi bafashwe amafoto yasakajwe kuri uyu wa Gatanu bivugwa ko bari basohokanye ku wa Gatatu w'iki cyumweru muri resitora yitwa Giorgio Baldi iherereye mu Mujyi wa Los Angeles muri Amerika .
Nyuma y'igihe bamaranye basangira baje kuva muri iyi resitora buri wese ari wenyine mu rwego rwo kwirinda itangazamakuru ariko n'ubundi byaje kurangira bafotowe .
PageSix yatangaje ko uyu mugore w'imyaka 46 yari yambaye ikanzu y'umukara yarengejeho ikote rirerire rya kaki .
Mu gihe The Weeknd yari yambaye ipantaro n'umupira n'inkweto by'umukara yarengejeho ikote ryo mu bwoko bwa Denim naryo rikozwe muri iri bara .
Iki kinyamakuru cyatangaje ko uyu musore w'imyaka 31 na Angelina Jolie bari bahuye bahujwe n'akazi cyane ko The Weeknd ashaka kwinjira mu ruganda rwa sinema ya Hollywood .
Umwe mu batanze amakuru yagize ati """" Ntabwo bigeze babihisha kuko nta kintu kidasanzwe kirimo .
The Weeknd ari kwita cyane ku kwinjira muri filime mu buryo bw'umwuga .
Afite iy'uruhererekane izaca kuri HBO [ televiziyo ] . """"
The Weeknd si ubwa mbere avuzwe muri sinema cyane ko yagaragaye muri filime yitwa """" Uncut Gems """" yagiye hanze mu 2019 ndetse aza kugira kugira uruhare mu banditse """" American Dad """" yasohotse umwaka ushize .
Bivugwa ko ari mu banditse indi filime yitwa """" The Idol """" izaca kuri HBO ari nayo mpamvu yatumye ahura na Angelina Jolie ngo bayunguraneho ibitekerezo .
Iyi filime yayanditse afatanyije na Reza Fahim na Sam Levinson .
Ivuga ku mukobwa w'umuririmbyi wa Pop wakundanye n'umunyemari ufite akabyiniro muri Los Angeles .
The Weeknd wari waketsweho kuba yaba yatangiye gukururana ndetse bakaba bashobora kuba bakundana bucece na Angelina Jolie umurusha imyaka 15 , yakundanye n'abandi bakobwa b'ibyamamare barimo Bella Hadid mu 2015 bagatandukana mu 2016 mu 2017 arongera bariyunga .
Yanakundanye na Selena Gomez baza gutandukana .
Naho Angelina Jolie we azwi cyane mu nkuru z'urukundo na Brad Pitt bakoze ubukwe mu 2014 , nyuma y'imyaka 10 bari bamaze bakundana .
Nyuma y'imyaka ibiri basezeranye , ni bwo batandukanye , aba bombi bafitanye abana batandatu .
Angelina Jolie yari yarabanje gushyingiranwa na John Lee Miller mu 1996 batandukana mu 1999 , kuva mu 2000 kugera mu 2003 yari umugore wa Billy Bob Thornton , waje gusimburwa na Brad Pitt .
Masamba na Mariya Yohana bagiye guhurira mu gitaramo cyo Kwibohora .
Ni igitaramo cyo kwiyibutsa ibihe by'ingenzi byaranze urugamba rwo kubohora igihugu rwabaye mu myaka 27 ishize .
Iki gitaramo kizaba kiri mu mujyo w'ibitaramo bya Iwacu Muzika Festival ariko cyo kikaba gifite umwihariko w'uko kizaba cyahariwe umunsi wo Kwibohora uzaba ku wa 4 Nyakanga 2021 ari nabwo nacyo kizaba .
Cyateguwe na East African Promoters kikazanyuzwa kuri Televiziyo y'u Rwanda guhera saa yine n'igice z'ijoro .
Mu minsi ishize nibwo Platini P yabimburiye abandi bahanzi mu bitaramo bya Iwacu Muzika Festival mu cyabaye tariki 26 Kamena 2021 .
Bitewe n'uko icyorezo cya Covid - 19 kitaratanga agahenge , ubuyobozi bwa East African Promoters ( EAP ) isanzwe itegura Iwacu Muzika Festival bwafashe icyemezo cyo kongera kuyitegura hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga , nyuma y'iyabaye mu 2020 nabwo arizo zifashishijwe .
Abahanzi bose bazatarama muri Iwacu Muzika Festival uyu mwaka bamaze kumvikana na EAP ndetse batangiye n'imyotozo bakorana n'abazabacurangira .
Umwaka ushize Iwacu Muzika Festival yaririmbyemo abahanzi 15 , mu bitaramo byatangiye mu ntangiriro za Nzeri 2020 .
Isomwa ry'urubanza rwa Fireman ryasubitswe , agiye kongera kuburana .
Me Bayisabe Irénée wunganira Fireman muri uru rubanza yabwiye IGIHE ko Urukiko rwabamenyesheje ko isomwa ryarwo ryasubitswe ahubwo hazasubukurwa iburanisha rizagibwamo impaka ku byavuye mu iperereza ry'Urukiko .
Uyu munyamategeko wunganira Uwimana Francis uzwi nka Fireman , yavuze ko kuba Urukiko rwakora iperereza ryarwo ari ibintu bisanzwe , ati """" Mu gihe urukiko rwaba rutaranyuzwe n'iperereza ryakozwe n'inzego z'Ubugenzacyaha ndetse n'Ubushinjacyaha , Umucamanza yemerewe gukora iperereza rye . """"
Urukiko rwakoze iperereza kuko rutanyuzwe n'iryabaye mbere yo kuregerwa abaregwa , Me Bayisabe yagize ati """" Nko muri uru rubanza wumvise inshuro nyinshi ko ababuranyi bagiye bagaragaza ko hari uburyo iperereza ritakozwe neza , ibyo wasanga ari byo umucamanza yanagendeyeho akora iperereza rye . """"
Isubukurwa ry'uru rubanza ryashyizwe ku wa 16 Nyakanga 2021 .
Fireman yaherukaga kwitaba Urukiko Rukuru rwa Gisirikare tariki 7 Kamena 2021 , ari kuregwa mu itsinda ry'abantu 11 bakurikiranyweho icyaha cyo gukubita no gukomeretsa abanyeshuri bagororerwaga Iwawa .
Mu mpera z'umwaka ushize Urukiko rwa Gisirikare rwari rwamukatiye igifungo cy'imyaka itatu n'ihazabu y'ibihumbi magana atanu y'amafaranga y'u Rwanda ( 500 000 Frw ) .
Muri 11 bakurikiranywe n'Urukiko rwa Gisirikare , batatu ni bo bagizwe abere hanyuma umunani barimo na Fireman bahabwa igihano cyo gufungwa imyaka itatu n'ihazabu y'amafaranga ibihumbi 500 .
Bitewe n'uko ibihano bahawe kimwe n'abagizwe abere bitanyuze Ubushinjacyaha bwa gisirikare , bwahise bujurira Urukiko Rukuru rwa Gisirikare .
Ubushinjacyaha buvuga ko butumva impamvu Urukiko rwa Gisirikare rwirengagije ibimenyetso byatanzwe , hakagira abagirwa abere naho abandi bagahabwa ibihano birimo inyoroshyacyaha kandi batarigeze bacyemera cyangwa ngo hagaragazwe ibyashingiweho bahabwa ibihano bito .
Ubu bujurire bw'Ubushinjacyaha bwahuriranye n'ubw'abaregwa barimo na Fireman bagaragarije Urukiko ko batanyuzwe n'imikirize y'urubanza kuko bahanwe kandi ku bwabo bumva ari abere .
Fireman ari kuregwa muri dosiye imwe n'abayobozi batatu bahoze bayobora Ikigo ngororamuco cya Iwawa , abasirikare batanu n'abandi bahoze ari abayobozi b'abanyeshuri babiri .
Kenny Sol uherutse gutandukana na Bruce Melodie yasohoye indirimbo ya nyuma bakoranye .
Kenny Sol yasohoye indirimbo nshya yise """" Haso , """" ahita yemerera IGIHE ko ari iya nyuma mu ndirimbo yakoze ari kumwe na Bruce Melodie .
Ati """" Iyi ni imwe mu ndirimbo nakoze ndi kumwe na Bruce Melodie , urebye ni wo mushinga wa nyuma w'indirimbo twakoranye . """"
Yavuze ko ashimira Bruce Melodie kuba yaremeye kumufasha , ati """" Mu Rwanda hari abanyempano benshi , ku ishuri barabizi njye banyitaga Melodie kuko narinzi kwigana indirimbo ze , ntababeshye nari umufana we .
Kwemera kumfasha mu muziki rero nabifashe nk'ikintu gikomeye kandi ndabimushimira . """"
Nyuma yo gutandukana na Bruce Melodie , Kenny Sol yemeje ko agiye gukomeza gukora umuziki afatanya n'inshuti ze mu gihe atarabona abamufasha bahoraho .
Kugeza ubu Kenny Sol ari gufatanya n'umusore witwa Billy Mugambage uzwi nka Billy Kapo wari usanzwe areberera inyungu ze mu muziki .
Kenny Sol we mu gihe yamaze mu maboko ya Bruce Melodie yakoze indirimbo zirimo You & I , Aga Fire , Umurego na Ikinyafu .
Iyi ndirimbo nshya ya Kenny Sol mu buryo bw'amajwi yakozwe na Element mu gihe amashusho yayo yo yafashwe anatunganywa na Fayzo .
Gaël Faye yatumiwe mu bitaramo azahuriramo na Youssou n'Dour , Angélique Kidjo na Fally Ipupa
Kuri gahunda y'ibi bitaramo , byitezwe ko Gaël Faye azataramira abazabyitabira ku wa 5 Nyakanga 2021 .
Ibitaramo """" Nuits du Peyrou """" byatumiwemo Gaël Faye ni byo bya mbere bikomeye bigiye kubera ku butaka bw'Ubufaransa kuva icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyakugariza Isi .
Mu majoro atandatu ibi bitaramo bizamara , byitezwe ko abahanzi barenga 30 b'ibyamamare ari bo bazataramira abakunzi b'umuziki .
Kugeza ubu abantu ibihumbi bitandatu ni bo bamaze kwemererwa kuzitabira ibi bitaramo bizabera i Montpellier .
Nibura abantu igihumbi ni bo bazajya bitabira igitaramo buri munsi , aho kugeza ubu nta cyangombwa icyo ari cyo cyose kijyanye no kwipimisha cyangwa kuba warikingije kizasabwa uzitabira .
Tariki 9 Nyakanga 2021 ubwo iri serukiramuco rizaba risozwa byitezwe ko hazatarama abahanzi nka Youssou N'Dour , Amadou & Mariam , Angélique Kidjo , Magic System , Lubiana , Khaled , Manu Katché , Enrico Macias , Faudel , Tayc , James BKS , DJ Youcef , Fally Ipupa n'abandi benshi .
Sex / Life , """" filime nshya iri guca ibintu kuri Netflix yavugishije benshi .
"""" Sex / Life """" yashyizwe kuri Netflix ku wa 25 Kamena 2021 ishingiye ku nkuru y'agatabo kitwa """" 44 Chapters About 4 Men """" ka BB Easton .
Ivuga ku nkuru y'umugore w'abana babiri witwa Billie Connelly washakanye n'umugabo witwa Cooper Connelly .
Billie Connelly nyuma yo kurushinga n'uyu mugabo ntabwo anyurwa n'uburyo bakoramo imibonano mpuzabitsina ku buryo atangira kujya yibuka uko yayikoranaga na Brad Simon bakundanye atarashaka .
Nyuma uyu mugore aza gutangira kwandika inkuru y'ubuzima bwe bw'urukundo rwe n'uwo musore buba bwiganjemo ibihe byiza bagiranye mu gutera akabariro aba akumbuye .
Cooper Connelly aza kugwa ku nyandiko y'uyu mugore we muri mudasobwa akamenya uburyo akundamo gutera akabariro akaba ari nabwo atangira kujya akoresha kugira ngo yigurire umutima we .
Season ya mbere ya """" Sex / Life """" ifite ibice umunani .
Iri mu bwoko bwa pornographie zoroheje buzwi nka erotic movie cyangwa soft porn .
Igaragaramo Sarah Shahi ukina ari Billie Connelly , Mike Vogel ukina ari Cooper Connelly , Adam Demos ukina ari Brad Simon na Margaret Odette ukina nka Sasha Snow .
"""" Sex / Life """" mu mashakiro y'imbuga nkoranyambaga iri kugarukwaho cyane bamwe bakavuga ko irimo ibyo abantu banyuramo mu buzima bwa buri munsi .
Nk'uwitwa @ Wizarab10 yanditse kuri Twitter ati """" Iyi filime y'uruhererekane ya Sex / Life ivuga ku kibazo rusange mu buzima bwa muntu .
Ukorana imibonano mpuzabitsina n'abantu benshi bagushimisha mutashyingiranwa ariko ugahura n'umusore ufite ejo hazaza kandi uguha amahoro ariko nyuma ugatangira kumunenga kutagushimisha mu gutera akabariro . """"
Covid - 19 yateje icyuho cy'abasura Ingoro y'Amateka y'Abami i Nyanza .
Mu Karere ka Nyanza ahitwa mu Rukari , ni ho hari Ingoro y'Abami b'u Rwanda igaragaramo amateka yihariye kandi ateye amatsiko , ku buryo buri wese uhasuye amara umwanya areba ibimenyetso bihari bigaragaza uko Abami b'u Rwanda babagaho ndese n'umuco wihariye w'abenegihugu .
Nyanza yafatwaga nk'Umurwa w'Ubwami kuva mu mpera z'ikinyejana cya 19 kugeza mu mwaka wa 1961 .
Aha mu Kagari ka Rwesero mu Murenge wa Busasamana niho hari Ingoro z'Abami , hahoze urugo rw'Umwami Mutara wa III Rudahigwa wabatijwe Charles Leon Pierre , watwaye u Rwanda kuva mu mwaka w """" 1931 kugeza mu mwaka w """" 1959 .
Gahongayire Yvonne uyobora Ingoro y'Amateka y'Abami mu Karere ka Nyanza avuga ko kuva icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyatumye abayisura bagabanuka cyane .
Ati """" Mu mwaka wa 2018 - 2019 twakiriye abashyitsi 65 , 017 ; mu 2019 - 2020 twakira abantu 35 , 965 kuko batangiye kugabanuka kubera Covid - 19 naho mu 2020 - 2021 hasuwe n'abantu 7 , 910 .
Avuga ko mu mwaka wa 2019 - 2020 ari bwo ababasura batangiye kugabanuka kuko icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyageze mu Rwanda muri Werurwe 2020 hashize amezi arindwi umwaka w'ingengo y'imari utangiye .
Ati """" Abantu bahise bagabanuka cyane bigaragara kandi nibwo igihe cyo kuza kw'abashyitsi benshi kiba kigeze kugera mu kwezi kwa gatanu n'ukwa gatandatu . """"
Umuyobozi w'Akarere ka Nyanza , Ntazinda Erasme , avuga ko igitaramo ngarukamwaka """" Nyanza Twataramye """" cyinjiririzaga Abanyenyanza benshi amafaranga mu gihe gito ariko na cyo Covid - 19 yatumye gisubikwa .
Icyo gitaramo cyahuzaga abarenga ibihumbi bitatu mu ijoro rimwe bakarara inkera i Nyanza ntabwo kikihabera kuko umwaka ushize cyabereye kuri televiziyo abantu ntibahura ngo bidagadure ndetse n'uyu mwaka bigaragara ko ari ko bizagenda .
Ntazinda avuga ko kuba kitakibera i Nyanza ngo abantu bahure basabane byateje icyuho mu basura akarere n'igihombo ku bakora ubucuruzi .
Ati """" Icyuho kirahari kinini kuko iyo uganiriye n'abacuruzi bo mu Mujyi wa Nyanza bavuga ko uwo munsi wri igitangaza kuri bo kuko kuva k'ufite hoteli kugera no ku munyonzi w'igare , kugera no k'ucuruza avoka mu gatebo , abo bose baracuruzaga bakanezererwa . . """"
Nyanza Twataramye ni igitaramo kibanziriza umuganura uba mu kwezi kwa Kanama buri mwaka .
Yatangiye kubera mu Karere ka Nyanza mu 2014 .
Bamwe mu bakorera ubucuruzi mu Mujyi wa Nyanza na bo bavuga ko kuri ubu batakibona abakiriya nka mbere kubera Covid - 19 .
Musengimana Gérard ati """" Abakiriya ni bake cyane ntabwo bakiza nka mbere kubera iki cyorezo .
Umuntu ashobora kumara umunsi wose nta bakiriya batanu yakiriye kuko nta bashyitsi bakiza i Nyanza . """"
Ingoro y'Amateka y'Abami igizwe n'ibice bine ; icya mbere ni Ingoro Umwami Yuhi V Musinga yabayemo n'abandi bamubanjirije bose , igaragiwe n'izindi nzu ebyiri za kagondo ( Iy'amata ndetse ndetse n'iy'inzoga ) .
Igice cya kabiri kigizwe n'inyambo ( inka z'amahembe ashyorongoshyoye ) .
Icya gatatu ni ingoro y'Umwami Mutara III Rudahigwa , naho icya kane kigizwe n'aho Abami batabarije i Mwima .
I Nyanza hatuwe n'Abami bane ari bo Kigeli IV Rwabugiri wari utuye ku misozi ya Mwima na Mushirarungu ; Yuhi IV Musinga watuye i Mwima na Gakenyeri ; Mutara III Rudahigwa watuye mu Rukali ndetse n'Umwami Kigeli V Ndahindurwa watuye i Busasamana .
Umugore wa Steve Harvey yasuye ingagi mu Birunga .
Uyu mugore ari mu Rwanda mu ruzinduko aho yasuye ingagi zo mu Birunga mu muryango wa Muhoza .
Yanditse ku rukuta rwe rwa Instagram , ati """" Mwarakoze Pariki y'Ibirunga gufata neza izi ngagi nziza ndetse no kundeka nkagirana igibe nazo mu buturo bwazo . """"
Marjorie Elaine Harvey yasezeranye kubana na Steve Harvey mu 2007 .
Uyu mugore w'imyaka 54 ri arushinze ku nshuro ya gatatu ndetse yari afite abana batatu mbere yo kubana na Steve Harvey .
Aba bombi kandi bafitanye abana babiri b'abakobwa Lori Harvey na Morgan Harvey .
Marjorie Elaine Harvey ni umuhanzi w'imideli ndetse afite umuryango udaharanira inyungu ufasha urubyiruko witwa The Steve and Marjorie Harvey Foundation .
Umugabo we ni icyamamare muri Amerika no ku Isi yose kubera ibikorwa bitandukanye akora mu ruhando rw'imyidagaduro .
Broderick Stephen Harvey [ Steve Harvey ] yavutse ku wa 17 Mutarama 1957 .
Ni umunyamakuru kuri televiziyo , umunyarwenya , umukinnyi wa filime , umwanditsi , umushabitsi n'ibindi byinshi .
Azwi mu biganiro nka The Steve Harvey Morning Show , Family Feud , Celebrity Family Feud ndetse ni na nawe uyobora irushanwa rya Miss Universe kuva mu 2015 .
Uyu mugabo yatangiye ari umunyarwenya mu myaka yo mu 1980 nyuma aza kwinjira no mu itangazamakuru .
Hotel Akagera Game Lodge izacumbikira abazitabira CHOGM yashyizwe ku rwego rw'inyenyeri enye
Iyi hoteli yubatswe mu 1974 , iza kugurwa na RSSB mu 2013 hagamijwe gushora amafaranga mu bikorwa bizagira uruhare mu iterambere ry'igihugu bikanahindura imibereho myiza y'abaturage .
Nyuma yo kuyigura RSSB yashatse kuyivugurura ikajya ku rwego rwiza rukurura ba mukerarugendo .
Mu 2018 yagiranye amasezerano na Sosiyete yo muri Afurika y'Epfo ikora ibijyanye n'amahoteli , Mantis kugira ngo ivugururwe .
Ubuyobozi bwa Mantis bwavuze ko mu mirimo yo kuyivugurura hibanzwe cyane mu kwagura ibyumba no kubishyira ku rwego rwiza kuruta uko byari bimeze mbere .
Hongewemo ibyumba bibiri bifite ubushobozi bwo kwakira abakuru b'ibihugu .
Uwari Umuyobozi wungirije ushinzwe Ishoramari n'Ubukungu muri RSSB , Gacandaga Jean Marie , yavuze ko uru rwego rumaze gushora amafaranga agera kuri miliyari 8 Frw kugira ngo iyi hoteli ivugururwe kuko yari ishaje .
Yagize ati """" Twayiguze ishaje , ni yo mpamvu twashoyemo amafaranga kugira ngo igere ku rwego rwiza .
Ubwo twayijyagamo yego abantu benshi barayisuraga amafaranga akaboneka ariko ntabwo yari ku rwego twifuza . """"
"""" Urwego ubu iriho ni inyenyeri enye kandi ni rwiza twizeye ko ari umushinga mwiza , rero iyo urebye n'imibare usanga amafaranga yashowemo azagaruzwa . """"
Gacandaga yavuze ko kugura iyi hoteli biri mu murongo bihaye wo gukora ishoramari mu mishinga igamije guteza imbere igihugu ndetse n'imibereho myiza y'abaturage .
Akagera Game Lodge iri mu mahoteli azakira abazitabira Inama ya 26 y'Abakuru b'Ibihugu bikoresha ururimi rw'Icyongereza , Commonwealth , izwi nka CHOGM , ibintu Gacandaga avuga ko ari amahirwe akomeye kuba bibaye n'imirimo yo kuyivugurura yarangiye .
CHOGM iteganyijwe kubera mu Rwanda ku wa 21 Kamena uyu mwaka .
Iyi nama iba nyuma ya buri myaka ibiri , yagombaga kubera mu Rwanda ku wa 22 - 27 Kamena 2020 ariko iza gusubikwa ku mpamvu z'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , cyahagaritse inama n'ibindi bikorwa bikomeye .
Guverineri w'Intara y'Uburasirazuba , Gasana Emmanuel , yavuze ko iyi hoteli igiye gukomeza kurushaho kubera abaturage ivomo ry'imibereho myiza n'iterambere ry'intara cyane ko ubukerarugendo buri mu nkingi za mwamba bifuza kubakiraho ubukungu .
Yakomeje ati """" Turifuza ko ubukerarugendo buba mu bintu bitatu tuzashingiraho iterambere ryacu , birimo guteza imbere ubuhinzi , ubukerarugendo ndetse n'ubucuruzi .
Ikindi ariko abaturiye aha ngaha imibereho izagenda ihinduka kuko babona akazi . """"
Umuyobozi w'Ishami ry'Ubukerarugendo mu Rwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) , Belise Kariza , yashimye intambwe imaze guterwa mu bukerarugendo , avuga ko n'ubwo Covid - 19 yakomye mu nkokora uru rwego , u Rwanda rudateze gucika intege mu kubushyigikira no kubuteza imbere .
Yashimiye Ubuyobozi bukuru bwa RSSB ku gikorwa cyo gushora imari mu bukerarugendo , avuga ko adashidikanya ko kizatanga umusaruro ushimije mu gihe Covid - 19 izaba yacogoye ndetse n'ingendo zigakomeza nk'uko byari bisanzwe .
Hotel Akagera Game Lodge ifite ibyumba 59 harimo igishobora kwakira Umukuru w'Igihugu ( Presidential Suite ) n'igishobora kwakira abandi bayobozi mu nzego nkuru ( Executive Suite ) .
Sosiyete ya Mantis ifite inshingano zo gukurikirana iyi hoteli umunsi ku wundi isanzwe icunga izindi ebyiri arizo Kivu Marina Bay iri mu karere ka Rusizi na Epic Hotel iherereye mu Karere ka Nyagatare .
Umukarani yatawe muri yombi akekwaho kwiba shebuja ibihumbi 10 $ ( Video ) .
Ku wa Mbere tariki ya 12 Mata 2021 ni bwo uyu mugabo ukekwaho kwiba shebuja amafaranga yafatiwe i Nyamirambo asigaranye ibihumbi 9 . 6 $ .
Uwo mugabo w'imyaka 38 , afite umuryango n'abana batanu , ubusanzwe atuye mu Karere ka Nyarugenge , mu Murenge wa Kimisagara .
Yavuze ko amafaranga yayatwaye ubwo umukoresha we yari amutumye kuyabitsa kuri banki , akagenda ntagaruke .
Yagize ati """" Yari antumye kuri banki ngo njye kuyabitsaho , hanyuma sinabikora ndayajyana .
Muri ako kanya ntacyo nari ndi gutekereza icyakoze naje gukuraho telefoni ngo hatagira unshaka akambona maze nyuma y'igihe gito nongera nyisubizaho ariko numvaga umutima uri kundya ko bashobora kumfata . """"
Akomeza agira ati """" Bamfashe nagiye mu rundi rugo , nari nahunze ntinya ko bashobora kumbona .
Icyo gihe nari mfite ubwoba , nari nakuyeho 200 $ [ agera ku 200 . 000 Frw ] ndayakoresha mu rugo . """"
Nyuma yo gufatwa uyu mugabo yemeye ko yakoze icyaha abisabira n'imbabazi ndetse aburira bagenzi be bashobora gukora ibisa n'ibyo ko baba bikururira akaga .
Uwibwe amafaranga ni umucuruzi ukorera mu Isoko rya Nyarugenge witwa Gihana Zabulon .
Ubwo yari amaze gushyikirizwa amafaranga ye yagarujwe ku bufatanye n'inzego z'umutekano , uyu mucuruzi yishimiye kongera kuyabona avuga ko atari ikintu cyoroshye .
Yagize ati """" Numvaga uko byagenda kose dufite ubuyobozi bwiza ndetse na RIB ishobora kumfasha uwo muntu yaba atarambuka umupaka agafatwa .
Uwo mukozi yari umuntu mwiza , twari dusanzwe dukorana neza ariko sinzi ukuntu uwo munsi byagenze kuko namuhaga n'arenze ayo ngayo .
Ni umuntu ufite umugore n'abana sinatekerezaga ko yagira umutima wo kunyiba . """"
Uyu mucuruzi yavuze ko yatangiye gutekereza ko yibwe hashize amasaha ane , kuko yabajije aho yamukekaga hose ntamubone kandi n'amafaranga atashyizwe kuri konti .
Icyo gihe yatekereje ko yibwe , ashyikiriza ikirego Ubugenzacyaha .
Yashimiye uruhare RIB yagize mu gikorwa cyo gukurikirana uwamwibye agafatwa .
Gihana yavuze ko mu byamubayeho yakuyemo isomo rikomeye ririmo no kugira amakenga mu bikorwa by'ubucuruzi .
Umuvugizi w'Umusigire wa RIB , Dr Murangira B . Thierry , yabwiye IGIHE ko hakoreshejwe imbaraga mu gukurikirana uwibye amafaranga kugira ngo atabwe muri yombi .
Ati """" Icyo tubwira abantu bose n'abo bakoranaga bose ni uko uwaba afite umutima wo kugerageza gutwara ibitari ibye , cyangwa kwiba ko ntaho yacikira ubutabera .
Icyiza n'uko bareka uwo mutima wo gukora ibyaha . """" """"
Yibukije abaturage kurushaho gukorana n'inzego mu guhanahana amakuru kugira ngo bakomeze umurongo wo guhashya ibyaha .
Uyu mugabo watawe muri yombi aramutse ahamwe n'icyaha cy'ubujura yahanishwa ingingo ya 166 , iteganya igihano cy'igifungo kitari munsi y'umwaka ariko kitarengeje imyaka ibiri .
Imyiteguro irarimbanyije ku bazakira n'ahazakirirwa abazitabira Inama ya CHOGM .
CHOGM iba nyuma ya buri myaka ibiri , yagombaga kubera mu Rwanda ku wa 22 - 27 Kamena 2020 ariko iza gusubikwa ku mpamvu z'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , cyahagaritse inama n'ibindi bikorwa bikomeye .
Nyuma yo gusuzuma imiterere ya COVID - 19 , Ubunyamabanga Bukuru bwa Commonwealth , bwanzuye ko iyi nama izaba mu Cyumweru cya tariki 21 Kamena 2021 .
Kuri ubu ibijyanye n'imyiteguro irimo za site inama izaberaho mu Mujyi wa Kigali , amahoteli azakira abazayitabira , imihanda ndetse n'ibindi bikorwa remezo irarimbanyije kugira ngo izasange biri ku murongo .
Iyi nama itegerezanyijwe amatsiko menshi i Kigali ndetse imyiteguro ku mahoteli no ku bantu bayobora abakerarugendo irarimbanyije .
Itanga ishusho y'igihugu cyayakiriye muri rusange , kuva ku mihanda inyuramo imodoka z'abashyitsi , kugera ku byumba bya hoteli bararamo , inyubako ziberamo inama , ndetse n'aho batemberezwa mu bice binyuranye by'igihugu , cyane ko yitabirwa n'abantu baturutse hirya no hino ku Isi mu bihugu 54 bibarizwa muri The Commonwealth .
Bitandukanye n'izindi nama zabayeho , iy'uyu mwaka isaba indi myiteguro irenze iyo kubaka imihanda cyangwa iyo kurimbisha ibyumba n'ahazakorerwa inama kubera icyorezo cya Covid - 19 kimaze umwaka urenga kibasiye Isi .
Igitezwe amaso kuruta ibindi , ni umutekano w'abazitayitabira , cyane ku byerekeye ubuzima , kureba niba hari uburyo buhagije bwo kwirinda Covid - 19 , kugira ngo hatazagira umushyitsi uyandurira mu Rwanda cyangwa se hakagira uyinjiza mu gihugu akanduza abo asanze .
Mu kiganiro IGIHE yagiranye n'abanyamahoteli batandukanye na bamwe mu bayobora ba mukerarugendo bazwi nka """" Tour guides , """" basobanuye uko biteguye iyi nama ndetse n'ingamba zafashwe mu kwirinda Covid - 19 .
Muri za hotel byifashe bite ?
Amahoteli ni yo zingiro ry'ishusho umushyitsi ashobora kuvana mu gihugu , kuko ariho amara igihe kinini kuruta ahandi .
Uburyo yakirwa aho afatira ifunguro , aho arara , hose hamusigira ishusho ituma azagaruka cyangwa akahazinukwa .
Ni iby'ingenzi rero ko yitegura neza bishoboka , hashyirwa ingufu mu bintu byose cyane mu kwirinda Covid - 19 , nk'icyorezo gihangayikishije Isi .
Mugesera Eric ushinzwe Abakozi muri Serena Hotel yasobanuye ko biteguye neza , baguze ibyuma bipima umuriro n'ibyibutsa abantu kwambara agapfukamunwa .
Ati """" Hari amatsinda yashyizweho ashinzwe gutegura iyi nama kugira imyiteguro yose ikorwe neza [ . . . ] Abakozi bacu twarabahuguye , Minisiteri y'Ubuzima n'Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe Ubuzima , RBC , baradufashije mu guhugura abakozi , nabo baraza bahugura bagenzi babo kugira ngo bamenye uko bazirinda barinde
n'abo bazakira .
Ndetse ubu abakozi bacu bose barakingiwe . """"
Ku bijyanye n'ibirori bisanzwe bibera muri hotel bizwi nka """" Gala dinner , """" """" cocktails """" n'ibindi , Mugesera yavuze ko bizakomeza kuba nkuko byahoze ariko hakurikizwa amabwiriza yose MINISANTE itanga ajyanye no kwirinda Covid - 19 cyane ko n'abakozi bahuguwe uburyo bazabyitwaramo .
Moges Hanna ushinzwe Itumanaho n'Imenyekanishabikorwa muri Kigali Convention Centre and Radisson Blu Hotel , yavuze ko iyi hotel yatangiye imyiteguro ya CHOGM mu ntangiriro za Werurwe , ndetse ko aho abashyitsi bazarara hateguwe .
Ati """" Twongereye imiti yica udukoko mu byumba by'abashyitsi , dukuramo ibikoresho byakoreshejwe birimo ibitabo byo gusoma , imisego myinshi n'ibyo kwiyorosa biri mu tubati tubikuramo dutera imiti ahantu hose mu byumba yaba ku ntebe , kuri telefoni , telekomande za televiziyo , ku nzugi , ku madirishya ku tubati n'ahandi . """"
Yavuze ko ibikorwa byose bizabera muri hotel birimo inama , gufata amafunguro , aho abashyitsi barara bizakorwa hirindwa Covid - 19 , basiga intera haba mu bashyitsi no mu bakozi , ndetse imiti yica udukoko igashyirwa ahantu hose , ku buryo yaba umukozi cyangwa umushyitsi yayibona . Abajijwe ku cyo Hotel zunguka iyo habaye inama nk'izi zikomeye
, Hanna yavuze ko icya mbere ari isura nziza abashyitsi bahavana , bigatuma Isi ibona ko u Rwanda rushoboye kwakira inama mpuzamahanga zikomeye , abasura igihugu bakiyongera n'abategura inama bakakigirira icyizere .
Abayobora abakerarugendo biteguye kubereka ibyiza bitatse u Rwanda
Mu gihe cy'inama zikomeye , benshi mu bazitabira banasura ibice bitandukanye bakareba ibyiza biri mu rw'Imisozi igihumbi kuva ku moko y'inyoni zirenga 300 zo muri Pariki ya Nyungwe kugera ku ngagi zo mu Birunga zikurura abanyamahanga benshi .
Abayobora ba mukerarugendo bazwi nk'aba - guides bavuga ko biteguye neza kwakira abashyitsi bazitabira CHOGM ndetse hari abatangiye kubasaba ko bazabatembereza .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa Home Rwanda Safaris , Tuyigire Aimable , yavuze ko nk'abatembereza ba mukerarugendo biteguye guhesha ishema n'isura nziza u Rwanda , cyane ko nyuma y'igihe kinini cyari gishize nta nama zikomeye ziba mu gihugu biteze kuzabona ababagana .
Ati """" Ubu twamaze guhugura abakozi batwara ba mukerarugendo bijyanye n'ibihe turimo byo kwirinda Covid - 19 ku buryo ntawe uzagira ikibazo mu rugendo .
Turi gukorana n'ibice bisurwa birimo pariki z'igihugu ndetse imodoka zabugenewe zarateguwe ku buryo twiteguye kuzereka Isi ko u Rwanda ari igihugu kibereye ubukerarugendo . """"
Umuyobozi wa Sosiyete itwara ba mukerarugendo ya Show me Around Rwanda Safaris , Bukuru Augustin , we yagize ati """" Twiteguranye kwakira abashyitsi n'ubwuzu bwinshi .
Twatangiye gutegura aho abantu bazasura by'iminsi mike hafi ya Kigali bijyanye n'umwanya muto baza bafite kugira ngo bizaborohere cyane . """"
Muri rusange imyiteguro mu bantu bose bafite aho bazahurira bya hafi n'abashyitsi bazitabira CHOGM imeze neza ndetse n'ubwo bataramenya umubare w'abantu bazitabira , mu mezi abiri gusa asigaye byitezwe ko imirimo yo kwitegura inama no gukingira abantu bizaba byarangiye .
Biteganyijwe ko iyi nama ishobora kuzitabirwa n'abagera ku bihumbi 10 .
Usibye ibijyanye n'imyiteguro y'amahoteli n'abayobora ba mukerarugendo , Umujyi wa Kigali nawo ukomeje ibikorwa byawo byo kurimbisha imihanda izakoreshwa ahanini n'abazitabira CHOGM hagamijwe kubafasha kuryoherwa n'igihe bazamara ku butaka bw'u Rwanda .
Inama ya CHOGM iheruka kubera mu Bwongereza mu 2018 , byari biteganyijwe ko izabera mu Rwanda mu 2020 irimurwa kubera Covid - 19 .
Ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje imibereho itangaje y'ingagi z'imfubyi
Byagaragajwe mu bushakashatsi bwakorewe ku ngagi 59 zifite hagati y'imyaka ibiri n'umunani zo muri Pariki y'Ibirunga iri mu Majyaruguru y'u Rwanda , kuva mu 1967 kugeza mu 2019 .
Hifashishijwe amakuru n'izindi nyigo zakozwe mu myaka yabanje , ibyabuvuyemo byerekanye ko kuba abana b'ingagi baba imfubyi bitababuza gukomeza kubaho , kororoka no kwisanga mu zindi .
Ni mu gihe abashakashatsi basobanura ko inguge ibuze nyina ikiri nto , bisa n'igikuba gicitse mu mibereho yayo , kuko nyina ari yo iyirinda ikanayitoza inzira nyinshi z'ubuzima bwayo .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na RFI , Umuyobozi w'itsinda ry'abashakashatsi bakoze iyo nyigo , Robin Morrison , yatangaje ko ibyo biterwa n'uko ingagi zikunze kubana mu matsinda kandi zigafashanya .
Ati """" Icyo twabonye muri ubu bushakashatsi ni uko uretse ukwita ku mwana kw'ingagi z'imbyeyi kuba kutagihari , iyo zigejeje ku myaka ibiri zishobora gukomeza kubaho kandi ntizihungabane .
Bisa n'aho biterwa n'uko zibana mu itsinda rigari , riba ryuzuyemo ngenzi zazo bifitanye isano zikuriwe n'ingabo ishobora kuba ari se cyangwa atari we . """"
Morrison yavuze ko mu mibereho yazo """" zose ziba zisa n'izishaka kuba hafi y'izo z'imfubyi """" bigatuma zisanga mu zindi bityo ntizigerweho cyane n'ingaruka z'ubupfubyi .
Muri uko kwisungana kandi ngo ingabo ikuriye itsinda ifasha abana batagifite ba nyina , ikabaryamisha buri joro kabone n'iyo yaba atari yo se .
Ku rundi ruhande , umuhanga mu by'imyitwarire y'ibinyabuzima , Matthew Zipple , yavuze ko kuba ingagi zibuze nyina zikiri nto zishobora gukomeza kubaho kandi neza """" bitangaje kandi byongeye urujijo . """"
Ati """" Ubundi mu bwoko bwa ziriya nyamaswa icyo tuba twiteze ni uko kubura nyina bishobora kuyigiraho ingaruka mbi zikomeye ku kuba yakomeza kubaho . """"
Icyakora n'inyigo Zipple aheruka gukorera mu mwaka ushize ku nkende , ingagi , inkima n'inguge yerekanye ko nta ngaruka mbi zigaragara ku ngagi iba yarabuze nyina ikiri nto .
Muri rusange , ingagi ziba imfubyi biturutse ku mpfu , ubushimusi cyangwa se kuba zakwimuka zikava mu gace kamwe zisize abana .
Iyo nyigo nshya yamuritswe muri eLife ku wa 23 Werurwe 2021 , yakozwe n'abashakashatsi bo muri Dian Fossey Gorilla Fund Rwanda , University of Exeter na University of Southern Denmark .
Radisson Blu Hotel & Kigali Convention Centre yabonye umuyobozi mushya .
Rob Kucera afite ubunararibonye burenga imyaka 20 mu bijyanye n'urwego rw'amahoteli .
Yakoze mu micungire y'amahoteli muri Afurika y'Epfo , Turikiya , Uganda na Kenya .
Yakoze mu mahoteli akomeye nka The Westin Cape Town and Arabella Hotel , Golf & Spa Resort , Movenpick Wilderness Hotel na Protea Hotels .
Si ubwa mbere Rob Kucera agiye kuyobora Radisson Blu Hotel kuko yayoboye iyo muri Turikiya izwi nka Radisson Blu Bosphorus Hotel , Istanbul ndetse n'iyo muri Kenya izwi nka Radisson Blu Hotel , Nairobi Upper Hill .
Rob Kucera asanzwe kandi ari we muyobozi wa hoteli za Radisson Blu mu Karere ka Afurika y'iburasirazuba .
Mu itangazo ubuyobozi bwa Radisson Blu Hotel na Kigali Convention Centre bwashyize hanze kuri uyu wa 30 Werurwe 2021 bwavuze ko ubunararibonye bwa Kucera mu bijyanye no kubera icyitegererezo abakozi , ndetse no kubashishikariza gufata inshingano mu bijyanye n'imicungire myiza ya hoteli biri mu byo bamwitezeho .
Izi ndangagaciro z'uyu mugabo mu bijyanye n'imiyoborere y'amahoteli byatumye we n'amatsinda y'abakozi bakorana babona ibihembo bitandukanye .
Mu 2015 ubwo yakoraga muri Starwood Hotels & amp , Resorts Group bahawe igihembo mpuzamahanga kijyanye n'imikoranire myiza nk'itsinda ry'abakozi .
Mu 2004 yahawe kandi igihembo nk'umuyobozi mwiza w'umwaka mu itsinda ry'amahoteli ya Protea ( Protea Hotels ) .
Rob Kucera yabaye kandi Umuyobozi w'Inama y'Ubutegetsi mu kigo kigenzura ibikorwa by'ibigo 700 biri mu bikorwa by'amahoteli n'ubukerarugendo mu Ntara ya Western Cape muri Afurika y'Epfo kizwi nka """" FEDHASA . """"
Radisson Blu Hotel Kigali ni hoteli y'inyenyeri eshanu fite ibyumba 292 , icyumba cy'inama cyakira abantu basaga 2500 , ibiro byo gukoreramo n'ibindi .
Yatashywe ku mugaragaro mu 2016 , ndetse ifatwa nk'inkingi ya mwamba muri gahunda Guverinoma y'u Rwanda yihaye yo kwagura ubukerarugendo hibandwa ku kwakira ibiganiro , inama mpuzamahanga n'ibikorwa bitandukanye byiswe MICE mu magambo ahinnye y'Icyongereza bizwi nka Meetings , Incentives , Conferences and Events .
Huye : Amayobera ku nkende yapfuye imanitse mu mugozi .
Umunyeshuri wo muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda , Rwamucyo Nsengimana Jean de Dieu , yabwiye IGIHE ko iyi nkende bayibonye mu masaha ya mu gitondo imanitse , bihutira kubimenyesha ubuyobozi .
Ati """" Byatubereye urujijo kuko twabibonye mu gitondo nka saa mbili , bivugwa ko yari imaze iminsi ifite umugozi mu ijosi , birashoboka ko yagiye hejuru kwa kundi ziba zikina akagozi kagafatwa mu ibati kagahita kayizirika . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Ubuyobozi bwahise buhagera ariko nta cyo bwayikoraho kuko hari izindi nkende zarakaye , urumva ni hejuru cyane kandi bisaba n'abantu kuba bakurira kandi n'izindi nkende zihari byari bigoye kuba wazihakura . """"
Hari amakuru ko urupfu rwayo rwatewe n'abantu bayiteze umugozi ku bushake , bakayambika agasinga mu ijosi bitewe n'uko hari abakunze kuvuga ko zibonera imyaka zikanabasagarira .
Umukozi wa RDB ushinzwe kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima , Ngoga Télesphore , yabwiye IGIHE ko bagiye gushaka amakuru y'icyaba cyayishe .
Ati """" Turi kubikurikirana kugira ngo turebe uko bimeze maze hashakishwe ikintu cyakorwa byihutirwa .
Ubu turi kuvugana n'abayobozi ba Kaminuza ngo tumenye uko bimeze . """"
Amakuru agera kuri IGIHE ni uko nyuma iyi nkende yamanuwe aho yari imanitse ikajyanwa ahakusanyirizwa inyamaswa muri Kaminuza Nkuru y'u Rwanda mu Ishami rya Huye , kugira ngo iterwe imiti itazangirika maze ijye yifashishwa mu bushakashatsi n'abanyeshuri biga ibijyanye n'imibereho y'inyamaswa .
Gusa kugeza ubu hategerejwe ko ibanza gukorerwa ibizamini hakarebwe niba nta ndwara ifite , mu gihe yasanganwa uburwayi igahita ishyingurwa .
Bimwe mu birwa bitatse ibyiza nyaburanga mu kiyaga cya Kivu .
Ikiyaga cya Kivu ni cyo kiyaga kinini mu Rwanda cyikaba gikurura imbaga y'abantu haba Abanyarwanda ndetse n'abandi baturutse mu bihugu bitandukanye .
Igice cyacyo kimwe kiri ku ruhande rw'u Rwanda mu gihe ikindi kiri muri Repuburika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Ku ruhande rw'u Rwanda gikora ku turere tune aritwo Rusizi , Nyamasheke , Karongi na Rubavu , aha hakaba harangwa n'ibyiza nyaburanga bitandukanye birimo nk'amahoteri akikije ikiyaga ndetse n'umucanga abantu bidagaduriramo .
Ibi ni ibigaragara inyuma ariko imbere muri iki kiyaga harimo ibirwa bitandukanye byuje ubwiza butandukanye bituma uwabigezeho atifuza gutaha .
Mu gushaka kumenya amakuru kuri ibyo birwa , IGIHE yaganiriye n'umwe mu bakozi ba sosiyete """" Golden Rwanda Safaris Ltd , """" izobereye mu gutembereza ba mukerarugendo .
Umwe mu bayikorera yavuze ko igikurura abantu kujya kuri ibi birwa ari ukurira imisozi bizwi nka """" Hiking """" ndetse no kureba inyoni .
Ati """" Abantu bajya ku turwa ni abantu baba bagira amatsiko cyane , wa wundi uba ushaka kumenya ikiri imbere mu kiyaga .
Abajyayo rero ibyo bakorayo ni ukurira imisozi ndetse no kureba inyoni kuko zibamo cyane haba ari heza iyo ukunda ibyo bintu . """"
Ibirwa biri mu kiyaga cya Kivu
Ikirwa cya Nkombo
Nkombo ni cyo kirwa kinini mu kiyaga cya Kivu kuko gifite ubuso bungana na kilometero kare 29 , 7 harimo 22 , 7 km2 z'ubutaka na 7 km2 z'amazi , uyu akaba ari umurenge wose uri mu Karere ka Rusizi .
Iki kirwa gituwe n'abaturage bakabakaba ibihumbi 18 , gikurura abatari bake bashaka kujya kureba ukuntu abantu batuye hagati mu mazi ndetse bakururwa n'imico yaho itandukanye n'isanzwe irimo nk'ururimi rw'Amashi rwumvwa n'abaho gusa ndetse n'imbyino zabo zizwi nko gusama .
Abaturage baho benshi batunzwe no kuroba n'ubundi bucuruzi butandukanye bakorera muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Ba mukerarugendo barahakunda kuko ubuzima bwaho butandukanye n'ubw'ahandi mu gihugu .
Iki kirwa nta terambere ryaharangwaga mu myaka yashize ariko muri iyi myaka ryarahageze kuko haboneka ibikorwa remezo bitandukanye nk'umuriro , amazi meza , amashuri , ivuriro ndetse na hoteli .
Ikirwa cya Gihaya
Gihaya na ho ni mu Karere ka Rusizi ndetse ni hafi na Nkombo ariko ho ni hato .
Ni ikirwa ba mukerarugendo bakunda kujya gusura bashaka kurira imisozi ndetse no gutembera mu bwato .
Ubuzima bwaho ni nk'ubwo ku Nkombo .
Akarwa k'Abakobwa
Aka ni akarwa kari mu Karere ka Nyamasheke gafite amateka akomeye mu Rwanda , kera bajyaga ku kajugunyaho abakobwa babaga baratwaye inda z'indaro ngo badateza ishyano ku musozi .
Abantu baturutse imihanda yose biganjemo igitsina gore bajya kuhasura bagira ngo barusheho kumenya amakuru y'uko byagendaga ku bakobwa bahajugunywaga .
Ikirwa cya Nyamunini
Nyamunini izwi cyane nka Napoleon Island , ni ikirwa kiri mu kiyaga cya Kivu ku ruhande rwa Karongi .
Iki ni kimwe mu birwa bikurura ba mukarerugendo bitewe n'ubwoko bw'inyoni butandukanye buhari ndetse n'imbuto zihari .
Ikirwa cy'Amahoro
Amahoro na cyo kiri ku ruhande rwa Karongi , nk'uko cyitwa amahoro koko ngo gitemberwa n'abantu babuze amahoro muri bo kandi ngo bahageze bakabona amazi agikikije n'amajwi y'inyoni ziririmba bakumva buzuye amahoro muri bo .
Ikirwa cya Nyakarwa
Nyakarwa ni ikirwa giherereye mu Karere ka Karongi cyizwiho kugira inyoni zitandukanye .
Uwahegeze nta yandi majwi aba yumva usibye urusobe rw'amajwi atandukanye y'inyoni .
Ikirwa cya Mpembe
Mpembe na yo iherereye muri Karongi akaba ari icyirwa kigengwa n'umuntu ku giti cye , aho yashyizeho ahantu hangana n'ibilometero bine abantu bagenda n'amaguru .
Gikurura benshi kuko kibafasha kuruhuka mu buryo bwihariye .
Si ibi birwa gusa biri muri iki kiyaga kuko muri 2012 , Ikigo cy'Igihugu cyo Kubungabunga Ibidukikije ( REMA ) , cyatangaje ko mu kiyaga cya Kivu habarizwamo ibirwa 250 .
Muri byo , 56 biri ku rahande rw'u Rwanda .
Ibi twavuzeho ni ibyo ba mukerarugendo bakunze muri gusura muri iki gihe .
Amaso ahanzwe u Rwanda mu kiganiro Echappées Belles cya France 5 .
