Mu busanzwe mu biganiro bibera kuri Twitter """" Tagging """" irakoreshwa cyane nk'igihe umuntu ashaka kuvuga izina ry'ufite aho ahuriye n'ibiri kuvugwa .
Tagging kandi ikoreshwa igihe umuntu ashaka kwerekana abo yageneye ubutumwa runaka .
Gusa imbogamizi zikunze kubaho ni uko nta buryo bubaho umuntu ashobora kwikura muri ubu butumwa igihe ibyamuvuzweho atabyishimiye cyangwa abona byamuteje ikindi kibazo .
Amakuru dukesha Ikinyamakuru """" Nerdist """" avuga ko itsinda ry'abahanga muri Twitter riri gukora ku mushinga wo gutangiza uburyo buzaba buzwi nka """" Unmention """" buzajya bufasha abantu kwikura muri ubu butumwa bashyizwemo batabishaka .
Umukozi ushinzwe kubika amakuru y'abantu muri Twitter , Dominic Camozzi yavuze ko izi mpinduka zigamije korohereza abantu .
Ati """" Ndashaka korohereza abantu kuba bakwikura mu butumwa cyangwa ibiganiro badashaka kugaragaramo . """"
Nubwo ubu buryo bwitezweho kuzafasha benshi ntiharatangazwa igihe buzatangira gukoreshwa .
MTN yakoze impinduka zigamije gukemura ikibazo cya """" réseau """" nke na internet igenda gahoro .
Nyuma y'aho bamwe mu bakiliya b'iyi sosiyete bagaragaje ko babangamiwe n'ikibazo cya réseau nke , aho bahamagaraga ntibabashe kumvikana n'abo bahamagaye ndetse na internet igenda gahoro , MTN Rwanda yashyizeho iminara mishya 40 hirya no hino mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Mu gukemura iki kibazo hibanzwe cyane ku Karere ka Gasabo kuko ariko kari kugarijwe cyane .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe itumanaho muri MTN Rwanda , Gakwerere Eugen , yavuze ko hari impamvu zitandukanye zishobora gutuma internet igenda gahoro .
Yagize ati """" Hari uburyo butatu butuma umuntu abura internet , ubwa mbere ni uko umufatabuguzi wacu yaba ari ahantu serivisi zacu zitagera .
Ubwa kabiri ni uko baba bari ahantu hamaze kuba ubucucike bwinshi bw'abakoresha umurongo wa MTN , ubwa gatatu ni uko wenda icyuma bafatiraho gishobora kuba cyagize ikibazo mu gihe runaka . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko mu gukemura ibi bibazo hashyizweho iminara kandi ko hari byinshi bikiri gukorwa kugira ngo babashe gutanga serivisi nziza .
Ati """" Icyo turi gukora , ku batuye ahantu hatagera réseau za MTN twabamara impungenge y'uko muri aya mezi atatu ashize twongereye iminara igera kuri 40 i Kigali , cyane cyane mu mirenge ikikije umujyi , harimo Nduba , Jabana , Rusororo , Bumbogo , aho hose n'ahandi , abafatabuguzi bacu bahatuye baraza kubona impinduka , cyane
cyane abakoresha internet . """"
"""" Hari n'indi minara ya MTN 27 igiye gushyirwa hirya no hino bitarenze muri Kanama kugira ngo abakiliya bayo barenga miliyoni esheshatu bagerweho na serivisi nziza kandi zinoze . """"
Yavuze ko kandi ibibazo bitandukanye mu byitumanaho abakiliya ba MTN Rwanda bagiye bahura na byo mu minsi yashize byatewe n'uko hari amavugurura yari ari gukorwa , abizeza ko bagiye gutangira kubona serivisi nziza .
MTN Rwanda yorohereje abakiliya bayo
Usibye kongera iminara bizatuma ikibazo cya réseau gikemuka , MTN Rwanda yanogeje serivisi zayo zitandukanye nk'aho ushobora kwihindurira umubare w'ibanga wa MTN mobile money bitagusabye kujya ku cyicaro cyayo .
Kuri ubu umuntu wibagiwe umubare w'ibanga we ariko afite amafaranga ari munsi ya 3 000 Frw kuri Mobile Money ye ashobora kuwihindurira atiriwe ajya aho MTN ikorera , akanda * 182 * 9 * 3 # agakurikiza amabwiriza ubundi akabasha kuwihindurira .
Ikindi cyashyizweho ni kode izajya ifasha abakiliya bayo kubona amakode yandi bakeneye bitabasabye kuyafata mu mutwe ibyiswe Shortcode , aho bazajya bakanda * 456 # .
Hagiye gushyirwaho kandi uburyo bushya bw'ikoranabuhanga , aho umuntu azajya yandikira abakozi ba MTN Rwanda bitamusabye kujya aho bakorera cyangwa ngo ahamagare .
Azajya aca ku rubuga rwa .
Mu kwegereza abakiliya bayo ikoranabuhanga hagiye gushyirwaho kandi nimero izajya ikoreshwa kuri Whatsapp ku buryo ushobora kubandikira ubamenyesha ikibazo cyawe , ugahita usubizwa .
Akarusho kandi MTN Rwanda ifite ni gahunda yatangije mu mpera za 2020 ya """" Ni Dilu """" aho umuntu ajyana telefone ishaje iyo ari yo yose , yaba Tecno , Samsung , iPhone , Infinix , n'izindi , akongeraho amafaranga make agahabwa indi nshya .
Bigakorerwa kuri Service Center za MTN cyangwa se hifashishijwe application ya """" Vuba Vuba . """"
Umuyobozi ushinzwe imitangire ya serivisi muri MTN , Dusabe Rosine , yavuze ko ibi byose bari kubikora kugira ngo abakiliya babo barusheho kugendana n'ikoranabuhanga .
Ati """" Abakiliya bacu turabasaba kugendana n'iterambere bagakoresha ikoranabuhanga bakikemurira ibibazo bari mu rugo batiriwe bajya kuri Service center za MTN . """"
Yongeyeho ko MTN izakomeza gukora ibishoboka byose kugira ngo abakiliya bayo babone serivisi nziza bishimiye .
Abafite ibibazo bya murandasi bitarakemuka bashobota kunyura kuri bagasiga ubutumwa buriho nimero bakoresha n'aho batuye kugira ngo babakemurire ibyo bibazo .
Icyogajuru cy'u Bushinwa kiri kuri Mars cyohereje amafoto
Kuwa Gatanu nibwo u Bushinwa bwashyize hanze amafoto yafashwe n'icyogajuru Zhurong kimaze iminsi kuri uwo mubumbe udatuwe , bikaba ari ikimenyetso cy'iterambere mu bushakashatsi ku isanzure icyo gihugu kigezeho .
U Bushinwa nicyo gihugu cya kabiri kigeze kuri Mars nyuma y'abashakashatsi bo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika .
Amashusho Zhurong yohereje ni aya kabiri nyuma y'andi yoherejwe muri Gicurasi uyu mwaka .
Amafoto mashya yafashwe arimo agaragaza agace gakikije aho icyo cyogajuru cyururukiye , n'andi yafashwe kiri gutembera kuri Mars .
Hari indi foto yafashwe igaragaza ubutaka bwo kuri Mars n'ibisate by'urutare ndetse n'umucanga mwinshi .
Indi foto ni igaragaza akantu icyogajuru Zhurong cyururukiyeho n'ibendera ry'u Bushinwa hafi aho .
Biteganyijwe ko Zhurong izamara amezi atatu kuri Mars mu bushakashatsi bugamije kumenya niba uwo mugabane warigeze guturwaho n'ibindi biremwa .
Ibiro Ntaramakuru by'Abashinwa , Xinhua byatangaje ko ibizava mu bushakashatsi bizatangarizwa isi yose .
Tanzania irashaka kuvanaho umusoro kuri telefoni zigezweho .
Intego ni ugufasha icyo gihugu kugera ku muhigo cyihaye w'uko mu 2025 abaturage 80 % bazaba bakoresha internet .
Minisitiri w'Imari n'Igenamigambi , Dr Mwigulu Nchemba , yavuze ko urwego rw'itumanaho mu ikoranabuhanga rufatiye igihugu runini no mu bukungu , nkuko The Citizen yabitangaje .
Kugeza ubu ikoreshwa rya internet muri Tanzania riri ku kigero cya 46 % , Nchemba akaba asanga ahanini biterwa no guhenda kw'ibikoresho by'ikoranabuhanga birimo na za telefoni zigezweho .
MTN yatanze miliyoni 100 Frw zo kubaka ibyumba byigishirizwamo mudasobwa mu mashuri ya TVET .
ya mafaranga yashyikirijwe Minisiteri y'Uburezi kuri uyu wa Gatanu , tariki 11 Kamena 2021 , muri gahunda ngarukamwaka y'iki kigo yo kugira uruhare mu gufasha abaturage mu bikorwa by'iterambere cyane ko ari nabo bakiriya bacyo .
Kuva mu myaka 15 ishize , MTN Rwanda itegura ukwezi kwahariwe ibikorwa byayo mu baturage , aho ukwezi k'uyu mwaka kwahawe insanganyamatsiko igira iti """" WeCare Month . """"
Iki kigo gitanga serivisi z'itumanaho cyiyemeje gukora ibikorwa birimo ibigamije gufasha leta muri gahunda yo kwimakaza ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rw'uburezi .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Misiteri y'Uburezi ushinzwe Ikoranabuhanga na TVET , Irere Claudette , yashimye iyi gahunda yatangijwe na MTN avuga ko bizafasha mu iterambere ry'urwego rw'uburezi muri rusange .
Ati """" Gukoresha ikoranabuhanga mu burezi ntibikiri ishema ahubwo ni ngombwa .
Niba hari icyo icyorezo cya Covid - 19 , cyatwigishije , ni uko kwinjiza ikoranabuhanga mu burezi byihutirwa . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Umusanzu wa MTN Rwanda urihutirwa , ibi ntabwo byakwirengagizwa .
Twishimiye kwakira iyi nkunga izadufasha mu kubaka ibyumba 10 byigishirizwamo mudasobwa mu turere dutandukanye . """"
Ubu bufasha MTN Rwanda yatanze kandi bwari buherekejwe na internet y'ubuntu izamara umwaka n'ubundi ikoreshwa muri ibyo byumba 10 byubatswe mu bigo by'amashuri 10 atandukanye .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa MTN Rwanda , Mitwa Ng'ambi , yavuze ko igihe cyo gukoresha ikoranabuhanga cyageze ndetse ikigo abereye umuyobozi gifite icyerekezo cyo gutanga ibisubizo mu rugendo rwo kwimakaza ikoranabuhanga mu Rwanda .
Yagize ati """" Uyu munsi twatanze miliyoni 100 Frw yo gushyiraho ibyumba byigishirizwamo mudasobwa 10 , nk'imwe mu ntambwe ziganisha ku kugera ku ntego zacu . """"
Muri uku kwezi kwiswe """" We Care , """" MTN izatanga umusanzu wayo mu yindi mishinga igamije kuzana impinduka nziza ku baturage mu rwego rwo guteza imbere ubukungu , uburezi n'ubuzima .
Apple yahishuye udushya turi muri iOS 15
Iyi iOS ibashisha abantu kuvugana kuri telefoni barebera filimi hamwe , bumvira indirimbo hamwe kandi bagakomeza no kuganira nk'abicaye hamwe mu cyumba cy'uruganiriro .
Ubu buryo kandi buzemerera abasanzwe bakoresha telefoni zikoresha Operating System ya Android na Windows kuba bavugana batyo n'ababukoresha bifashishije iza Apple .
Apple iranateganya gutangiza utundi dushya twinshi muri telefoni ngendanwa zayo harimo gukurikirana gahunda zo mu rugo , ku kazi no kuri hoteli , kuba umuntu yafunga cyangwa agafungura imiryango y'inzu , imodoka n'ibindi yifashishije ikoranabuhanga riri muri iyi iOS .
iOS 15 kandi izajya ifasha abagenzi ku bibuga by'indege mu gihe cyo kugenzura no gusuzuma ibyangombwa .
iOS 15 izaba ifite uburyo bwihariye bufasha nyirayo guhitamo amatangazo ahabwa bitewe n'ibyo ahugiyemo nk'aho ashobora kujya yemezamo """" work """" mu gihe ari mu kazi maze akajya yakira ubutumwa bwerekeranye n'akazi gusa cyangwa se ubwoherejwe n'abo bakorana .
Mu gihe nyirayo atari mu mwanya wo gusubiza abandi bamwandikira ashobora kwemezamo """" do not disturb """" nk'ubutumwa buzajya bwiyohereza kuri abo bantu atarindiriye kwandikamo cyangwa gufata kuri telefoni .
Jeff Bezos agiye gutemberera mu isanzure mu cyogajuru cyakozwe na sosiyete yashinze . Icyogajuru bazagendamo cyiswe """" New Shepard , """" cyitiriwe Alan Shepard , umuntu wa kabiri akaba n'Umunyamerika wa mbere wagiye mu isanzure .
Mu butumwa yanyujije kuri Instagram , Bezos yavuze ko gutemberera mu isanzure ari ikntu yifuje kuva akiri muto .
Ati """" Ku wa 20 Nyakanga , nzakora urwo rugendo ndi kumwe n'umuvandimwe wanjye , ikintu kidasanzwe hamwe n'inshuti yanjye magara . """"
Umuvandimwe wa Bezos na we yavuze ko ari amahirwe akomeye kuri we .
Umwanya w'umuntu uzajyana n'abo bavandimwe , Blue Origin yawushyize ku isoko ukaba wari ugeze ku gaciro ka miliyoni 2 , 8 z'Amadolari ya Amerika .
Jeff Bezos afite umutungo mbumbe wa miliyari 186 , 2 z'amadolari ya Amerika .
IHS Rwanda yaguze imodoka 11 zikoresha amashanyarazi
Iki gikorwa cyabereye ku cyicaro cya IHS Rwanda i Remera kuri uyu wa 4 Kanama 2021 kikaba cyitabiriwe n'abantu bo mu nzego zitandukanye barimo na Mbasaderi w'u Buyapani mu Rwanda .
Iki gikorwa kandi cyahuriranye no gutangiza ku mugaragaro , Station z'imodoka zikoresha umuriro w'amashanyarazi izaba iherereye ku cyicaro cya IHS .
Umuyobozi wa GreenLeaf Autofast Rwanda , Judith Muhongerwa , yashimiye IHS Rwanda ku bwo kugura izi modoka zikoresha umuriro w'amashanyarazi kuko bijyanye na gahunda ya leta yo kurengera ibidukikije hirindwa gukoresha imodoka zohereza imyuka ihumanye mu kirere .
Yagize ati """" Dufite icyizere kandi dutewe ishema cyane n'uko u Rwanda ruri imbere mu kwimakaza ibikorwa birengera ibidukikije , binyuze mu gukoresha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho muri Afurika .
Nka GreenLeaf Autofast Rwanda twishimiye kuba bamwe mu bateza imbere iri koranabuhanga rirengera ibidukikije . """"
Muhongerwa yavuze ko Ikigo ayoboye ndetse n'uruganda rwa Mitsubishi bazakomeza kugendera mu murongo w'u Rwanda wo kurengera ibidukikije .
Ambasaderi w'u Buyapani mu Rwanda , Imai Masahiro , yavuze ko gukoresha imodoka z'amashanyarazi ari iby'ingenzi , kuko hagendewe ku mihindagurikire y'ikirere cy'u Rwanda ndetse n'icyerekezo rufite cya 2050 , imodoka z'ubu bwoko zizagenda ziyongera ndetse bikanafasha mu kurengera ibidukikije no kubungabunga umwuka """" duhumeka .
""""
Yakomeje agira ati """" Umubano mwiza usanzwe hagati y'u Buyapani n'u Rwanda , wavuyemo imbuto nziza kuko wemereye sosiyete nyinshi zo mu Buyapani kuza gukorera mu Rwanda , ndetse n'indi mishinga myinshi ibihugu byombi bifitanye , harimo n'uwo gushyira satellite y'u Rwanda mu kirere . """"
Ambasaderi Imai Masahiro yakomeje avuga ko imodoka zikoresha umuriro w'amashanyarazi zihendutse kurusha izikoresha ibikomoka kuri peteroli kandi zikanarangera ibidukikije kuko zitoherereza imyuka ihumanya mu kirere .
IHS yahawe na """" chargeurs """" z'izi modoka zishyiramo umuriro mu minota iri hagati ya 15 na 25 ndetse umuriro ugiyemo ukaba wafasha imodoka kugenda ibirometero hagati ya 60 na 80 .
Gusa hari izindi zo mu rugo ushobora kuzirazaho cyangwa ukayicomeka mu gihe utari kuyikoresha kuko zo zishyiramo umuriro mu masaha atatu .
U Rwanda rurakataje mu gukoresha imodoka zikoresha umuriro w'amashanyarazi ndetse muri Werurwe 2021 Uruganda rwa Volkswagen rufite imodoka 20 zikoresha umuriro w'amashanyarazi , rwamuritse Station ya kabiri yongera umuriro mu modoka .
Mu Rwanda hatangijwe amasomo y'igihe gito yo kwerekana amashusho imbonankubone , Live Streaming .
Live streaming ni uburyo bwo gufata amajwi n'amashusho bigasakazwa imbonankubone ( live ) ku batabashije kugera aho igikorwa runaka kiri kubera , ukaba wagikurikira nk'uhibereye wifashsishije internet .
Ayo mashusho n'amajwi bishobora kunyuzwa ku mbuga nkoranyambaga cyangwa urundi rubuga rwatoranyijwe , maze wahanyura ukaba wabasha kugendana n'abandi muri gahunda bitagusabye kugera aho igikorwa nyirizina kiri kubera .
Ntabwo byahabwaga agaciro cyane mu myaka yashize , ariko uwavuga ko ari kimwe mu masomo Coronavirus yahwituriye abantu ko ari ngombwa ntiyaba agiye kure y'ukuri .
Guhuriza abantu benshi hamwe mu bihugu byinshi byarahagaritswe kandi kwitabira inama , ibitaramo , imihango y'ubukwe n'iyo gushyingura , kwiga , kureba umupira n'ibindi bikorwa byari bisanzwe bihuza imbaga biracyakorwa ariko noneho mu gihe umubare ugenwe urenze bigasaba ko hitabazwa ikoranabuhanga .
Ibyo byose live streaming n'iyo ibikora neza kandi mu buryo bworoshye .
Uretse kukugeza ahabereye igikorwa iki n'iki bitagusabye ingendo , ubikora biramwinjiriza ku buryo byamutunga nk'umwuga .
Uko abakenera iyo serivisi bagenda biyongera , ni ko n'ababikora bagenda binjiza cyane kuko uko ayo mashusho arebwa n'abantu benshi mu gihe runaka ni ko n'uyabagezaho ifaranga riba ryibara .
Si ibyo gusa kuko no mu gihe abantu bananiwe bavuye mu mirimo live streaming ibafasha kuruhura ubwonko bakina imikino y'amashusho .
Aho naho nyir'ukuyibagezaho aba yinjiza .
Nk'ubu byitezwe ko abagera kuri miliyoni 383 mu Isi yose bazareba amashusho banyuze ku mbuga zitandukanye mu 2021 , naho Ifluencer Marketing Hub ikerekana ko mu 2025 isoko rya streaming y'amashusho rizaba rigeze ku gaciro ka miliyari 124 , 6 $ mu 2025 .
Ni muri urwo rwego AHUPA Business Network ishaka gufasha n'Abanyarwanda kubona kuri ayo mafaranga cyane ko imirimo yagabanutse benshi bakaba bataka ibura ry'akazi .
Yatangije amasomo y'ingenzi mu gihe gito ku bashaka kubikora , mu mahugurwa yise """" Live Streaming Master Class . """"
Ayo masomo azajya amara iminsi irindwi kuva ku wa 31 Gicurasi kugeza ku wa 30 Kamena 2021 , ahabwe abantu bose bafite ubumenyi bw'ibanze mu gukoresha mudasobwa babyifuza kandi ku musozo wayo bahabwe impamyabushobozi .
Uwitabira asabwa kuba kandi afite mudasobwa ye , ndetse akaba yamaze kwishyura 100 . 000 Frw .
Mu gihe yaba yifuza ibikoresho bijyanye no gutangira umwuga arangije ayo mahugurwa , nabyo hateganyijwe uburyo bwo kubibona byoroshye .

Ni umwe mu bashinze BTN TV ndetse ni na we Muyobozi Mukuru wayo .

United Airlines irateganya kugura indege zifite umuvuduko uruta uw'ijwi .
Aya masezerano y'agateganyo avuga ko United Airlines izagura indege 15 zakozwe n'icyo kigo , ku giciro cya miliyoni 2004 ku ndege imwe , zikazaba zigenda ku muvuduko ukubye kabiri uw'indege zisanzwe .
Byitezwe ko izi indege zikiri kubakwa , zizatangira gukorerwa amagerageza mu mwaka wa 2026 , akazarangira muri 2029 ari nabwo United Airlines izatangira kuzitwaramo abagenzi .
Urugendo rwavaga New York rugana i Londres rwatwaraga amasaha atandatu , ruzajya rutwara nibura amasaha atatu n'igice , mu gihe urugendo rugana Tokyo ruvuye Amerika ruzakorwa munsi y'amasaha ane .
Indege United Airlines iteganya kugura zizaba zigendera ku muvuduko wa kilometero zirenga 1800 ku isaha imwe , ndetse ibindi byose nibugenda neza ikazagura izindi ndege 35 , ibizatuma yuzuza indege 50 zifite ubushobozi bwo kugenda ku muvuduko uruta uw'ijwi .
Boom Supersonic izakora izi ndege yatangaje ko bari gukora ikoranabuhanga rizatuma izo ndege zitangiza ikirere , kuko bitewe n'umuvuduko uri hejuru izi ndege zigenderaho , zikoresha mazutu nyinshi bityo zikohereza umwuka wangiza ikirere ari mwinshi .
Si ubwa mbere indege zifite umuvuduko uruta uw'ijwi zivuzwe , kuko ahagana mu 1978 zakoreshwaga n'ibigo nka British Airways na Air France , ariko zikaza guhagarikwa muri 2003 kuko zangizaga ikirere , zikagira urusaku rukabije ndetse zikaba zinahenze , kuko urugendo ruva Londres rujya New York rwashoboraga gutwara 10 000 $ .
Ibirwa bya Maurice bigiye kohereza icyogajuru cya mbere mu isanzure .
Iki cyogajuru kiroherezwa mu ijoro ryo kuri uyu wa Kane , gihagurukire mu Kigo cyo muri Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika cyitwa Kennedy Space Center giherereye muri Florida .
Icyo cyogajuru nikigera mu isanzure , kizatangira kuzenguruka Isi , cyohereze amakuru mu kigo gishinzwe ubushakashatsi no guhanga udushya muri Maurice .
BBC yatangaje ko icyo cyogajuru kizajya cyohereza amakuru inshuro enye cyangwa eshanu ku munsi .
Ayo makuru azajya asesengurwa afashe icyo gihugu kiri mu Nyanja y'Abahinde , gufata ingamba zigamije gukumira ibiza .
Byitezwe ko kandi amakuru kizatanga azafasha kugenzura ibinyabuzima n'undi mutungo wo mu nyanja no guhangana n'ikibazo cy'igabanuka ry'amafi mu nyanja .
Mu bindi amakuru icyo cyogajuru kizatanga azajya yifashishwamo ni ukumenya kare ahashobora kwibasirwa n'imyuzure .
Uburyo bworoshye bwagufasha kumenya ko waciwe amande na Polisi mu muhanda .
Hari umuntu ufite ikinyabiziga RA . . 305 H , ashobora kuba atazi ko afite umwenda w'ibihumbi 300 Frw , yandikiwe na camera ku wa 1 Kamena .
Ni cyo kimwe na RAE400 . . . wandikiwe ibihumbi 25 Frw ku wa 2 Kamena ku bwo kutubahiriza ibyapa .
Ubwo twandikaga iyi nkuru , twagiye ku rubuga rwa Irembo , tukajya dutomboza Pulake tutazi ba nyirazo .
Ugerageje nk'icumi , usangamo nibura eshatu zifite umwenda zitarishyura .
Ibyo biterwa n'impamvu nyinshi .
Imwe muri zo ni uko umuntu ashobora kuba ari mu muhanda , wenda camera ikamwandikira kubera amakosa runaka , hanyuma ntahite abona ubwo butumwa kuri telefoni ye .
Ibyo bishobora gutuma amande aba menshi ariko we ntabimenye .
Ubusanzwe ibihano bihabwa uwakoze amakosa yo mu muhanda bishyirwaho mu rwego rwo kwirinda impanuka zihitana ubuzima bwa benshi ndetse zikanangiza .
Mbere iyo Polisi yaguhagarikaga mu muhanda wakoze amakosa yakwandikiraga agapapuro , ukakajyana muri banki , bakagufasha kwishyura .
Kuva aho ikoranabuhanga riziye , ubu umuntu akora akosa mu muhanda , akakira ubutumwa bw'amande aciwe kuri telefoni ye bitewe n'ikosa yakoze , buriho uburyo ashobora kwishyura , ku buryo ibyo kujya kuri banki bitakibaho .
Kubera ko ubutumwa bw'amande bwoherezwa kuri telefone , hari benshi baba batazi umubare w'amafaranga barimo bitewe n'uko hari igihe ikinyabiziga kiba kitabanditseho cyangwa rimwe na rimwe yaba yafashwe na camera yo mu muhanda ubutumwa ntibuze .
Kubera izo mbogamizi zose , Polisi y'u Rwanda yashyizeho uburyo umuntu ufite telefoni ngendanwa igezweho """" smartphone """" cyangwa mudasobwa ashobora kwirebera umubare w'amafaranga ikinyabiziga cye gifite yifashishije urubuga rwa Irembo , atiriwe ajya kubarisha cyangwa se ngo abimenye kuko polisi yahagaritse
ikinyabiziga cye .
Kimwe nk'izindi serivisi za leta zose , kureba amande [ Contravention ] urimo ujya ku rubuga rwa Irembo ukamanuka hasi ukareba umutwe w'amagambo wanditseho """" Polisi """" , haba hariho serivisi nyinshi zihatangirwa .
Iyo uhageze ubona interuro ya kabiri yanditseho ngo """" Kwishyura Konterevasiyo """" ukayikandaho , hakaza imbonerahamwe nto iriho ibisobanuro by'uko iyo serivisi ikoreshwa , ubundi ugakora ahanditse ngo """" Saba """" mu mabara y'ubururu .
Iyo umaze kuhakanda ureba mu mbonerahamwe , ugakanda ahanditse """" Nimero ya Pulaki , """" munsi yaho ukandikamo izo nimero ukagakora ku ruhande ahari ibara ry'ubururu .
Ako kanya uhita ubona amafaranga ikinyabiziga cyawe kirimo , iyo ntayo gifite nabwo bakubwira ko ntayo .
Ibyo ni ukureba umubare w'amafaranga ikinyabiziga cyawe kirimo , ariko ushobora no kwishyura amafaranga unyuze muri iyo nzira .
Ku ruhande rw'ahanditse """" Nimero ya Pulaki """" handitseho ngo """" Nimero ya Tike , """" urahakanda maze munsi yaho ugashyiramo izo nimero ubundi ugakurikiza amabwiriza .
Nubwo hari bamwe binubira amande bacibwa mu muhanda , ni iby'ingenzi ko umushoferi utwara imodoka akwiriye kwitwararika ntarenge ku mategeko yo mu muhanda hato adatanga amafaranga atari yateganyije azize amakosa yari kwirinda bigashoboka .
Microsoft igiye gushyira ku isoko """" Windows """" nshya
Microsoft yaherukaga gushyira hanze porogaramu y'ibanze ya mudasobwa mu 2015 ubwo yasohoraga """" Windows 10 """" gusa uko imyaka yagiye ishira yagiye ikorerwa amavugurura .
Windows 10 yagiye ku isoko ikurikira """" Windows 8 . 1 . """"
Amakuru y'uko Microsoft yaba igiye gushyira hanze ubwoko bushya bwa """" operating system """" yatangiye gucicikana ubwo yatangiraga gutanga impapuro z'ubutumire ku bitangazamakuru ivuga ko kuwa 24 Kamena 2021 ifite umuhango ukomeye izamurikiramo porogaramu nshya .
Icyatumye abantu barushaho gukeka ko Microsoft kuri iyi tariki aribwo izashyira hanze iyi Operating System shya ni uko ubu butumire bwaje nyuma y'icyumweru kimwe Umuyobozi Mukuru wayo , Satya Nadella , avuze ko amaze igihe agerageraza ubwoko bushya bwa Windows .
Amakuru dukesha The Verge avuga ko iyi Windows nshya izaba itandukanye na Windows 10 ndetse n'izindi zose zari zisanzwe ku isoko , uhereye k'uko igaragaza ibintu .
Zimwe mu mpinduka zizayigaragaramo n'uko icons zizaba zigaragara mu buryo butandukanye kandi igihe ufunguye nka """" folder """" impande zayo zizajya ziba ziburungushuye aho kugira dogere 90 nk'uko byari bisanzwe .
Ubu bwoko bushya bwa Operating System buzajya ku isoko busanga ubundi Microsoft yagiye ishyira hanze mu bihe bitandukanye burimo Windows 8 , Windows 7 na Windows Vista .
Kugeza ubu ntiharatangazwa uko iyi Windows izaba yitwa gusa hari amakuru avuga ko izitwa """" Windows 11 . """"
U Rwanda n'u Budage byatangije irushanwa rizavumbura abanyempano mu ikoranabuhanga .
Ni irushanwa ryiswe """" Tech Upskill Talent Detection """" rigamije kubaka no kongera ubushobozi bw'abanyadushya n'abanyempano mu by'ikoranabuhanga bo mu Rwanda .
Mu kiganiro n'abanyamakuru cyabereye muri IPRC Kicukiro ku wa 2 Kamena 2021 , hasobanuwe ko iryo rushanwa rireba abafite ubumenyi mu bijyanye n'ikoranabuhanga ( ICT & Engineering ) , haba mu gukora za porogaramu ( software ) cyangwa ibindi byakora hifashishijwe mudasobwa ( hardware ) n'ubundi buryo bwafasha mu gutunganya ibintu runaka mu nganda ( manufacturing )
.
Abo bazatoranywa mu Ishuri Rikuru ry'Imyuga n'Ubumenyingiro ( RP ) n'andi yigisha amasomo nk'ayo ( TVETs ) n'abandi babyifuza bataba muri ayo mashuri ariko bafite imishinga bazaba babisabye .
Umuyobozi ushinzwe gukurikirana Ishyirwa mu bikorwa ry'uyu mushinga muri ICT Chamber , Dushime Christophe , yatangaje ko imishinga myinshi y'udushya mu ikoranabuhanga ikunze kuba iri mu Mujyi wa Kigali , bityo ko iyi gahunda yatangijwe izagezwa mu bice by'icyaro kugira ngo icyo cyuho kizibwe .
Yagize ati """" Twasanze ibikorwa by'ikoranabuhanga byinshi biherereye muri Kigali , kandi niba dushaka ko u Rwanda ruba icyitegererezo mu by'ikoranabuhanga muri Afurika nta n'umwe ugomba gusigara inyuma . """"
"""" Ni yo mpamvu twatekereje ko tugomba gusanga no kugaragaza za mpano ziri hanze ya Kigali , kuko ikibazo ntabwo ari ugufasha sosiyete zatangiye gukora , [ ahubwo ] ikibazo ni ukumenya uko dukora umuyoboro ku buryo abanyeshuri barangije bafite ubumenyi buhagije bwo kuba bahanga imirimo n'udushya babigeraho . """"
Ishyirwa mu bikorwa ry'uyu mushinga ryashyizwe mu maboko ya 250STARTUPS isanzwe ifasha imishinga itandukanye kugera ku baterankunga , FabLab izwiho kuba uruhumbikiro rw'imishinga y'ikoranabuhanga ndetse na KLab ihuza ba rwiyemezamirimo mu by'ikoranabuhanga bagahanga udushya .
Umuyobozi w'Ishuri Rikuru ry'Imyuga n'Ubumenyingiro ( Rwanda Polytechnic ) , Dr Gashumba James , yabwiye itangazamakuru ko iri rushanwa ari ingenzi kuko rizatuma abanyeshuri berekana impano bafite zagirira igihugu akamaro .
Yakomeje ati """" Nka Kaminuza tuba dufite ingengo y'imari idahagije , amikoro yacu ari make .
Guhuza abo banyeshuri n'abashoramari n'abandi bantu bareba bakavuga bati """" hano hari akantu keza """" nashyiramo amafaranga , uwo mwana na we akabyungukiramo bikagira aho bimugeza .
Niko gufatanya n'ibikorwa nk'ibi bya ICT Chamber bigiye kuduhuza n'abandi bashobora kuba bafite ubushobozi kuturusha dusanga ari igisubizo . """"
Biteganyijwe ko abanyadushya mu ikoranabuhanga bazatoranywa muri iri rushanwa bazahabwa amahirwe yo gukorana n'imishinga ya 250STARTUPS , naho abanyempano bo bemererwe gukora imenyerezamwuga mu miryango y'imbere mu gihugu na sosiyete z'Abadage .
Bashobora no kuhakura amahirwe yo kubona akazi binyuze muri KLab .
Kuri iyi nshuro ya mbere y'iri rushanwa hazafatwa abanyempano 30 bose hamwe muri ibyo byiciro byombi , bafashwe kugeza mu Ukuboza 2021 .
Gusaba kuba umwe muri abo banyamahirwe bizarangira ku wa 17 Kamena 2021 , aho usaba azajya anyura kuri :
Ku banyempano uwiyandikisha asabwa kuba hari umushinga umwe cyangwa myinshi yakozeho ku ishuri , ushobora kwerekanwa hakoreshejwe amafoto cyangwa link ; kuba azi neza ibyo gukora porogaramu za telefoni no guhanga website no kuba azi gukoresha porogaramu ya CAD .
Abanyadushya biyandikisha basabwa kuba imishinga yaba iya software cyangwa iya hardware no kuba ishushanyije cyangwa yarakorewe inyigo ishobora kwerekanwa mu mafoto cyangwa link .
Hasinywe amasezerano agamije kubaka ubushobozi bw'urubyiruko rwa Afurika mu bijyanye n'ikoranabuhanga .
Ubusanzwe Digital Opportunity Trust ( DOT ) ikorana bya hafi n'urubyiruko , ibigo byigenga , guverinoma zitandukanye n'imiryango igamije kurengera sosiyete , mu bihugu bisaga 25 kuva yashingwa mu 2001 , ifite urubyiruko rusaga 6000 rwahinduye ubuzima bw'agera kuri miliyoni muri Afurika , Aziya , Amerika y'Epfo na Canada .
DOT yatangaje ko yagiranye amasezerano y'imikoranire na IBM agamije kubakira ubushobozi urubyiruko rw'abakobwa n'abasore mu bijyanye no gukoresha ikoranabuhanga , kubagira abashobora guhangana ku isoko ry'umurimo , ubumenyi mu bijyanye no kwihangira imirimo , imibereho myiza n'iterambere ry'ubukungu .
Imikoranire hagati y'impande zombi ishingiye ku bwuzuzanye aho IBM izakoresha ikoranabuhanga ryayo n'abahanga bafite inararibonye mu guhanga imirimo , naho DOT yo ikaba ari inzira yo kugera ku rubyiruko rwifuzwa .
Muri ibi bikorwa bigamije kubakira urubyiruko ubushobozi , DOT yatangaje ko izakorana n'imiryango itandukanye y'imbere mu bihugu kugira ngo bafashe abakiri bato kwisanga muri porogaramu ya IBM izwi nka Open P - Tech .
Open P - Tech ni uburyo bwo kwigisha ikoranabuhanga no kubaka ubushobozi mu ikoranabuhanga uwayigishijwe , ifasha kandi kugira ubumenyi bw'ibanze no guhangana mu ikoreshwa ikoranabuhanga .
Ubu ni uburyo bugamije guhereza abanyeshuri ubumenyi bw'ibanze mu ikoranabuhanga bukenerwa mu nguni zose , burimo gukoresha Al , Cloud computing , gukumira ibitero n'ibyaha bikorerwa ku ikoranabuhanga ( Cybersecurity ) no gukora igishushanyo mbonera """" design thinging , """" teaming na Presentation .
Biteganyijwe ko uyu mushinga uzafasha abagera ku bihumbi 40 bo mu bihugu birimo u Rwanda , Tanzania , Uganda , Zambia , Malawi , Ghana , Jordan na Lebanon .
Muri aba bagera kuri 70 % bazaba ari ab'igitsina gore .
Kuba abagore bari mu barebwa cyane n'iyi gahunda byatewe n'uko umubare w'abari mu bijyanye n'ikoranabuhanga ukiri muto , aho abasaga 50 % by'abagore bo mu bihugu bikiri mu nzira y'amajyambere bagaragaraga gake gashoboka mu ikoreshwa ry'ikoranabuhanga .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wungirije ushinzwe Imikoranire ku rwego Mpuzamahanga muri IBM , Justina Nixon - Saintil , yavuze ko iyo myumvire ariyo bifuza guhindura binyuze mu gukorana na Digital Opportunity Trust , cyane ko isanzwe ifite umubano mwiza n'urubyiruko hirya no hino ku Isi .
Yagize ati """" Gutanga ubumenyi ku mwuga mu rubyiruko , by'umwihariko abagore na ba bandi baturuka mu miryango y'amikoro make , bishobora guhindura ubuzima .
Hamwe n'ikigo nka IBM binyuze muri porogaramu ya Open P - Tech n'imbaraga z'imiryango irimo na DOT twifuza kongera ubumenyi no kubaremera amahirwe . """"
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa DOT , Janet Longmore , yavuze ko ashingiye ku mikoranire isanzwe hagati y'impande zombi yizeye ko bizatanga umusaruro .
Ati """" DOT na IBM bifitanye amateka akomeye y'imikoranire kandi icyizere cy'iterambere gihuriweho gituma habaho imikoranire myiza .
Ubu bufatanye binyuze muri iyi porogaramu ya Open P - Tech , ni urugero rwiza rw'uburyo inzego z'abikorera n'ibigo byita ku mibereho myiza y'abaturage byakorana , bigakoresha umutungo ukagirira akamaro urubyiruko , haba mu bice by'icyaro n'ibice bya kure .
Twese twizera ko urubyiruko rwifuza guhanga udushya no kuba umusemburo w'impinduka mu mirimo y'ahazaza . """"
Ubushakashatsi DOT yakoze bwagaragaje ko urubyiruko rufite ubumenyi mu ikoreshwa ry'ikoranabuhanga ari rwo ruvamo abayobozi n'abagamije guhindura sosiyete barimo , igihugu ndetse n'ubukungu .
Wari uziko umuvuduko Isi igenderaho wiyongereye ; Uku niko byagenze .
Ibi babishingira ku buryo kera mu myaka miliyoni 600 ishize , Isi yizengurukaga amasaha 21 gusa , bivuze ko umunsi wamaraga amasaha 21 , ariko uko imyaka yagiye ihita igihe yizenguruka cyagiye cyiyongera ku buryo ubu umunsi umara amasa 24 byerekana ko Isi yagiye igenda gahoro .
Gusa mu 2020 byarahindutse , abashakashatsi bo mu Kigo Mpuzamahanga gishinzwe uko Isi izenguruka ( The International Earth Rotation and Reference Systems Service , IERS ) gihereye i Paris mu Bufaransa bagaragaje ko aho kugenda gahoro ahubwo isigaye yihuta .
Ni ibintu bitigeze bibaho mu myaka 50 ishize ndetse mu 2020 habayeho iminsi 28 ifite amasegonda make ku yo umunsi ugomba kugira 86 . 400 .
Forbes itangaza ko muri iyi minsi harimo umunsi umwe , ku itariki 19 Nyakanga 2020 wagize igihe gito kuva igihe kubara amasaha byatangiriye , umara amasegonda ari munsi ya 86 . 400 ho milliseconde 1 . 4602 [ milliseconde ingana n'isegonda rimwe ugabanyije 1000 ] .
Umunsi muto waherukaga kubaho hari tariki 5 Nyagakanga 2005 , aho Isi yizengurutse amasegonda ari munsi ya 86 . 400 ho milliseconde 1 . 0516 .
Ibi bishobora kugaragara nk'aho ari igihe gito ariko bigira ingaruka ku isaha , cyane ko hari système nyinshi zigendera ku myubakire y'isaha zihereye kuri milliseconde , ku buryo igihe habayeho impinduka niyo yaba nto bishobora guteza ikibazo .
Izo harimo ikoranabuhanga rya GPS rikoreshwa na Satellite , uburyo bwa NTP bukoreshwa mu kugena isaha muri telefoni zigezweho ( smart phone ) , mudasobwa ndetse no muri serivisi zitandukanye z'itumanaho zikoresha murandasi .
Ibi byose bishobora kugirwaho ingaruka n'uku kwihuta kwisi .
Abashakashatsi bavuga ko batazi impamvu nyakuri yatumye Isi yihuta bitandukanye n'uko byahoze .
Ariko hari impamvu nyinshi bakeka zishobora kubitera zirimo imitingito , imitere y'ikirere , inyanja ndetse n'ukwezi .
Indi impamvu ikomeye bakeka ni ugushyuha ku Isi guterwa n'imyuka ihumanya ikirere , kwatumye urubura ruba rwarabaye nk'umusozi ruherereye hafi y'aho Isi yikaragira ( pôle ) rwaratangiye kuyonga bigatuma amazi y'inyanja ziri kuri pôle yiyongera , Isi ikaremera bigatuma yihuta .
Nubwo bimeze bitya ariko , nta ngaruka na nke bizagira ku mibereho y'abantu ndetse aba bashakashatsi bavuze ko bizamara igihe runaka kitari kinini , ubundi Isi igasubira ku kugenda gahoro nk'uko byahoze .
Menya ibidasanzwe kuri Cotam Unité , indege Perezida Macron agendamo .
Cotam Unité cyangwa se COTAM 001 ni izina rihabwa indege itwaye Perezida w'u Bufaransa .
Mu Ugushyingo 2010 ni bwo indege Airbus A330 - 200 yasimbuye indege zari zisanzwe zikoreshwa mu gutwara Perezida w'u Bufaransa .
Iyi ndege ni nayo iherutse kugeza Perezida Emmanuel Macron ku Kibuga cy'Indege Mpuzamahanga cya Kigali mu ruzinduko rw'iminsi ibiri yagiriye mu Rwanda .
Iyi ndege ifatwa nk'iya gisirikare cyane ko aricyo gishinzwe kuyigenzura umunsi ku munsi aha ni naho ikomora izina ryayo kuko mu busanzwe Cotam ni impine y'umutwe w'Igisirikare cy'u Bufaransa kirwanira mu kirere uzwi nka ( Commandement du transport aérien militaire ) gusa mu 1994 uyu mutwe waje guhindura izina ariko indege itwaye Perezida yose
ikomeza kwitwa gutya .
Mu 2010 Nicolas Sarkozy wayoboraga u Bufaransa niwe watanze igitekerezo cy'uko hagurwa indege nshya izajya itwara Perezida w'iki gihugu .
Iki gihe yasabaga ko hagurwa indege yagutse kandi ishobora gukora urugendo rurerure idahagaze kuko yavugaga ko ebyiri zakoreshwaga zo mu bwoko bwa Airbus A319CJ zifite ubushobozi buri hasi .
Iki gitekerezo cya Sarkozy cyakiriwe neza na Leta y'u Bufaransa ariko Minisiteri y'Ingabo igaragaza ko idafite amafaranga ahagije yatuma igura indege nshya , ahubwo ifata umwanzuro wo kugura iyakoreshejwe ariko ikavugururwa .
Aha niho Minisiteri y'Ingabo yarambagije indege nziza ikwiriye Perezida w'Igihugu maze iza guhitamo Airbus A330 - 200 yari isanzwe ari iy'ikigo gikora ubwikorezi bwo mu kirere cya Air Caraïbes .
Amakuru avuga ko iyi ndege yaguzwe arenga miliyari 60Frw ariko ikaza kugenda yongerwamo ikoranabuhanga ritandukanye ari nako ikorerwa amavugurura atuma iva ku kuba indege y'abagenzi ikaba indege itwara Umukuru w'Igihugu .
Iyi ndege kugeza uyu munsi itwara Perezida Macron ikunze guhabwa akazina k'Inyoni n'abasirikare bamurinda .
Iyi ndege yihariye ikoreshwa na Perezida w'u Bufaransa , ifite icyumba cyihariye cya perezida kirimo ibitanda bibiri , urwambariro , ubwogero n'ubwiherero bubiri .
Ifitemo ibiro bya Perezida ashobora gukoreramo akazi ke ka buri munsi akanatangiramo amabwiriza ku ngabo cyangwa abandi bose ashatse kugezaho ijambo .
Iyi Airbus A330 - 200 ya Perezida w'u Bufaransa kandi ifite aho Perezida ashobora kunywera ikawa , ikagira ibiro by'umunyamabanga we ndetse n'icyumba cy'inama cyayo gifite uburyo butuma amajwi adasohoka , iki cyumba cy'inama kandi kirimo ameza ashobora gukikizwa n'abantu 12 bicaye bari mu nama .
Itumanaho rikoreshwa muri iyi ndege rimufasha gukomeza inshingano nk'umukuru w'igihugu , afite gutanga ubutumwa ashaka aho ashaka amasaha 24 ku yandi .
Indege ya Macron kandi mu gihe akiri ku mwanya w'umukuru w'Igihugu ifite gahunda z'ubuvuzi buteye imbere aho muri yo harimo icyumba gito kirimo serivisi z'ubuvuzi mu gihe cyose haba hari uzikeneye .
Cotam Unité kandi ifite igice gishobora kujyamo abantu 60 baherekeje Perezida barimo abanyamakuru , abakozi n'abandi b'ingenzi umukuru w'igihugu yakwifuza guherekezwa na bo .
Iyi ndege ya Macron ihuriye na Air Force One itwara perezida wa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ku buryo bwo kwirinda ibisasu bikomeye nka misile , zikomora ku gisirikare cya Israel kiri mu bikomeye ku isi nk'uko byatangajwe n'urubuga rwa Mako rwo muri Israel aho ruvuga ko uburyo bw'ubwirinzi izi ndege zidasanzwe zikoresha bwakozwe
n'Ikigo cy'Aba - Israel cyitwa Elbit Systems .
Mu zindi ndege zakoreshejwe mu gutwara abaperezida b'u Bufaransa harimo Falcon7X kuva mu 2009 kugeza 2010 , iyi yo iracyanifashishwa mu gihe perezida agiye hafi cyangwa ahantu hadafite ubushobozi bwo kwakira indege nini nka Airbus A330 - 200 , ikoreshwa kandi mu gutwara Minisitiri w'Intebe n'abandi bayobozi bakuru .
Google yatangije impinduka zizatuma ushaka kuyibikaho ibintu byinshi yishyura .
Umuntu wese ufunguye konti kuri Google , binyuze nko muri Gmail , aba afite uburenganzira bwo kubika amakuru ari munsi ya 15GB kuri """" Google Drive , """" serivise ibika amakuru y'abakiliya ba Google .
Kuva muri 2015 , Google ifite indi serivise yitwa """" Google Photos , """" ifasha abantu mu kubika amafoto na video zabo zitaremereye ku buntu , kandi ikaba itagira umupaka mu bijyanye n'amakuru ishobora kubikwaho .
Nyuma yo kubona uburyo abantu bakomeje kugira inyota yo kubika amakuru arimo amafoto na video ahantu hizewe , mu 2018 Google yazanye indi serivise izwi nka """" Google One , """" icuruza umwanya wo kubikaho amakuru ku bantu bamaze kuzuza za 15GB z'ubuntu kuri """" Google Drive , """" ariko bakaba bifuza undi mwanya wo kubikaho
amakuru yabo .
Mu gutera ingabo mu bitugu iyi serivise nshya , Google yavuze ko abantu bakoresha Google Photos batari basanzwe bafite umwanya ntarengwa wo kubikaho amakuru , bazajya bahabwa 15GB z'ubuntu nk'uko bigenda kuri Google Drive , ubundi umuntu yamara umwanya yateganyirijwe , agomba kugura uwundi kuri """" Google One . """"
Ku bantu bari basanzwe bafite amafoto na video kuri Google Photos , iki cyemezo ntikizagira ingaruka ku makuru bari barabitseho , ahubwo kizagira ingaruka ku makuru bazatangira gushyiraho nyuma ya tariki ya 1 Kamena 2021 .
Igiciro cya macye kuri Google One ni 2 $ ( arenga 1 , 900 Frw ) ku kwezi , umuntu akazajya ahabwa umwanya ungana na 100GB cyangwa se 20 $ ku mwaka .
Uwifuza 200GB azajya yishyura 3 $ ku kwezi na 30 $ ku mwaka mu gihe ushaka 2TB azajya yishyura 10 $ ku kwezi na 100 $ ku kwezi .
Umuntu ukoresha Google One kandi azaba afite uburenganzira bwo kuyisangira n'abandi bantu batanu .
Bivugwa ko 80 % by'abasanzwe bakoresha serivise za Google Drive batazakenera kugura serivise za Google One vuba kuko ibyo babikaho bidasaba umwanya munini , icyakora bitewe n'uburyo abantu bashishikajwe no kubika amakuru yabo ahantu hizewe ,
byitezwe ko abazakenera serivise zo kubika amakuru yabo mu buryo bw'ikoranabuhanga baziyongera mu minsi iri imbere .
Microsoft yashinje u Burusiya igitero cy'ikoranabuhanga cyagabwe kuri emails zisaga ibihumbi bitatu .
Microsoft yavuze ko igitero cyo muri iki Cyumweru cyagabwe kuri emails 3 . 000 z'abo mu miryango n'ibigo byiganjemo ibyo muri Amerika , ariko ba nyirazo bakaba ari abo mu bihugu 24 .
Iyo Sosiyete yasobanuye ko ibigo byari bigenderewe cyane ari ibya Guverinoma kandi bifite aho bihuriye n'amahanga , bityo ko """" ubutasi bw'u Burusiya ari bwo bwabikoze """" kuko no mu mwaka ushize hari ikindi kijya gusa n'icyo cyagabwe kuri Sosiyete ya Solar Winds hagenderewe kwiba amakuru nk'ayo .
Icyo gihe igitero cyageze ku bigo bya Leta ya Amerika , sosiyete 100 z'abikorera n'indi miryango mike y'Abongereza .
Abantu 18 . 000 ni bo bagizweho ingaruka nacyo .
Igitero giheruka ngo cyatangiye hinjirirwa email ikoreshwa mu kumenyekanisha ibikorwa by'Ikigega cy'Abanyamerika gishinzwe Iterambere Mpuzamahanga ( USAID ) , abakigabye bayikoresha bohereza ubutumwa busa n'ubw'ubugiraneza ariko burimo link ukandaho ikazana virus kuri mudasobwa , ukibwa amakuru ndetse n'izindi mudasobwa zihuriye ku
muyoboro wa internet umwe n'iyo zikagerwaho na virus .
Microsoft yatangaje ko icyo gitero cyagiye gihagarikwa kuri mudasobwa nyinshi ariko ntiharamenyekana umubare w'ab'ibwe amakuru na mudasobwa zashyizweho virus .
U Burusiya bwabihakanye buvuga ko ntaho buhuriye n'ibyo bitero byombi , nk'uko no mu mwaka ushize bwabigenje
Hagiye gutoranywa imishinga mito y'ishoramari rishingiye ku ikoranabuhanga izahabwa ubufasha bwa miliyoni 19 Frw .
Ni ku nshuro ya kabiri iyo mishinga igiye gutoranywa muri gahunda yiswe FinTech Hub ibaho ku bufatanye n'Ikigega cy'Umuryango w'Abibumbye gishyigikira Iterambere ry'Imishinga yo mu bihugu bikiri mu nzira y'amajyambere ( UNCDF ) Ishami ry'u Rwanda , Minisiteri y'Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo na Kigali Innovation City .
Ine yatoranyijwe ku ikubitiro mu Ukwakira 2020 irimo Benefactors , Hepta Pay Ltd , Raisin Ltd na Exuus .
Mu kiganiro n'itangazamakuru cyabaye kuri uyu wa 25 Gicurasi 2021 , Umuyobozi w'Ishami rishinzwe Ikoranabuhanga muri PSF ari naryo rigenzura ishyirwa mu bikorwa ry'iyo gahunda , Ntale Alex , yavuze ko buri nyuma y'amezi atandatu hazajya hatoranywa imishinga itanu , ifashwe hagamijwe kongerera ba nyirayo ubumenyi , kubahuza
n'abafatanyabikorwa , kubafasha kubona igishoro no kugera ku isoko , ndetse no kugaragaza amahirwe ahari .
Yavuze ko intego ya FinTech Hub ari uko 80 % by'imishinga ikora iryo shoramari mu Rwanda yagerwaho n'iyo gahunda , byarimba bikaba 100 % .
Yakomeje ati """" Turashaka gushyigikira imishinga yacu ku buryo ibasha kongera umubare w'abakiliya ikaguka , ari nako tubafasha mu bukangurambaga bwo gutangiza imishyikirano n'imikoranire izayifasha [ imishinga ] gukura . """"
Umuyobozi wa UNCDF Ishami ry'u Rwanda , Uwamahoro Roselyne , yavuze ko icyo Kigega cyagize ubufatanye muri FinTech Hub hagamijwe gushyigikira uburyo bwo gushaka ibisubizo by'ibibazo byugarije ubukungu hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga ; by'umwihariko nyuma y'ingaruka bwagizweho n'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Yagize ati """" Turi gushaka uko twakorana na za guverinoma zitandukanye by'umwihariko iy'u Rwanda , mu guteza imbere ubukungu bushingiye ku ikoranabuhanga . """"
Umusesesenguzi w'Ikoranabuhanga ry'Ibigo bya Leta muri Minisiteri y'Ikoranabuhanga na Inovasiyo , Munezero Angelos , yatangaje ko FinTechHub iri mu murongo umwe na gahunda Leta y'u Rwanda yihaye yo guteza imbere ihangwa ry'udushya mu ikoranabuhanga , haba imbere mu gihugu no mu Karere .
Yifashishije urugero rw'indege za Drone zifashishwa mu buvuzi , yagize ati """" Ikoranabuhanga ritangirizwa mu Rwanda hashakishwa ibisubizo [ by'ibibazo bihari ] nyuma rikitabazwa n'ibihugu by'amahanga . """"
Drone za Zipline zatangiye gukoreshwa mu rwego rw'ubuzima mu 2016 , nyuma ziza kwitabazwa na Ghana , Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika n'u Buyapani .
Imishinga itoranywa muri FinTech Hub ihabwa ubufasha mu buryo bw'ubumenyi ikeneye , ubw'imikorere ndetse igahabwa amafaranga y'igishoro ku musozo w'iyo gahunda imara amezi atandatu .
Inyungu umushinga watoranyijwe ukuramo zibarirwa agaciro ka 20 . 000 $ .
Imishinga iri gutoranywa binyuze mu gukora igenzura ku rwego igezeho ikura ( kuko hafashwa iyatangiye gukora ) , igihe ishobora kuramba ndetse n'ibisubizo itanga mu ishoramari ryimakaza ikoranabuhanga .
Abashaka kurushanwa babisaba banyuze kuri rubuga
NASA muri gahunda yo kohereza icyogajuru ku Kwezi mu 2023 .
Icyo kigo gisanzwe gifite umushinga wiswe Artemis ugamije kuzageza umushakashatsi w'umugore wa mbere ku Kwezi mu 2024 , hakagezwayo n'uw'umugabo bwa kabiri nyuma ya Neil Armstrong na Edwin Aldrin Buzz bahageze ku wa 20 Nyakanga 1969 .
Mu gutegura urugendo rw'abo bahanga mu by'isanzure , NASA izohereza icyogajuru cyiswe VIPER mu mpera za 2023 , kizaba gifite amatara kikahagendagenda mu gihe cy'iminsi 100 ya hano ku Isi igereranywa n'itatu yo ku Kwezi .
Cyateguranywe batiri y'imirasire y'izuba ifite ubushobozi bwo kubika 450 watts .
Dail Mail yatangaje ko icyo cyogajuru kizaba cyoherejwe ngo kijye gushaka ahantu heza abashakasahatsi bo mu 2024 bazashinga ibirindiro n'uduce turimo amazi .
Umuyobozi w'Itsinda rishinzwe Ubushakashatsi bwo kuri uwo mubumbe muri NASA , Lori Glaze , yavuze ko amakuru VIPER izafata azafasha abazoherezwayo kumenya ahantu hatuje bajya ndetse n'aho urubura ruherereye .
Yagize ati """" Amakuru tuzahabwa na VIPER afite ikintu gikomeye azafasha abashakashatsi bacu mu kumenya ahantu hakwiye [ bakorera ] n'ahari urubura ku Kwezi . """"
Byitezwe ko VIPER izagwa mu gice cy'Amajyepfo , ikagenda kilometero 20 .
Umushinga wayo ufite agaciro ka miliyoni 433 . 5 $ .
Umushinga wa Artemis witezweho ko nyuma yo kugeza umugore ku Kwezi nk'agashya mu 2024 , hazakurikiraho gutuza umuntu kuri uwo mubumbe mu 2028 .
BAL yatanze mudasobwa 150 ku barimu bo mu mashuri y'i Kigali ( Amafoto )
Iki gikorwa cyabaye kuri uyu wa 23 Gicurasi 2021 hagati y'umukino w'umunsi wa karindwi wa Basketball Africa League wahuje AS Douanes na Zamalek muri Kigali Arena .
Ubuyobozi bwa Basketall Africa League bwahisemo gushyigikira uburezi muri Afurika nyuma y'uko bukomwe mu nkokora n'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 cyerekanye ko hakwiye ko nabwo bugendana n'ikoranabuhanga rigezweho mu myigishirize , mu kazi no mu itumanaho .
BAL yatanze mudasobwa 150 kugira ngo ishyigikire umushinga wo kugeza mudasobwa kuri buri munyeshuri na buri mwarimu mu Rwanda nk'uko byagarutsweho na Perezida wayo , Amadou Gallo Fall mu butumwa bwe .
Ati """" Kuva mu mwaka ushize , BAL yashyigikiye imiryango itandukanye mu kurwanya icyorezo cya COVID - 19 .
Uyu munsi twishimiye gushyigikira abarezi binyuze mu mushinga wa REB wo gufasha buri mwarimu kubona ibyo akeneye bijyanye n'iki kinyejana cya 21 . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Buri mwarimu hano , iri joro arabona mudasobwa yo gushyigikira iterambere ry'umwuga wabo .
Uyu munsi ndashaka gushimira Umuyobozi Mukuru wa REB , Dr Nelson Mbarushimana n'ikipe ye bari kumwe natwe hano .
Uyu munsi ni uwanyu barimu , ndabashimira ubwitange mugirira urubyiruko rwacu . """"
Umuyobozi Mukuru w'Urwego rw'Igihugu rushinzwe Uburezi bw'Ibanze ( REB ) , Dr . Nelson Mbarushimana , yavuze ko kuba BAL yatanze izi mudasobwa ari ikimenyetso cy'uko ishyigikiye ikoranabuhanga kandi bijyanye n'intego ziyemejwe mu burezi bw'u Rwanda .
Ati """" Ni ikimenyetso cyiza kigaragaza ko bakunda ikoranabuhanga cyane ko natwe twatangiye gahunda yo guha mudasobwa buri mwarimu .
Dufite intego y'uko tuzaha buri mwarimu mudasobwa kuko iki cyorezo cyatwigishije ko umwarimu agomba kuba ayifite kugira ngo abashe kwigisha neza , anakoreshe ikoranabuhanga ahashyira amasomo ye , anavugana n'abanyeshuri aho bari , bityo ireme ry'uburezi rigatera imbere . """"
Uwimana Pétronille uri mu bahawe izi mudasobwa , yavuze ko bigiye kuzamura imyigishirize kuko wasangaga umwarimu akoresha ibitabo bihari gusa , ariko ubu bakaba zajya banashakisha ibintu bitandukanye bazifashishije .
Ati """" Ziraza kudufasha gukora ubushakashatsi , ubundi twigishaga twifashishije ibitabo biri mu ishuri .
Bizazamura urwego rw'imyigishirize . """"
Mbarushimana Steven wigisha muri GS Kimisagara na we yavuze ko bigiye kuzamura imyigishirize kuko hari ubumenyi bazungukira kuri internet .
Ati """" Iyi mudasobwa mpawe iraza kumfasha gufasha abanyeshuri mu myigire ya buri munsi .
Twibandaga mu bitabo , ariko ubu dushobora kujya kuri Google tukahabona amakuru menshi , ziradufasha gusobanukirwa . """"
Abarimu 150 bahawe izi mudasobwa ni abo mu bigo by'amashuri 65 byo mu Turere twa Nyarugenge , Kicukiro na Gasabo .
Muri iki gihe cya vuba , u Rwanda rwubatse ibyumba bishya by'amashuri 22 . 000 ndetse rutanga akazi ku barimu bashya 29 . 000 .
Irushanwa rya Basketball Africa League riri kuba ku nshuro ya mbere , ryateguwe na FIBA Afrique ku bufatanye na Shampiyona ya Basketball muri Amerika , NBA .
Amakipe 12 yo mu bihugu 12 bya Afurika ni yo yaryitabiriye , aho rizasozwa tariki ya 30 Gicurasi 2021 .
Microsoft yatangaje ihagarikwa rya burundu rya Internet Explorer . Sean Lyndersay uhagarariye porogaramu nshya y'uru ruganda yitwa Microsoft Edge yasimbuye Internet Explorer , yavuze ko izahagarikwa tariki 15 Kamena 2022 .
Bivuze ko hakiri umwaka wo kuyifashisha ku bayikoresha .
Internet Explorer yatangiye tariki 16 Kanama 1995 , yagiye yigarurira Isi y'ikoranabuhanga uko murandasi yagendaga irushaho gukoreshwa , kugeza ubwo mu 2004 iciye agahigo ikiharira isoko ry'abantu bakoresha murandasi bashakisha , ku gipimo cya 95 % .
Yakomeje muri iyo nzira kugeza mu 2012 , ubundi nyuma yaho itangira kubura abafana .
Icyo gihe izindi porogaramu zifasha abantu gushakisha ibintu kuri internet zari zimaze igihe zivutse , zizana udushya Internet Explorer itagiraga zitangira kwigarurira imitima y'abakoresha murandasi , harimo nka Chrome ya Google yatangiye mu 2008 yazanye umwihariko wo gukoreshwa muri telefone ngendanwa , bituma imenyekana cyane .
Kugeza ubu Chrome ni yo ifite isoko rinini ku Isi , aho yihariye 65 % by'abashakisha kuri murandasi , igakurikirwa n'iyitwa Safari y'Ikigo Apple gikora telefone za iPhone , ifite 19 % , iya gatatu ikaba Firefox ya Mozilla ifite 3 . 59 % , iya kane ni Edge yasimbuye Internet Explorer ifite 3 . 39 % nk'uko bitangazwa n'ikigo cya Statscounter gikora ubusesenguzi
bw'imbuga z'ikoranabuhanga .
Sean Lyndersay watangaje iby'ihagarikwa rya Internet Explorer , yavuze ko Microsoft Edge yayisimbuye ifite udushya twinshi ndetse yaje ikosora amakosa yose ya Internet Explorer , aho yihuta cyane kuyirusha , ikagira n'uburyo bugezweho bwo gushakisha ibintu bitandukanye .
Guhagarikwa kw'iyi porogaramu ntabwo bije bitunguranye kuko muri Kanama 2020 Microsoft yatangaje ko iyi porogaramu izaba yahagaritswe muri Kanama 2021 , gusa igihe kiza kwigizwa inyuma .
Nubwo izahagarikwa mu 2022 , tariki 17 Kanama 2021 ntibizaba bigishoboka ko Internet Explorer ikoreshwa muri serivisi zitandukanye za Microsoft nka Microsoft 365 , Outlook ikoreshwa mu kohererezanya email ndetse na One Drive ikoreshwa mu kubika ibintu ubikuye kuri murandasi ( download ) .
Amerika : Ikigo cy'Itumanaho AT & T na Discovery bigiye guhuzwa .
Ubu bufatanye bufite agaciro ka miliyari 150 z'amadolari ya Amerika bwitezweho gutangiza muri Hollywood studio y'akataraboneka nyuma y'aho AT & T yegukanye CNN , HBO na studio ya Warner Bros ikora filime kuva mu 2018 .
Aganira na BBC , Dan Ives , Umuyobozi w'Ikigo cy'Ubushakashatsi mu Ikoranabuhanga , Wedbush Securities , yavuze ko ubu bufatanye bwa AT & T na Discovery bwitezweho kuzafasha ibikorwa byayo mu guhangana n'ibindi bigo nka Netflix , Disney na Amazon , yongeraho ko iyi ari intambwe nziza itewe n'iki kigo .
Uku guhuza amaboko kuzahuriza hamwe inzu ikora film ya Warner Bros . WarnerMedia ifitwe na HBO na HBO Max ubu ifite abafatabuguzi bagera kuri miliyoni 64 ku Isi yose na ho Discovery izwiho kwerekana ibyerekeye inyamaswa imaze kugeza ku bayikurikira muri Amerika miliyoni 88 .
Ubwo AT & T yegukanaga Time Werner mu myaka itatu ishize yateganyaga gushyiraho igitangazamakuru n'ikigo cy'itumanaho gikomeye .
AT & T yafashe ideni rya miliyari 14 ryiyongera kuryo yari isanganywe aho yiteze ko ubu bufatanye na Discovery buzakemura ibibazo by'amadeni .
Mu kwezi kwa kabiri AT & T yemeye kugurisha igice cy'imigabane televiziyo ya DirecTV ikorera kuri Satellite .
AT & T ni Ikigo cy'Itumanaho cya mbere ku Isi cyinjiza agatubutse , cyashinzwe na Alexander Graham Bell mu mwaka wa 1877 .
André Gromyko yavumbuye ubwoko bushya bwa feri ishobora gushyirwa mu modoka nini mu kwirinda impanuka .
Uyu mugabo w'imyaka 49 yifata nk'impirimbanyi y'umutekano wo mu muhanda kuko iyo yivuga agaragaza ko yatangiye gutwara imodoka akiri muto , kuva icyo gihe atangira no guhirimbanira ko umutekano wo mu muhanda waba usesuye .
Mu 2009 yatangiye kwandika ku mutekano wo mu muhanda mu mushinga yise """" Road Safety Initiative Project """" urimo na feri yamaze kurangiza gutunganya afata nk'urukingo rw'impanuka cyane zikorwa n'imodoka nini .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE , yavuze ko iyi feri ifite umwihariko w'uko yahuje amavuta n'umwuka ku buryo ari nabyo biyiha imbaraga nyinshi zidasanganzwe .
Ati """" Iyi feri ifite umwihariko wo kuba yarakozwe hahujwe amavuta n'umwuka bityo bikaba biyiha ububasha bwo kubasha gufata neza kandi cyane .
Amavuta ni ikintu kigira ingufu ariko kitihuta cyane mu gihe umwuka wo wihuta cyane .
Iyo ubihuje rero birafatanya . """"
Yavuze ko iyi feri izajya ishyirwa mu modoka nini gusa .
Ati """" Kuyishyira mu modoka ni ugupfusha ubusa .
Ni ingufu nyinshi waba ushyize ku kantu gato ntabwo imodoka nto zikunze kubura feri . """"
Avuga ubu bushakashatsi bujyanye n'iyi feri yabutangiye mu 2009 ariko ubu mu 2021 akaba aribwo abashije gusohoza umuhigo yari yarihaye .
Ati """" Ni ubushakashatsi natangiye nyuma y'impanuka ziba cyane cyane iz'amakamyo , bus , mini - bus ndetse n'amakamyoneti . """"
Arakomeza ati """" Ni feri izajya ikora nyuma y'aho izindi feri zose bidashoboka .
Ubu nakoreye ubu bushakashatsi ku modoka nto kubera igerageza .
Yari ukuyifashisha mu bushakashatsi nsigaye kuyifata nkayishyira mu modoka nini .
Ni feri y'ingoboka izajya ikora izindi zose zananiwe .
Nta kindi kintu umuntu asigaranye uretse gufata imodoka ukayiroha mu mukingo . """"
Avuga ko iyi feri nta ngaruka na nkeya ifite ku modoka ko ahubwo ari igisubizo ku mpanuka zahitanaga abantu benshi , zikangiza byinshi .
Ati """" Nta ngaruka ifite ahubwo nagiye mbaza abantu batwara imodoka igenewe , bambwira ko umunsi izaba yatangiye kwifashishwa ku bwinshi bizabafasha kugira ngo batazongera kugira ibibazo bya feri .
Nta ngaruka ziza ku mudoka yashyizwemo iyi feri .
Ni ikintu gishya umuntu agishyiraho nk'uko amategeko ya tekiniki abisaba . """"
Iyi feri yamaze kuyandikisha mu Kigo cy'Igihugu cy'Iterambere , RDB , nk'umutungo mu by'ubwenge akaba asigaje kuyijyana kuyipima agahabwa icyangombwa cy'uko yujuje ubuziranenge kigaragaza ko mu buryo bwa tekiniki yizewe ishobora gukora noneho ababishaka bakaba bamugana akayibashyiriramo .
Kuri we iyi feri ni urukingo kuko yemeza ko igiye kugabanya ibibazo bikurikiraho iyo umuntu yakoze impanuka ndetse bikanorohereza ibigo by'ubwishingizi na banyiri imodoka .
Ati """" Bitewe n'ubwishingizi ufite bishyura ibyo waryojwe ariko ibyawe bashobora kutabyishyura bitewe n'uko wishingiye , mu gihe iyi feri izajya ikingira imodoka y'umuntu ndetse n'abantu ntibapfe .
Ari ibyo yakagombye kuryozwa ntabwo azabiryozwa ndetse n'ibyo yakagombye kubura ntabyo azabura .
Abishingizi ntabwo bazongera kugira ibibazo by'impanuka nyinshi . """"
Mu myaka yose yamaze akora iyi feri yemeza ko ikibazo gikomeye yahuye nacyo ari ukubura ubushobozi bw'amafaranga , gusa akaba yishimira ko yabashije kugera ku cyo yifuzaga ndetse feri ubu akaba atakiri kuyifata nk'iye ahubwo ari iy'igihugu .
Ati """" Iyi feri ntabwo ari iyanjye .
Ni iy'igihugu , izava ku gihugu ijya ku Isi .
Kuko niba uyu munsi ushaka kugura ikamyo ya miliyoni izi cyangwa izi ashobora kubwira uruganda rwaje guhaha hano ubu bumenyi noneho abo bakajya bavuga bati reka ntumize ikamyo ariko bongereho na feri y'ingoboka . """"
Iyo umubajije akamuri ku mutima nyuma y'aho iyi feri isa nk'aho yamaze kuyisoza avuga ko yaruhutse ku mutima we , ubu nta kintu azongera kwishinja .
Ati """" Ndaruhutse .
Mu myaka yashize najyaga mbona habayeho impanuka yatewe no kubura feri nkishinja ko ntacyo nakoze .
Ariko , uyu munsi ni nko gukaraba feri igiye mu maboko y'igihugu .
Nyuma yo kureba ko feri ikora tugiye kuyishyira mu ikamyo yikoreye ibintu byinshi .
Iyo urukingo rwakoreshaga doze runaka mu mbeba , iyo ugiye kurushyira mu muntu urayongera . """"
Nikobisanzwe wakoze iyi feri , ubusanzwe yize mécanique automobile .
Mu bindi yakoze harimo umushinga w'umuriro uzajya ubyarwa no guhita kw'imodoka ku muhanda gusa nturarangira .
Yakoze n'uburyo bushyirwa ku modoka bugatuma rétroviseurs zitibwa .
Iyi feri yakoze nta gihe runaka yashyiriweho igomba kumara mu modoka ahubwo izajya igenzurwa mu gihe imodoka irimo nayo igiye kugenzurwa muri controle technique .
Icyogajuru cya NASA cyakoraga ubushakashatsi ku mibumbe igaragiye izuba cyagarutse ku Isi .
Umushinga wo kwiga imiterere n'uko byagenze kugira ngo imibumbe igaragire izuba watangijwe na NASA mu 2016 iwita """" OSIRIS - REx , """" aho yahise yohereza icyogajuru mu isanzure kijya gucukura utumanyu ku ibuye ryegereye Isi ryiswe """" 101955 Benu """" nyuma yo kuvumburwa mu 1999 .
Ni urugendo rurerure rwa kilometero miliyari 2 , 25 rwagitwaye imyaka ibiri kugira ngo kigereyo mu 2018 , kihamara indi myaka ibiri gicukura utuvungukira kuri iryo buye .
Dail Mail yatangaje ko cyazanye udufite uburemere bwa garagama 60 .
Muri izo garama ngo NASA izakoreshaho 25 % maze 75 % bisigazwe bizajye byifashishwa n'abandi bashakashatsi bo mu bihe bizaza bazaba baragize ikoranabuhanga ryisumbuye .
Biteganyijwe ko ku wa 24 Nzeri 2023 ari bwo icyo cyogajuru kizashyika ku butaka .
Twitter yashyizeho uburyo bwo koherereza ishimwe umuntu watanze igitekerezo cyiza
Ubu buryo bwashyizweho mu rwego rwo kugira ngo abantu batambutsa ibitekerezo byiza bifitiye sosiyete umumaro bajye babishimirwa .
Uru rubuga rwatangaje ko mu ntangiriro iyi gahunda hari abantu igenewe barimo abanyamakuru , inzobere mu bintu bitandukanye , n'abantu bavugira rubanda batagamije inyungu .
Uburyo bwa """" tip jar """" bwashyizwe kuri Twitter niho ushaka koherereza undi amafaranga azajya akanda ubundi ahabwe uburyo butandukanye bwo kohereza burimo Bandcamp , Cash App , Patreon , PayPal na Venmo .
Gusa ubu buryo bwo gutanga amafaranga abantu ntibabuvuzeho rumwe kuko bugaragaza imyirondoro y'uwohereje amafaranga , bifuzaga ko byagirwa ibanga .
Ikindi cyanenzwe kuri iyi serivisi ni ku ruhande rw'abanyamakuru abantu bavuga ko kuboherereza amafaranga bishobora gutuma bashyira amarangamutima mu byo batangaza .
Impungenge ku cyogajuru cyo mu Bushinwa byitezwe ko kiri bugwe ku Isi , ahantu hataramenyekana .
Iki cyogajuru cyahawe izina rya Long March - 5b gipima toni 22 , gifite uburebure bwa metero 53 . 7 , cyagiye mu isanzure tariki 29 Mata , muri kilometero 160 kuri 375 z'ubutumburuke uvuye ku Isi , gusa kuva ubwo cyagiye gitakaza imbaraga , rukuruzi y'Isi ikagenda igikurura bikaba ariyo mpamvu kigiye kugwa bitari
biteganyijwe .
Ikigo cy'i Burayi kigenzura ibyogajuru , European Space Agency , cyatangaje ko aho iki cyogajuru kiri bugwe hataramenyekana , ariko gishobora kugwa aho ari ho hose hagati ya dogere 41 . 5 uvuye mu majyaraguru y'Isi na dogere 41 . 5 uvuye mu Majyepfo yayo .
Uduce duherereye hagati y'izo dogere , harimo igice gito cya Amerika y'Amajyaruguru harimo n'Umujyi wa New York , igice kinini cya Amerika y'Amajyepfo , Afurika yose , Australie ,
ibice bimwe byo muri Aziya harimo Amajyepfo y'u Buyapani n """" ibice bimwe byo mu Bushinwa , ibihugu by'i Burayi birimo Espagne , Portugal , u Butaliyani n'u Bugereki .
Umunyamabanga muri Minisiteri y'Ingabo muri Amerika , Lloyd Austin , yavuze ko bizeye ko kiza kugwa ahantu kitari bwangize ubuzima bw'abantu nko mu nyanja cyangwa ahandi hataba abantu .
Jonathan McDowell , umuhanga mu by'ubumenyi bw'ikirere ukora muri Harvard University yabwiye CNN ati """" Ibyago by'uko iki cyogajuru kiri bwangize ibintu cyangwa kikica umuntu biri ku rugero rwo hasi , nubwo bishobora kubaho , ariko ni ruto cyane . """"
"""" Turateganya ko kiri bugaruke ku Isi hagati y'itariki umunani n'icyenda za Gicurasi , kandi muri iyo minsi ibiri kiraba kizengurutse isi inshuro 30 .
Iki cyogajuru kiri kugenda kilometero hafi ibihumbi 29 ku isaha rero ntushobora kumenya isaha kiri bugwe ku Isi . """"
Amahirwe ahari ni uko iki cyogajuru gishobora kugwa mu nyanja kubera ko igice kinini cy'Isi ari amazi kandi n'ahari ubutaka henshi hakaba hadatuwe .
Ubusanzwe ibyogajuru byinshi bigwa ku Isi bikunda gushwanyukira mu kirere bitaragera ku butaka bw'Isi , ku buryo bidashobora kugira uwo byaginza .
Gusa birashoboka nanone ko gishobora kugera ku Isi kitarashwanyuka nubwo bibaho gake .
Icyogajuru cya Space X cyitezweho kugeza abantu mu isanzure cyagarutse ku butaka nticyaturika .
Umushinga iyo sosiyete y'umuherwe Elon Musk irimo wiswe Starship ugamije gukora ibyogajuru bizajya bigeza abantu n'imizigo ku mibumbe itandukanye yo mu isanzure nka Mars ndetse no ku Kwezi mu gihe bazaba batangiye kuhashyira ibikorwa no kuhatura .
Ni ibyogajuru bikorwa ku buryo amavuta ashyirwa muri moteri yongera agakoreshwa mu rwego rwo kugabanya ikoreshwa ry'ingufu .
Muri bitanu bimaze gusuzumwa byoherezwa mu kirere , icyoherejwe ku wa 5 Gicurasi 2021 cyiswe SN15 ni cyo cyonyine cyagarutse kikagera ku butaka kidaturitse , nyuma yo koherezwa muri kilometero zisaga icumi .
Elon Musk n'akanyamuneza kenshi yahise yandika kuri Twitter ati """" Starship igeze ku butaka mu buryo busanzwe . """"
Ni intambwe ikomeye uwo muherwe yateye ndetse imuha icyizere ko umushinga we uzagerwaho .
Space X ni yo yahawe ikiraka cyo kuzageza ku Kwezi abashakashatsi b'Ikigo cy'Abanyamerika gikorera ubushakashatsi mu isanzure , NASA , mu 2024 .
Ni amasezerano afite agaciro ka miliyari 2 , 89 $ .
Mu 2023 , iyo sosiyete ifite gahunda yo kuzageza bwa mbere abagenzi ku kwezi bagiye mu butembere , bazaba barangajwe imbere n'umuherwe w'Umuyapani , Yusaku Maezawa .
Facebook ishobora kwisubiraho ku gufunga konti ya Trump burundu .
BBC yatangaje ko ako kanama kerekanye ko uwo mwanzuro """" utagena igihe runaka konti izafungurwamo , kandi udakwiye . """"
Facebook yasabwe kugira icyo ibikoraho mu gihe cy'amezi atandatu , """" ikongera kuwusuzuma """" hakubahirizwa amabwiriza asanzwe agenderwaho no ku bandi bakoresha urwo rubuga basanzwe .
Impamvu ako kanama gaheraho kagaragaza ko uwo mwanzuro wafashwe mu buryo budakwiye , ngo n'uko hatagendewe ku mabwiriza Facebook isanzwe ikoresha agena igihe runaka konti ifungwa .
Mu kiganiro n'itangazamakuru , umwe mu bagize ako kanama , Helle Thorning - Schmidt , yavuze ko basabye Facebook gufata umwanzuro unyuze mu mucyo .
Yagize ati """" Turimo kubwira Facebook ngo isubize amaso inyuma kandi ishyire umucyo mu buryo yakoze ibi bintu .
Ikwiye gufata kimwe abakoresha urubuga bose , kandi igahana byubahirije amategeko itabogama . """"
Ubuyobozi bwa Facebook bwatangaje ko bugiye """" gusuzuma umwanzuro bwagejejweho n'ako kanama , hanyuma bukore igikwiye kandi gisobanutse . """"
Donald Trump yakumiwe kuri Facebook na Instagram mu ntangiriro z'uyu mwaka , nyuma y'ubutumwa yahashyize bwagaragazaga ko ari ku ruhande rw'abateje imvururu zabaye ku Ngoro y'Inteko Ishinga Amategeko ya Amerika ku wa 6 Mutarama 2021 zigahitana batanu .
Uretse kuri izo mbuga , Trump yanakumiwe kuri Twitter na You Tube .
Canal + yagaragaje icyifuzo cyo gushyira televiziyo zose zo mu Rwanda ku muyoboro wayo .
Byatangajwe n'Umuyobozi wa Canal + mu Rwanda , Sophie Tchatchoua mu muhango wo kumurika Pacis TV ya Kiliziya Gatolika , nayo yahise yiyongera ku mubare w'izizajya ziboneka kuri uyu muyoboro wa Canal + .
Pacis TV yaje yiyongera ku zindi zisanzwe zigaragara kuri Canal + zirimo BTN Tv , Isango Tv , Authentic Tv , Genesis Tv , KC2 , Flash Tv , TV1 , Televiziyo y'Igihugu ( RTV ) na Tv10 .
Tchatchoua yavuze ko kugeza ubu bagize televiziyo 10 zo mu Rwanda ziboneka ku muyoboro wabo ariko hari gahunda y'uko n'izindi zisigaye bazakorana nazo .
Ati """" Hari abaturage batabashaga gukurikira Pacis Tv mu bihe bya Covid - 19 , twumvise tugomba kugira uruhare mu guha abantu ubushobozi bwo gukurikirana Pacis TV by'umwihariko gahunda zayo za Gikirisitu . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Ubu ibaye shene ya 10 hano mu Rwanda igiye kuri Canal + , twifuza ko televiziyo zose zo mu Rwanda zajya zigaragara kuri Canal + ariko atari aho gusa ahubwo no mu bihugu byose bikoresha ururimi rw'Igifaransa muri Afurika . """"
Tchatchoua yavuze ko bizafasha mu kugaragaza ibyiza bikorerwa mu Rwanda no kubimenyekanisha muri Afurika yose ikoresha Igifaransa n'Abanyarwanda batuye muri ibyo bihugu bakabasha kumenya ibibera iwabo .
Padiri Mukuru wa Paruwasi Remera ari naho Pacis TV yatangiriye , Ntagungira Jean Bosco , yavuze ko ubufatanye na Canal + buziye igihe kuko hari ahantu hatandukanye iyi televiziyo itageraga ariko kuri ubu abantu bakaba bagiye kujya bayibona .
Ati """" Tuzagera mu bihugu byinshi na cya gice cy'abanyarwanda bakoresha satellite nabo tuzabasha kubageraho bityo ubutumwa bwiza dutanga bukomeze kugera kuri benshi . """"
Kugaragara kuri Canal + iri mu bihugu birenga 20 muri Afurika ni uburyo bukomeye bwo kugeza ubutumwa bwa televiziyo nyarwanda kure .
kubera ikoresha Satellite , bigiye kongera aho televiziyo zo mu Rwanda zigeza ibyo zitangaza .
Rurageretse hagati ya Apple na Spotify bapfa inyungu y'umurengera icibwa abakoresha porogaramu z'umuziki .
Komisiyo y'uwo muryango ishinzwe ubugenzuzi yatangaje ko hari abakiliya benshi bamaze igihe binubira amafaranga bacibwa kugira ngo babashe gukoresha porogaramu zikinirwaho umuziki mu bikoresho bya Apple nka telefone n'ibindi .
Ikirego cyatanzwe mu myaka ibiri ishize gitangwa na Spotify , porogaramu yifashishwa na benshi kumva umuziki bihitiyemo .
Iyo sosiyete yatangaje ko Apple iri kwica isoko kuko porogaramu yose ikinirwaho umuziki , iyo isabye gushyirwa muri App Store icibwa inyungu y'umurengera , bigatuma n'abakiliya binuba .
Ibi birego biramutse bihamye Apple , BBC yatangaje ko yabihanirwa cyane kandi igasabwa guhindura imikorere .
Porogaramu zikina umuziki zikoreshwa n'abifashisha ibikoresho bya Apple , zisabwa kwishyura iyo sosiyete 30 % by'ayo zaciye umukiliya .
Spotify yatanze ikirego ivuga ko ayo mafaranga ari menshi .
Komisiyo ya EU ishinzwe ubugenzuzi yagaragaje ko ibyo Apple ikora biri kwica isoko ry'abakora porogaramu zikinirwaho umuziki , bikagira n'ingaruka ku bifashisha ibikoresho byifashiha iOS ya Apple , aribo bakiliya .
Ibyo bihabanye n'amabwiriza ya EU .
Apple yahise nayo isohora itangazo , ivuga ko Spotify itakabaye ibarega mu gihe na 99 % by'amafaranga yinjije nta nyungu Apple irayabonera .
Bavuze ko ikigaragara , Spotify ishaka kwikubira inyungu zose ziva muri porogaramu yayo , ariko ikirengagiza ko kugira ngo abakiliya bayibone hari abandi baba babigizemo uruhare bakwiriye gushimirwa .
Hashize igihe bamwe mu bakora porogaramu zifashishwa na Apple binubira uburyo inyungu bacibwa ihanitse .
Byatumye iyo sosiyete igabanya , ishyiraho inyungu ya 15 % ku bafite porogaramu zinjiza munsi ya miliyoni y'amadolari ku mwaka .
Epic Games yakoze umukino uzwi nka Fortnite nayo iheruka kurega Apple igaragaza ko bacibwa amafaranga menshi , basaba ko 30 % bishyura Apple kuri buri mukiliya babonye agabanywa .
Byarangiye Apple ivanye uwo mukino muri App Store nubwo rukigeretse mu nkiko hagati y'izo sosiyete zombi .
Urubanza rwazo ruzasubukurwa mu cyumweru gitaha .
Abiga mu yisumbuye bashyiriweho ikoranabuhanga ribafasha mu masomo ya siyansi n'imibare .
Iki kigo cyatangiye gukorera mu Rwanda mu Ukwakira 2020 , gisanzwe gikorera muri Afurika y'Epfo , Ghana no muri Nigeria , aho gitanga imyitozo y'imibare , ubugenge ( Physique ) n'ubutabire ( Chimie ) ku banyeshuri biga muwa Mbere w'amashuri yisumbuye kugera mu wa Kane .
Uko bikorwa , umunyeshuri wiyandikishije muri iyi gahunda , ajya ku rubuga rwa Siyavula haba harimo imyitozo ya buri somo bijyanye n'inyigisho zaryo , ubundi akayikora .
Haba hariho n'ibisubizo ku buryo iyo acyishe bamwereka igisubizo n'inzira cyakozwemo .
Iyi gahunda ifasha abanyeshuri gusubira mu byo bize , ndetse hari n'uburyo umwarimu wabo abasha kureba ibyo bakoze bityo akamenya aho ashyira ingufu mu masomo .
Bamwe mu banyeshuri baganiriye na IGIHE biga King David Academy , bavuze ko iyi porogaramu ibafasha mu kwimenyereza amasomo baba bize .
Sesonga Brian Bugingo wiga mu mwaka wa Kabiri yagize ati """" iyi gahunda imfasha cyane cyane mu kwitegura ibizamini , nkakora imyitozo ikanamfasha kumenya birushijeho amasomo , cyane cyane mu mibare na physique ( ubugenge ) . """"
Umwangange Anaise Norah wiga mu mwaka wa Mbere we yagize ati """" Mu bihe bya Coronavirus hari igihe cyigeze kugera tukajya muri guma mu rugo , Siyavula yamfashije kwiyibutsa amasomo nize [ . . . ] ubu iyo umwarimu yakwigishije ibintu ntubyumve neza , ukoresha Siyavula ukiha imyitozo kugira ngo urebe ko ibyo yakwigishije
wabifashe . """"
Umwarimu w'aba banyeshuri mu isomo ry'ubugenge , Nawugaba Stephen , avuga ko gahunda ya Siyavula imufasha cyane mu kureba urwego abanyeshuri be bumviseho isomo .
Ati """" Siyavula igira imyitozo myinshi , rero iyo nigishije isomo runaka mbaha isuzuma bumenyi nkoresheje Siyavula , nkabaha umwanya bakajya muri """" computer lab """" ( icyuma kibamo mudasobwa ) kurikora .
Iyo nsanze benshi batsinzwe , mbaha undi mwanya bagakomeza kwitoza . """"
Kugeza ubu iki kigo gikorana n'ibigo icyenda mu Rwanda , birimo King David Academy , Lycée Notre Dame de Cîteaux , Collège Saint André , Groupe Scolaire Gahini , Group Scolaire Nsanga , Groupe Scolaire Duha , Groupe Scolaire Bumba , Group Scolaire Juru , na Group Scolaire Bigugu .
Uretse ibigo bikorana n'iki kigo hari n'abandi banyeshuri barenga 800 baturuka mu bigo binyuranye hirya no hino mu Rwanda bakorana n'iyi gahunda ya Siyavula .
Mu ruzinduko abayobozi bayo bagiriye mu Rwanda mu ishuri rya King David Academy tariki 29 Mata 2021 , bavuze ko Siyavula iri gufasha abanyeshuri mu Rwanda ndetse ko bafite intego yo kuyigeza mu mashuri yose nubwo hakiboneka imbogamizi .
Uwitwa Chiara Walsh ushinzwe ibikorwa bya Siyavula mu Rwanda , yagize ati """" Twagiye duhura n'imbogamizi mu bigo by'amashuri , aho hari ibidafite internet , ibindi bikagira mudasobwa nkeya kandi muri iyi gahunda dukoresha ikoranabuhanga , niyo mpamvu twahereye ku bigo byigenga n'ibifite ubushobozi , ariko dufite gahunda yo
kuyigeza no mu yandi mashuri mu Rwanda hose . """"
Ibigo by'amashuri birashishikarizwa gukoresha iyi gahunda
Umwe mu bahagarariye Siyavula mu Rwanda , Habimana Jean Damascene , avuga ko iyi gahunda kuyikoresha byorohereza abarimu n'abanyeshuri mu myigire n'imyigishirize kuko bituma abana bamenyera gukora imyitozo myinshi , bityo bikabafasha gutsinda mu ishuri .
Yongeyeho ati """" Ibigo bitaratangira gukoresha uburyo bwo kwigisha abanyeshuri hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga , nababwira ko ari byiza bifasha .
Iyi gahunda ni ubuntu ntabwo duca amafaranga ngo umwana atangire kuyikoresha , rero turasaba ko abana bakomeza kuyikunda , uwo ari we wese yakwandika rw . siyavula . com akiyandika agatangira kuyikoresha . """"
Umuyobozi ushinzwe ibikorwa by'ikoranabuhanga muri King David Academy , Alex Sasu , yavuze ko iyi gahunda ya Siyavula iri gufasha abanyeshuri babo gukora imyitozo myinshi nka bumwe mu buryo bufasha umunyeshuri kumva neza isomo .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Njye ku giti cyanjye ndashishikariza ibigo byose bishoboka mu Rwanda gukorana na Siyavula , kuko nibayikoresha bazabona ko hari byinshi izahindura mu myigire y'abanyeshuri , kuko ibaha amahirwe yo kumenya uko basubiza ibibazo . """"
Uretse gufasha abanyeshuri gukora imyitozo , Siyavula igira n'amarushanwa buri kwezi , aho ihemba abanyeshuri n'abarimu b'indashyikirwa ikabaha telefone zigezweho ( smartphone ) , ndetse n'ama - unite ya telefone .
Iki kigo kandi kizagira amarushanwa y'umwaka muri Kanama 2021 , aho kizahemba ibigo , abanyeshuri n'abarimu b'indashyikirwa .
Igihembo gikuru kizaba ari mudasobwa .
Umunyeshuri cyangwa umwarimu ukeneye kumenya birushijeho imikorere ya Siyavula yabahamagara kuri 0789 068 321 .
Abarimo Miss Kalimpinya bakoze ikoranabuhanga ryifashishwa n'amahoteli hirindwa Covid - 19 .
Igitekerezo cyabo bakigize bagamije gufasha abagana za resitora na hoteli kujya basaba bakanahabwa serivisi n'ibindi bashaka batagombye kujya kuvugana n'abakozi baho cyangwa ngo bafate ku rupapuro ruriho urutonde rw'ibihari n'ibiciro byabyo ( menu ) cyane ko byanaba intandaro yo gukwirakwiza icyorezo .
Ni muri urwo rwego Miss Kalimpinya wize iby'Ishoramari , Rushita Alfene wize iby'Ikoranabuhanga na Bisamaza Ismaïl wize ibya Politiki mpuzamahanga bishyize hamwe bakora application bise """" Ordefene """" ifasha umukiliya kubona ibiribwa n'ibinyobwa biteguye , agahitamo ibyo atumiza , maze akabishyikirizwa aho ari .
Mu kiganiro Rushita Alfene uhagarariye iryo tsinda yagiranye na IGIHE yavuze ko basanze """" ikintu cya mbere umuntu akenera ageze muri resitora na hoteli ni menu """" maze batangira kureba uko yashyirwa mu ikoranabuhanga .
Yagie ati """" Twahisemo kubishyira mu ikoranabuhanga ku buryo umukiliya abasha gufotora ( scan ) QR Code akabona menu y'iyo resitora cyangwa hoteli , akaba yatumiza ibyo ashaka yagaragaje n'ameza yicayeho , cyangwa icyumba arimo .
Icyo gihe byakirwa n'ubishinzwe , ndetse akabona n'igihe bikenewe , na we akagaragaza ko bije umukiliya akabona ko babimuzaniye . """"
Gukoresha Orderfene """" bisaba kuba ufite telefoni igezweho [ smartphone ] """" na resitora cyangwa hoteli ugiyemo ikaba ifite QR code y'iyo application .
Ugera ku meza yawe ukahasanga urupapuro ruriho ya code , maze ukayifotora na camera ya telefoni bagahita bakwereka menu ugasaba ibyo ukeneye .
Haba ibiryo , ibinyobwa cyangwa izindi serivisi zo mu cyumba cya hoteli wabasha kuzihasabira .
Kuva yatangira gukoreshwa muri Kanama 2020 , iratanga icyizere cyo kudatenguha abayikoresha mu gihe internet yaba ikora neza , cyane ko basigaye banayitangana Wifi nyuma y'uko abayikoresheje bwa mbere batenguhwaga na internet .
Icyongereza n'Igifaransa ni zo ndimi zikoreshwa kuri iyo application kugeza ubu , ariko hari gahunda yo kuzashyiramo n'Ikinyarwanda kugira ngo hatagira uhura n'imbogamizi z'ururimi mu gihe ashaka kuyikoresha .
ifasha umukiliya n'umucuruzi gutanga no guhabwa serivisi mu buryo bwihuse , bunoze kandi bujyanye n'igihe .
U Rwanda ku mwanya wa 13 muri Afurika mu kugira internet ihendutse .
Iyo raporo ikorwa n'Ikigo cy'Abongereza gikora ubushakashatsi ku ikoranabuhanga , Cable , igaragaraho ibihugu 230 byo hirya no hino ku Isi .
Urutonde rwakozwe hashingiwe ku mpuzandengo y'igiciro cya gigabyte imwe ya internet mu gihugu maze ako gaciro kagashyirwa mu madorali ya Amerika .
Ku Rwanda , hagaragajwe ko gigabyte imwe mu 2021 iri ku mpuzandengo ya 1 . 133 , 33 Frw angana na 1 , 25 $ ivuye ku 1 , 48 $ mu 2020 , mu gihe mu 2019 yabarirwaga 3 , 79 $ .
Ibikorwa remezo nk'iminara na internet ya 4G na 5G zigezweho nabyo byarebweho kuko bishobora gutuma ikiguzi cyiyongera cyangwa kikaganuka .
Raporo iragira iti """" Ibihugu bimaze igihe kinini bifite 4G na 5G nshya , byagiye bigaragara ko internet yaho ihendutse .
Ibyo biterwa n'uko umubare wa gigabyte abakoresha internet bagenerwa warenze kuba hagati y'imwe na 10 , ukagera mu magana cyangwa ugasanga nta n'urugero ntarengwa ruhari .
Igiciro cya gigabyte muri ibyo bihugu kizaba kiri hasi cyane . """"
U Rwanda ntiruragira 5G ariko mu gihugu hagera 4G ndetse yagejejwe mu mu gihugu mu 2014 .
Ku bw'izo mpamvu , iyo raporo yerekanye ko gigabyte ihenze cyane mu Rwanda muri uyu mwaka igura 21 . 000 Frw ( 23 , 1 $ ) naho ihendutse ikaba igura 315 , 79 Frw ( 0 , 35 $ ) .
Uretse umwanya wa 70 mu bihugu 230 byo ku Isi byakorewemo inyigo , u Rwanda ruri ku mwanya wa 13 muri Afurika yo munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara , no ku wa kabiri muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba inyuma ya Tanzania ifite impuzandengo ya 0 , 75 $ .
Muri ako karere kandi rukurikiwe na Uganda ibarirwa 1 , 56 $ , u Burundi bubarirwa 2 , 1 $ naho Kenya yatangiye gukoresha 5G ni 2 , 25 $ .
Ku Isi urutonde rubimburiwe na Israel ifite impuzandengo ya 0 , 5 $ kuri gigabyte imwe , Kyrgyzstan iri kuri 0 , 15 $ , Fiji kuri 0 , 19 $ , u Butaliyani kuri 0 , 27 $ .
Guinée Equatorial niyo ya nyuma ku kiguzi cya 49 , 67 $ .
Cable yatangaje ko hari ibihugu bitashyizwe ku rutonde kuko amakuru yabyo yagiye abura cyangwa agaciro k'amafaranga bikoresha kukagereranya n'amadorali ya Amerika bikagorana .
Ibyo birimo Sudani y'Epfo , RDC , Erythrée , Zimbabwe , Koreya ya Ruguru , Venezuela n'ibindi .
Ibihugu bifite ubukungu buteye imbere nabyo ntibiri mu myanya y'imbere cyane kuko internet igurishwa ku giciro cyo hejuru bijyanye n'uko ababituye baba banashoboye kuyigura kuri menshi nk'uko iyo raporo ibivuga .
Nk'u Bushinwa buri ku mwanya wa 18 n'impuzandengo ya 0 , 52 $ , Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ziri ku wa 155 na 3 , 33 $ .
U Burusiya bwo buri ku mwanya wa karindwa n'impuzandengo ya 0 , 29 $ kuri gigabyte .
Kugeza muri Mutarama 2021 , habarurwaga ko abakoresha internet mu Rwanda bageze kuri miliyoni 4 , 12 bangana na 31 , 4 % by'Abaturarwanda , biyongeyeho ibihumbi 806 ugereranyije no mu 2020 .
Abakoresha imbuga nkoranyambaga bo biyongeyeho ibihumbi 240 bagera ku bihumbi 850 bangana na 6 , 5 by'abaturarwanda .
Abatunze telefoni mu Rwanda bo ni miliyoni 9 , 69 bangana na 73 , 9 % , umubare wiyongeyeho ibihumbi 175 ugereranyije n'umwaka ushize .
Elon Musk mu mushinga wo gushyira utwuma mu bwonko bwa muntu ibyo atekereza bikikora kuri mudasobwa .
Sky News yatangaje ko iyo nkende yabashije kubikora nyuma y'ibyumweru bitandatu utwo twuma tuyishyizwe mu bice byose by'ubwonko , ikina umukino kuri mudasobwa irimo kunywa umutobe w'umuneke yari yashyiriwe hafi aho .
Uko utwo twuma dukora , icyo ubwonko butekereje duhita tugikora kuri mudasobwa kuko biba byahujwe ariko mu buryo bw'inziramugozi ( wireless ) .
Ni duto cyane ku buryo tugereranywa na kimwe cya cumi cy'ubwoya , ariko tukabasha kugenzura utunyangingo tw'ubwonko dusaga 1000 .
Neuralink ivuga ko ifite intego y'uko iryo koranabuhanga ryakoreshwa ku bantu .
Yagize iti """" Intego yacu ni ugutuma umuntu wagagaye abasha gukoresha mudasobwa cyangwa telefoni , bigizwemo uruhare n'ubwonko gusa . """"
Icyo kigo kandi giheruka gutangaza ko cyashyize utwuma nk'utwo tujya kungana n'igiceri mu bwonko bw'ingurube ebyiri , byose bigendanye n'iyo nyigo .
Avuga kuri iyo nkende yakinaga umukino w'amashusho , Musk yagize ati """" Ntiwabasha kubona aho utwo twuma twashyizwe kandi ni inkende yishimye . """"
Neuralink yemeza ko ubu bushakashatsi nibugenda neza buzanafasha kuzana igisubizo ku ndwara z'ubwonko cyangwa izindi zatuma ingingo zidakora neza nko kutumva , kwibagirwa n'izindi .
Ku rundi ruhande , hari n'ibitekerezo Musk afite muri uwo mushinga abashakashatsi bataremeza ko bishoboka , birimo nko guhindura imikorere y'umubiri mu gihe umuntu yaba yapfuye .
Ati """" Rero niba ugiye gupfa uko umeze bishobora guhindurwa mu bundi buryo cyangwa ukagirwa Robot .
Ushobora guhitamo niba ushaka kuba Robot , umuntu cyangwa ikindi kintu . """"
Elon Musk asanzwe afite n'izindi sosiyete zikomeye zizwi mu bya siyansi n'ikoranabuhanga nka Space X ikora ibyogajuru n'ubushakashatsi bwo mu isanzure , ndetse n'iyitwa Tesla ikora imodoka zifashisha amashanyarazi .
Afite kandi umushinga wo kuzageza abantu kuri Mars mu 2024 .
U Bufaransa : Umushoramari yahisemo kwikorera iperereza ku bamwibye kuko Polisi yananiwe .
Pagani yabwiye AFP ko umukozi ushinzwe icungamutungo muri sosiyete ye yitwa Avon yandikiwe n'umuntu kuri email isa n'aho ari iye ( Pagani ) , maze aramubaza ati """" Ese Bertrand yaguhamagaye ? . """"
Aho hari kuwa 8 Mata 2021 .
Mu minota mike , uwo mukozi yahise ahamagarwa n'umugabo amubwira ko ari we witwa Bertrand , amusaba ko amwoherereza byihuse ibihumbi 27 by'amayero ( 325 . 911 $ ) ngo yo kugura indi sosiyete muri Hongrie .
Barakomeje barandikirana kuri email ariko amubuza kugira undi muntu yabibwira .
Pagani yavuze ko abo batekamutwe bari bazi neza imikorere ya sosiyete ye ku buryo bayobeje uwo mukozi akayohereza .
Ku munsi wakurikiyeho umukozi wa banki yohererejwemo ayo mafaranga yabimenyesheje Pagani agwa mu kantu , ariko ku bw'amahirwe birakurikiranywa aragaruzwa .
Pagani yahise asaba uwo mucungamutungo we gukomeza kwandikirana n'abo bantu kugira ngo amenye aho baherereye abakurikirane , kuko polisi yo yavuze ko """" ikurikirana ibyo ishobora gukora mu buryo bwubahiriza amategeko . """"
Ubu uwo munyemari yamaze gushyira ikoranabuhanga rishya muri mudasobwa ye kugira ngo batongera kumwiba amakuru , ndetse yatangiye gukoresha uburyo bwose bushoboka ngo amenye aho abo batekamutwe baherereye yifashishije ikoranabuhanga .
Yagize ati """" Sinshaka kubareka ngo bagende gutyo gusa .
Sinshobora kwihanganira abo batekamutwe , kandi mu gihe mbona abakabikurikiranye badakora akazi kabo ndabyikorera . """"
Polisi y'icyo gihugu yavuze ko gukurikirana icyo kibazo bigoye cyane kuko bisaba imikoranire mpuzamahanga no kuba ifite amakuru ahagije ku buryo abo batekamutwe bakoresheje bahisha imyirondoro yabo .
Ibyo wamenya kuri Breakthrough Starshot , umushinga uri kureba ko ubuzima bushoboka ku nyenyeri .
Magingo aya , abantu baba ku Isi gusa kandi nta n'ikimenyetso kiragaragaza ko hari ahandi babaye mu isanzure .
Uretse umuntu , nta n'ibindi binyabuzima bizwi neza ko biba mu isanzure kuko ntabyo siyansi yari yemeza .
Ibivejuru ( Aliens ) ni byo bikekwa ko biba mu isanzure , ariko nabyo ntibyemezwa na siyansi ahubwo bamwe bemera ko bibaho abandi bakabihakana .
Umushinga wa Breakthrough Starshot watangijwe mu 2016 , ugamije gukora ubushakashatsi bwifashisha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho hagenzurwa imiterere y'inyenyeri yitwa Alpha Centauri .
Muri uwo mushinga washowemo miliyoni 100 $ , hazoherezwa mu isanzure udukoresho tw'ikoranabuhanga wagereranya na twa mudasobwa duto cyane [ batwise nonocrafts ) .
Ni udukoresho duto ku buryo kamwe kabumbatirwa mu kiganza , ariko tugira uburyo bwo kubika umuriro , aho tubasha kubonwa n'ikoranabuhanga , ndetse tukagira Camera zizafata amafoto yo kuri iyo nyenyeri .
Amafoto afatwa azajya yoherezwa ku Isi .
