Byatumye mu biganiro bya Addis Abeba aho u Burundi bwari buhagarariwe na Minisitiri w'Intebe , bwamaganye icyemezo cyo kugumisha ingabo za Loni mu gihugu .
U Rwanda rwo rwarifashe cyane , ruvuga ko ruzabyigaho rukareba niba bitaba ngombwa ko zihaguma cyangwa se zikahava .
Impungenge zari zihari , kwari uko ibihugu byombi nta ngabo byari bifite ku buryo ikibazo cy'umutekano cyavuka nyuma yo kugenda kw'Ababiligi , nta bushobozi byari kubona bwo guhangana na cyo .
Ikinyamakuru Le Monde muri Gashyantare 1962 cyatangaje ko ibihugu by'aba - Communistes byashakaga ko ingabo z'u Bubiligi zihita zivanwa mu Rwanda n'u Burundi , ahubwo Loni igashyiraho uburyo bufasha gutoza abasirikare b'ibyo bihugu bazahita bafata inshingano Ababiligi bakihava mbere y'ubwigenge .
Loni yo yatangarije ibyo bihugu ko u Rwanda n'u Burundi nibitemera ko ingabo z'u Bubiligi zihaguma , nta mafaranga izabiha yo kubifasha gutoza no kwita ku mutekano wabyo kuko nta bushobozi ibifitiye .
Byakomeje kuzurungutana kugeza ubwo tariki 27 Kamena 1962 , Inteko rusange ya Loni yatoye umwanzuro uvuga ko u Bubiligi bwambuwe inshingano zo kurebera u Rwanda n'u Burundi nk'indagizo bwahawe na Loni , bityo ko ibihugu bihawe ubwigenge buzatangira kubahirizwa tariki 1 Nyakanga uwo mwaka .
Ingabo z'u Bubiligi zahawe kuba zahavuye bitarenze Kanama 1962 kandi Loni igahita yohereza intumwa ziyihagararira mu Rwanda gukurikirana ishyirwa mu bikorwa ry'iyo myanzuro no gufasha ibyo bihugu bishya kwisuganya mu nzego zitandukanye z'iterambere .
Ibihugu byombi hemejwe ko bizakomeza gukorera hamwe ku bijyanye n'ubukungu nka gasutamo n'imicungire y'amafaranga , Banki nkuru ikomeza kuba Banque d'Emission du Rwanda et du Burundi ( BERB ) yari iherereye i Bujumbura .
Tariki ya 1 Mutarama 1964 nibwo ibihugu byombi byatandukanye mu by'ubukungu , buri cyose kigira Banki yacyo na gasutamo .
Umurwa Mukuru w'u Burundi byemejwe ko ukomeza kuba Bujumbura mu gihe u Rwanda rwahisemo Kigali kuko ariho hagaragaraga nko hagati mu gihugu .
Kubera ko mu Rwanda nta kibuga cy'indege mpuzamahanga cyahabaga , u Burundi bwemeye ko Abanyarwanda bazakomeza gukoresha ikibuga cy'indege cya Bujumbura kugeza babonye icyabo kiri ku rwego mpuzamahanga .
Minisitiri w'Intebe Dr Ngirente yitabiriye ibirori by'Isabukuru y'Ubwigenge bw'u Burundi .
Abarundi n'inshuti zabo kuri uyu wa 1 Nyakanga 2021 , bitabiriye Ibirori ngarukamwaka byo kwizihiza Umunsi Mukuru w'Ubwigenge mu Burundi , bibera ku Gicumbi cy'Intwari Igikomangoma Louis Rwagasore ufatwa nk'intwari yaharaniye Ubwigenge bw'Abarundi .
Tariki ya 1 Nyakanga ni nayo u Rwanda rwaboneyeho ubwigenge , nyuma y'igihe ibihugu byombi bikolonijwe n'u Bubiligi .
Ibiro bya Minisitiri w'Intebe byagize biti """" Minisitiri w'Intebe , Dr Ngirente Edouard yageze i Bujumbura guhagararira Perezida Kagame mu birori byo kwizihiza isabukuru y'imyaka 59 y'Ubwigenge bwa Repubulika y'u Burundi . """"
Minisitiri w'Intebe Dr Ngirente ubwo yageraga ku Kibuga cy'Indege cyitiriwe Melchior Ndadaye yakiriwe na Visi Perezida w'u Burundi , Prosper Bazombanza .
Bahaye icyubahiro Igikomangoma Louis Rwagasore
Ibirori byo kwizihiza Ubwigenge mu Burundi , byabimburiwe no guha icyubahiro Igikomangoma Louis Rwagasore , aho abanyacyubahiro bayobowe n'Umukuru w'Igihugu , Gen . Évariste Ndayishimiye bashyize indabo ahari imva ye .
Igikomangoma Louis Rwagasore yagizwe Minisitiri w'Intebe mbere gato y'Ubwigenge ariko araswa nyuma y'amezi atandatu n'umucuruzi w'umugereki wari kumwe n'abarundi batatu , kuri hoteli i Bujumbura , ku wa 13 Ukwakira 1961 .
Ni mbere y'amezi make ngo hatangazwe ubwigenge ku wa 1 Nyakanga 1962 .
Rwagasore ni umwe mu ntwari z'Abarundi ndetse yanitiriwe Stade Nkuru y'Igihugu .
Afite amashuri n'imihanda yagiye imwitirirwa .
Rwagasore yari umuhungu mukuru w'Umwami Mwambutsa IV .
Sarkozy utaranyuzwe no kwirengagizwa na Macron i Kigali babiganiriyeho .
Agahinda ka Nicolas Sarkozy katumye nyuma y'iminsi ine Macron avuye mu Rwanda , amutumira mu biro bya Perezida ( Elysée ) , babiganiraho .
Ikinyamakuru Opinion cyatangaje ko Sarkozy yababajwe n'uburyo atatumiwe ngo aherekeze mugenzi we mu ruzinduko rw'amateka yagiriye i Kigali , akaba ataranakomojweho mu ijambo yahavugiye uwo munsi , ryagaragaje ukwicuza no kwemera uruhare igihugu cye cyagize muri politiki yagejeje kuri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Mu baherekeje Macron i Kigali harimo abayobozi batandukanye mu nzego nkuru z'u Bufaransa nka Minisitiri w'Ububanyi n'Amahanga , Jean - Yves Le Drian n'abandi barimo n'abashoramari bashaka gutangira gukorera mu Rwanda .
Harimo kandi abantu bazi amateka y'u Rwanda nka Gen Jean Varret wahoze ari Umuyobozi ukuriye Ibikorwa bya Gisirikare by'u Bufaransa mu Rwanda hagati ya 1990 na 1993 .
Kwinuba kwa Sarkozy gufite imizi mu kuba ari we Perezida wa mbere w'u Bufaransa wasuye u Rwanda nyuma ya Jenoside mu 2010 , akemera ko igihugu cye cyakoze amakosa .
Nubwo igihu hagati y'u Bufaransa n'u Rwanda cyakomeje nyuma ya Sarkozy kubera politiki , uyu mugabo yakomeje kugaragaza ko yumva u Rwanda n'ingaruka z'ubufasha igihugu cye cyahaye abakoze Jenoside .
Na nyuma yo kuva ku buyobozi yakomeje gusura u Rwanda ndetse tariki 5 Gicurasi 2021 abinyujije muri Le Point , Sarkozy yasabye Macron gusura u Rwanda kandi akahava asabye imbabazi kuko gukomeza gutegereza birambiranye .
Umwe mu ba hafi ba Sarkozy yabwiye Opinion ko """" yatunguwe cyane n'iyi myitwarire """" ya Macron yo kutamutumira ngo bajyane i Kigali , yanahagera ntagaragaze ko hari mugenzi we wagerageje kubyutsa umubano mbere ye nubwo bitakunze neza .
Macron agihaguruka mu Rwanda , Sarkozy yanze kuripfana atangira kugaragaza akababaro ke .
Byatumye tariki 31 Gicurasi Macron amutumira basasa inzobe baraganira .
Muri icyo kiganiro , Macron yamubwiye ko imbwirwaruhame yavugiye mu Rwanda yifuzaga ko iba rusange aho kwibanda ku bantu ku giti cyabo , ari nayo mpamvu atamukomojeho .
Bamwe mu ba hafi ba Macron batangaje ko ibiganiro by'abo bombi byagenze neza kandi babyishimiye .
Uruzinduko rwa Emmanuel Macron mu Rwanda rwafunguye amarembo y'imibanire myiza hagati y'ibihugu byombi , nyuma y'imyaka 27 yo kurebana ay'ingwe kuko icyo gihugu kitemeraga uruhare rwacyo muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Kuva yava ku buyobozi , Sarkozy yakomeje gushimangira umubano mwiza n'u Rwanda ; by'umwihariko akunda kurangira abashoramari b'Abafaransa ingeri bashoramo imari yabo mu Rwanda .
Ku wa 15 Mutarama 2018 , yagiriye uruzinduko mu Rwanda anabonana na Perezida Kagame .
Ni urugendo yazanyemo n'Umuyobozi Mukuru w'Ikigo gikora Ubwikorezi bw'ibicuruzwa byambuka imipaka mu ndege , ku butaka no mu mazi , Cyrille Bolloré .
Umusaruro wavuye muri uru ruzinduko , ni uko Vivendi Group , ikigo gishamikiye kuri Bolloré Holdings ya Cyrille Bolloré cyemeye gushora imari ya miliyoni 40 z'amadolari ya Amerika mu bikorwa bitandukanye bizakorerwa muri Kigali Cultural Village i Rebero mu Karere ka Kicukiro .
Hari n'amakuru avuga ko Sarkozy yaba yaragize uruhare mu koroshya ibikorwa byo gusinya amasezerano y'imikoranire hagati y'u Rwanda na PSG .
Bivugwa ko byaba byarashingiye ku mubano afitanye na QSi iyoborwa na Al - Khelaifi ari na we Perezida wa PSG cyane ko uyu wahoze ari Perezida w'u Bufaransa ariwe watumye igurwa ry'iyi kipe ryoroha .
Ibidasanzwe mu byaranze uruzinduko rwa Tshisekedi i Rubavu na Kagame i Goma .
Ku munsi wa nyuma w'iyo nama yabereye muri Kigali Convention Centre ikitabirwa n'abasaga 1800 mu 2019 , Tshisekedi yavuze ko ibyo abanyapolitiki bakwigira byose """" ibihugu byacu [ u Rwanda na Congo ] bizahora bituranye . """"
Uwabonye cyangwa wumvise u Rwanda na Congo ku bwa Joseph Kabila , biragoye kumwemeza ukuri kw'amashusho amaze iminsi acicikana ku mbuga nkoranyambaga y'abasirikare babiri , uw'u Rwanda na Congo basuhuzanya , bacunze umutekano mu bwubahane nta n'umwe usagariye undi .
Biragoye kumvisha uwo muntu ko Perezida Tshisekedi yasuye u Rwanda kuwa Gatanu , bugacya kuwa Gatandatu Perezida Kagame na we amusura , bakajyana kureba ingaruka zatewe n'iruka rya Nyiragongo ryanashegeshe u Rwanda mu kwezi gushize .
IGIHE yakusanyije bimwe mu bintu bidasanzwe byaranze uruzinduko rw'abakuru b'ibihugu byombi mu mpera z'icyumweru gishize , bishimangira ko Abanyarwanda n'Abanye - Congo ari abavandimwe kurusha uko bamwe babitekereza .
Ubusabane mu bashinzwe kurinda umutekano
Ingabo z'u Rwanda na Congo mu myaka yashize , zahoraga zirebana ay'ingwe cyangwa se bagahura bakozanyaho bya hato na hato ku mupaka , umwe yakwibeshya akarenga ku rubibi rw'igihugu cye , imirwano ikarota .
Itsinda rishinzwe kugenzura imipaka y'u Rwanda na Congo , Expanded Joint Verification Mechanism ( EJVM ) ryari ryarahagorewe .
Ryahoraga mu mpaka zo guhosha umwuka mubi , ufite inkomoko mu myaka isaga 20 ishize ubwo Ingabo z'u Rwanda zambukaga muri icyo gihugu cya kabiri mu bunini muri Afurika , zigiye gusenya inkambi z'impunzi zari ziri kwisuganya ngo zigaruke guteza umutekano muke , nyuma y'aho benshi basize bagize uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe
Abatutsi .
Kuri ubu uwo mwuka w'intambara ku mpande zombi warashize , ibyo bikagaragazwa n'amashusho ndetse n'amafoto yakwirakwijwe mu mpera z'icyumweru gishize , agaragaza umusirikare w'u Rwanda n'uwa Congo bahagararanye ku burinzi ntawe usagariye mugenzi we .
Hari andi mashusho yakoze benshi ku mutima , y'umusirikare w'u Rwanda n'uwa Congo ku nkengero z'ikiyaga cya Kivu , aho umusirikare w'u Rwanda asanga uwa Congo akamusuhuza ( bimwe urubyiruko rwita gutanga chance ) , bakaganira gato imbere yabo mu mazi hari ubwato bugenda .
Ni ikimenyetso cy'uko umugani wa Tshisekedi , abanyapolitiki b'ibihugu byombi babishatse batahiriza umugozi umwe mu gushaka amahoro , akaba umusingi w'iterambere ry'abaturage b'ibihugu byombi , aho gushora imari mu ntambara """" isenya itubaka . """"
Ntabwo ari kenshi Umukuru w'Igihugu kimwe ashobora gusura ikindi , ngo bucye uwo yasuye amwishyura .
Akenshi biterwa n'uko imyiteguro ikomeye ibanziriza uruzinduko rwa Perezida , ifata igihe .
Mu mpera z'icyumweru gishize si ko byagenze , kuko ubwo Perezida Tshisekedi yasozaga uruzinduko rw'umunsi umwe yagiriye mu karere ka Rubavu ku ruhande rw'u Rwanda , Perezida Kagame yazindutse kuwa Gatandatu amusura mu Mujyi wa Goma , banajyana kureba ingaruka zatewe n'Iruka ry'Ikirunga cya Nyiragongo .
Ibi ubwabyo bitanga ubutumwa bukomeye .
Icya mbere ni uko kwa kwishishanya hagati y'ibihugu byombi kwashize , aho igihe cyose umuyobozi ashakiye gusura mugenzi we , ashobora kubikora kandi bigakunda .
Ikindi ni icyizere Perezida Kagame afitiye ubuyobozi bwa Congo , ku buryo yemera gusura agace nka Goma kari muri Kivu y'Amajyaruguru , yakunze kuvugwamo umutekano muke uterwa n'imitwe yitwaje intwaro irimo n'igamije guhungabanya u Rwanda .
Ni icyizere kandi n'umusanzu ku ngamba Tshisekedi aherutse gufata zo guhashya iyo mitwe , byanatumye ubuyobozi bwa Kivu y'Amajyepfo n'Amajyaruguru bushyirwa mu maboko y'igisirikare .
Perezida Kagame yavuze Igifaransa
Ntabwo ari kenshi Perezida Kagame yagiye yumvikana mu ruhame avuga Igifaransa , inshuro zose yabikoze byabaga bifite igisobanuro gikomeye , yishimye cyangwa ashaka gutanga ubutumwa bukomeye .
Inshuro yibukwa ni tariki 7 Mata 2014 muri Stade Amahoro , ubwo yagarukaga ku ruhare rw'u Bufaransa muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu muhango wo Kwibuka Jenoside ku nshuro ya 20 .
Perezida Kagame wavuze ijambo mu gihe umubano w'ibihugu byombi wari ukirimo agatotsi , yavuze ijambo ry'Igifaransa ryabaye ikimenyabose aho yagize ati """" les faits sont têtus """" [ Ibimenyetso birivugira ] .
Indi nshuro ni mu Ugushyingo 2018 ubwo yari Erevan muri Armenia mu nama ya Francophonie .
Mu muhango wo kwishimira intsinzi ya Mushikiwabo mbere y'uko atangira inshingano ze nk'Umunyamabanga Mukuru wa OIF , Perezida Kagame yahishuye uko ari i Erevan yavuze Igifaransa mu kuranga uyu wahoze ari Minisitiri w'Ububanyi n'Amahanga .
Ati """" None se n'icya """" on est ensemble """" cyananira ?
Louise """" a dit qu'on est ensemble . """" """"
Kuba kuri uyu wa Gatandatu yarongeye avugira Igifaransa i Goma , ururimi ubundi adakunze gukoresha dore ko yigeze kuvuga ko rumugora .
Na Tshisekedi ubwe yaratangaye ubwo Perezida Kagame yavugaga ati """" Monsieur le president , vraiment je vous remercie """" [ Nyakubahwa Perezida , ni ukuri ndabashimira ] . """"
Umwambaro mushya ku basirikare barinda Perezida Kagame
Ingabo zishinzwe kurinda Umukuru w'Igihugu [ Republican Guards ) nazo zaserukanye umucyo mu ruzundiko Tshisekedi yagiriye mu Rwanda n'urwo Perezida Kagame yagiriye muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Ahanini izo ngabo zari zimenyerwe mu ipantalo z'umukara n'ishati zijya gusa n'ubururu bw'ikirere , bakarenzaho gillets z'umukara .
Hari ubwo kandi bajyaga bagaragara bambaye amakositimu asanzwe .
Mu cyumweru gishize byari byahindutse .
Haba i Rubavu n'i Goma , izi ngabo zagaragaye mu mwambaro mushya .
Ni ukuvuga amapantalo y'imikara , imipira y'imikara inyuma barengejeho gillets za kaki .
Ni ubwa mbere bari bagaragaye muri iyo myenda , ijya kumera nk'iy'abarinda Minisitiri w'Intebe wa Israel .
Perezida Kagame yatwaye Tshisekedi mu modoka
Tapi itukura , icyubahiro cya gisirikare n'ibindi ni bimwe bisanzwe bimenyerewe ku mukuru w'igihugu wasuye mugenzi we , icyakora si kenshi Perezida akunze kugaragara ari mu modoka kuri """" volant """" atwaye mugenzi we .
Mu ruzinduko Tshisekedi yagiriye mu Rwanda kuwa Gatanu , Perezida Kagame yamutwaye mu modoka bagenda baganira ubwo bajyaga gusura ibikorwa remezo byangijwe n'imitingito yakurikiye iruka ry'Ikirunga cya Nyiragongo ryabaye ku wa 22 Gicurasi 2021 .
Si kenshi Perezida Kagame akunze kugaragara yitwaye mu modoka cyangwa atwaye mugenzi we wamusuye , icyakora nanone si ubwa mbere .
Gusa inshuro nke byabaye hari mu Ukuboza 2016 ubwo umwami wa Maroc , Mohammed VI yasuraga u Rwanda .
Muri Gashyantare 2018 ubwo Perezida Ali Bongo wa Gabon yasuraga u Rwanda , nabwo Perezida Kagame yagaragaye amutwaye mu modoka .
Muri Werurwe 2019 , Kagame yongeye gutwara mu modoka Uhuru Kenyatta wa Kenya mu ruzinduko rw'umunsi umwe yagiriye mu Rwanda .
Muri Mata uwo mwaka , nabwo Perezida Kagame yatwaye mu modoka Umuyobozi w'Ikirenga wa Qatar , Sheikh Tamim bin Hamad Al - Thani wari wasuye u Rwanda .
Ubufatanye mu gucukura no gutunganya zahabu
Wumvise ibivugwa n'abanyapolitiki batavuga rumwe na Leta ya Congo cyangwa se abandi batifuza ko umubano w'ibihugu byombi wasagamba , watekereza ko gufatanya by'umwihariko mu bijyanye n'iby'amabuye y'agaciro ari sakirirego hagati y'u Rwanda na Congo .
Umuhanda mwiza cyangwa inzu nziza yuzuye i Kigali , uzasanga bavuga ngo ni """" amabuye ya Congo . """"
Ni ibintu u Rwanda rwakunze guhakana kenshi nyamara bidasiba kugaragara muri raporo za Loni ku mutekano wo mu Burasirazuba bwa Congo .
Icyiza ni uko Leta ya Congo nta na rimwe yo ubwayo irabishinja u Rwanda .
Kubera ayo makuru ahora mu kirere , nta wakekaga ko kuri uyu wa Gatandatu ibihugu byombi bishobora gusinya amasezerano y'ubufatanye mu kwimakaza umucyo mu bucukuzi n'ubucuruzi bwa Zahabu hagamijwe guhashya ubucuruzi bwayo bukorwa n'imitwe yitwaje intwaro ikorera muri RDC .
Ibigo bibiri , Sakima yo muri RDC na Dither SA yo mu Rwanda nibyo bizagenzura urugendo rwose kuva mu gucukura zahabu bizakorwa na Sakima kugeza mu kuyitunganya bizakorwa na Dither SA , hirindwa ko yakomeza kujya mu maboko y'imitwe yitwaje intwaro ikoresha amafaranga yavuye muri ayo mabuye y'agaciro , mu gukomeza guteza umutekano muke
.
Uku kurenga ku bivugwa no ku byakabaye bitanya ibihugu byombi ahubwo bigashyira imbere ibibihuza , ni ikimenyetso cy'uko u Rwanda na Congo ari ibihugu """" bivandimwe , """" abaturanyi bahoraho byabishaka bitabishaka .
Dr Vincent Biruta yasabye urubyiruko rwa PSD gutinyuka kwiyamamaza mu matora y'inzego z'ibanze .
Ibi Dr Vincent Biruta yabisabye kuri uyu wa Gatandatu ya 19 Kamena 2021 , mu mahugurwa y'iminsi ibiri y'urubyiruko n'abagore bo muri PSD agamije gushishikariza abagore n'urubyiruko kugira uruhare mu bikorwa bya politiki bikorerwa mu mutwe wa politiki n'ibiteza imbere Igihugu muri rusange .
Yagize ati """" Mu gihugu cyacu ubu harategurwa amatora y'inzego z'ibanze , iz'urubyiruko n'izabagore mukaba musabwa kubigiramo uruhare muharanira imigendekere myiza yayo ariko kandi munatinyuka kwiyamamaza ndetse mukanabishishikariza abandi . """"
Yavuze ko kwiyamamaza biba bivuga ko umuntu aba yiteguye gutanga umusanzu we mu miyoborere y'Igihugu kandi yiyumvamo ubushobozi n'ubushake bwo gutanga umusanzu we mu kucyubaka .
Dr Biruta yashishikarije kandi abitabiriye inama , kwirinda no kudaha umwanya abakwirakwiza ku mbuga nkoranyambaga amakuru asebya leta y'u Rwanda , apfobya Jenoside yakorewe abatutsi mu 1994 n'andi yose adafite akamaro , ko ahubwo bakwiye guharanira ibiteza imbere igihugu .
Uhagarariye PSD mu Murenge wa Bwisige mu Karere ka Gicumbi , Munyaneza Vianney yabwiye IGIHE ko aya mahugurwa yatumye yiyumvamo ubushobozi n'ubushake bwo kwiyamamaza mu nzego zifata ibyemezo .
Ati """" Mbere urubyiruko twitinyaga kuko tutari twagasobanukiwe uburenganzira bwo kuba urubyiruko twajya mu nzego bwite za Leta zifata ibyemezo ariko aya mahugurwa twahawe agiye gutuma dushishikariza bagenzi bacu batari bagatinyutse gutera iyo ntambwe ijya imbere mu kwiyamamaza muri izo nzego zifata ibyemezo . """"
Nibagwire Leonia na we uri mu bahuguwe yavuze ko bagomba kwiyamamaza kugira ngo bagire umusanzu batanga mu kubaka Igihugu .
Ati """" Kudushishikariza kwiyamamaza tujya mu myanya y'ubuyobozi ni kimwe mu bintu nk'abagore n'urubyiruko tugomba kwitabira kuko natwe tugomba gutanga umusanzu mu gihugu cyacu . """"
Yongeyeho ko mbere inshuro nyinshi bitinyaga ariko aya mahugurwa yabatinyuye ku buryo babonye ko bashobora kwiyamamaza bagatanga umusanzu wubaka igihugu muri rusange .
Aya mahugurwa yitezweho kongerera abagore n'urubyiruko ubumenyi ku buhanga bwo kwiyamamariza kujya mu myanya y'ubuyobozi bw'umutwe wa politiki n'indi myanya y'ubuyobozi ifatirwamo ibyemezo hagamijwe kugira uruhare rugaragara mu nzego zinyuranye z'ubuyobozi , Gushishikariza abayoboke ba PSD gukomeza gushimangira
ihame ry'uburinganire n'ubwuzuzanye , kwishyirahamwe hagamije kwiteza imbere , kwishakamo ibisubizo no kwigira ndetse no kuganira ku mategeko azagenga urugaga rw'urubyiruko n'urw'abagore rushamikiye kuri PSD .
U Rwanda rwamaganye ibyo kuba icyambu cy'amabuye ya magendu acukurwa muri RDC .
Raporo yakozwe kuri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo mu 2020 , igashyikirizwa Perezida w'Akanama k'Umuryango w'Abibumbye gashinzwe Umutekano , yagaragaje ko kimwe mu bibazo bituma umutekano muri icyo gihugu utaboneka , ari imitwe y'iterabwoba n'inyeshyamba zikorera mu Burasirazuba bwa Congo , kandi zose zigatungwa
n'amabuye y'agaciro zicuruza mu bihugu by'amahanga .
Bibarwa ko Uburasirazuba bwa Congo bukoreramo imitwe y'inyeshyamba irenga 130 , yose ivuga ko ifite impamvu z'intambara imbere muri Congo ndetse no mu bihugu icyenda bihana imbibi na Congo .
Iyi mitwe imaze gutuma nibura abaturage bari hagati ya miliyoni enye n'eshanu bahungira imbere muri Congo , mu gihe abandi benshi bahungiye mu bihugu by'ibituranyi , byose biturutse ku bitero bisaga 100 byagabwe n'imitwe y'iterabwoba mu mwaka ushize .
Raporo yashyikirijwe Akanama k'Umuryango w'Abibumbye gashinzwe Umutekano , igaragaza ko imyinshi muri iyo mitwe ikura amikoro mu bikorwa by'ubucukuzi bw'amabuye y'agaciro , ndetse ikavuga ko amwe muri ayo mabuye anyuzwa mu Rwanda mbere yo kujyanwa ku isoko mpuzamahanga ,
mu bihugu birimo u Bushinwa , Leta Zunze Ubumwe z'Abarabu na Hong Kong .
Abakoze raporo ahanini bashingira ku byavuzwe n'ababahaye ubuhamya badatangaza amazina , bavuga ko ngo amabuye anyuzwa mu Rwanda kuko ari byo bihendutse , akinjira anyuze mu Kiyaga cya Kivu ndetse no ku mipaka ya Rubavu na Rusizi , avuye muri Kivu ya Ruguru n'iy'Epfo .
Batanze urugero rw'abantu batatu babwiye iri tsinda ryari mu bushakashatsi ko amabuye y'agaciro yabo bayacuruza ku bacuruzi banini bari i Goma , nabo baba bazayambutsa bakayageza mu Rwanda akajyanwa mu ndege .
Iyi raporo kandi ivuga ko mu Ukuboza 2020 , sosiyete ya Avanish Sarl ikorera i Bukavu yohereje Sosiyete ya Al - Hallaq Jewellery LLC y'i Dubai ibiro 5 103 bya zahabu binyujijwe mu Rwanda , ndetse na sosiyete yitwa KMC Sarl , nayo ikorera i Bukavu , ngo ikaba yarohereje ibiro 4 795 bya zahabu kuri sosiyete ya Gold Fun Corporation Ltd y'i Hong Kong , kandi
nabyo bikanyuzwa mu Rwanda .
U Rwanda rwabihakanye rwivuye inyuma
Nyuma yo kumva ibirego ku Rwanda , iri tsinda ryagerageje kuvugana n'uruhande rwarwo kugira ngo ryumve icyo u Rwanda rubivugaho , rubitera utwatsi .
U Rwanda ni kimwe mu bihugu bike byemeye gusubiza kuri iyo raporo kuko ibindi byinshi byahisemo kwinumira burundu .
Muri iyi raporo harimo ko umwe mu bayobozi b'u Rwanda utarashatse ko amazina ye atangazwa , yagize ati """" Nta na rimwe u Rwanda rwabonye amabuye ya magendu afite aho ahuriye na Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo kuva mu Ugushyingo 2020 kugera muri Mata uyu mwaka . """"
Ubusanzwe u Rwanda rufite inzego z'umutekano ku mupaka uruhuza na Congo zishinzwe gukurikirana no kurinda ko hari amabuye yaturuka muri icyo gihugu yinjira mu Rwanda .
Mu 2020 , u Rwanda rwari rweretse iryo tsinda ry'abashakashatsi ko hari ibiro 155 bya Coltan rwafashe kuwa 23 Mutarama 2020 , biturutse muri RDC mu buryo bwa magendu .
Izi coltan zari zibitse mu Karere ka Rubavu .
Iri tsinda kandi ryaneretswe andi mabuye menshi yafatiwe hirya no hino mu gihugu kuva muri Kamena 2019 .
Yarimo ibiro 360 by'ayakekwaga ko ari beryllium , ibiro 293 bya cassiterite , ibiro 250 bya wolfram n'ibindi biro 54 bya coltan .
Ambasade y'u Rwanda mu Muryango w'Abibumbye nayo yahakanye aya makuru y'icuruzwa ry'amabuye mu buryo bwa magendu , ndetse ibwira aba bashakashakatsi ko """" RwandAir idafite ibyemezo by'uko ariyo yatwaye ayo mabuye ya magendu . """"
Si ubwa mbere u Rwanda rugaragaza ko amakuru atangwa muri bene izi raporo ku bijyanye na magendu y'amabuye y'agaciro anyuzwa mu Rwanda atari ukuri kuko n'umwaka ushize , rwashimangiye ko bitemewe n'amategeko kurunyuzamo amabuye hatabanje kwerekanwa inkomoko yayo .
U Rwanda rwemeje Antoine Anfré nka Ambasaderi w'u Bufaransa
Mu ruzinduko Perezida w'u Bufaransa , Emmanuel Macron yagiriye mu Rwanda mu kwezi gushize nibwo yagennye ugomba guhagararira igihugu cye nka Amabasaderi .
Ambasaderi Anfré umaze kwemezwa n'u Rwanda azaba afite icyicaro i Kigali .
Ni mu gihe ibikorwa bya Ambasade y'u Bufaransa mu Rwanda byayoborwaga na Chargé d'affaires witwa Jérémie Blin wasimbuye Etienne de Souza , kuva aho Michel Flesch , wasoje imirimo ye muri Nzeri 2015 nka Ambasaderi agendeye .
Anfré w'imyaka 58 asanzwe ari amenyereye dipolomasi ; yari Umugenzuzi w'Ibijyanye n'Ububanyi n'Amahanga muri Minisiteri y'Ububanyi n'Amahanga mu Bufaransa .
Izina rye rigaragara muri Raporo ivuga ku ruhare rw'u Bufaransa muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi yitiriwe Vincent Duclert .
Mu myaka ya 1990 , Anfré yari Umuyobozi w'Ishami rishinzwe Ibikorwa bya Afurika na Malgaches [ ikirwa cya Madagascar ] ryitwaga DAM rikaba ryarakoreraga i Quai d'Orsay muri Minisiteri y'Ububanyi n'Amahanga .
Muri raporo Duclert agaragazwa nk'uwari ushyigikiye ko Politiki y'u Bufaransa ku Rwanda ihinduka , umurongo wari uhabanye cyane na Politiki y'u Bufaransa ku Rwanda .
Antoine Anfré yakoze mu nzego zitandukanye mu bijyanye n'ububanyi n'amahanga kugeza ubwo mu 2014 yagizwe Ambasaderi wihariye w'u Bufaransa muri Niger kugeza muri Nyakanga 2015 ubwo yahamagazwaga n'igihugu cye .
Yahawe izindi nshingano nyuma y'aho , agirwa Ambasaderi ushinzwe Siporo muri Minisiteri y'u Bufaransa , inshingano yamazeho umwaka hagati ya 2015 na 2016 .
Hari mbere yo gusubira kuba Umugenzuzi muri Minisiteri y'Ububanyi n'Amahanga y'u Bufaransa .
Guhera mu 1962 , u Bufaransa bumaze kohereza mu Rwanda ba ambasaderi 16 , kuva kuri Jean - Marc Barbey wabimburiye abandi kugeza kuri Michel Flesh wagiye mu 2015 .
Amb Rugwabiza yagaye ibihugu bikomeje kugenda biguru ntege mu gufata abakekwaho Jenoside .
Yabitangaje kuri uyu wa Kabiri ubwo afatanyije n'Ubuyobozi bw'Urwego Mpuzamahanga Rwashyiriweho Gukora Imirimo y'Insigarira y'Inkiko Mpanabyaha ( IRMICT ) , bagezaga ku Kanama k'Umutekano ka Loni raporo y'ibikorwa ya 18 .
Rugwabiza yasabye akanama gashinzwe umutekano kugira icyo gakora ku kibazo cy'ubufatanye buke mu korohereza akazi IRMICT , ni ukuvuga kuyifasha gufata abakekwaho Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi bakidegembya hirya no hino .
Yagize ati """" Twibukiranye ko u Rwanda rwohereje impapuro zisaga igihumbi zo guta muri yombi abakekwaho Jenoside bari hirya no hino ku Isi , rusaba ko bafatwa bagacirwa imanza cyangwa bakoherezwa mu Rwanda .
Ibihugu bike nibyo byagize icyo bikorwa . """"
Kugeza ubu impapuro 1145 nizo zimaze gutangwa zisaba ko abagize uruhare muri Jenoside bihishe mu bihugu 33 bafatwa , abafashwe ni mbarwa .
Rugwabiza yashimiye ibihugu bike byagaragaje ubushake mu gufata cyangwa kuburanisha ababyihishemo bakekwaho uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Ibyo bihugu birimo u Bufaransa biturutse ku mbwirwaruhame Perezida Emmanuel Macron aherutse kuvugira i Kigali , yizeza ko u Bufaransa butzaha umwanya abakekwaho Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Yashimiye iki gihugu kandi ku bufatanbye bwagaragaje umwaka ushize mu itabwa muri yombi rya Felicien Kabuga wari umaze imyaka isaga 20 ashakishwa n'ubutabera nk'umwe mu baterankunga b'imena ba Jenoside .
Iki gihugu kandi giherutse gutangaza ko muri Gicurasi 2022 aribwo urubanza rwa Laurent Bucyibaruta wahoze ari Perefe wa Gikongoro ruzatangira .
Ni igikorwa Rugwabiza yagaragaje ko gitanga icyizere .
Yashimiye kandi Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika ku bufatanye ziherutse kugaragaza bwohereza mu Rwanda Béatrice Munyenyezi ukekwaho uruhare muri Jenoside .
Ati """" Ibi bigaragaza ko nta kabuza ubutabera bushobora gutangwa iyo hari ubushake bwa politiki n'ubufatanye mu kugeza mu butabera abakekwaho uruhare mu byaha byibasiye inyokomuntu . """"
Icyakora , Rugwabiza yagaye bimwe mu bihugu bya Afurika ari nabyo bibarizwamo umubare munini w'abakekwaho uruhare muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ariko abafatwa bakaba ari mbarwa .
Yibukije umwanzuro w'akanama k'Umuryango wa Afurika Yunze Ubumwe gashinzwe Umutekano wo ku itariki 12 Mata 2021 usaba ibihugu byose bigize uwo muryango gukora iperereza , guta muri yombi , gucira imanza cyangw akohereza abakekwaho uruhare muri Jenoside babibarizwamo .
Yavuze ko kudashyira mu bikorwa ibikubiye muri uwo mwanzuro ari amakosa .
Insiriri n'uruhumbikiro rw'ibibazo bya Uganda n'u Rwanda : Depite Mukasa Mbidde yabivuye imuzi .
Mbidde ni Umunyapolitiki wo muri Uganda uhagarariye iki gihugu mu Nteko Ishinga Amategeko y'Umuryango wa Afurika y'Iburasirazuba , EALA .
Hari umuntu ushobora kuba azi Icyongereza , yaracyize yewe yaranakiminujemo ariko ugasanga hari amagambo runaka atajya avuga n'umunsi n'umwe .
Bene uwo ashobora guhura na Mbidde agataha ubwumvane bwanze kuko akoresha amagambo akakaye , amwe asaba kuyumva usubije inyuma cyangwa inkoranyamagambo za Longman cyangwa Oxford ziri hafi aho .
Mu mwaka ushize ubwo hizihizwaga Noheli , abinyujije kuri Twitter yandikiye abamukurikira ubutumwa bugira buti """" ​Hon Fred Mbidde Musaka wishes you a splendiferous , supercalifragilisticexpialidociou​s , droll , chuppy​ and frolicsome Christmas """" .
Aya magambo yose yakoresheje nubwo adakoreshwa na benshi , ari mu y'Icyongereza cyemewe .
Wifashishije inkoranyamagambo , Supercalifragilisticexpialidocious bisobanura ikintu cyiza by'agatangaza , nubwo kurisoma byumvikana nk'ikigeragezo .
Kuri we ni nko kunywa amazi .
Ni cyo kimwe na splendiferous ugenekereje mu Kinyarwanda risobanura agahebuzo .
Mu yandi magambo adakoreshwa na benshi mu Cyongereza ariko usanga akoresha kenshi harimo nka """" poohoo """" risobanurwa kurira bimwe bita kuboroga ariko iyo umuntu afite ububabare , """" Kowtow """" rishatse kuvuga guca bugufi , cyangwa """" Jabberwocky """" akunda gukoresha risobanura ibintu bidafite ishingiro
.
Yigeze kuvuga ati """" Abantu bavuga ko nkoresha Icyongereza gikomeye ndetse bakanenga bavuga ko ntari umuntu uzi gusobanura ibintu , ariko ndashaka kubabwira ko narangije Kaminuza mu itangazamakuru muri Makerere University , kandi twari 60 gusa bigaga iryo somo . """"
Ni umunyamategeko w'umwuga , winjiye mu ruhando rwa Politiki guhera mu myaka ya 1999 ariko ntiyahirwa n'imyanya y'imbere mu gihugu kugeza ubwo mu 2011 yatsindwaga amatora y'Abadepite ariko akabona inenge mu mategeko yahaga uburenganzira ishyaka rya NRM bwo kugira umuntu urihagararira mu Nteko ya EALA .
Yuririye kuri iyo nenge , atanga ikirego anatsinda urubanza yinjira muri EALA atyo .
Muri iyi nteko yabaye muri Komisiyo zitandukanye ndetse aranaziyobora zirimo ishinzwe Itumanaho , Ubucuruzi n'Ishoramari ; ubu anayobora agashami kayo gashinzwe amategeko .
Mu kiganiro cyihariye yagiranye na IGIHE , yasesenguye byimbitse imvano y'ikibazo cy'umubano mubi umaze igihe hagati y'u Rwanda na Uganda , umuti wacyo n'igihombo bikomeje gutera .
Gufunga umupaka byari igisubizo , si ikibazo
Mbidde yasobanuye ko hari bamwe bakeka ko ikibazo cy'u Rwanda na Uganda cyatangiye mu 2019 ubwo Umupaka wa Gatuna wafungwaga , nyamara yemeza ko bifite imvano ya kure cyane .
Ati """" Gufunga umupaka , byari bigamije gukemura ikibazo .
Ntabwo byo ubwabyo ari ikibazo .
Icyo rero umuntu yakwibaza , ikibazo cyari ikihe ? """"
Uyu mugabo yavuze ko kuba abantu baravaga mu Rwanda , bakambuka umupaka bajya muri Uganda , bagahura n'ibibazo birimo gutabwa muri yombi n'inzego z'umutekano za Uganda , bakamara umwaka bari muri gereza nta muntu ubizi batotezwa , ari impamvu ikomeye yagombaga gutuma umupaka ufungwa .
Ati """" Ibyo ubwabyo byatumye biba ikintu cy'ingenzi cyane kuri Guverinoma y'u Rwanda ifunga umupaka wayo ku buryo abaturage baguma ari bazima .
Icya kabiri , Uganda yatangiye guhishira abantu bikekwa ko bashaka guhungabanya umutekano w'u Rwanda . """"
Yatanze urugero kuri Mukankusi Charlotte uri mu buyobozi bwa RNC wahawe Pasiporo na Uganda .
Uyu na bagenzi be banahuye na Perezida Museveni ndetse aza kubyiyemerera , avuga ko ngo guhura na bo """" byari impanuka . """"
Ibi bikubitana n'uko imbere muri Uganda , abantu bose baruciye bakarumira ntihagira n'umwe uhaguruka ngo asabe ko iki kibazo gikemurwa .
Mbidde yagize ati """" Ni njye muntu wa mbere wavuze mu ruhame kuri ibi bibazo muri Uganda kuko abandi bose bari barabitinye .
Kandi icyo nakubwira ni uko Guverinoma yafashe umurongo wo kuruca ikarumira . """"
Usibye Abanyarwanda bagirirwa nabi muri Uganda , Mbidde yavuze ko n'Abanya - Uganda bafite inkomoko mu Rwanda bakunze kwibasirwa , ati """" N'ubu baracyahungabanywa . """"
Yagize ati """" Nibuka umunsi umwe Abanya - Uganda 40 bafite inkomoko mu Rwanda bafatiwe mu rusengero bashinjwa kuba intasi .
Niba atari Politiki yo guhutaza Abanyarwanda , ni ukubera iki intasi 40 zahurira mu rusengero ?
Bari gushinga ishyaka se ?
Cyangwa se gutata ni umurimo ukorwa abantu bahuriye hamwe ? """"
Mbidde yavuze ko abantu bose bakekwaho kugira uruhare mu bikorwa byo guhungabanya umutekano , barimo Tribert Rujugiro bose ubushabitsi bwabo bwahawe rugari muri Uganda nta nkomyi .
Igiteye inkeke kurushaho ni uko abo mu bwoko bw'Abanyarwanda bwemewe muri Uganda bakomeje guhohoterwa .
Ati """" Mfite ikirego ndi gukurikirana cy'Abanyarwanda , Abanya - Uganda bafite inkomoko mu Rwanda no muri iki gihe bivugwa ko ibihugu byombi biri mu nzira y'amahoro , bo barirukanwe bajyanwa mu Rwanda .
Bamaze hafi umwaka baba muri hotel mu Rwanda , kuko birukanwe mu gihugu cyabo , basiga ibikorwa byabo , ni njye uri gukurikirana imitungo yabo iri muri banki . """"
Mbidde yavumbuye ikintu kidasanzwe amaze guhura na Museveni
Hari benshi bahuza ikibazo cy'uyu munsi cy'u Rwanda na Uganda n'amateka ari hagati y'ibihugu byombi ahera mu rugamba rwo kubohora Uganda cyangwa se urwo guhagarika Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi n'intambara yo muri Congo .
Mbidde yavuze ko yagize amahirwe yo guhura n'abakuru b'ibihugu byombi , aza gutahura ko bishoboka cyane ko Museveni yaba afitiye Abanyarwanda urwango rwa karande .
Ati """" Icyo natahuye ni uko bishoboka cyane ko Museveni afitiye urwango Abanyarwanda .
Urwango rukomeye , ku mpamvu ntazi ; ku buryo uba Umunyarwanda mwiza mu gihe umushyigikiye .
Ariko iyo uri umuntu wumva ko ufite uburenganzira bwo kubaho nk'ikiremwamuntu , aho uba ufitanye ibibazo na we . """"
Yavuze kuba hari abantu bafite inkomoko mu Rwanda bakoranye na Museveni ariko bahagarika iyo mikoranire , """" bakagarukira hafi y'urupfu . """"
Kuri we ngo uramutse ufashe urutonde rw'ababohoye Uganda bo muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba , mu mazina , abenshi uyu munsi wabasanga mu Rwanda .
Ati """" Aho kubashima , arabarwanya .
Ibyo bigomba kuba bifitanye isano n'amateka ku buryo bari beza mu gihe bamukoreraga ariko ubu bari kwikorera ubwabo , ni babi . """"
Urwo rwango si urwa none !
Mu 1987 ngo Museveni yasabye ko Prof Karugire Samwiri atangiza urugendo rwo kwandika Itegeko Nshinga rishya rya Uganda .
Birangiye , yazaniwe imiterere yaryo , ariko arakazwa n'ikintu kimwe gikomeye .
Ati """" Mfite amakuru yizewe ko ubwo yarizanirwaga , yarakajwe no gushyira Abanyarwanda mu bwoko bumwe bwa Uganda .
Yajugunyiye icyo gitabo uwo """" Professor , """" avuga amagambo abo bantu bananiwe kwakira .
Kuri we Abanyankole ni abantu beza kurusha Abanyarwanda .
Kuri we , ababohoye u Rwanda si abantu beza . """"
Mbidde yavuze ko igikwiriye gukorwa ari ugukomeza kubwira Museveni ko ibyo ari gukora atari byo , kandi ngo urwo rugendo rwaratangiye .
Yashingiye ku kuba igice kinini gituwemo abo mu bwoko bw'Abanyarwanda cyaranze kumutora nk'abatuye Masaka , Mityana , Luwero , Mubende n'ahandi .
Ufite agatwe gato akarinda ubuhiri
Mbidde yavuze ko Abanyapolitiki benshi bo muri Uganda bahisemo inzira yo guceceka kugira ngo babeho atari uko bayobewe ukuri .
Ati """" Navumbuye ko bahisemo ihame rimwe ry'ingenzi rivuga ngo """" ubwoba ni ubuzima . """"
Bahitamo guceceka kugira ngo babeho .
Hanyuma abandi badaceceka , bashyigikiye ibyo turi kurwanya . """"
Uyu mugabo yavuze ko nk'abaturage bari batunzwe n'ubucuruzi bwambukiranya imipaka , bazi neza ikibazo .
Yatanze urugero rw'abarenga 600 mu gihe cy'amezi ane mu 2019 banditse basaba ko iki kibazo cyakemurwa kubera igihombo .
Ati """" Abantu 600 mu mezi ane , nawe wakwibaza ayo abo bantu bahombye .
Kubera iki ?
Kuko umuntu umwe yafashe umwanzuro wo gushotora igihugu kirengana ku mpamvu yananiwe gusobanura .
Kandi turabizi , iyo Museveni afite ingingo , ntabwo ashobora kuyiceceka .
Yaracecetse kuko nta ngingo afite kuri iki kibazo . """"
Ukuri ni ko kuzakemura ikibazo
Mbidde yavuze ko bikwiye ko igihugu cye cyemera ko ari cyo """" gishotora """" u Rwanda , kandi ko ibyo bizavaho mu gihe kizaba cyemeye kuvugisha ukuri .
Uko kuri kugomba kujyana no gushyira mu bikorwa amasezerano yasinywe n'ibihugu byombi , nk'uburyo bwo gukemura ikibazo .
Ati """" Hasinywe amasezerano yo guhererekanya abanyabyaha .
Ibyo bivuze iki ?
Biravuze ngo Uganda ikwiriye guhagarika gushyigikira abarwanya u Rwanda ahubwo ikaruboherereza bakaburanishwa .
Hari uwakeka ko ibyo na byo bizakemura ikibazo , oya , ikibazo kizakemurwa n'ubushake bwo gukorera hamwe , bwo kubana neza . """"
"""" Icyo ni cyo kikibura ku ruhande rwa Uganda .
Turasenga dusaba Imana ko kuri iyi nshuro Perezida uherutse kurahira , yumva neza ko u Rwanda na Uganda biva inda imwe . """"
Kuki Museveni yishyizemo u Rwanda ?
Mbidde asobanura ko bishoboka cyane ko Museveni afitiye u Rwanda urwango rushingiye no ku byo rumaze kugeraho kurusha igihugu cye .
Ati """" Uganda imaze imyaka irenga 35 ifite amahoro , ifite ubutunzi kamere [ . . . ] yananiwe kugira ibintu byinshi igeraho . """"
Mbidde yavuze ko impamvu Museveni agikora ibyo ashaka ari uko mu nzego zitandukanye za Uganda , hari abantu bamushyigikiye , atanga urugero kuri Abel Kandiho uyobora CMI n'abandi biganjemo abinjiye mu gisirikare mu myaka ya 1990 n'abandi bari muri Guverinoma .
Ati """" Afite abantu bafite imyumvire imwe gusa si benshi .
Abenshi bigira nk'abumva ibintu kimwe na we kugira ngo bakomeze kubona umugati cyangwa se abandi bakumva ko umutekano uzava mu kwemeranya na we . """"
Politiki imeze nk'igikinisho cya muzika
Iki kiganiro na Mbidde twagikoze ku munsi Museveni yarahiraga .
Mu gusobanura niba hari icyo umuntu yakwitega muri iyi myaka igiye kuza , yagarutse ku nkuru z'ibicurangisho bya muzika .
Yifashishije urugero rw'igikinisho cyashyirwagamo igiceri , hanyuma kigacuranga indirimbo yabaga yarashyizwemo mbere n'uwagikoze .
Ati """" Umbajije niba hari amakuru mashya tuzabona muri iyi manda nshya atangiye , azakora nk'iyo mashini .
Azakora ibyo asanzwe akora kuko ni byo azi gukora .
Ntiwitege ikintu gitandukanye . """"
Mbidde yakomeje avuga ko uko iminsi ishira , ibimenyetso byerekana ko nta bushake Museveni afite mu gukemura ikibazo cy'u Rwanda na Uganda .
Yatanze urugero ku buryo Museveni yohereje Dr Adonia Ayebare nk'intumwa ye kugira ngo aganire na Perezida Kagame ku kibazo kimaze igihe hagati y'ibihugu byombi , ariko murumuna we akaba ari we ushyirwa mu majwi mu gukorera iyicarubozo Abanyarwanda .
Ati """" Niba Museveni yohereje Dr Ayebare ngo ahure na Perezida Kagame nk'umuhuza mu gihe azi neza ko umuvandimwe we , Abel Kandiho , ari umuyobozi wa CMI iri kwica Abanyarwanda , kuri njye ibyo bisa nk'umukino na none . """"
Mbidde yavuze ko nk'umunyapolitiki utavuga rumwe na Leta , ari gukora ibishoboka kugira ngo ikibazo gikemuke ariko byose abikora ashingiye ku kuvuga ukuri .
Ati """" Ukuri kutavuzwe , iki kibazo ntikizigera gikemuka .
Ikindi , njye nafunguye amarembo , igihe cyose Perezida wa Uganda yashaka kumenya ukuri , nabwiye abaturage ukuri kandi na we sinagira impungenge zo kumubwira ukuri . """"
Yakomeje avuga ko nk'umunyapolitiki , undi mwanzuro ari uko Museveni yava ku butegetsi nubwo """" bitoroshye """" ariko icyo we na bagenzi be bari gukora ari """" ugukora cyane . """"
Mbidde yavuze ko nk'abadepite ba EALA ntacyo bakora mu gukemura iki kibazo kuko na bo ubwabo bafite byinshi bitaboroheye birimo kuba batabona umushahara wabo uko bikwiriye n'ibindi .
U Rwanda na Uganda hashize hafi imyaka ibiri bisinye amasezerano yo gukemura ibibazo biri hagati y'ibihugu byombi , icyakora umusaruro wayo ugerwa ku mashyi kuko Abanyarwanda bacyumvikana batawe muri yombi mu buryo budakurikije amategeko .
Ikindi imitwe igamije guhungabanya umutekano w'u Rwanda iracyafite ibirindiro muri Uganda .
U Rwanda rwamaganye ibyo kwicisha inzara Rusesabagina byakwirakwijwe na The New York Times
Ni amakuru yatangajwe n'Ikinyamakuru The New York Times kimaze igihe gisohora inkuru zisa n'izigamije guharabika isura y'u Rwanda , by'umwihariko ku kibazo cya Paul Rusesabagina ukurikiranyweho ibyaha by'iterabwoba .
Inkuru y'icyo kinyamakuru yasohotse kuri uyu wa Gatandatu yavugaga ko umuryango wa Rusesabagina ngo yawumenyesheje ko agiye guhagarikirwa ibiribwa , amazi n'imiti yahabwaga .
Mu nkuru ntabwo hagaragazwa ikigomba gushingirwaho Rusesabagina yimwa amafunguro n'imiti .
Umunyamakuru Abdi Latif Dahir nta nubwo yigeze atera intambwe ngo abaze inzego bireba mu Rwanda ngo zibitangeho ibisobanuro cyangwa zibyange mbere yo gusohora inkuru .
RCS ibinyujije kuri Twitter , yamaganye ayo makuru y'ibihuha kuri Rusesabagina , ivuga ko atigeze yimwa ibiribwa cyangwa imiti .
Iti """" Urwego rushinzwe amagereza mu Rwanda rufata imfungwa n'abagororwa bose kimwe kandi rwita ku bakenewe kwitabwaho byihariye .
Ku kibazo cya Rusesabagina Paul , ubwo yoherezwaga muri Gereza ya Nyarugenge yahawe icyumba cyihariye n'amafunguro yihariye . """"
"""" Mu minsi ishize yashyizwe mu cyumba rusange kirimo n'izindi mfungwa nyuma yo kwinubira icyo yise """" gufungirwa mu kato , """" ibintu bitaba mu magereza yo mu Rwanda .
Kuri ubu ahabwa ifunguro rimwe nk'iry'izindi mfungwa kandi abonana na muganga igihe cyose abikeneye nkuko byari bimeze na mbere . """"
Rusesabagina uri imbere y'ubutabera bw'u Rwanda aregwa ibyaha icyenda birimo kurema umutwe w'ingabo utemewe , Kuba mu mutwe w'iterabwoba , gutera inkunga iterabwoba , ubwicanyi nk'igikorwa cy'iterabwoba , itwarwa ry'umuntu ritemewe n'amategeko nk'igikorwa cy'iterabwoba no kwiba hakoreshejwe
intwaro nk'igikorwa cy'iterabwoba .
New York Times , umusangirangendo w'umuryango wa Rusesabagina ?
Mu mboni z'ibinyamakuru byinshi byo mu Burengerazuba , usanga u Rwanda rugaragazwa nk'igihugu kitagira akeza kakirangwamo .
N'ibyiza u Rwanda rwagezeho , abanyamakuru bo mu Burengerazuba usanga babyihunza , banabitangazaho inkuru runaka ugasanga bisa na ba bandi bataha ubukwe baje gutara imishono .
The New York Times ni kimwe muri byo .
Hashize igihe isohora inkuru ziteye kwibaza ku Rwanda ndetse rimwe na rimwe zakwitwa nk'ubushotoranyi .
Byageze ku kibazo cya Rusesabagina ho isya itanzitse .
Iki kinyamakuru kiri mu bya mbere bike ku Isi byabashije kuvugana na Rusesabagina akigezwa mu Rwanda muri Nzeri 2020 .
Mu byo bavuganye icyo gihe , we ubwe yivugiye neza ko afashwe neza .
Inkuru ya New York Times yasohotse tariki 18 Nzeri 2020 , Rusesabagina wari ukiri mu maboko y'Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Ubugenzacyaha ( RIB ) yagize ati """" yego nyuma y'iyo minsi itatu , nafashwe neza cyane , nta kintu na kimwe nanenga kugeza ubu .
Ndya ibyo buri munyarwanda wese arya , mpabwa buri kimwe cyose nshatse .
Ubwo rero mfashwe kimwe nk'undi munyarwanda wese . """"
Umuntu yakwibaza uburyo Rusesabagina yaba yarafashwe neza ari muri kasho , yagera muri gereza akaba ariho afatwa nabi kurushaho .
Ikindi kigaragaza ko inkuru ya New York Times igamije guteza byacitse , ni uburyo ishimangira ko agiye guhagarikirwa amafunguro , amazi n'imiti !
Ni mu gihe bizwi neza ko umuntu abeshwaho n'ibiryo , u Rwanda rwaba rufite nyungu ki mu kwima umuntu ibiryo cyangwa imiti , kandi ari kimwe mu mahame y'uburenganzira bwa muntu ? .
Mu mahame agenga umwuga w'itangazamakuru ubusanzwe inkuru ivuzwe ku mpande ebyiri zitumva ibintu kimwe , buri ruhande ruhabwa umwanya rukagira icyo ruyivugaho .
Mu nkuru ya The New York Times nta na hamwe bigeze bavugisha Guverinoma y'u Rwanda kuri ibyo birego by'umuryango wa Rusesabagina , ngo wenda yange kugira icyo ibitangazaho ariko yabimenye !
Ni imikorere y'abanyamakuru bo mu biro ( armchair journalists ) , bicara bakandika amabwire gusa nta kugenzura ukuri na guke mu byo babwiwe cyangwa se ngo biyererutse bavangemo ukuri guke , babaze impande bireba .
Mu nkuru , hagaragazwa ko umunyamategeko wa Rusesabagina n'umuryango we bagerageje kujya kumusura mu mpera z'iki cyumweru ntibabashe kumugeraho .
Umuntu aha yakwibaza uburyo nyiri ugufungwa yabamenyesheje ko agiye guhagarikirwa imiti , amazi n'ibiribwa kandi bataramugezeho .
Icyakora ku bamaze iminsi bakurikiranira hafi ibya New York Times ku Rwanda nta gitangaza kirimo .
Iki gitangazamakuru kuva Rusesabagina yafatwa , cyakomeje kumubogamiraho bidasanzwe , kimwerekana nk'intwari ngo """" yarokoye """" amagana muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , inkuru itavugwaho rumwe n'abitirirwa ko barokowe kuko bemeza ko babanzaga kwishyura kugira ngo bahabwe ubuhungiro muri Hotel des Mille Collines Rusesabagina
yacungaga .
Ntacyo icyo kinyamakuru kivuga ku baturage ba Nyabimata n'ahandi ibitero by'umutwe w'iterabwoba wa FLN byagabwe , bigahitana inzirakarengane z'abaturage cyangwa se ibindi byaha ushinjwa aregwa .
Ikindi kigaragara , New York Times iri mu murongo uhishe wo gufasha umuryango wa Rusesabagina gukomeza guharabika u Rwanda , no kwereka amahanga ko adafashwe neza .
Umuntu yavuga ko ibya New York Times n'Umuryango wa Rusesabagina ari bimwe by'ushaka kukurya atabura imboga agukoza .
Kuva Rusesabagina yatabwa muri yombi muri Kanama 2020 , abo mu muryango we bagerageje kweza no gusibanganya ibyaha akurikiranyweho .
Mu kubigeraho , bagiye bakoresha uburyo bwose bafitiye ubushobozi burimo no gukorana n'ibinyamakuru bikomeye bisanganywe umurongo wo kugaragaza nabi isura y'u Rwanda .
Uwo muryango wabanje kuvuga ko Rusesabagina yakorewe iyicarubozo , New York Times iri mu bamugezeho bwa mbere akigera mu Rwanda kandi ibyo by'iyicarubozo ntabyo yababwiye , nta n'aho mu nkuru yabo bagaragaje ko wenda bamusanganye ibikomere cyangwa ihungabana , nyamara inkuru bakomeje kugenda bwamwandikaho zimugaragaza nk'inzirakarengane .
Umuryango wa Rusesabagina ahanini bigizwemo uruhare n'umukobwa we , Carine Kanimba wakomeje kwiruka mu bihugu by'u Burayi na Amerika ushaka uburyo ifungwa ndetse no kugezwa imbere y'ubutabera kwa Rusesabagina byaburizwamo ndetse ngo byaba ngombwa na Leta y'u Rwanda ikaba yashyirwaho igitutu .
Carine Kanimba , yageze n'aho anenga imyitwarire y'u Bubiligi nk'igihugu cya kabiri cya se , aho yibazaga icyo kuba se afite ubwenegihugu bw'iki gihugu bimumariye mu gihe kidashobora kumukurikirana ngo arekurwe .
Ibi byose byakorwaga n'umuryango wa Rusesabagina ushaka ko Leta y'u Rwanda ishyirwaho igitutu n'amahanga ikamurekura , gusa ntibyabahiriye kuko u Rwanda rutasibye kugaragaza ko ikibazo cye kiri mu rukiko , hakwiye gutegerezwa umwanzuro ruzagifataho .
Uwanditse iyi nkuru ihimba imibereho itariyo ya Rusesabagina ni Umunya - Kenya ufite inkomoko muri Somalia , Abdi Latif Dahir , Ushinzwe Akarere ka Afurika y'Iburasirazuba muri The New York Times kuva mu 2019 .
Numvise nduhutse , nkeye ku mutima - Rtd Lt Col Guillaume Ancel avuga ku rugendo rwa Macron i Kigali .
Guillaume Ancel wahoze ari Umusirikare Mukuru w'u Bufaransa wari mu Rwanda mu gihe cya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi muri Mata 1994 , yatangaje ko yashimishijwe n'imbwirwaruhame Perezida Emmnuel Macron yavugiye mu Rwanda kuko irimo ukuri ku ruhare rw'iki gihugu muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi .
Perezida w'u Bufaransa , Emmanuel Macron yasuye u Rwanda ku wa 27 Gicurasi mu ruzinduko rw'iminsi ibiri , rwarangiye ibihugu byombi biteye intambwe mu kuzahura umubano wari umaze imyaka 27 ucumbagira .
U Rwanda rwashinjaga u Bufaransa kugira uruhare mu gutera inkunga umugambi wa Jenoside n'ishyirwa mu bikorwa ryawo ariko u Bufaransa ntibwari bwarigeze bushaka kugaragaza uruhande buhereyemo .
Perezida Macron ubwo yasuraga Urwibutso rwa Jenoside rwa Kigali yemeye uruhare iki gihugu cyagize muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi mu 1994 .
Mu Kiganiro IGIHE yagiranye na Rtd Lieutenant Colonel Guillaume Ancel wari mu Rwanda mu gihe cya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , yavuze ko kuba Perezida Macron yaraje i Kigali akajya ku Rwibutso agasaba abarokotse Jenoside impano y'imbabazi yicishije bugufi ari ikintu cyamukoze ku mutima .
Ancel yari amaze igihe agaragaza uruhare rw'iguhugu cye muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi ndetse yabyanditseho ibitabo bitandukanye .
Yagize ati """" Numvise nduhutse , nkeye .
Numvise nduhutse kuko imyaka 27 yo guhakana uruhande rw'u Bufaransa yari ishize .
Twari tumaze imyaka myinshi twibeshya , twibeshye mu gihe cya Jenoside , twibeshya na nyuma ya Jenoside . """"
Ancel ashima intambwe Macron yateye akemera uruhare u Bufaransa bwagize muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi
Guillaume yakomeje avuga ko igihe cyari kigeze ngo u Bufaransa bubare inkuru itandukanye nyuma y'igihe kinini bwifatanyije n'abo yise """" Aba - Nazi bo mu Rwanda , """" ikuraho ihakana kandi ihoza abarokotse Jenoside .
Ati """" Ibyo ni byo Macron yazirikanye muri iyo mbwirwaruhame , ntekereza ko ari iy'amateka ikwiye .
Numvise nkeye kuko hari hashize igihe duharanira ko ukuri kuri iyi ngingo kujya ahabona . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Ibyo ntacyo bivuze ugereranyije n'akababaro k'abarokotse Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi no ku Banyarwanda ariko nari mfite ipfunwe kubera igihugu cyanjye .
Nari mfite ipfunwe ku bwanjye nk'umuntu wahoze ari umusirikare mukuru kuba narabaye mu mwanya nafatanyijemo n'abicanyi bo mu Rwanda ( yagereranyije n'aba - Nazi ) nari mfite ipfunwe ku bw'abarokotse tutahaga icyubahiro tubagomba mu gihe bibuka ababo barenga miliyoni twashoboraga kuba twaratabaye . """"
Guillaume ashima intambwe ya Macron utariyibagijeumwanya arimo mu Bufaransa , akagira imbaraga zo guhagarara imbere ya Perezida Kagame yemera ko """" bibeshye """" kandi basaba abarokotse jenoside impano y'imbabazi .
Ati """" Ni ibintu bindema umutima mu buryo budasanzwe . """"
Intambwe ya Kagame ni ikimenyetso cy'ubwiyunge
Perezida Paul Kagame uherutse mu ruzinduko mu Bufaransa , yagiranye ibiganiro n'abahoze ari abasirikare bakuru b'iki gihugu bari mu Rwanda kuva mu 1990 kugeza mu 1994 .
Guillaume Ancel abajijwe uko yakiriye uyu mubonano aho Kagame yicaranye n'abantu bari bahanganye mu gihe cya Operation Turquoise , yavuze ko ari ikimenyetso cy'amahoro n'ubwiyunge .
Ati """" Ntacyo mpisha , nashimye uyu mubonano .
Ni ikimenyetso cy'amahoro yagaragaje .
Ntiyigeze ashaka kurwana n'u Bufaransa kandi twagombye kuba twaramwumvise mu gihe cya Operation Turquoise .
Inshuro nyinshi abasirikare [ Inkotanyi ] babaga bafite uburyo bwo kwica cyangwa gukomeretsa Abafaransa ariko Kagame yarababujije .
Ntekereza ko Abafaransa batari bazi ko Kagame atigeze ashaka kurwana n'u Bufaransa . """"
Uyu mubonamo ngo ni inzira yo kugarura amahoro no kubaka ahazaza mu mubano w'u Bufaransa n'u Rwanda .
"""" Byaranshimishje cyane , ndashimira Kagame ku bw'iki kimenyetso yakoze .
Ni ikimenyetso cy'ubwiyunge , ni ikimenyetso cy'ahazaza . """"
Umunyamakuru yabajije Ancel uko yakiriye guhura kw'abahoze ari abasirikare b'u Bufaransa na Perezida Kagame , asubiza agira ati """" Ntakubeshye nanjye nifuzaga kuba naba ndi muri bariya basirikare bakuru bakiriye Perezida Kagame , ariko bahisemo abagize uruhare mu kuyobora ibyo Ingabo z'ubufaransa zakoze mu Rwanda hagati ya 1990 na 1994 .
""""
Yavuze ko iyo aza kugira amahirwe yo guhura na Perezida Kagame yari kumushimira , akamubwira ko ari """" umuyobozi w'intangarugero n'umugabo udasanzwe wanditse amateka akomeye . """"
Ancel nubwo yanditse ibitabo bitandukanye ku ruhare rw'u Bufaransa muri Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi , ntabwo yaherukaga mu Rwanda .
Yagiye ahabwa kenshi ubutumire ariko akanga kuza .
Kuri ubu Ancel yavuze ko icyamubuzaga kuza Perezida Macron yagikuyeho .
Ati """" Ubu uyu munsi niteguye kuza mu Rwanda nkeye igihe cyose natumirwa kuko inzitizi Perezida Macron yazikuyeho . """"
Guillaume Ancel yavuze ko uruzinduko rwa Macron mu Rwanda n'imbabazi yahasabiye byamuruhuye umutima
Guillaume Ancel yavuze ko kuba Kagame yaricaranye n'abantu bari bahanganye mu gihe cya Operation Turquoise ari ikimenyetso cy'amahoro n'ubwiyunge
U Rwanda na Afurika y'Epfo byashashe inzobe , byiyemeza kuzahura umubano umaze igihe mu rwijiji .
Byatangajwe kuri uyu wa Gatanu , tariki ya 4 Kamena 2021 , nyuma y'ibiganiro byahuje Minisitiri w'Ububanyi n'Amahanga w'u Rwanda , Dr Vincent Biruta na mugenzi we wa Afurika y'Epfo , Dr Naledi Pandor .
Muri ibyo biganiro byabaye mu ruzinduko Dr Biruta yagiriye muri Afurika y'Epfo , aba bombi bemeranyije ko bagiye gusubiza mu buryo umubano w'ibihugu byombi nyuma y'ibiganiro Perezida Paul Kagame na Cyril Ramaphosa bagiye bagirana mu bihe bitandukanye .
Itangazo ryasohowe n'Ibiro bya Minisiteri y'Ububanyi n'Amahanga n'Ubutwererane ya Afurika y'Epfo , ryavuze ko abo bayobozi bahuye hagamijwe gusesengura uko umubano w'ibihugu byombi wifashe n'imbogamizi zikiwuzitira kugira ngo zikurweho .
Bemeranyije kugarura umubano wari uhari mbere y'uko ibintu bitangira kudogera mu 2013 .
Ryakomeje riti """" Mu biganiro birambuye kandi birimo ukuri , ba minisitiri bombi biyemeje gusubiza umubano mu buryo nk'uko Perezida Kagame na Cyril Ramaphosa babyemeranyije nyuma y'ibiganiro bagiranye . """"
Ibihugu byombi kandi byashyizeho ibikorwa n'ingamba bihuriweho biganisha ku nzira yazana inyungu ku baturage b'ibihugu byombi .
Hanemejwe ko hagomba gushyirwaho uburyo bwo gufasha inzira yo gusubiza uwo mubano mu buryo , hubahirizwa amategeko mpuzamahanga .
Hashyizweho itsinda rihuriweho riyobowe na Minisitiri Biruta ndetse na Pandor rigamije kuyobora urugendo rwo kuzahura umubano w'ibihugu byombi .
Iryo tsinda rizasesengura ibibazo byose bibangamiye umubano w'ibihugu byombi , raporo ishyikirizwe abaminisitiri bombi .
Ibi biganiro bije bikurikira ibyahuje abakuru b'ibihugu byombi tariki 18 Gicurasi 2021 i Paris aho bari bitabiriye Ihuriro ryiga ku Iterambere ry'Ubukungu bwa Afurika .
Umuhanzi Julio Kamungu yasubukuye umuziki nyuma y'imyaka icyenda .
Uyu mugabo yakoze umuziki mu 2003 aririmba muri za korali kugeza mu 2009 ubwo yafataga umwanzuro wo gukora umuziki ku giti cye ariko mu 2012 aza kuba awuretse akajya aririmba mu nsengero gusa .
Mu kiganiro yagiranye na IGIHE yavuze ko mu 2012 yahisemo kuba asubitse umuziki akajya mu bindi .
Yakomeje ati """" Kuva icyo gihe nakoze indirimbo zigeze kuri esheshatu ariko guhera mu 2012 naje guhagarika nsigara ndirimba mu rusengero gusa . """"
Avuga ko afite intego yo kubwira abantu ubwami bw'Imana , akabereka ko bakwiriye kuva mu mwijima .
Ati """" Intego mfite ikubiye mu ijambo riri muri Habakuki 2 : 14 ; rigira riti """" Kuko Isi izakwirwa no kumenya ubwiza bw'Uwiteka , nk'uko inyanja y'amazi isendera . """" """"
Ubutumwa nibandaho ni ubw'Ubwami , kubwira abantu ko ubwami bw'Imana bwaje ko umwanzi nta mwanya agifite mu bana b'Imana , ukubimenya bikaba aribwo buzima kandi ko hamwe na Kirisitu dukwiye kuba mu buzima buzira umwijima . """"
Ubu Julio Kamungu yamaze gushyira hanze indirimbo nshya yise """" """" Ni wowe """" """" avuga ko ikubiyemo iby'Ubwami bw'Imana .
Yakomeje agira ati """" Nayihawe nk'ihishurirwa nagize ku by'Ubwami bw'Imana aho Yesu yabwiye abamwitaga ngo ni umukuru w'abadayimoni bavuga ko ariyo mpamvu abasha kwirukana abadayimoni , we akababwira ko nta bwami bwirwanya ahubwo ko iyo bwirwanyije buba busenyuka . """"
Amajwi y'iyi ndirimbo """" Ni wowe """" yakozwe na Bruce & Boris , amashusho yayo afatwa ndetse atunganywa na Fleury Legend .
Uyu muhanzi avuga ko agiye gufatiraho agakora ibindi bihangano kandi yizera ko bizafasha benshi .
Julio Kamungu ni umugabo w'umugore umwe bafitanye abana babiri b'abahungu .
Batuye i Gikondo mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
"""" Africa Haguruka """" igiye kongera kuba hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga .
Iki gikorwa ubusanzwe gitegurwa n'Umuryango Authentic Word Ministries n'amatorero ya Zion Temple Celebration Center giteganijwe kuva ku cyumweru tariki 11 kugera ku wa 18 Nyakanga 2021 .
"""" Africa Haguruka """" uyu mwaka izibanda ku ijambo riboneka muri Bibiliya , mu Gitabo cya Ezekiyeli 37 : 1 - 10 .
Insanganyamatsiko yacyo igira iti """" Afurika akira umuyaga w'impinduka nziza . """"
Mu iki gikorwa haba ibiterane , gutanga inyigisho , ibiganiro cyangwa guhuza abantu baturutse mu bihugu bitandukanye , byose bigamije kuzamura iterambere rya Afurika no guhembura abawutuye binyuze mu gusobanukirwa umugambi Imana ifitiye uyu mugabane no kuwugenderamo .
Apôtre Dr Paul Gitwaza watangije iki gikorwa yemera ko Imana ifitiye Afurika n'abaturage bayo basaga miliyali 1 na miliyoni 200 umugambi mwiza n'amasezerano akomeye bakwiriye gusingira .
Ati """" Africa Haguruka rero ni urubuga aho Abanyafurika n'inshuti zabo bahura ngo baganire , basengane kandi bige icyo Imana ivuga ku Mugabane wa Afurika maze babashe kuzana impinduka nziza mu mibereho y'abatuye uyu mugabane , banamamaza ubutumwa bwiza bwa Kirisitu . """"
Africa Haguruka ya 2021 izaba mu buryo bw'iyakure kubera icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , izatangirwamo inyigisho ku miryango , uburezi n'ubuyobozi .
Mu minsi umunani y'igiterane kandi hazigwa n'uburyo Afurika ikeneye ubucuruzi buzana iterambere kandi bwubahisha Imana .
Inzobere n'abakozi b'Imana bazajya batanga ibiganiro bizajya bisozwa n'ibihe byo guhimbaza no kuramya Imana ndetse hatangwe n'ijambo ry'ububyutse .
Hazabamo na Gahunda y'urubyiruko izwi nka Youth Arise , aho abasore n'inkumi bazaganira uko bahaguruka mu nzego z'iterambere no mu kubaha Imana .
Iki giterane kizaca kuri YouTube na Facebook kikananyuzwa kuri Authentic TV , igaragara kuri shene ya 111 kuri StarTimes ndetse no kuri Canal + kuri shene ya 384 .
Kizananyuzwa kuri Radio Authentic n'amaradiyo y'abaturage yigenga .
Africa Haguruka yashibutse mu iyerekwa Dr Paul Gitwaza uyobora Itorero Zion Temple Celebration Center yagize mu 2000 , rigamije kuzamura iterambere ry'Umugabane wa Afurika no guhembura abawutuye binyuze mu ijambo ry'Imana .
Dr Paul Gitwaza watangije iki gikorwa cya Africa Haguruka Urabagirane yavuze ko muri iki gihe igikwiye guhabwa agaciro ari ubuzima n'umutekano by'abantu .
Light Of Christ yakoranye indirimbo na Kadogo wo muri Healing Worship Team ( Video ) .
Indirimbo """" Ndi Uwo Ndiwe """" yubakiye ku butumwa buhumuriza abantu , ibibutsa ko Imana ari umwungeri utazimiza intama ze .
Umuyobozi wungirije wa Light Of Christ Group , Tuyizere Emmanuel """" Smith , """" yavuze ko icyatumye bakora iyo ndirimbo , bashaka kubwira abantu ko Imana itajya itererana abayo .
Yagize ati """" Muri ibi bihe bikomeye natwe uyu ni umusanzu wacu w'isanamitima , duhumuriza abantu ko Imana itabataye .
Mu gice cya nyuma turaririmba ngo """" Uhumure , ukomere ndagukingiye , uhishanwe na Kirisitu muri njye . """"
Yasobanuye ko """" Kwibutsa abantu ko duhishanwe na Kirisitu mu Mana ni yo ntego , ko ikizakugeraho cyose kizaba cyabanje guca ku Mana . """"
Tuyizere yavuze ko impamvu bahisemo gukorana na Kadogo ari uko ari umuririmbyi w'umuhanga ndetse wicisha bugufi .
Yagize ati """" Kadogo ni umuhanga akaba imfura cyane , aca bugufi , akunda Imana .
Ni byinshi byatumye aba ari we duhitamo , gusa byavuye no mu kuba ari inshuti na bamwe muri twe bihita byoroha gukorana na we , Imana imuhe umugisha ko twavuze rimwe we akabyumva kabiri . """"
Light Of Christ ni itsinda rikorera umurimo muri EPR - Kamuhoza rikaba rihuje abaririmbyi bava mu matorero ya gikirisitu atandukanye harimo ADEPR , Evangelical Restoration Church , EAR n'andi atandukanye .
"""" Ndi Uwo Ndiwe """" ni indirimbo ya gatatu iri tsinda ryakoze muri gahunda ryihaye ryo gusohora iz'amajwi ziherekejwe n'amashusho .
Iyi ndirimbo yatunganyijwe na Bob Pro naho amashusho yayo akorwa na Smith uri no mu bagize Light Of Christ .
Umuhanzi Christian Irimbere yambitse impeta umukunzi we bitegura kurushinga .
Nk'uko abemera Bibiliya babisoma mu gitabo cy'Itangiriro 2 : 24 hagira hati """" Ni cyo gituma umuntu azasiga se na nyina , akabana n'umugore we akaramata , bombi bakaba umubiri umwe , """" Irimbere Jean Christian na we yatangiye urugendo ruganisha ku gutera umugongo ubugaragu asaba Semutakirwa Cheline kumubera umufasha .
Irimbere yateye ivi hasi , asaba umukunzi we kumubera umugore w'inzozi ze , undi na we ntiyazuyaza ahita avuga """" Yego . """"
Iki gikorwa cyabaye ku wa Mbere w'iki cyumweru muri imwe muri hoteli zikomeye zo mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Irimbere yavuze ko yakundiye umukunzi we kuba ari umukobwa w'umutima mwiza kandi wubaha Imana .
Yagize ati """" Iyo ukunze umuntu akenshi ureba ubwiza bw'inyuma bugaragarira buri wese ariko igituma umutindaho ni umuntu w'imbere .
Njyewe nakunze Imana iri muri we . """"
IGIHE yamenye ko Irimbere Jean Christian na Semutakirwa Cheline bazarushinga bitarenze uyu mwaka wa 2021 .
Irimbere Jean Christian umenyerewe mu ndirimbo zo kuramya no guhimbaza Imana aherutse gusohora indirimbo nshya yise """" Aho ugeze """" irimo ubutumwa bwo guhimbaza Imana mu bushobozi bwayo no gukomeza abafite imitima yihebye ko hari Umwami ushobora byose .
Uyu musore usengera muri Evangelical Restoration Church , itorero riyobowe na Apôtre Ndagijimana Joshua Masasu .
Yatangiye kwiyumvamo indirimbo yo kuririmba akiri muto .
Mu 2016 ni bwo yatangiye gukora umuziki nk'umuhanzi wigenga mu buryo bw'umwuga ; kuri ubu afite indirimbo esheshatu zirimo izamuzamuriye igikundiro nka """" Ni umugabo , """" """" Obrigado """" na """" Ndi hano . """"
Reba indirimbo ya Irimbere Jean Christian yise """" Aho ugeze """"
Korali Ukuboko kw'Iburyo yasohoye """" Si ku Kidendezi gusa """" , """" ivuga ko imirimo y'Imana itagira imipaka
Iyi ndirimbo y'iminota itandatu n'amasegonda 39 , yubakiye ku butumwa bushimangira ko imirimo ya Yesu Kirisitu itarangiriye ku kidendezi ubwo yakizaga umurwayi kuko kugeza n'uyu munsi agikora ibitangaza .
"""" """" Si Kukidendezi gusa """" """" ikubiyemo ubutumwa buhumuriza abantu ko mu makuba n'ibibazo bahura nabyo , Imana itabibagiwe kuko isaha yayo iyo igeze iratabara .
Umuyobozi wa Korali Ukuboko kw'Iburyo , Kwizera Seth , yatangaje ko icyatumye bakora iyi ndirimbo bashakaga kubwira abantu ko Yesu agikora imirimo ikomeye .
Yagize ati """" """" Kugera n'uyu munsi Yesu Kirisitu aracyakora ibitangaza .
Mu bihe nk'ibi Isi yose yugarijwe n'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , abantu ntibakwiye gukuka umutima ahubwo bizere Umwami Yesu kuko uko yari ari kera n'ubu niko akiri kandi niko azahora iteka ryose ( Abaheburayo 13 : 8 ) . """" """"
"""" """" Ikidendezi """" """" ni indirimbo yigaruriye imitima ya benshi mu Rwanda , yanarenze imipaka ikundwa n'abatumva Ikinyarwanda cyane cyane muri Afurika y'Uburasirazuba .
Nyuma yo gukundwa bihebuje , Korali Ukuboko kw'Iburyo yahisemo no kuyishyira mu Giswahili iyita """" Kisima """" kugira ngo n'abanyamahanga bumve ubutumwa buyirimo .
Iyi ndirimbo irimo ubutumwa buboneka muri Yohana 5 : 1 - 9 ahari inkuru y'umurwayi wari umaze imyaka 38 ku Kidendezi cya Betesayida , cyihindurizaga maze utanzemo abandi barwayi agakira , we kuko atagiraga umuterera mu Kidendezi yamaze imyaka myinshi ategereje gukira .
Igihe cyarageze Yesu rimwe ahanyuze amenya ko arwaye igihe kirekire amukiza atagombye kwiterera mu kidendezi .
Korali Ukuboko kw'Iburyo ni imwe mu nkuru mu Itorero ADEPR mu Rwanda kuko yashinzwe ahagana mu 1989 .
Igizwe n'abaririmbyi barenga 150 .
Kuva yashingwa yakoze ibikorwa binyuranye , itegura kandi yitabira ibitaramo bitandukanye mu Rwanda no muri Uganda .

Patient Bizimana ​yerekanywe mu rusengero n'umukunzi we bitegura kurushinga .
Kuri uyu munsi ni bwo aba bombi berekanwe bwa mbere mu rusengero rwa Evangelical Restoration Church ( ERC ) Masoro , Patient asanzwe ateraniramo .
Intambwe yo kwerekanwa kw'abasore n'inkumi bitegura kurushinga iri mu z'ibanze zibanziriza umuhango wo gusezeranira imbere y'itorero .
Kiba kigamije no gushimangira ko abagiye kurushinga ari indakemwa mu mico n'imyifatire kandi abanyetorero babitangamo ubuhamya .
Mu materaniro yo ku Cyumweru ni bwo Patient Bizimana na Uwera Gentille bamaze igihe bari mu rukundo berekanwe imbere y'abakirisitu ba ERC Masoro .
Ni igikorwa cyabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga mu kwirinda ikwirakwira rya Coronavirus .
Hahamagarwaga couple imwe ku yindi hanyuma hakerekanwa ifoto yabo .

Patient Bizimana yamaze kuba umugabo byemewe n'amategeko kuko yasezeranye na Uwera muri Kamena 2019 mu Karere ka Rubavu .
