Gakunzi Willy yasohoye indirimbo """" Amaraso """" """" ikomoza ku gaciro k'urupfu rwa Yesu .
Iyi ndirimbo mu buryo bw'amajwi yakozwe na Producer Nicolas , umuziki watunganyijwe [ music director ] na Rwisimbura Yves mu gihe amashusho yayo yayobowe na Doux afatanyije n'abarimo Musinga Patrick .
"""" Amaraso """" """" yakozwe mu buryo bumaze kumenyerwa buzwi nka """" Live recording """" aho umuhanzi afata amashusho n'amajwi byayo mu buryo bw'ako kanya nk'uri mu gitaramo .
Mu kiganiro cyihariye na IGIHE , Willy Gakunzi , yavuze ko indirimbo yayanditse nyuma yo gusoma amagambo ari mu Ibyahishuwe yerekana umunsi Isi yabuze umucunguzi ariko Yesu akitangira Isi .
Yagize ati """" Ubutumwa buri muri iyi ndirimbo ni uko mu maraso ya Yesu , mu kuza mu Isi kuducungura twabonye indangamuntu yacu .
Ni uko turi abaragwa baraganwa na Yesu .
Icya kabiri twabaye abana b'Imana kuko mbere twari twaratandukanyijwe nayo kubera ibyaha byacu ariko Yesu araza aratugura .
Isomo rya gatatu ni uko twaguzwe amaraso y'igiciro kuko Imana yashimishijwe no kohereza umwana wayo . """" """"
Yakomeje avuga ko Imana yemeye gutanga umwana wayo ngo apfire abari mu Isi .
"""" Amaraso """" """" ni indirimbo iri mu Kinyarwanda ariko mu gukora amashusho yayo amagambo ayigize yashyizwe mu Cyongereza kugira ngo ubutumwa buyikubiyemo bugere ku bantu benshi .
Gakunzi ni umwe mu bahanzi bagezweho mu bakorera umuziki hanze y'u Rwanda .
Izina rye rizwi cyane mu bihangano birimo """" Izina ryawe """" """" yanashyizwe mu Lingala , """" Mu mababa yawe """" """" na """" Uhoraho . """"
Yahisemo kwinjira mu muziki kuko abifata nk'impano Imana yamuhaye ngo atange ubutumwa bwiza mu mahanga yose no gutanga umusanzu mu kubaka Ubwami bw'Imana ku Isi .
Umuhanzi Willy Gakunzi asanzwe afite ibikorwa bitandukanye akora abinyujije mu Muryango Heart of Worship in Action ugamije guhindura imibereho y'abaturage mu buzima bw'umwuka n'umubiri .
Heart of Worship in Action Foundation yashinzwe mu mwaka wa 2019 ; ifite intego yo gushyigikira ibikorwa bitandukanye bigamije guhindura ubuzima bwa benshi binyuze mu kubaka no kongerera ubushobozi bw'abari mu muryango Nyarwanda .
ADEPR yakoze impinduka zidasanzwe muri paruwasi , inatangaza """" inyito """" nshya mu nzego zayo .
Ubusanzwe ADEPR yari ifite paruwasi 401 mu gihugu hose ariko mu mpinduka nshya zakozwe , zagabanyijwe zigirwa 143 mu gihe imidugudu [ ubu yahindutse amatorero ari 3125 ] .
Impinduka nshya muri ADEPR zatangajwe ku mugoroba wo ku wa Gatandatu , tariki ya 3 Mata 2021 .
Igikorwa cyo kugabanya Paruwasi kiri mu rugendo rw'impinduka muri ADEPR no kubaka Umudugudu na Paruwasi byifuzwa n'abanyetorero .
Cyatangajwe nyuma y'ikurwaho ry'itorero ry'akarere no kuvugurura indembo .
Ku wa 21 Gashyantare 2021 ni bwo hashyizweho abashumba b'indembo icyenda , na zo zongerewe kuko mbere zari eshanu .
Ibi byemezo biri gufatwa hashingiwe ku nshingano zikubiye mu ibaruwa y'Urwego rw'Igihugu rw'Imiyoborere , RGB , yashyizeho Komite nshya y'Inzibacyuho muri ADEPR ikayiha inshingano zo kuvugurura iri torero mu ngeri zitandukanye z'imiyoborere .
Aya mavugurura agomba gukorwa mu miyoborere , amategeko , inzego z'imiyoborere ndetse n'inzego z'imirimo , imikoranire n'imikorere muri ADEPR no kwemeza no gushyira mu bikorwa amavugurura muri ADEPR .
Umuvugizi w'Itorero ADEPR , Pasiteri Ndayizeye Isaïe , yabwiye Life Radio y'iri torero , ko mu gukora impinduka hifashishijwe ikusanyabitekerezo mu bagize ibyiciro bitandukanye hagamijwe guhurizwa hamwe icyariteza imbere .
Yagize ati """" Bikorwa humvwa ibitekerezo by'abanyetorero , abashumba , abapasiteri n'abandi bose binyuze mu matsinda yihariye yasesenguye ibyarushaho gukosorwa no kunozwa . """" """"
Yavuze ko impinduka zikorwa zigamije kureba uko itorero ryiyubaka , uko rikura no kwita ku hazaza haryo .
Ati """" Ese imikurire y'itorero ifasha n'abazadukomokaho kurikuriramo .
ADEPR uko imeze ni ko abakirisitu bayifuza .
Twashyizeho uburyo bwo gukoresha audit harebwa ibikorwa n'impinduka bigira ku mukirisitu . """" """"
Inyito nshya muri ADEPR
Mu mpinduka ADEPR yakoze harimo no guhindura inyito aho urwego rusanzwe rwitwa """" Umudugudu """" rwagizwe """" Itorero """" , """" ntibikuraho ya nyito isanzwe ikoreshwa ku rwego rw'igihugu .
Pasiteri Ndayizeye Isaïe yavuze ko hakiri kuvugururwa inzego z'imirimo ariko hazanakurikizwa iz'ubuyobozi .
Ati """" Muri uru rugendo icyifuzwa ni uko Umudugudu ariho hantu umukirisitu abonera ibyangombwa byose bimufasha gukura mu buryo bwuzuye kandi na serivisi akenera mu itorero akayihabonera . """" """"
Izi mpinduka zakozwe binyuze mu itsinda ry'abanyetorero bari mu byiciro birimo abakirisitu , abashumba , abapasiteri basesenguye ibyo Umudugudu ugomba kuba wujuje n'ibyo ukora .
Pasiteri Ndayizeye yakomeje ati """" Mu kurushaho gushyira umutima ku itorero , ntibikwiye ko turifata nka za nzego zo hejuru , aho umuntu yumva ko yageze ku itorero ari uko byageze kuri Biro Nyobozi .
Itorero ni hariya abakirisitu bari , ni hariya umukumbi uri , ni yo mpamvu mu ngamba nshya twifuje no guhindura inyito aho gukoresha Umudugudu hagakoreshwa Itorero . """" """"
Ntidushaka kwirukana abashumba
ADEPR igitangaza impinduka nshya muri za paruwasi , abakirisitu benshi bumvikanye bavuga ko zizasiga benshi mu bapasiteri babuze imirimo .
Umuvugizi wa ADEPR , Pasiteri Ndayizeye yavuze ko abashumba nta gahunda ihari yo kubaheza mu nshingano .
Ati """" Ntabwo dushaka kwirukana cyangwa guheza abashumba , turashaka ko umushumba akora umurimo we wo kwegera intama , akabana na zo kuko aricyo Kirisitu yaduhamagariye .
Nta rusengero rwafunzwe , zose zagumyeho . """" """"
Umudugudu wahinduriwe inyito ukitwa itorero uzajya uhabwa umushumba wawo uhoraho hagamijwe kuwongerera ubushobozi .
Inzego nyinshi zegerejwe abakirisitu mu gihe Paruwasi yagizwe nk'urwego ruhuza ibikorwa byose biri ku rw'amatorero .
Umushumba wa Paruwasi azaba afite inshingano zo guhuza abayobozi hagamijwe kubongerera ubushobozi .
Kuri ubu ADEPR ifite amatorero [ ayahoze yitwa imidugudu ] 3125 mu gihugu hose ari mu ndembo icyenda aho urwa Kigali rufite amatorero 163 na Paruwasi 12 ; urwa Gicumbi rufite Paruwasi 12 n'amatorero 306 ; urwa Muhoza ni Paruwasi 14 n'amatorero 259 , urwa Gihundwe ni Paruwasi 21 ; urwa Huye ni Paruwasi 18 n'amatorero 286 ; urwa Rubavu ni
Paruwasi 24 n'amatorero 528 ; urwa Ngoma ni Paruwasi 15 n'amatorero 370 ; urwa Nyagatare ni Paruwasi 16 n'amatorero 452 mu gihe Ururembo rwa Nyabisindu rufite Paruwasi 11 n'amatorero 262 .
Abakiristu bizihije Pasika bwa kabiri mu bihe bidasanzwe byo kwirinda Covid - 19 ( Amafoto ) .
Buri mwaka Abakirisitu bizihiza Umunsi Mukuru wa Pasika bakunze gushushanya nk'umunsi ubibutsa urupfu rwa Yezu ( Yesu ) Kirisitu wabitangiye akabapfira ku musaraba .
Ibirori bya Pasika byabaye kuri iki Cyumweru tariki 4 Mata 2021 , mu gihe mu Rwanda hari insengero zitari nke zigifunze kubera kutuzuza amabwiriza yo gukumira icyorezo .
Izemerewe gukora zategetswe kutarenza 30 % by'ubushobozi bw'abo zisanzwe zakira .
Hirya no hino hari bamwe mu bakirisitu bari bagiye mu Misa n'Amateraniro biba ngombwa ko basabwa gusubirayo bitewe n'uko umubare insengero zabo zigomba kwakira wari wamaze kuzura .
Nko kuri Paruwasi Gatolika ya Regina Pacis mu mujyi wa Kigali , hari abakiristu bahageze bakererewe basanga umubare w'abemerewe kwinjiramo wuzuye , basabwa gusubirayo .
Abakirisitu benshi basabwe gukurikirana ubutumwa butangwa bifashishije ikoranabuhanga ririmo Radio , Televiziyo ndetse n'imbuga nkoranyambaga zirimo YouTube .
Ubutumwa bwatanzwe n'Abayobozi b'amwe mu madini n'amatorero bwagarutse ku kwizihiza Umunsi Mukuru wa Pasika hanagarukwa ku kubahiriza amabwiriza yo kwirinda icyorezo cya Covid - 19 .
Musenyeri Thadée Ntihinyurwa wahoze ari arkiyepiskopi wa Kigali yibukije Abakirisitu ko Yezu Kristu ari urukundo ruhoraho ndetse yarukomereje ku musaraba ubwo yemeraga gupfira Abemeramana .
Ati """" Bakristu , ni mwakire urwo rukundo rw'Imana , urukundo rw'ibyishimo ruturuka kuri Yezu wazutse .
Urukundo rusanga bose , ntirurobanura , ntirusanga gusa ukunda ariko urukundo rusanga n'abanzi kandi rugasanga n'abataruzi . """"
Umushumba w'Itorero Angilikani muri Paruwasi ya Remera , Pasiteri Antoine Rutayisire , yavuze ko Covid - 19 , yaje bwa mbere ubwo Abakristo biteguraga kwizihiza Pasika yo mu 2020 , asaba ko mubyo basengera basaba Imana guhagarika iki cyorezo .
Ati """" Maze iminsi mbwira Imana nti tugeze kuri Pasika ya kabiri Coronavirus igihari , ugire ikintu ukora .
Nagira ngo uyu munsi mu bintu dusengera , twizerere ko [ . . . ] Coronavirus igiye kurangira , Imana dusenga ni Imana ifite ubushobozi kandi ishobora guhagarika ibintu . """"
Umuyobozi w'Itorero Zion Temple , Apôtre Dr Paul Gitwaza , yibukije Abakristo b'iri torero n'abandi bari bakurikiye amateraniro mu buryo bw'ikoranabuhanga ko Yesu yatsinze urupfu kandi ari muzima bityo na Coronavirus izatsindwa .
Apôtre Dr Gitwaza yavuze ko uyu mwaka bagiriwe ubuntu bwo guterana kugira ngo bishimire Pasika bari hamwe cyane ko umwaka ushize batabashije kubona ayo mahirwe .
Ati """" Umwaka ushize ntabwo twabashije guterana kuri Pasika nk'uku , abantu benshi twari muri guma mu rugo , murabona ko Imana irimo igenda ikingura gahoro gahoro , twizeye ko imiryango izagenda ikinguka abantu bakabasha guterana . """"
Apôtre Joshua Masasu Ndagijimana , Umuyobozi w'Itorero ry'Isanamitima rya ERC [ Evangelical Restoration church ] , yavuze ko Kristo witangiye abantu yaje kuba imfura yo kuzuka kugira ngo areme ibyiringiro mu bamwizera .
Ati """" Umwami wacu Yesu Kristu yatubereye umuganura cyangwa imfura yo kuzuka kugira ngo muri we aturemere ibyiringiro bizima , bihoraho kandi bidashobora kutubeshya cyangwa kubura burundu . """"
Papa Francis mu butumwa yatanze kuri iki Cyumweru tariki 4 Mata , ubwo yari ayoboye Igitambo cya Misa I Vatican muri Bazilika ya Mutagatifu Petero [ St . Peter's Basilica ] , yavuze ko icyorezo cya Covid - 19 , gikomeje kuzahaza abatuye Isi haba mu buryo bw'imibereho n'ubukungu , asaba by'umwihariko ibihugu bikize gusaranganya inkingo
z'iki cyorezo .
Nyuma y'igihe acecetse , Dominic Ashimwe yanzikanye indirimbo """" Gwiza imbaraga . """"
Ashimwe wamenyekanye mu njyana z'indirimbo zihimbaza Imana yavuze ko kumara igihe kinini nta gihangano gishya ashyira hanze byatewe n'izindi nshingano yari afite mu muryango we yagombaga kuzuza .
Yagize ati """" Ni njye mukuru mu muryango , byansabaga kwita ku bavandimwe banjye mu buryo buhagije , hanyuma kandi ndi umunyeshuri muri kaminuza ku buryo ngomba gukurikirana amasomo nta kujenjeka kugira ngo abanze arangire ajye ku ruhande bityo nzoroherwe no gukomeza umuziki neza nta nkomyi .
Ntabwo naretse kuririmba , nta na gahunda mfite yo kubihagarika kuko ni umuhamagaro nitabye ntazuyaje , ndabikunda cyane . """"
Ashimwe uri gusoza amasomo ye muri Mount Kenya University mu Ishami ry'Itangazamakuru n'Itumanaho , avuga ko yifuje kugenda gake mu rugendo rwo kwita ku muryango we , gukurikirana amasomo no gukora umuziki .
Ati """" Nari kubifatanya n'umuziki bikemera ariko nta cyizere nari mfite ko byose byagenda neza uko bikwiye .
Byari byiza gukora kimwe kikarangira nkabona gukora ikindi , ni bwo buryo nasanze butanga umusaruro wizewe kandi uhamye uzira kwicuza nyuma .
Ntabwo Imana izaguhembera ko wakoze byinshi cyane , izaguhembera gusa uburyo wabikozemo niba bwari buhuje n'ugushaka kwayo . """" """"
Mu mikorere y'umuziki wa Dominic Ashimwe nkuko yagiye abitangaza mu myaka yo ha mbere , avuga ko kuririmba atabikora nk'umwuga umuha amafaranga y'imibereho ahubwo ko abikora nk'umuhamagaro gusa .
Ibi bigaragarira ku cyemezo gikomeye azwiho ko atajya yishyuza ibitaramo bye ahubwo gahunda ye ni ukugeza ubutumwa ku ngeri zose z'abantu .
Icyo gihe yagize ati """" Nahisemo kudakora muzika nyishakamo amafaranga ambeshaho ahubwo mpitamo gushaka akandi kazi kamfasha kubaho nk'abandi bose .
Gukora ibi byari amahitamo yanjye gusa ntaho bihuriye n'ibindi undi wese yatekereza ko nagendeyeho .
Nifuza ko ubutumwa bwiza ndirimba bugera ku ngeri n'inzego zose z'abantu : abakire n'abakene , abakomeye n'aboroheje . . . . Imana nishima kumpera umugisha mu murimo wayo izabinkorera ku bw'ubuntu bwayo gusa , ariko si cyo mpanze amaso . """" """"
"""" Nshishikajwe no gukora ibishoboka byose ngo ubutumwa ndirimba ntihagire n'umwe ucikanwa na bwo biturutse ku mpamvu iyo ari yo yose .
Hirya y'ibi byose mbikiwe ingororano nziza zitangirika .
Uko ni ko mbyizera . """" """"
Indirimbo nshya Dominic Ashimwe yashyize hanze yayise """" Gwiza imbaraga """" , """" yumvikanamo amagambo akomeza abantu , akabaremamo ibyiringiro .
Mu kiganiro na IGIHE , Ashimwe yavuze ko indirimbo ye nshya yayikoze agamije kwibutsa abantu gukora kw'Imana .
Yagize ati """" Ntabwo Imana ijya gutira imbaraga ku wundi muntu ngo ibashe kudutabara , Oya !
Uko yakwiyeretse mu bihe byashize , kwa kundi yitamuruye usumbirijwe ukayibona n'ubu iracyabishoboye kugutabara rwose kandi ibikora ku bw'ubuntu bwayo gusa nta kindi irebyeho .
Ni Imana idahindurwa n'ibihe .
Gwiza imbaraga z'umutima ukomere , Uwiteka ntajya ananirwa , ntasinzira ahora ari maso ku bwawe nanjye . """"
Indirimbo """" Gwiza imbaraga """" yasohotse isanga izindi ndirimbo zirimo iyitwa """" Ndishimye , """" """" Akadomo ka nyuma """" na """" Wambereye imfura """" zizaba ziri kuri album ye nshya yise """" Urufatiro . """"
Reba hano indirimbo nshya ya Dominic Ashimwe yise """" Gwiza imbaraga """"
Papi Clever n'umugore we bishimiwe mu ndirimbo nshya bise """" Ni Yesu """"
Mu ndirimbo """" Ni Yesu """" """" igizwe n'iminota itandatu n'amasegonda ane , itangirana n'amagambo avuga ko imitwaro """" nari nikoreye nayituriye ku musaraba . """"
Ikomeza iti """" Yesu yancunguje amaraso ye y'igiciro , yampaye umugabane mu bwami bwe .
[ . . . ] Nta wundi wari kubikora ni Yesu .
Yangezemo ndahinduka .
Ndi ibihamya by'uko ashoboye . """" """"
Papi Clever yabwiye IGIHE ko yatekereje kwandika iyi ndirimbo mu gushimangira uko Yesu yahinduye byinshi kuri we no ku buzima bwe .
Ati """" Igitekerezo cyavuye kuri Kristo Yesu waje kudupfira ngo tubone ubugingo , tuvugamo aho yadukuye habi tukemeza ko nta wundi wari kubishobora atari we .
Yesu yatugezemo tubona amahoro tutari kubonera ahandi . """" """"
Indirimbo """" Ni Yesu """" """" yasohokanye n'amashusho yayo yishimiwe cyane n'abakunzi b'ibihangano bya Papi Clever n'umugore we .
Abayitanzeho ibitekerezo berekanye ko ari indirimbo nziza kandi yahembuye abafite umwuma mu buryo butandukanye .
Umugwaneza Solange yagize ati """" Muhabwe umugisha abanjye nkunda ; ndabakunda n'umutima wanjye wose . """" """"
Mategeko Benjamin we yasabiye uyu muryango kurindwa n'Imana n'Umwana wayo kugezaagarutse .
Yagize ati """" Papi na Dorcas , muri abagabuzi b'umutsima n'amazi y'ubugingo .
Uyu muhamagaro mwakiriye urimo gukiza imitima myinshi . """" """"
Niyombikesha Eustache yavuze ati """" Papi & Dorcas mbakunda kubi , gusa muri iyi minsi biri kurenga urugero kabisa , iyi ndirimbo yanyu NI YESU ndi kuyicuranga bukira nyisubijemo nka 20 .
Ndabakunda cyane , iyi hamwe n'iyindi yitwa Unkomereze Amaboko ndaziharaye bikomeye muri iyi minsi . """" """"
Nyuma yo gukora indirimbo """" Ni Yesu , """" Papi Clever yijeje abakunzi b'ibihangano byabo ko bagiye gushyira imbaraga mu gukora byinshi .
Ati """" Ni byo tugiye kujya tubaha indirimbo zacu uko Imana izagenda iziduha , ntabwo tuzi niba zizaba ari nyinshi cyangwa ari nke kuko ni Umwuka Wera uzaziduha . """" """"
Papi Clever na Ingabire Dorcas basanzwe bamenyerewe cyane mu gusubiramo indirimbo zo mu Gitabo ndetse barateganya """" kuzikora zikarangira . """"
Yakomeje ati """" Tuzakora izo mu Cyongereza n'izindi ndimi kandi turashaka kujya tubikora mu buryo bwiza yaba audio na video . """" """"
Tuyizere Papi Clever na Ingabire Dorcas bashyingiwe ku wa 7 Ukuboza 2019 , ubu bafitanye umwana umwe w'umukobwa bise Ineza Oaklynn Clever .
Nyuma yo kurushinga batangiye gukorana umuziki .
Papi Clever yari asanzwe akora umuziki nk'umuhanzi wigenga mu gihe Ingabire yaririmbaga muri Korali Goshen ikorera ivugabutumwa muri ADEPR Musanze .
Papi Clever ni we watangije umushinga wo gusubiramo indirimbo zo mu gitabo uko ari 547 .
Album ya mbere y'izi ndirimbo yayise """" Amakuru y'Umurwa """" [ iyi ndirimbo imaze kurebwa n'abasaga miliyoni kuri YouTube ] ikubiyeho indirimbo 12 zo mu gitabo .
Nyuma yo kurushinga , urwo rugendo yarukomezanyije n'umugore we .
Reba indirimbo """" Ni Yesu """" ya Papi Clever na Ingabire Dorcas
Pasiteri Antoine Rutayisire yakomoje ku bikwiriye kuranga ubuyobozi buzana impinduka
Ibi yabigarutseho kuri iki Cyumweru tariki ya 28 Werurwe 2021 , ubwo yari mu masengesho yo gusengera igihugu ( National Prayer Breakfast ) .
Ni amasengesho yabaye mu buryo bw'ikoranabuhanga mu rwego rwo gukomeza kwirinda icyorezo cya Coronavirus .
Rev . Dr Rutayisire Antoine yavuze ko umuyobozi adakwiye gucika intege mu gihe cy'amage ahubwo akwiye gukomeza urugendo .
Yavuze ko buri gihe ubuyobozi buba bufite ibibazo bityo ko umuyobozi akwiriye gushaka impinduka no mu gihe cy'ibibazo .
Ati """" Nutagira ibibazo by'abakozi , uzagira ibibazo by'ibikoresho , nutagira iby'ibikoresho uzagira iby'abashaka gutwara umwanya wawe .
Nutagira ikibazo cy'ibyo , uzagira kibazo cy'umunaniro kuko ushaka gukora akazi kugira ngo uzane impinduka .
Ubuyobozi ni umurimo iteka ubamo ibibazo kandi iteka bisaba ko wowe nk'umuyobozi uzana impinduka . """"
Dr Rev . Rutayisire yavuze ko umuyobozi iteka akwiriye kugirira impuhwe abo ayobora kuko iteka ryose ahagarara hagati y'ikibazo n'abo ayoboye .
Ati """" """" Hari abayobozi iyo havutse ikibazo aho kuzana ibisubizo bongera ibibazo .
Akongeramo kuvuga nabi , agakuraho telefoni cyangwa agafunga ibiro cyangwa akigendera . """"
Dr Rutayisire yakomeje avuga ko umuyobozi mwiza akwiye kuvugana n'abantu akabaha icyizere kuko iyo bitabaye bishakira ibisubizo kandi ari we muyobozi .
Ati """" Niba udafite icyizere wowe cyubake mu bantu bawe .
Bashyiremo icyizere ubabwire uti ibibazo birahari , turabibona ariko mwihangane Imana igiye kuzana ibisubizo . """"
Dr Antoine Rutayisire yavuze kandi ko mu bindi umuyobozi mwiza akwiye kurangwa no gutuza .
Ati """" Umuyobozi akwiye gutuza kandi ntahunge ibibazo .
Mu ituze no mu byiringiro niho uzakura imbaraga mu gihe cy'ibibazo noneho iri tuze rigomba kwiyongera . """"
Antoine Rutayise yavuze ko umuyobozi mwiza akwiye kubwira abantu gukomeza bakagenda kabone nubwo baba bari mu kaga .
Ati """" Umuyobozi akwiye kubwira abantu bagakomeza bakagenda nubwo hari ibibazo , ibibazo ntibidukura mu ntego zacu .
Ibibazo icyo bikora ni ukutugendesha gahoro """" .
Rev . Dr Rutayisire yatanze urugero , avuga ko u Rwanda rwahuye n'ikibazo cya Coronavirus ariko bitarubujije gukomeza .
Avuga ko u Rwanda rwanyuze mu ntambara , amashuri agasenyuka , abantu bagapfa ariko ibyo byose bitaruhagaritse bityo ko umuyobozi agomba kwigirira icyizere kandi agafatanya n'abo ayobora .
Amasengesho ngarukamwaka yo gusengera igihugu azwi nka """" National Prayer Breakfast """" ategurwa n'umuryango Rwanda Leaders Fellowship , ukaba umaze imyaka 26 uyategura .
National Prayer Breakfast yitabirwaga n'Abayobozi bahagarariye Amadini n'Amatorero n'abandi Bihayimana , Abayobozi muri Guverinoma , abikorera ku giti cyabo , abagize sosiyete sivile n'inshuti z'u Rwanda ziba zaturutse mu bihugu bitandukanye .
Nazareen Worship Team yatangiye ivugabutumwa ry'indirimbo zihembura bahereye ku Banyarwanda bo muri Amerika .
Nazareen Worship Team isanzwe ikorera umurimo w'Imana mu rusengero rwa Pasiteri Kawaya Pascal muri Michigan .
Iri tsinda ryamaze gushyira hanze indirimbo yaryo ya mbere bise """" Wamenyesheje Inzira """" intego akaba ari ugukomeza gukora indirimbo nyinshi zitandukanye .
Emile Ngoga , umwe mu bagize iri tsinda yabwiye IGIHE ko intego yabo ari ukugeza ubutumwa bwa Yesu Kristo kuri bose , kuko ari imwe mu nshingano yahaye abamwizera .
Ati """" Iyi ndirimbo ndetse n'izindi ziri mu nzira turifuza ko abantu bose bamenya kandi bakizera izina rihebuje rya Kristo Yesu .
Birababaje cyane cyangwa se bizaba bibabaje birenzeho Kristo aramutse agarutse abantu bataramwizera . """"
Yavuze ko intego ya Nazareen Worship Team ari ukubwiriza ubutumwa bwiza bukiza , bubohora kandi bukangurira isi yose kwizera Yesu .
Ngoga yavuze ko iryo tsinda ryifuza gushyira hanze album ya mbere igizwe n'indirimbo umunani mu mwaka wa 2021 .
Yavuze ko kuri ubu bafite itsinda ry'Abanyarwanda basengana mu rusengero rwabo , ari naho haturutse igitekerezo cyo kwagura ivugabutumwa ryabo rikava mu rusengero rikagera kure .
Ati """" Mbere twakoreraga mu Itorero n'abandi banyamerika ariko tumaze kuba benshi twahisemo gukora amateraniro yacu .
Iyo bibaye ngombwa ko dukorana n'abanyamahanga turirimba indirimbo zo kuramya zisanzwe mu Cyongereza ariko mu materaniro y'Ikinyarwanda turirimba indirimbo nyinshi mu Kinyarwanda . """"
Indirimbo """" Wamenyesheje Inzira """" ya Nazareen Worship Team yari imaze amezi ane itunganywa na Producer Boris .
Amashusho yayo yakozwe na Fayzo , ayoborwa na GM Brown .
Lewis Vocal Band yasohoye amashusho y'indirimbo ibwira abantu kwiringira Imana no mu bikomeye .
Indirimbo """" Ndakwiringiye """" irimo ubutumwa bwo kubwira abantu ko no mu bihe bikomeye , inzira zose zifunze n'inshuti zananiwe , bakwiriye guhora biringira Imana kuko ari yo idahemuka .
Umuyobozi wa Lewis Vocal Band , Tuyiramye Protogène , yabwiye IGIHE ko basohoye iyi ndirimbo by'umwihariko muri ibi bihe Isi yugarijwe n'icyorezo cya Coronavirus cyahungabanyije ibintu byinshi mu mibereho ya benshi kugira ngo abantu bongere kwibuka ko Imana itahindutse .
Yagize ati """" Ni indirimbo ikoze mu buryo bw'isengesho umuntu wese yasenga abwira Imana ko akiyiringiye n'ubwo ibibazo byaba byinshi bite . """"
"""" Turashaka kwibutsa abantu ko n'ubwo Isi iri mu bihe bitoroshye , benshi bahuye n'ibibazo ntibakwiye kwiheba cyangwa ngo bumve ko byarangiye , bakwiye kugirira Imana icyizere bakagumya kuyiringira kuko yo itajya ihemuka . """"
Tuyiramye yakomeje avuga ko uretse iyi ndirimbo hari n'izindi zikiri gutunganywa muri studio bitegura kuzasohora mu minsi iri imbere nazo zatunganyijwe mu buryo bwa """" Live """" ari amajwi ndetse n'amashusho .
Lewis Vocal Band ni itsinda rigizwe ahanini n'urubyiruko rubarizwa mu Itorero ADEPR , bahuriye ku kuba bakuriye mu ishuri ry'icyumweru ( Sunday school ) .
Yashinzwe mu 2014 itangijwe n'abasore batatu bishyize hamwe bashaka gukora umuziki wa acappella , nyuma itsinda rigenda ryaguka hiyongeramo n'abandi ndetse n'imikorere irahinduka , kugeza mu 2018 ubwo bavuga ko ari bwo basa n'aho ari bwo binjiye mu ruhando byeruye .
Intego y'iri tsinda nk'uko Tuyiramye yabitangaje ngo ni ukwamamaza ubutumwa bwiza hafi na kure ndetse no kurushaho kuba icyitegererezo bigatuma n'abagiye bava ku Mana bahindukira bakayigarukira .
Bashishikariye gukomeza kubwira urundi rubyiruko kuva mu byaha rukizera Umwami Yesu n'abakiri bato bagakomeza gukurira mu murongo wo kubaha Imana ndetse impano zabo bakazikoresha ku bw'Ubwami bw'Imana .
Tuyiramye yasabye abantu gukomeza kubashyigikira kuko hari ibikorwa byinshi bitegura gukomeza gukora mu bihe biri imbere , birimo gusohora n'izindi ndirimbo zirimo iziri gutunganywa muri studio kuri ubu .
Jabiru d'Afrique , imwe mu nyoni ziramba cyane ku isi zizirana no gucana inyuma .
Mu muryango mugari w'abantu hari abantu twita ba nyamwigendaho baba babikora mu gushaka amahoro cyangwa kubera ikibazo runaka bagize mu mibanire n'abandi ariko ahantu henshi abantu bameze batyo babasha kuboneka .
Tumaze igihe kinini tuvuga ku nyoni zikunda gusabana n'izindi zihuje ubwoko cyangwa se zifite ibindi bintu runaka zihuriyeho .
Ibyo siko bimeze ku nyoni z'amazi zitwa Jabiru d'Afrique ( Jabiru ) kuko zo zikunda kuba zonyine haba mu gushaka ibyo kurya cyangwa mu kororoka .
Uretse kuba wabona ikigabo n'ikigore biri kumwe , kongera kubona izi nyoni ziri kumwe n'izindi nka zo , cyangwa se izindi zo mu bundi bwoko ni ibintu bidasanzwe .
Imiterere ya Jabiru d'Afrique ( African Saddle - billed Stork )
Jabiru ni inyoni yo ku mazi ifitanye isano n'ibiyongoyongo na Nyirabarazana , kandi ikaba ari yo ndende muri uwo muryango mugari .
Ikigabo gikuze kiba gifite amababa y'umukara n'umweru .
Ku gice cyo hejuru ku mugongo hasa n'umweru ariko wagana inyuma hakaba ibara ry'umukara .
Amababa n'imirizo ni umukara ugaragaramo icyatsi kibisi gishashagirana .
Ku gice cyo hasi mu gatuza no kunda hasa n'umweru .
Iyo amababa arambuye , ukayabona inyuze hejuru yawe ubona asa n'umukara .
Iyo iyi nyoni irimo kuguruka ku mpera z'amababa ubona ibara ry'umweru .
Umutwe n'ijosi ni umukara .
Aho umunwa utangirira haratukuye kandi hagati hagaragaramo igice cy'umukara hanyuma hakongera kugaragaraho igice cy'umutuku .
Jabiru y'ikigabo igira amaso y'ikijuju .
Amaguru n'amano arirabura kandi ikagira mu mavi hasa n'ibara rya move .
Ikigore kiba ari gito ugereranyije n'ikigabo ariko bigira amabara asa nubwo ikigore kigira amaso y'umuhondo .
Iyi nyoni ishobora kugira uburebure bwa santimetero 145 - 150 , n'ubugari bw'amababa bwa santimetero 240 - 270 .
Iyi nyoni ishobora kandi kugira ibilo 5 - 7 . 5 ku ngabo n'ibilo 5 - 7 ku ngore .
Iyi nyoni ishobora kurama imyaka 36 .
Inyoni ikunda kuba ku migezi
Jabiru iba ahantu hari amazi nko mu bishanga , ku nkengero z'imigezi , mu bishanga birimo ibiti bigufi , ibiyaga birimo amazi arimo umunyu n'ahandi hatandukanye .
Izi nyoni ntabwo zikunda ahantu h'ishyamba ariko zishobora kuboneka ahantu hatumagara cyane mu gihe cy'izuba .
Iyi nyoni ni indyanyama kuko itungwa n'amafi harimo Tilapiya , imitubu n'ibikeri .
Inarya kandi ibikururanda bitoya nk'imiserebanya , ibinyamunjonjorerwa , amagi y'izindi nyoni n'ibyana byazo , inyamabere ntoya n'ibindi .
Kuberako iyi nyoni igenda mu mazi igashoramo umunwa ishakamo ibyo kurya nk'amafi n'ibindi , inshuro nyinshi amazi ashobora kwandura .
Ni yo mpamvu mbere yo kurya ifi ibanza kuyoza yarangiza ikayimira bunguri ihereye ku mutwe .
Jabiru d'Afrique yororoka ite ?
Jabiru ntabwo buri mwaka yororoka ahubwo imishwi imaze umwaka umwe cyangwa ibiri ikomeza kubana n'ababyeyi bayo kugeza ikindi gihe cyo kororoka kw'ababyeyi bayo .
Umushwi umaze imyaka itatu uba ukuze ku buryo uba ushobora kororoka na wo .
Iyi nyoni ikunda gutangira kororoka iyo igihe cy'imvura kirangiye , ni ukuvuga ko yororoka mu gihe cy'impeshyi .
Ingabo n'ingore bibana ubuzima bwabyo bwose kuko bikora umuryango udacana inyuma ( Monogamie ) .
Jabiru yubaka icyari ahantu ha yonyine mu giti kirekire hafi y'amazi .
Izi nyoni kandi zikunda gukoresha icyari inshuro zirenze imwe .
Ingabo n'ingore bifatanya kubaka icyari gikoze mu byatsi bikurungiye n'ibyondo .
Iyo icyari kimaze kubakwa ikigore gitera amagi abiri cyangwa atatu .
Igihe cyo kurarira ayo magi ni iminsi iri hagati ya 30 - 35 kandi bigakorwa n'ingabo n'ingore .
Imishwi ikimara kuvuka iba isa n'umweru kandi igaburirwa n'ababyeyi bombi .
Imishwi imaze iminsi iri hagati ya 70 - 100 iba imaze gukura bihagije .
Muri rusange ibi bisiga biracyagaragara ahantu henshi akaba ariyo mpamvu Umuryango Mpuzamahanga wita ku bidukikije ubishyira ku rutonde rw'ibitageramiwe , nubwo muri iki gihe birimo kubangamirwa cyane no kubura ibishanga byo kubamo ndetse n'imiti myinshi ikoreshwa mu kwica udukoko .
Mu Rwanda , iyi nyoni isigaye muri parike y'Akagera gusa .
Mu myaka 30 ishize , yanabonekagaga ku biyaga byo mu Bugesera .
Minisitiri Mujawamariya yasabye abanya - Gicumbi kwita ku mashyamba birinda akaga kazanwa n'ubutayu .
Ibi Minisitiri yabigarutseho ku wa 7 Ugushyingo 2020 mu Karere ka Gicumbi , ho murenge wa Byumba , ubwo hatangizwaga igihembwe cyo gutera amashyamba muri gahunda z'umushinga ugamije kongerera abaturage ubushobozi ku guhangana n'ingaruka z'imihindagurikire y'ibihe uzwi nka Green Gicumbi .
Ahatewe amashyamba kuri uyu wa Gatandatu ni ahahoze hari amashyamba y'abaturage yangiritse cyangwa yashaje .
Akarere ka Gicumbi , gasanzwe ari akarere karangwamo imisozi miremire kandi ihanamye , kakaba gakunze kwibasirwa n'ibiza .
Aha niho Minisitiri w'Ibidukikije yahereye avuga ko hatagize igikorwa abaturage bakwisanga mu byago , abasaba guhuza ubutaka kugira ngo buterweho amashyamba .
Ati """" Kuri ziriya hegitari 20 twateyeho amashyamba , mwabonye ko hariho ubuhaname buri kugera kuri hafi 80 % .
Hatagize igikorwa rero Gicumbi yagerwaho n'akaga gakomeye . """"
Yakomeje agira ati """" Gicumbi rero nkuko mubizi ni akarere k'imisozi miremire , ni akarere gafite n'ubukungu .
Niyo mpamvu tugomba kubungabunga iyo misozi ndetse n'ubwo butaka , tukabufata kugira ngo tubuhinge ariko tubungabunga ibidukikije . """"
Minisitiri Mujawamariya yavuze ko ahatewe amashyamba hari hasanzwe ari ubutaka bw'abaturage bwarimo ibiti bishaje , aboneraho gusaba abaturage kwita ku biti byatewe banashyiraho amaterasi y'indinganire aho bishoboka .
Ati """" Abaturage ibyo basabwa ni uguhuza imirima yabo kugira ngo dushobore guteraho amashyamba .
Bari basanzwe bafite amashyamba ariko ashaje tubafasha kuyavugurura . """"
"""" Mu byukuri icyo dusaba abaturage ni uguhuza imirima yabo tukabungabunga iyo mirima dushyiraho amaterasi y'indinganire aho bishoboka , cyangwa se imiringoti aho bishoboka tugateraho amashyamba . """"
Yavuze ko abaturage bakwiriye gukurikirana bakareba ko ibiti bateye bikura , icyangiritse bakagisimbuza vuba .
Muri rusange hatewe ibiti ibihumbi 50 ku buso bungana na hegitari 20 bwagenewe amashyamba .
Guverineri w'Intara y'Amajyarugu , Gatabazi Jean Marie Vianney , yavuze ko abaturage basigaranye umukoro wo kurinda ibiti ari nako batangira kwiga umuco wo gukoresha rondereza cyangwa gaz hagamijwe kubungabunga amashyamba .
Ati """" Turemera ko ibicanwa bikenerwa umunsi ku munsi ariko bagomba kwinjira mu buryo umuturage akoresha ibikoresho bituma acana bike mu buryo bushoboka , yaba rondereza ndetse na gaz aho bishoboka .
Abaturage babishyigikire , babigire ibyabo hanyuma na ya mashyamba bayarinde dukomeze twagure ubuso tugomba guteraho amashyamba . """"
Usibye kuba aka karere katewemo amashyamba , biteganyijwe ko uyu mwaka mu gihugu hose hazaterwa ibiti bivangwa n'imyaka kuri hegitari 7 410 , amashyamba kuri hegitari 909 2 , n'ibiti by'imbuto ziribwa bisaga 803 , 947 .
Ni mugihe amashyamba yangiritse azasazurwa angana na hegitari 500 .
Leta y'u Rwanda yihaye intego y'uko kugera mu 2024 , 30 % by'ubuso bw'igihugu buzaba buteyeho amashyamba kandi acunzwe mu buryo burambye kugira ngo arusheho kubyazwa umusaruro uhagije .
Integuza ku byago bishobora kuzagwira Isi kubera kutita ku bidukikije .
Uru ni rumwe mu rugero rw'imibanire itari myiza ya none hagati y'umuntu n'ibidukikije , aho igihe muntu yimutse , ibimera bisagamba , bikaba inganzamarumbo .
Uburyo ibikorwa bya muntu bikomeje kubangamira ibidukikije bigarukwaho by'umwihariko muri filime """" A Life on Our Planet , """" yakozwe n'Umwongereza , David Attenborough w'imyaka 93 .
Yagiye hanze ku wa 4 Ukwakira 2020 , ibanza kwerekanwa kuri Netflix .
Igaruka ku rugendo rwa Attenborough wazengurutse ibihugu byinshi ku mibumbe yose y'Isi , aho yiboneye impinduka n'ibyago ibikorwa bya muntu byagiye bigira kuri uyu mubumbe dutuye , uko umubare w'abawutuye wagendaga utumbagira , ibidukikije byo bikagabanyuka .
Muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba yahageze mu 1960 .
Uko amashyamba yagendaga atemwa cyangwa atwikwa , inyamaswa zo mu gasozi zarakendereye .
Uyu munsi bibarwa ko inkoko zihariye 70 % by'inyoni zose zo ku Isi , mu gihe inyamaswa muri rusange nazo zisigaye mu matungo abantu borora , ku buryo izo mu gasozi zingana na 4 % .
Bibarwa ko mu gihe muntu adahinduye imikorere mu bijyanye n'ibidukikije , akiga gukorera ibidukikije bimuri iruhande aho kubanza kubyigizayo , ibibazo bitazabura kuvuka .
Bitabaye ibyo , ubushyuhe bw'Isi buzakomeza kuzamuka ku buryo mu 2100 buzaba bumaze kwiyongeraho dogere Celcius 4 .
Attenborough yavuze ko mu guhangana n'iki kibazo , ibihugu byashyira imbaraga mu gutera amashyamba ku bwinshi , ndetse bigakoresha ingufu zisubira nk'izikomoka ku zuba cyangwa amazi , aho kuba amakara atuma ibiti bitemwa cyangwa ibikomoka kuri peteroli byohereza imyuka myinshi yangiza ikirere .
Bibarwa ko gutera amashyamba menshi ari ingenzi , kuko ashobora kugabanya nibura bibiri bya gatatu bya carbone yoherezwa mu kirere .
Ibyo bigahuzwa n'uko abantu batangira kwiga uburyo bakora ubuhinzi bakoresheje guhinga ku butaka buto , urugero ni nk'u Buholandi bwabashije kubigeraho , ku buryo buri ku mwanya wa kabiri ku isi mu kohereza mu mahanga ibiribwa byinshi .
David akomeza ati """" Ibi dukwiye kubikora tutazirikana ko ari ugutabara umubumbe wacu , ahubwo ni ukwitabara ubwacu . """"
Ibihugu byasabwe gufata ingambaUbwo herekanwaga iyi filime yakozwe na David Attenborough , Ambasaderi w'u Bwongereza mu Rwanda , Jo Lomas , yavuze ko muri uku kwezi u Bwongereza bwari bwiteguye kwakira Perezida Paul Kagame n'abandi banyacyubahiro , mu nama ku kurengera ibidukikije no gihangana n'ihindagurika ry'ibihe , izwi nka COP26 .
Gusa kubera icyorezo cya Coronavirus , yimuriwe umwaka utaha .
Ambasaderi Lomas yashimangiye ko COVID - 19 ariko idakwiriye kubuza abantu guhangana n'ikibazo gikomeye cy'ihindagurika ry'ibihe .
Yakomeje ati """" Imihindagurikire nicyo kibazo gikomeye kibangamiye ibisekuru bizaza .
Muri Afurika , ukwiyongera k'ubushyuhe bikomeje kugira ingaruka ku mibereho y'abaturage , nubwo ibihugu by'uyu mubumbe byihariye gusa 2 - 3 % by'imyuka isi yohereza mu kirere .
U Rwanda rwohereza imyuka mike yangiza ikirere , ariko rukomeje kugerwaho n'ingaruka z'imihindagurikire y'ibihe nk'imyuzure n'inkangu . """"
Ibyo ngo bigaragaza ko ari uruhare rwa buri wese mu guhangana n'imihindagurikire y'ibihe , aho gutekereza ko ari inshingano z'igihugu cyangwa urwego rumwe .
Yavuze ko kwita ku bidukikije byatanga umusanzu mu ngamba zo kugabanya imyuka ihumanya ikirere bitarenze 2030 , agaragaza ko u Bwongereza bushishikajwe no gutera inkunga imishinga iri muri urwo rwego , harimo no mu Rwanda .
Mu mishinga batera inkunga harimo uwa FONERWA ugira uruhare mu bikorwa birimo kubungabunga igishanga cya Nyandungu , ndetse ikigo Bboxx cyo mu Bwongereza kiri gutanga umusanzu mu gutuma Abanyarwanda bakoresha ingufu zitangiza ikirere , zikomoka ku mirasire y'izuba .
Minisitiri w'Ibidukikije , Jeanne d'Arc Mujawamariya , yavuze ko Guverinoma y'u Rwanda ishishikajwe no gukemura ibibazo by'ibidukikije hagamijwe guhangana n'ingaruka z'imihindagurikire y'ibihe .
Yavuze ko nubwo hari intambwe iterwa buri mwaka mu kugabanya ingano y'imyuka yoherezwa mu kirere , hari intambwe ukomeye igomba guterwa .
U Rwanda ruheruka kwiyemeza kugabanya imyuka yoherezwa mu kirere ho 38 % bitarenze umwaka wa 2020 , gahunda biteganywa ko izatwara miliyari $ 11 mu myaka icumi iri imbere , u Rwanda rukazakorana n'abafatanyabikorwa batandukanye .
Bizakorwa binyuze mu mishinga irimo amazi , ubuhinzi , ibimera n'amashyamba , ubucukuzi bw'amabuye burengera ibidukikije n'ibindi .
Minisitiri Mujawamariya yakomeje ati """" Ikindi nta mushinga uzajya utangira mu Rwanda hatabayeho inyigo ijyanye no kurengera ibidukikije ngo hatangwe icyemezo . """"
U Rwanda rwashyizeho FONERWA mu 2012 ku bufatanye n'u Bwongereza , aho gitera inkunga imishinga ijyanye kurengera ibidukikije .
Mu myaka isaga umunani ishize , iki kigega kimaze gushyira hamwe miliyoni $ 180 , kandi aho aya mafaranga yaguye ahorwa hamaze gutanga imirimo 140 000 .
Minisitiri Mujawamariya yashishikarije abikorera kongera ishoramari mu mishinga ibyara inyungu ariko irengera ibidukikije , anasaba ababyeyi kwigisha abato aho gutera igiti bagatera ishyamba , nk'uburyo bwo kubaka umuco wo kurengera ibidukikije n'urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Nsengimana Olivier uyobora Rwanda Wildlife Conservation Association , yavuze ko bafite imishinga igamije gushishikariza abantu kongera ibiti batera .
Ati """" Igihe kirageze ko buri wese abigire ibye , ari nacyo ntekereza ko COP26 igamije .
Nk'urugero hari gahunda turimo gutangiza mu muryango wacu , ku wa Mbere tuzasinyana amasezerano n'abaturage , barimo kuduha ubutaka bwabo ngo dutere ibiti , tukajya tubaha idolari rimwe kugiti , ku mwaka . """"
Inyamaswa zikomeye muri Pariki y'Akagera ziri kwambikwa ikoranabuhanga ryo koroshya kuzikurikirana ( Amafoto ) .
Mu nkura kandi hari ebyiri zongewe mu mahembe yazo akuma karanga amerekezo yazo kazwi nka GPS transmitters .
Utwuma twa GPS twambitswe inyamaswa tuzajya twifashishisha iminara , maze twohereze mu cyumba kigenzurirwamo amakuru ajyanye n'aho inyamaswa runaka zadushyizwemo ziherereye .
"""" VHF transmitters """" nazo zishobora gufasha umuntu igihe arimo gushakisha izo nyamaswa , akabasha kubona aho ziri .
Umwe mu bagize uruhare mu gushyira utu twuma mu nyamaswa , Richard Harvey , hamwe n'itsinda bakoranaga , babanzaga guzisinziriza inyamaswa kugira ngo bazambike inigi cyangwa utwuma twohereza amakuru , nk'utwo bashyize mu mahembe y'inkura .
Kwambika inyamaswa iri koranabuhanga kandi bituma abazikurikirana babasha kumenya uko zifashe mu mibereho yazo , uko zikora ingendo zimuka ziva ahantu hamwe zijya ahandi , kimwe no kuzibungabunga mu bijyanye n'umutekano wazo .
Mu Ugushyingo 2020 mu Rwanda hateganyijwe kugwa imvura nyinshi .
Icyo kigo cyagaragaje ko hazagwa imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 100 na milimetero 300 .
Kugira ngo byumvikane ubukana bwayo , ni uko imvura imaze iminsi mike igwa hirya no hino mu gihugu , yari milimetero ziri hagati ya 60 na milimetero 150 , iteganyijwe izaba ikubye kabiri .
Ubwiyongere bw'iyi mvura buzaterwa ahanini n'ubuhehere bw'umwuka n'isangano ry'imiyaga byiganje mu karere u Rwanda ruherereyemo .
Umuyobozi w'ishami ry'iteganyagihe muri Meteo Rwanda , Mathieu Mbati Mugunga , yavuze ko iyo mvura nta mpungenge nyinshi iteye , gusa aburira abantu kwitwararika cyane cyane abatuye mu bice bibamo ubutaka bworoshye .
Mu itangazo ryashyizwe hanze na Meteo Rwanda , rivuga ko imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 100 na 130 iteganyijwe mu majyaruguru y'Intara y'Iburasirazuba mu gice cy'Iburasirazuba bw'Akarere ka Nyagatare , Gatsibo ndetse n'aka Kayonza .
Ikaba kandi iteganyijwe mu Burengerazuba bw'Akarere ka Gatsibo , mu Majyepfo y'Akarere ka Gicumbi , mu gice kinini cy'Akarere ka Huye ndetse n'aka Gisagara .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 130 na 160 iteganyijwe mu Mujyi wa Kigali , ahandi hasigaye mu Karere ka Gatsibo , igice kinini cy'Uburasirazuba bwa Kayonza ndetse na Kirehe , uburengerazuba bwa Rwamagana na Nyagatare , agace gato ka Ngoma gahana imbibi na Bugesera , uburasirazuba bwa Nyamagabe , Nyaruguru na Gisagara ndetse ikaba iteganyijwe mu Karere
kose ka Nyanza .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 160 na 190 iteganyijwe mu bice byinshi by'Uturere twa Kirehe , Ngoma , Bugesera , Ruhango , Ngororero , Rubavu na Gakenke .
Iteganyijwe kandi mu majyaruguru y'Uturere twa Rulindo , Gicumbi na Nyamagabe ndetse no mu gice cyo hagati cy'Akarere ka Kamonyi , mu Burengerazuba bwa Rusizi na Nyagatare .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 190 na 210 iteganyijwe mu Majyepfo y'Uturere twa Kirehe , Ngororero na Muhanga , mu Burengerazuba bwa Kamonyi , mu Burasirazuba bwa Karongi ndetse no Majyaruguru ya Rutsiro na Gakenke .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 210 na 240 iteganyijwe mu Majyepfo y'Uturere twa Musanze , Burera na Rutsiro , agace ko hagati ka Rusizi ndetse n'igice kinini cy'Akarere ka Karongi n'igice cy'ishyamba rya Nyungwe mu turere twa Nyamagabe na Nyaruguru .
Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura yashyizwe mu byanya kimeza byemewe na UNESCO .
Iki cyanya cya Gishwati - Mukura cyatangarijwe rimwe n'ibindi byanya 23 .
Iki cyanya kigiye muri urwo rutonde gisangamo icyanya cy'ibirunga giherereye mu majyaruguru ashyira uburengerazuba bw'u Rwanda , cyo cyashyizwemo mu 1983 .
Ibi byanya kimeza bibungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima bigamije gufasha abantu kurushaho gusobanukirwa no gukurikiranira hafi isano y'ibikorwa bya muntu n'ibidukikije hagamijwe gukomeza kurinda urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima n'ibidukikije .
Ibyo byanya kandi bifasha mu bushakashatsi , gushakira ibisubizo ibibazo bijyanye n'ibidukikije byugarije Isi , ari nako byifashishwa mu kubibungabunga no guhanga udushya .
Kuba icyanya cya Gishwati - Mukura gishyizwe muri uru rutonde , bizafasha u Rwanda gukomeza kumenya neza ingaruka z'ibikorwa bya muntu ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima biboneka muri iryo shyamba , ingaruka bigira ku baturiye iryo shyamba no ku bidukikije muri rusange ndetse no ku mihindagurukire y'ibihe nk'ikibazo gihangayikishije isi muri iki
gihe .
Umuyobozi w'Ishami ry'Ubukerarugendo mu rwego rw'Igihugu rw'Iterambere ( RDB ) , Belise Kariza , yatangaje ko kuba pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura igiye mu byanya byemewe na UNESCO , ari umusaruro w'imbaraga zashyizwe mu kugarura iryo shyamba ryari ritangiye gucika .
Yagize ati """" Icyanya cya Gishwati - Mukura ni ahantu heza kandi hakungahaye ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
U Rwanda rumaze igihe rushaka uburyo rwaribungabunga , hashyirwa imbaraga mu bikorwa karemano no kongera kuhagarura ishyamba .
Ndashimira imbaraga zatanzwe n'abafatanyabikorwa bose bakoze batizigama akaba ariyo ntandaro y'umusaruro twishimira uyu munsi . """"
Kariza yavuze ko kubungabunga ibidukikije atari inyungu gusa ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima n'umurage ku bazaza , ahubwo ari n'uburyo bwo guteza imbere ubukungu bw'igihugu .
Muri Gashyantare 2016 nibwo ishyamba cyimeza rya Gishwati - Mukura riherereye mu ruhererekane rw'Imisozi y'isunzu rya Congo - Nil , ryemejwe nka Pariki y'Igihugu ya kane , yitezweho gutanga umusanzu mu kwinjiza amadevize binyuze mu bukerarugendo n'izindi nyungu zituruka ku bidukikije .
Iyo pariki iherereye mu Turere twa Rutsiro na Ngororero mu Ntara y'i Burengerazuba bw'igihugu , ingana na hegitari 3 558 , harimo icyanya cya Gishwati gifite ubuso bungana na Hegitari 1 570 , n'icya Mukura kingana na Hegitari 1 988 .
Ayo mashyamba azwimo ibimera gakondo n'ubwoko bw'inyamaswa zinyuranye ziganjemo inkende n'impundu ( chimpanzee ) n'inkima ( golden monkey ) , inyoni n'izindi nyamaswa nto zinyuranye .
Ni pariki yabashije kubaho kubera uruhare rwa leta n'abaturage , kuko nyuma ya Jenoside yakorewe Abatutsi iyi pariki yari yakendereye , ituzwamo abaturage ndetse ibindi bikorwa byabo birushaho kuyangiza .
Mu mwaka wa 2009 yatangiye kubungabungwa no gusubiranywa , ngo yongere ibe igicumbi cy'urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Muri Mata 2019 , Ikigo cy'Igihugu cy'Iterambere , RDB , cyagiranye amasezerano y'imyaka 25 n'ikigo Imizi Eco - Tourism Development Ltd , yo gutunganya no gucunga Pariki y'Igihugu ya Gishwati - Mukura , ku buryo ihinduka igice gikorerwamo ubukerarugendo mu gihugu .
Imihindagurikire y'ibihe ishobora kuvana mu byabo abantu miliyari 1 . 2 mu myaka 30 iri imbere .
Muri iyi raporo yasohotse ku wa Gatatu , igaragaza ko nta gihugu na kimwe kizabasha gucika ingaruka z'imihindagurikire y'ibihe mu myaka 30 iri imbere , ariko ko by'umwihariko ibihugu bikennye n'abaturage batishoboye ari bo bahazaharira cyane .
Bavuga ko impamvu ari uko ibihugu bikennye iyo bihuye n'ibibazo bikomoka ku mihindagurikire y'ibihe bikunze kubura amikoro , bigatuma abaturage bigaragambya , byakubitiraho uburyo bw'imiyoborere budahamye n'igabanuka rikomeye ry'ubukungu bikaba bibi kurushaho .
Bashingiye ku mibare n'ubushakashatsi bwagiye bukorwa n'imiryango mpuzamahanga , abakoze iyi raporo bagaragaza ko bashingiye cyane ku mibare y'ubwiyongere bw'abaturage , kugeza amazi meza ku baturage , amapfa , imyuzure , inkubi z'imiyaga n'ubwiyongere bw'ubushyuhe ku Isi .
Baje gusanga ko abasaga miliyari batuye mu bihugu 31 ku Isi bifite ubushobozi buke bwo guhangana n'ibyo biza igihe byaba bije .
Afurika yo Munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara niyo yugarijwe cyane , hagakurikiraho Amajyepfo ya Aziya , mu Burasirazuba bwo Hagati no muri Afurika y'Amajyaruguru .
Raporo ivuga ko mu gihe kimwe muri ibyo biza cyaba kigeze kuri ibyo bihugu , benshi mu babituye bazava mu byabo .
Ibihugu bifite amikoro ahagije muri Amerika y'Amajyaruguru n'i Burayi nibyo bavuga ko bizabasha guhangana n'ibyo biza , ahubwo bikazagorwa no kwakira abimukira benshi baturutse muri bya bihugu bizaba byazahajwe n'ibiza .
Ubwiyongere bw'abaturage byitezwe ko buzagira uruhare runini mu guteza ibyo bibazo by'ibiza , dore ko mu 2050 abatuye Isi bazaba ari miliyari icumi bavuye kuri miliyari 7 . 8 bariho uyu munsi .
Abaturage benshi muri aba bazaba baturuka mu bihugu bikirimo imvururu n'intambara nko muri Afurika yo Munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara .
Raporo ivuga kandi ko nibura abantu miliyari 3 . 5 ku Isi bazaba bugarijwe n'inzara .
Icyo gihe kandi abantu badafite amazi meza baziyongera , dore ko n'ubusanzwe kuri ubu bagera kuri miliyari 2 . 6 ku Isi .
Imihindagurikire y'ibihe ishobora kuvana mu byabo abantu miliyari 1 . 2 mu myaka 30 iri imbere .
Muri iyi raporo yasohotse ku wa Gatatu , igaragaza ko nta gihugu na kimwe kizabasha gucika ingaruka z'imihindagurikire y'ibihe mu myaka 30 iri imbere , ariko ko by'umwihariko ibihugu bikennye n'abaturage batishoboye ari bo bahazaharira cyane .
Bavuga ko impamvu ari uko ibihugu bikennye iyo bihuye n'ibibazo bikomoka ku mihindagurikire y'ibihe bikunze kubura amikoro , bigatuma abaturage bigaragambya , byakubitiraho uburyo bw'imiyoborere budahamye n'igabanuka rikomeye ry'ubukungu bikaba bibi kurushaho .
Bashingiye ku mibare n'ubushakashatsi bwagiye bukorwa n'imiryango mpuzamahanga , abakoze iyi raporo bagaragaza ko bashingiye cyane ku mibare y'ubwiyongere bw'abaturage , kugeza amazi meza ku baturage , amapfa , imyuzure , inkubi z'imiyaga n'ubwiyongere bw'ubushyuhe ku Isi .
Baje gusanga ko abasaga miliyari batuye mu bihugu 31 ku Isi bifite ubushobozi buke bwo guhangana n'ibyo biza igihe byaba bije .
Afurika yo Munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara niyo yugarijwe cyane , hagakurikiraho Amajyepfo ya Aziya , mu Burasirazuba bwo Hagati no muri Afurika y'Amajyaruguru .
Raporo ivuga ko mu gihe kimwe muri ibyo biza cyaba kigeze kuri ibyo bihugu , benshi mu babituye bazava mu byabo .
Ibihugu bifite amikoro ahagije muri Amerika y'Amajyaruguru n'i Burayi nibyo bavuga ko bizabasha guhangana n'ibyo biza , ahubwo bikazagorwa no kwakira abimukira benshi baturutse muri bya bihugu bizaba byazahajwe n'ibiza .
Ubwiyongere bw'abaturage byitezwe ko buzagira uruhare runini mu guteza ibyo bibazo by'ibiza , dore ko mu 2050 abatuye Isi bazaba ari miliyari icumi bavuye kuri miliyari 7 . 8 bariho uyu munsi .
Abaturage benshi muri aba bazaba baturuka mu bihugu bikirimo imvururu n'intambara nko muri Afurika yo Munsi y'Ubutayu bwa Sahara .

Icyo gihe kandi abantu badafite amazi meza baziyongera , dore ko n'ubusanzwe kuri ubu bagera kuri miliyari 2 . 6 ku Isi .
Rusizi : Amazi y'amashyuza aherutse gukama ashobora kugaruka aho yahoze .
Ku wa Mbere w'iki cyumweru , amazi y'amashyuza yarakamye yimukira hafi y'uruganda rwa Cimerwa rukora sima , akajya atemba ajya mu Mugezi wa Rubyiro .
Aya mayobera yateye akababaro abaturage bahakuraga amaramuko binyuze mu gukanda abagiye kuhivuriza amavunane .
Impuguke mu bijyanye n'Ubumenyi bw'Isi , Dr Emmanuel Havugimana , yabwiye IGIHE ko ubushakashatsi bukiri gukorwa ariko we asanga gutemba kw'amashyuza byaba byaraturutse ku mitingito yabaye muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo n'u Burundi .
Itsinda ry'abakozi bo mu Kigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe Mine , Gaz na Peteroli kuri uyu wa 27 Kanama 2020 , ryagiye kureba ibivugwa n'abantu batandukanye ndetse naryo rikora ubushakashatsi ku byabaye .
Ngaruye Jean Claude ushinzwe Ubushakashatsi bw'Amabuye y'agaciro muri icyo kigo , yavuze ko iby'imitingito ntaho bihuriye nabyo kuko iyo biba n'isoko iba yarabuze .
Ati """" Nasanze iby'imitingito nta ruhare rurimo kuko iyaba birimo isoko ntituba twayisanzemo , tuba twarasanze yararigise kandi irahari .
Kubera imiterere yayo yashwanyaguje urutare iruhindura ibumba rugabanya imbaraga rwari rusanzwe rufite , byagura inzira y'amazi maze amanuka ajya mu mugezi . """"
Aya amazi ari kumanuka aca aho Cimerwa iri gucukura amabuye .
Ni imbogamizi cyane ku mikorere yayo ku buryo babagiriye inama yo gushaka uburyo ayo mazi yasubira aho yahoze .
Ngaruye Jean Claude yagize ati """" Kuko amazi agihari twabagiriye inama ko bashaka inzobere bakabanza bagatiyura isayo ririmo kuko ryanatezaga impanuka , bahagirira isuku bagacukura bakagera ku rutare rukomeye ubundi bakazamura inkuta , ariya mazi bayahamisha hariya bakajya bayaruhukiraro nkuko byari bisanzwe ndetse ntanagire ingaruka ku bantu . """"
Aya mazi yari asanzwe amanuka ashyushye yagera ahantu akaguma hamwe abantu bakabasha kuyoga no kuyikandisha kuko ngo yabavuraga amavunane .
Mbere y'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , wasangaga abantu ari benshi baje kuyivurizamo harimo n'abaturutse mu Burundi no muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Byagenze gute ngo amazi y'amashyuza i Rusizi yimukire ahandi ?
Aya mazi yari asanzwe amanuka ashyushye yagera ahantu akaguma hamwe abantu bakabasha kuyoga no kuyikandisha kuko ngo yabavuraga amavunane .
Mbere y'icyorezo cya COVID - 19 , wasangaga abantu ari benshi baje kuyivurizamo harimo n'abaturutse mu Burundi no muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo .
Bamwe mu bahaturiye babwiye IGIHE ko babibonye batyo bagasanga hari kugaragagara amabuye gusa amazi akaba yamanutse akagenda ari menshi , bakaba bumva bahombye kuko hari bamwe bahakuraga amaramuko bakora akazi ko gukanda abantu bahaje .
Uwitwa Nikobatuye Octave ati """" Natwe twabibonye gutya ariko turacyeka ko ari urutambi rwaturikijwe rwatumye amanuka ari menshi yagiye hepfo y'aho yari asanzwe . """"
Minani Japheth yunzemo ati """" Nibyo koko yagiye ariko ni agahinda , uzi ukuntu twabonaga amafaranga yo gukanda abantu no kubafasha koga , niho nakuraga agasabune n'akunyu . """"
Umuyobozi w'Akarere ka Rusizi , Kayumba Euphrem , yabwiye IGIHE ko boherejeyo itsinda ririmo abakurikirana hafi ibijyanye n'ibiza , ibidukikije n'abashinzwe ibya mine kugira ngo harebwe icyabiteye n'icyo bakora .
Ati """" Twoherejeyo itsinda ntabwo riraduha raporo , uretse ariya mafoto ameze kuriya ntacyo twarenzaho .
Itsinda ry'abakozi rirajya kureba ubundi baduhe amakuru .
Twoherejeyo abakora mu bigo nka za REMA , abashinzwe ibya Mine , ntabwo nakubwira ngo tuzayagarura . """"
Dr Emmanuel Havugimana , Impuguke mu bijyanye n'Ubumenyi bw'Isi , avuga ko ubushakashatsi bukiri gukorwa ariko we asanga byaba byaraturutse ku mitingito yabaye muri Repubulika Iharanira Demokarasi ya Congo n'u Burundi .
Ati """" Ubushakashatsi buracyakorwa ariko ndabona icyo navuga ari imitingito yabaye ku tariki ya 14 na 16 z'ukwa karindwi n'undi mutingito wabaye ejo saa munani mu kiyaga cya Tanganyika , ibyo byose iyo bibaye bigatuma ibintu by'amabuye yo mu kuzimu binyeganyega cyane , ntabwo bitangaje ko ahantu nka hariya hari amashyuza ,
amazi yahita agenda . """"
"""" Njyewe ni byo nashyize imbere abandi bavugaga ibikorwa by'amabuye acukurwa hariya ariko numvise igifite imbaraga gikomeye cyane ari iyo mitingito itatu yabaye mu buryo bukurikirana , ishobora kuba yahungabanyije amabuye yo mu kuzimu amazi akabona ahantu arigitira akagenda . """"
Dr Havugimana akomeza agira ati """" Niba umaze kuhagera amabuye yaho asa umukara nk'ariya yo mu majyaruguru , biragaragara ko ari ahantu habaye iruka ry'ibirunga cyera cyane mbere ya biriya birunga byo mu Majyaruguru . """"
"""" Ubwo rero urumva ko habaye umutingito mu Kivu wabereye kuri kilometero 13 uvuye hejuru y'ubutaka , Epicentre ( izingiro ry'iruka ry'ikirunga ) ikaba iri i Karehe , hakurya ya Kivu muri Congo , nibyo mbona njye byabiteye , nta kintu kidasanzwe cyabaye . """"
Dr Havugimana avuga ko ahavuye amashyuza hazamera ibyatsi bikarangira , abazabaho mu myaka ijana iri mbere bazajya babyumva nk'amateka ko habaga amazi .
Gusa ngo ntiyakwemeza ko amazi azagaruka .
Abatuye Isi bamaze gukoresha umutungo kamere wose wari ugenewe umwaka wa 2020 .
Umunsi aho abatuye Isi bose baba bamaze gukoresha umutungo kamere Isi iba ifite ubushobozi bwo gutanga muri uwo mwaka , uzwi nka """" Earth Overshoot Day , """" muri uyu mwaka wari ku wa 22 Kanama .
Mu busanzwe ibyo ikiremwa muntu cyangiza ku Isi , nk'imyuka yangiza cyohereza mu kirere , umubumbe uba ufite ubushobozi bwo kuzongera ukabisubiranya mu gihe runaka , gusa umunsi wa """" EarthOvershoot Day """" uvuze ko abantu baba bamaze gukoresha ibyari byarabagenewe byose muri uwo mwaka ndetse Isi ikaba idafite
ubushobozi bwo kubisubiranya muri uwo mwaka .
Ibijyanye n'uko abatuye Isi bamaze gukoresha umutungo kamere w'umwaka wose , kuri uyu wa Gatandatu byatangajwe n'ikigo cyo muri Amerika cyagiye gikunda kugaragaza ikibazo cy'uko abantu bagenda biyongera mu gihe Isi yo itiyongera , kizwi nka """" American NGO Global Footprint Network . """"
Kibinyujije kuri Twitter cyagize kiti """" Uyu munsi ni italiki aho twese nk'ibiremwa muntu twakoresheje byinshi biturutse mu mutungo kamere kurusha ibyo umubumbe ushobora kugaruza mu mwaka wose . """"
Mu yindi minsi aho abatuye Isi bagiye bakoresha umutungo kamere urenze uwo Isi ishobora gusubiranya mu mwaka , harimo ku wa 29 Ukuboza 1970 , ku wa 11 Ukwakira 1990 , ku wa 23 Nzeri 2000 ndetse uwaherukaga wari ku wa 29 Nyakanga 2019 .
Abahanga mu by'ibidukikije bavuga ko muri uyu mwaka , uyu munsi watinze kugera ugereranyije n'umwaka ushize kubera ko icyorezo cya Covid - 19 cyahagaritse bimwe mu bikorwa by'abantu , bityo nabo ntibakoresha umutungo kamere mwinshi .
Mu byumweru bibiri hazagwa imvura nke cyane mu duce tumwe tw'igihugu .
Meteo Rwanda yatangaje ko mu gice cya gatatu cy'ukwezi kwa Kanama 2020 hagati y'itariki ya 21 n'iya 31 ; mu Rwanda hateganyijwe kugwa imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 0 na milimetero 15 .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 10 na 15 iteganyijwe mu karere ka Musanze , agace gato ka Burera gahana imbibi na Musanze , mu karere ka Nyabihu mu bice bihana imbibi n'uturere twa Musanze , Gakenke na Ngororero .
Iteganyijwe kandi mu gice kinini cy'akarere ka Ngororero gihana imbibi na Musanze , mu karere ka Muhanga ahegereye Ngororero na Nyabihu , agace gato ka Gakenke kegereye Nyabihu , ndetse n'agace ka Nyamagabe kegereye Nyamasheke .
Imvura iri hagati ya milimetero 1 n'eshanu iteganyijwe mu turere twa Nyagatare na Gatsibo , mu bice by'Intara y'Amajyepfo , mu majyaruguru mu turere twa Rulindo na Gicumbi .
Imvura kandi izagwa muri Gasabo mu duce twegereye Rulindo no mu karere ka Nyarugenge mu duce twegereye Kamonyi .
Imvura iri hagati ya 0 na 1 iteganyijwe mu tundi turere tw'intara y'Iburasirazuba no mu mujyi wa Kigali .
Meteo Rwanda yatangaje ko imvura izagwa muri ibi bihe ingana n'isanzwe iboneka muri ibyo bihe .
Icyo kigo cyatangaje ko biragaragaza ko imvura iteganyijwe muri rusange ari nkeya cyane .
Gukunda ibyo yize muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda byamuhesheje kujya kubitangamo umusanzu muri Centrafrique .
Tumwesigye yarangije Kaminuza mu 2014 , ntabwo yahise abona akazi gahoraho , gusa yakundaga gukora imirimo itandukanye yerekeye kubungabunga ibidukikije no kwita ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima nk'uko yabyize .
Mu 2018 Ikigo cy'igihugu cy'Iterambere ( RDB ) cyaje kumuha amezi atandatu yo kwimenyereza umwuga , bimwongerera ubumenyi .
Muri uko kwimenyereza , yahabwaga ibihumbi 50 Frw buri kwezi yo kwifashisha .
Yatangiye kujya akuraho make akayizigamira kugira ngo azayakoreshe yihangira umurimo mu byo yize .
Amezi atandatu arangiye yaje kongererwa igihe bituma arushaho kwizigamira no kugira ubumenyi .
Ati """" Nagiye mbikaho make kugira ngo nzatangire gushyira mu bikorwa ibyo nize nihangira umurimo kubera ko ntatekerezaga guhita mbona akazi . """"
Nyuma y'iryo menyerezamwuga yaje kwihuza n'urundi rubyiruko bose hamwe bagera kuri 12 bashinga umuryango utegamiye kuri leta ugamije kwita ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima no kurengera ibidukikije witwa SAEB ( Social Actions for Environment protection and Biodiversity conservation ) .
Batangiye gufatanya n'abaturage n'urubyiruko gutera ibiti by'imbuto ziribwa n'amashyamba no gushyira ubusitani mu bigo by'amashuri .
Ati """" Intego kwari ugufasha urubyiruko n'abaturage guhanga imirimo ibyara inyungu ariko igamije kurengera ibidukikije .
Bivuze ko iyo bafite ibikorwa bibazanira amafaranga bikabatunga , ntabwo bajya kwangiza amashyamba cyangwa ngo bajye mu buhigi . """"
Abarenga 2000 bateye ibiti by'imbuto bigishwa gukora imirima y'igikoni
Tumwesigye yavuze ko yatangiranye n'urubyiruko rwo mu mashuri hirya no hino mu gihugu , aruhugurira kubaka imirima y'igikoni no gutera ibiti by'imbuto mu bigo byabo bikarangira bagiye no kubikora mu ngo zabo .
Uretse kurwanya imirire mibi , ibyo biti by'imbuto byinjirizaga amafaranga urubyiruko n'abandi baturage babikora .
Ni mu gihe kandi biri mu murongo wa Guverinoma wo kugira umurima w'igikoni n'ibiti by'imbuto nibura bitatu kuri buri muryango .
Ati """" Niba abana bateye ibinyomoro , avoka , indimu cyangwa imyembe , ni ibintu bishobora kubazanira amafaranga bakaba bakwigurira n'ibikoresho by'ishuri cyangwa ibindi . """"
Yavuze ko abanyeshuri barenga 2000 bahuguwe kandi bagatera ibiti by'imbuto bitandukanye birimo ; ibinyomoro , imyembe , orange n'ibindi bishobora kubunganira mu mirire kandi bikabazanira inyungu y'amafaranga .
Muri rusange ngo bateye ibiti by'imbuto birenga 6000 mu ngo zabo no mu bigo by'amashuri mu bice by'icyaro mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Uko yagiye gutanga umusanzu muri Centrafrique
Mu Ukuboza 2018 , Ambasade ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu Rwanda ku bufatanye n'Ikigo cy'Indashyikirwa mu micungire y'ibinyabuzima n'umutungo kamere kibarizwa muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda ( Center of Excellence in Biodiversity conservation and Natural Resources management ) , yazanye urubyiruko 10 rwa Centrafrique kwigira ku Rwanda ibijyanye no kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima no kwita ku
bidukikije .
Abo baje guhuzwa n'abandi banyarwanda 12 barimo Tumwesigye .
Nyuma yo gusoza urugendo rwabo mu Rwanda , baje kumutumira kugira ngo ajye kubunganira mu guhugura abantu bo muri icyo gihugu .
Mu mpera za 2019 yerekeje muri Centrafrique ku nkunga ya Kaminuza y'u Rwanda na Ambasade ya Amerika muri Centrafrique .
Ati """" Kubera ko ari igihugu cyazahajwe n'intambara , kwita ku bidukikije nta mwanya bihabwa cyane .
Nabahuguye kureka guhiga inyamanswa .
Twabubakiye ubuhumbikiro bw'imboga n'iz'ibiti by'imbuto n'ibiti bisanzwe bazajya bifashisha mu gutunganya amakara babikora nk'ubucuruzi . """"
Urubyiruko rwahuguwe muri Centrafrique rwateye ibihumbi 21 by'ibiti by'imbuto ziganjemo avoka , ibinyomoro , amatunda , orange , amapapayi n'ibindi biti bisanzwe byo kubungabunga amashyamba .
Hashinzwe amatsinda ( Clubs ) y'urubyiruko yo kwita ku bidukikije agera kuri arindwi rimwe rigizwe n'abantu 50 hashingwa n'imiryango 11 y'abahoze ari abahigi yiyemeza kurengera ibidukikije .
Umuyobozi w'Ikigo cy'Indashyikirwa mu micungire y'ibinyabuzima n'umutungo kamere kibarizwa muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda , Professor Beth Kaplin , yavuze ko Tumwesigye ari urugero rwiza rwerekana ko urubyiruko rwo mu Rwanda rugeze ahashimishije mu kubungabunga ibidukikije , ibyo bizatuma ruhanga imirimo urundi rukayibona mu miryango yita
ku bidukikije no kurengera urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Kuri ubu Elisa Tumwesigye akomeje ibikorwa byo kwita ku bidukikije no kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima mu Rwanda nyuma yo kuva gutanga umusanzu muri Repubulika ya Centrafrique .
Gukunda ibyo yize muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda byamuhesheje kujya kubitangamo umusanzu muri Centrafrique .
Tumwesigye yarangije Kaminuza mu 2014 , ntabwo yahise abona akazi gahoraho , gusa yakundaga gukora imirimo itandukanye yerekeye kubungabunga ibidukikije no kwita ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima nk'uko yabyize .
Mu 2018 Ikigo cy'igihugu cy'Iterambere ( RDB ) cyaje kumuha amezi atandatu yo kwimenyereza umwuga , bimwongerera ubumenyi .
Muri uko kwimenyereza , yahabwaga ibihumbi 50 Frw buri kwezi yo kwifashisha .

Ati """" Nagiye mbikaho make kugira ngo nzatangire gushyira mu bikorwa ibyo nize nihangira umurimo kubera ko ntatekerezaga guhita mbona akazi . """"

Batangiye gufatanya n'abaturage n'urubyiruko gutera ibiti by'imbuto ziribwa n'amashyamba no gushyira ubusitani mu bigo by'amashuri .
Ati """" Intego kwari ugufasha urubyiruko n'abaturage guhanga imirimo ibyara inyungu ariko igamije kurengera ibidukikije .
Bivuze ko iyo bafite ibikorwa bibazanira amafaranga bikabatunga , ntabwo bajya kwangiza amashyamba cyangwa ngo bajye mu buhigi . """"
Abarenga 2000 bateye ibiti by'imbuto bigishwa gukora imirima y'igikoni
Tumwesigye yavuze ko yatangiranye n'urubyiruko rwo mu mashuri hirya no hino mu gihugu , aruhugurira kubaka imirima y'igikoni no gutera ibiti by'imbuto mu bigo byabo bikarangira bagiye no kubikora mu ngo zabo .

Ni mu gihe kandi biri mu murongo wa Guverinoma wo kugira umurima w'igikoni n'ibiti by'imbuto nibura bitatu kuri buri muryango .
