Yavuze ko abanyeshuri barenga 2000 bahuguwe kandi bagatera ibiti by'imbuto bitandukanye birimo ; ibinyomoro , imyembe , orange n'ibindi bishobora kubunganira mu mirire kandi bikabazanira inyungu y'amafaranga .
Muri rusange ngo bateye ibiti by'imbuto birenga 6000 mu ngo zabo no mu bigo by'amashuri mu bice by'icyaro mu Karere ka Gasabo .
Uko yagiye gutanga umusanzu muri Centrafrique
Mu Ukuboza 2018 , Ambasade ya Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika mu Rwanda ku bufatanye n'Ikigo cy'Indashyikirwa mu micungire y'ibinyabuzima n'umutungo kamere kibarizwa muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda ( Center of Excellence in Biodiversity conservation and Natural Resources management ) , yazanye urubyiruko 10 rwa Centrafrique kwigira ku Rwanda ibijyanye no kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima no kwita ku
bidukikije .
Abo baje guhuzwa n'abandi banyarwanda 12 barimo Tumwesigye .
Nyuma yo gusoza urugendo rwabo mu Rwanda , baje kumutumira kugira ngo ajye kubunganira mu guhugura abantu bo muri icyo gihugu .
Mu mpera za 2019 yerekeje muri Centrafrique ku nkunga ya Kaminuza y'u Rwanda na Ambasade ya Amerika muri Centrafrique .
Ati """" Kubera ko ari igihugu cyazahajwe n'intambara , kwita ku bidukikije nta mwanya bihabwa cyane .
Nabahuguye kureka guhiga inyamanswa .
Twabubakiye ubuhumbikiro bw'imboga n'iz'ibiti by'imbuto n'ibiti bisanzwe bazajya bifashisha mu gutunganya amakara babikora nk'ubucuruzi . """"
Urubyiruko rwahuguwe muri Centrafrique rwateye ibihumbi 21 by'ibiti by'imbuto ziganjemo avoka , ibinyomoro , amatunda , orange , amapapayi n'ibindi biti bisanzwe byo kubungabunga amashyamba .
Hashinzwe amatsinda ( Clubs ) y'urubyiruko yo kwita ku bidukikije agera kuri arindwi rimwe rigizwe n'abantu 50 hashingwa n'imiryango 11 y'abahoze ari abahigi yiyemeza kurengera ibidukikije .
Umuyobozi w'Ikigo cy'Indashyikirwa mu micungire y'ibinyabuzima n'umutungo kamere kibarizwa muri Kaminuza y'u Rwanda , Professor Beth Kaplin , yavuze ko Tumwesigye ari urugero rwiza rwerekana ko urubyiruko rwo mu Rwanda rugeze ahashimishije mu kubungabunga ibidukikije , ibyo bizatuma ruhanga imirimo urundi rukayibona mu miryango yita
ku bidukikije no kurengera urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Kuri ubu Elisa Tumwesigye akomeje ibikorwa byo kwita ku bidukikije no kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima mu Rwanda nyuma yo kuva gutanga umusanzu muri Repubulika ya Centrafrique .
Ubushakashatsi bwagaragaje ingaruka zo gutwara imodoka ibirahuri bimanuye .
Ubu bushakashatsi bwakorewe mu mijyi icumi itandukanye , ari yo Dhaka ( Bangladesh ) , Chennai ( u Buhinde ) , Guangzhou ( u Bushinwa ) , Medellin ( Colombia ) , São Paulo ( Brazil ) , Cairo ( Misiri ) , Sulaymaniyah ( Iraq ) , Addis Ababa ( Ethiopia ) , Blantyre ( Malawi ) , na Dar - es - Salaam ( Tanzania ) .
Ubu bushakashatsi bwakozwe na kaminuza ya Surrey , bugaragaza ko gutwara imodoka umanuye ibirahuri byongera umwuka mubi uhumekwa ku kigero cya 80 % , bikaba byanaba bibi kurushaho mu masaha arimo ingendo nyinshi .
Abashakashatsi bavuga ko abatwara imodoka mu bihugu biri mu nzira y'amajyambere bahura n'iki kibazo kurusha abandi , kuko imihanda yo mu bihugu bikennye iba irimo imodoka nyinshi zishaje , zohereza imyuka mibi myinshi kandi uburyo bwo kwirinda , nko gukoresha imashini zitanga umwuka mu modoka , bukaba buri hacye cyane muri ibyo
bihugu .
Inama zitangwa n'ubu bushakashatsi zirimo kwirinda gukora ingendo mu masaha arimo imodoka nyinshi , cyane aya mu gitondo na nimugoroba .
Harimo kandi gukoresha ubundi buryo bwo kubona umwuka mwiza , nko kugura imodoka zifite imashini zitanga umwuka ndetse zitanasohora imyuka mibi .
Ishami ry'Umuryango w'Abibumbye , rivuga ko ikibazo cy'ubwiyongere bw'imyuka mibi giteye inkeke .
Miliyoni zirindwi z'abatuye Isi zipfa buri mwaka kubera indwara zifitanye isano n'imyuka mibi mu gihe abantu icyenda mu 10 bahumeka umwuka udasukuye ku bipimo byiza .
Ibidasanzwe biri mu gishushanyo mbonera gishya cy'imikoreshereze y'ubutaka .
Ubutaka ni imwe mu ngingo zidakunze kuvugwaho rumwe kuri ubu cyane cyane iyo bigeze ku mikoreshereze yabwo .
Buri muturage yumva umutungo ukomeye akwiriye kugira mu gihugu ari ubutaka , bigatuma benshi babushaka cyangwa babukoresha mu buryo bunyuranyije n'amategeko .
Ikibazo cyari kimaze iminsi kivugwa ni uburyo ubutaka buhingwa bwari bukomeje kubakwaho inzu ku buryo budacunzwe neza , mu minsi iri imbere igihugu cyazasigara ari inzu gusa bigateza ikibazo gikomeye cyo kutihaza mu biribwa .
Igishushanyo mbonera gishya cy'imikoreshereze y'ubutaka cyemejwe n'inama y'abaminisitiri iherutse , cyatanze umucyo ku buryo ubutaka bugomba gukoreshwa mu gihugu , ubirenzeho agahanwa .
Mu bishya birimo ni uko ubuhinzi bwagenewe 47 , 2 % by'ubuso bw'igihugu , amashyamba yahariwe 29 , 3 % , imiturire n'ibikorwaremezo bigenerwa 15 % , mu gihe amazi n'ibishanga bibungabunzwe byagenewe 8 , 5 % by'ubuso bw'igihugu .
Iyemezwa ry'iki gishushanyo mbonera kiruta ibindi bizafungurira amarembo n'ibindi bishushanyo mbonera by'imiturire mu Mujyi wa Kigali n'indi mijyi kugira ngo buri muturage amenye icyagenewe aho ubutaka bwe buherereye .
Ntawe uzongera kubaka inzu ukwe mu murima we
Abanyarwanda kuri ubu bagera kuri miliyoni 12 . 5 , bakaba biyongera ku kigero cya 2 . 4 % .
Bakomeje kwiyongera kuri uwo muvuduko , mu mwaka wa 2050 bazaba bageze kuri miliyoni 25 . 8 % cyangwa miliyoni 22 baramutse biyongereye ku muvuduko wa 2 % .
Mu miturire , igishushanyo kigaragaza ko kuri ubu 18 . 4 % batuye mu mijyi naho 81 . 6 % batuye bacucitse mu byaro .
Muri gahunda ya Guverinoma y'imyaka irindwi , abatuye mu mijyi byitezwe ko bazagera kuri 35 % bitarenze mu 2024 naho mu 2050 bakazaba ari 70 % .
Igishushanyo mbonera kigaragaza imijyi yose ikenewe mu gihugu ndetse na site zo guturaho mu cyaro .
Mu guteza imbere iyo gahunda , hateganyijwe ko umurwa mukuru uzakomeza kuba Kigali , habeho indi mijyi itatu iwukikije ( Satellite cities ) , indi mijyi y'uturere 16 n'udusantere 73 dukomeye two mu byaro .
Imijyi igwa mu ntege Kigali yateganyijwe ni Bugesera , Rwamagana na Muhanga kugira ngo ifashe Kigali kwakira abantu n'ibikorwa bimwe na bimwe byatumaga benshi baza gushakira ubuzima muri Kigali ariko imbaraga zigashyirwa mu kuyirinda ko ikomeza gukura mu kajagari .
Imijyi izakomeza kuba iyunganira Kigali iherereye hafi y'imipaka ni Musanze , Rubavu , Rusizi , Nyagatare , na Huye aho umwe ubarirwa kuzajya uba utuwe n'abaturage bari hagati ya 300 , 000 na 650 , 000 .
Iyo mijyi izakomeza kunganirwa na Karongi , Kayonza na Kirehe yo izaba ituwe n'abaturage bari hagati ya 150 , 000 na 300 , 000 .
Mu dusantere dukomeye twateganyijwe 73 , buri kamwe kazajya kaba gafite abaturage 24 , 500 .
Byagaragaye ku mu Rwanda ubu hari inzu zo guturamo miliyoni 2 . 8 , mu gihe hakenewe inzu miliyoni 5 . 5 zizahaza miliyoni zisaga 22 zizaba zituye igihugu mu 2050 .
Ibyo bituma hakenewe kubakwa inzu 150 000 buri mwaka kugira ngo habe icyizere cy'uko abanyarwanda bose bizagera mu 2050 nta kibazo cy'aho kuba bafite .
Nubwo hari icyo kibazo cy'ubuke bw'inzu , igishushanyo mbonera gisaba ko uburyo bwo kubaka bwitonderwa , inzu zikubakwa bazamuka bajya hejuru , munsi y'ubutaka hagakoreshwa hubakwa parikingi n'ibindi .
Nubwo hagikenewe inzu nyinshi , igishushanyo mbonera gisaba ko uburyo bwo kubaka bwitonderwa cyane kugira ngo abantu batototera n'ubutaka buhingwaho .
Imyubakire mu cyaro , abasaga miliyoni 6 . 6 ni ukuvuga 30 % by'abazaba batuye u Rwanda mu 2050 bazaba batuye mu midugudu 3000 .
Nibura buri kagali kazajya kaba gafite site imwe cyangwa ebyiri zo gutuzamo abaturage bako abe ari naho hashyirwa ibikorwa remezo nk'amazi , amashanyarazi , amashuri , amavuriro n'ibindi .
Kubera ko akagali kazaba gafite ahantu hamwe cyangwa habiri hatuwe , ibyo biraca amarenga ko imidugudu isanzwe nk'inzego z'ubutegetsi izavaho ahubwo hagashyirwaho inzego nshya zishingiye ku miturire mishya .
Mu kubaka inzu mu cyaro ahagenewe imidugudu , hazakoreshwa uburyo bwo kubaka inzu enye muri imwe n'umunani muri imwe , cyangwa ubundi buryo butuza abaturage benshi ahantu hato .
Umusaruro w'ubuhinzi uzongerwa
Mu gushaka uko ubutaka buhingwa bwongerwa kugira ngo abazaba batuye igihugu mu 2050 bazabone ibibatunga bihagije , ubutaka buhingwa bwavanywe kuri 41 . 5 % by'ubuso bw'igihugu , bugirwa 47 , 2 % .
Nubwo bimeze gutyo , ukurikije umusaruro uboneka ku buso buhingwa kuri ubu bikomeje bityo ntabwo uwo musaruro wazabasha guhaza miliyoni 22 bazaba batuye igihugu mu 2050 .
Ubuhinzi bukomeje gutanga umusaruro butanga kuri ubu , kugira ngo haboneke ibizahaza abazaba batuye u Rwanda icyo gihe hasaba ubutaka bungana na kilometero kare 103 , 000 , ni ukuvuga ubuso bwikubye inshuro enye ubw'igihugu gifite .
Mu gihe haba hakoreshejwe ikoranabuhanga mu buhinzi no kongera umusaruro , haba hakenewe ubuso bungana na kilometero kare 14 , 500 km² bwo guhingaho ibizahaza abaturage .
Mu nama igishushanyo cyatanze , ni ugukomeza kurinda ubutaka buhingwa kuri ubu bungana na kilometero kare 12 , 433 kugira ngo budakoreshwa nabi cyangwa mu bindi .
Inzira za Gari ya Moshi zihuta
Mu bijyanye no gutwara abantu n'ibintu , kuri ubu mu Rwanda hari imihanda ingana na kilometero 37 896 .
Imihanda ya kaburimbo izongerwa cyane , hazubakwa inzira za gari ya moshi zihuza u Rwanda n'ibihugu bituranye ndetse n'imihanda yihuta ihuza imijyi minini .
Ku bijyanye n'ibidukikije igishushanyo mbonera gisaba ko ubuso bwa kilometero kare 1389 buteweho amashyamba ya kimeza bukomeza kubungabungwa , no kurinda amashyamba yandi ari mu gihugu angana na kilometero kare 3 , 873 km² .
Gutera amashyamba mashya bizibanda ku misozi ihanamye , mu gihe gutera amashyamba ahagenewe ubuhinzi bitemewe keretse bikozwe haterwa ibiti bivangwa n'imyaka .
Igishushanyo mbonera gisaba ko gucukura amabuye y'agaciro bikorwa habanje kurebwa niba byunguka kurusha ibigiye kuvanwaho .
Minisiteri y'ibidukikije igaragaza ko hagiye gushyirwaho uburyo bw'ikoranabuhanga buzafasha mu ikurikiranwa ry'imikoreshereze y'ubutaka ku buryo unyuranyije nabyo babibona kare bitabaye ngombwa ko bifata igihe .
Hari gutegurwa amategeko azahana abazanyuranya nabyo .
Ibisubizo by'ibibazo byibazwa ku iruka rya Nyiragongo
Ku wa 22 Gicurasi 2021 cyongeye kuruka nyuma y'aho cyaherukaga kuruka mu 2002 .
Ubu habarurwa abantu barenga 30 bapfuye kubera iruka ryacyo , ibikorwa remezo bigasenyuka ndetse abaturage bagakwira imishwaro bahunga .
Iruka ryacyo rimaze iminsi ritera imitingito mu bice hafi ya byose by'u Rwanda ku buryo nk'Akarere ka Rubavu kari mu icuraburindi .
Hari bimwe mu bibazo abantu bakomeje kwibaza ku iruka ryacyo n'ingaruka zabyo .
Ni byo tugiye kugarukaho nyuma y'uko bisubijwe n'ishami ribishinzwe mu Kigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe Peteroli , Gazi na Mine , RMB .
1 . Ko twumva imitingito yaba ari ikimenyetso ko ikirunga kizongera kuruka ?
Oya !
Imitingito nk'iyi iterwa no gutogota kw'amazuku ( magma ) mu nda y'ikirunga .
Umwuka ushyushye mu nda y'isi uba mwinshi , urutare ruhazengurutse rugasa n'uruturika bigatuma humvikana imitingito mito mito y'uruhererekane .
Ibipimo by'umwuka wo hejuru ya Nyiragongo byafashwe bigaragaza ko nta myuka ituruka mu mazuku ihari .
Ibi bivuze ko nta mazuku ari hafi ku buryo ikirunga cyakongera kuruka .
2 . Iyi mitingito izahagarara ryari ?
Ntawapfa kuvuga itariki cyangwa isaha imitingito izahagarariraho kuko nta gipimo kiyipima kugeza uyu munsi .
Ariko umuntu arebeye uko byagiye bigenda ( amateka y'iruka rya buri kirunga ) mu myaka yashize ntabwo imitingito ikurikira iruka ry'ikirunga irenza ibyumweru bibiri .
Ubwo Nyiragongo iheruka kuruka mu 2002 imitingito yamaze iminsi 10 .
3 . Iruka ry'ikirunga ryatewe n'iki ?
Iruka ry'ibirunga rigaragarira mu ivuburwa ry'urusukume rw'ibikoma bishyushye cyane binyura ahagaragaza imbaraga nke mu gishishwa cy'Isi .
Ikirunga kiruka kuko hari urutare mu nda y'Isi ruba rwashonze kubera ubushyuhe buri hagati ya dogere 700 na dogere 1200 .
Ibi bikajyana n'umwuka mwinshi ushyushye noneho ugatera ibikoma byashonze kuzamuka bikanyura mu myenge bikazamuka hejuru mu buryo bwo guturika bishaka aho binyura bitewe na wa mwuka mwinshi ushyushye urimo .
4 . Imitingito yatewe n'iki ?
Imitingito nk'iyi iterwa no gutogota kw'amazuku ( magma ) ari mu nda y'Isi no gukubana hagati y'ibisate mu bice byiyashije .
Umwuka n'igikoma bishyushye mu nda y'isi biba byinshi urutare ruhazengurutse rugasa n'uruturika bigatuma humvikana imitingito mito mito y'uruhererekane .
5 . Kuki imitingito ituruka i Rubavu gusa ?
Imitingito yose mwumvise nyuma y'iruka rya Nyiragongo yabaga iturutse mu izingiro ryayo ( epicenter ) i Rubavu .
Iyi mitingito yashoboraga no kumvikana ahandi bitewe n'uburemere bwayo kandi yanagendaga icika intege uko yagendaga ijya kure y'iryo zingiro ryayo .
Urugero ni uko iyo uteye ibuye cyangwa ikindi kintu mu mazi hari imirongo y'uruziga igenda inyuranamo yerekana ko hari ikintu kidasanzwe cyajugunywe muri ayo mazi ( waves ) .
Ku bayumviraga ahandi si ukuvuga ko aho bari naho habaga hari indi mitingito .
6 . Ni ukuri ko ikirunga kirutse bikagera mu Kivu byateza ibibazo ?
Ntabwo byapfa gushoboka !
Urugero ni uko mu 2002 ubwo Nyiragongo yarukagaga , amahindure ari ku muvuduko wa 100km ku isaha , ibyageze mu kiyaga cya Kivu byamanutse kugera muri metero 140 z'ubujyakuzimu kandi gas methane iba muri metero hafi 200 .
Nyuma y'iruka rya Nyiragongo uyu mwaka leta yafashe ingamba zo gukorana n'abaturanyi bya hafi mu kugenzura biriya birunga byegereye u Rwanda ku buryo n'igihe byaruka byaba bizwi hagashyirwaho ingamba z'ubwirinzi .
7 . Muri Congo ko ubuyobozi bwaburiye abaturage guhunga , natwe duhunge ?
Oya , ibipimo bigaragazwa n'impuguke za RMB bigaragaza ko nta kibazo gihari ku ruhande rw'u Rwanda .
Ikibazo cyabaye ni imitingito gusa kandi nayo ibipimo bigaragaza ko yagiye igabanuka mu ngano no mu bukana ku buryo nta mpungenge biteye .
Gusa birasaba gukora gahunda y'igihe kirekire ifasha abaturage gukomeza kubana n'iruka ry'ibirunga ndetse n'imitingito kuko kugeza uyu munsi bikiriho muri aka gace duherereyemo .
Minisiteri y'Ibidukikije yatanze impuruza ku bishora mu bikorwa byangiza urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Ibi yabivuze mu muhango wo kwizihiza Umunsi Mpuzamahanga wo kwita ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima usanzwe wizihizwa tariki 22 Gicurasi , ariko ukaba wizihijwe kuri uyu wa 31 Gicurasi 2021 , mu cyumweru cyahariwe kubungabunga ibidukikije .
Patrick Karera yavuze ko u Rwanda rumaze gutera intambwe ishimishije mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima harimo kwita ku nyamaswa , imigezi , ibishanga n'amashyamba .
Ati """" Turabona hari byinshi tumaze kugeraho mu rwego rw'amashyamba mwabonye ko pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura yashyizwe mu byanya bikomye bigomba kwitabwaho nk'umurage w'Isi .
Ibi ni ibintu twishimiye cyane mu Rwanda n'abafatanyabikorwa twakoranye . """"
Iyi Pariki ya Gishwati - Mukura yabayeho kubera ingufu za Guverinoma y'u Rwanda , mu gihe mbere yari yaratangiye guturwamo n'abaturage , ikorerwamo ibikorwa by'ubuhinzi n'ibindi bitandukanye ariko byose byarahagaritswe , abaturage barimurwa haterwa amashyamba , harongera hasubira uko hahoze .
Patrick Karera yakomeje avuga ko nubwo bimeze gutyo ariko hakiri byinshi byo gukora .
Yagize Ati """" Nubwo twungukira mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima , ibikorwa dukora mu buzima bwa buri munsi birarwangiza . Turi kimwe mu bigize urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima ariko turi kuruma ukuboko kutugaburira .
Kwangiza ibidukikije bitugiraho ingaruka , rero ni byiza ko tuba kimwe mu bisubizo mu kwita ku bidukikije . """"
Ambasaderi w'Umuryango w'Ubumwe bw'u Burayi mu Rwanda , Nicola Bellomo , yavuze ko u Rwanda ari kimwe mu bihugu by'intangarugero mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima ndetse ko uyu muryango uri kurufasha gukomeza muri iyo nzira binyuze mu gutera inkunga imishinga itandukanye .
Yongeyeho ati """" Hari ubushakashatsi bwinshi bwakozwe , hari byinshi byagezweho , ariko haracyari inzira ndende .
Nka EU turi gufasha cyane Guverinoma y'u Rwanda n'Abanyarwanda muri uru rugendo , binyuze muri gahunda nyinshi zitandukanye .
Uyu munsi by'umwihariko turi kugerageza kwereka abantu uruhare rwabo mu kurinda urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima . """"
Zimwe mu mbogamizi u Rwanda rugihura na zo mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinybuzima harimo ubwiyongere bw'abaturage butuma hakenerwa ubutaka bwinshi bwo guturaho , guhinga no gukoreraho imirimo ya buri munsi , gutema ibiti hashakwa inkwi n'amakara , ihindagurika ry'ikirere , impanuka zivamo gutwika amashyamba , imyumvire ikiri hasi n'ibindi
.
Intego u Rwanda rwari rwarihaye yo kuba rufite amashyamba ari kuri 30 % by'ubuso bwarwo yagezweho buranarenga buba 30 . 4 % nk'uko ibarura rya 2019 ryabigaragaje .
Hatangijwe umushinga wo kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima biciye mu mashuri y'u Rwanda na Israël .
Rwatangijwe n'urubuga ruhuza Urubyiruko rw'Abanyarwanda baba muri Canada ( IRYD ) ku bufatanye n'Umuryango Mpuzamahanga urengera Ibidukikije ( TiME ) , Umuryango Mpuzamahanga w'Abanya - Canada udaharanira inyungu , Harmony Foundation ndetse n'Umuryango ukorera ibikorwa by'ubugiraneza mu Rwanda , Shelter Them .
Uwo mushinga wiswe Israël - Rwanda School Biodiversity Program watangijwe ku mugaragaro ku wa 25 Gicurasi 2021 , aho imikoranire izaba hagati y'abanyeshuri bo mu Rwunge rw'amashuri rwa Rugando ho mu karere ka Bugesera , ndetse n'abo mu ishuri rya Rogozin Educational Campus riherereye i Kiryat mu Majyepfo ya Tel - Aviv .
Ni umushina ufite intego yo kurema ubufatanye mu myigire n'imikorere y'abanyeshuri b'ibihugu byombi mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Biteganyijwe ko binyuze muri uwo mushinga , abanyeshuri b'ibihugu byombi bazigira hamwe akamaro k'ibikorwa byo kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima , uburyo bwo gufata imyanzuro mu matsinda mu gihe bazaba bagena ahakwiye kurindwa mu bidukikije , bakongera ubumenyi bwabo mu rurimi n'ubwumvane ( communication ) , imico mishya
n'ubumenyi mu mikoranire hagati y'imico itandukanye , guteza imbere ubumenyi bushya mu buhinzi n'izindi nzego mu kurinda urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Mu muhango uwo gutangiza umushinga wabaye hifashishijwe ikoranabuhanga , Ambasaderi w'u Rwanda muri Canada , Higiro Prosper yashimiye Harmony Foundation ku bwo gufata umwanzuro wo gushyigikira uwo mushinga .
Yakomeje ati """" Iki gikorwa kigaragaza neza uko urubyiruko rufite intego rushobora gutanga umusanzu ku iterambere rirambye ry'Isi . """"
Ambasaderi wa Israël mu Rwanda , Dr Ron Adam , yavuze ko kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima ari byo bizagira uruhare mu gutuma ahazaza h'Isi hamera neza mu rwego rw'ibidukikije no kurinda imihindagurikire y'ikirere .
Ati """" Nishimiye uyu mushinga uhuza abanyeshuri bo mu bihugu byombi , ukabafasha kugira ubumenyi bwisumbuye , ariko icy'ingenzi cyane n'ubufatanye mu kubungabunga ibidukikije . """"
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa TiME , Uri Shanas , yagaragaje ko buri segonda hari ubuso bw'ishyamba bungana n'ikibuga cy'umupira butakara , bityo ko hakwiye kwigishwa uburyo bwo kuyabungabunga hamwe n'ibindi binyabuzima ; haherewe ku bakiri bato .
Ati """" Turashaka ko buri muntu wese mu Isi haba n'umwana muto agira uruhare mu kugabanya iri yangirika . """"
Umuyobozi wa IRYD , Gashirabake Moses , yavuze ko nubwo kugeza ubu hamaze guhuzwa amashuri abiri ( rimwe ryo mu Rwanda na rimwe ryo muri Israël ) """" hari intego yo guhuza amashuri menshi ashoboka . """"
Intego nyamukuru y'uwo mushinga ni iyo kongerera ubumenyi ababyiruka mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima hakiri kare binyuze mu bigo by'amashuri .
Meyer's Parrot , gasuku zidasanzwe ziboneka no mu Bugesera ziri gukendera .
Bugesera ni akarere mu myaka yashize habonekaga inyamaswa zitangaje nk'imvubu n'izindi zitandukanye .
Muri izo nyamaswa habamo n'inyoni nziza cyane ziba mu biti zizwi nka Gasuku , by'umwihariko izo mu bwoko bwa Meyer's Parrots .
Izi nyoni ziboneka mu karere ka Bugesera hafi y'icyuzi cy'igikorano mu kibaya cya Kamatana .
Inyoni y'amabara ateye amabengeza
Ubaye warigeze kubona Gasuku zororwa kuko mu Rwanda hamwe na hamwe zibasha kuhaboneka , ubonye Meyer's Parrot ushobora gukeka ko ubonye Gasuku isanzwe kuko imiterere yazo isa neza n'izindi ngenzi zazo .
Amababa ya Meyer's Parrot ahenshi asa n'ikijuju cyangwa se ibara rijya gusa n'ivu ariko kandi ikagira ibara ry'umuhondo hamwe na hamwe nko hafi yo ku mpera z'amababa zigurukisha .
Ibara ry'umuhondo hari n'ubwo riboneka ku mutwe wayo .
Ku nda hazo ni icyatsi kibisi .
Hejuru ku mirizo ku ruhande hasa n'ikijuju mu gihe mu mirizo hasa n'ikijuju cyijimye .
Umuzenguruko wo ku maso ndetse n'umunwa bifite ibara ry'umukara .
Meyer's Parrot uburebure bwayo bubarirwa hagati ya sentimetero ya 21 na 25 .
Uburemere bwayo buri buri gahati ya garama 100 - 135 .
Uburebure bw'amababa yayo iyarambuye ni santimetero 141 - 149 .
Iyi nyoni ibasha kurama kugera ku myaka hagati ya 25 - 35 .
Meyers's Parrot ishobora kurya ibyo kurya bifite intungamubiri nk'ibyo abantu barya .
Muri ibyo twavuga nk'intoryi , ibigori bibisi , karoti , inkeri , imbuto , ubunyobwa , amababi ya epinari , inyanya , inanasi , udusimba duto , indabo zimwe na zimwe , pommes , imineke n'izindi mbuto zitandukanye .
Ntitera amagi arenze ane
Izi Gasuku hamwe na hamwe barazifata bakazorora .
Iyo ziba mu gasozi by'umwihariko iziba muri Afurika zikunda kororoka iyo igihe cy'imvura kirangiye .
Meyer's Parrot itera amagi mu mwobo w'igiti by'umwihariko iyo uwo mwobo uri hejuru cyane uvuye ku butaka .
Iyi nyoni itera amagi hagati y'abiri n'ane .
Mu gutera ayo imagi hagati y'igi rimwe n'irindi hacamo iminsi ibiri .
Iyo igi rya kabiri rimaze guterwa , kurarira bihita bitangira .
Ingabo n'ingore bifatanya kurarira ayo magi cyane cyane ingore .
Kurarira bimara iminsi hagati ya 26 na 31 .
Imishwi igaburirwa n'ababyeyi bombi .
Umushwi umaze ibyumweru icyenda uba ukuze bihagije .
Meyer's Parrot iba ikuze bihagije ku buryo ishobora kororoka iyo imaze imyaka itatu cyangwa ine .
Izi Gasuku zitwa Meyer """" Parrots zifite inkomoko munsi y'ubutayu bwa Sahara muri iki gihe zirimo guhura n'ibibazo bitandukanye harimo kuba ziribwa n'ibisiga birya inyama n'inzoka , imihindagurikire y'ikirere , kwangirika kw'amashyamba , imiti ikoreshwa mu buhinzi ndetse na ba rushimusi bazitega kugira ngo bazigurishe ku masoko
mpuzamahanga .
Imiterere y'inzu ya mbere nini ku Isi igenewe guhingwamo .
Biteganyijwe ko igisenge cy'iyi nzu kizaba kiriho imisego ishobora gutanga ubushyuhe izashyirwa ku byuma bitwikiriye bikoze muri aluminium .
Imbere h'iyi nyubako hazaba hari ubushyuhe bwa 28 ° C buzajya bufasha ibihingwa birimo gukura bimeze neza .
Thomas Coldefy , watangije igitekerezo cy'uyu mushinga , ubwo yaganiraga n'itangazamakuru yavuze ko intekerezo ze zihoramo ihurizo ryo kwibaza uko uyu mubumbe dutuye wakomeza kubungwabungwa .
Yanongeyeho ko amakuru menshi atangazwa ku ihindagurika ry'ikirere ashobora kuba isoko y'imihangayiko ku batuye Isi .
Ati """" Amakuru yerekeye ihindagurika ry'ikirere akenshi atangazwa mu buryo butifuzwa , bishobora kuba mu buryo bwihuse , isoko nshya y'impungenge . """"
Coldefy yavuze ko mu imurikagurisha ndetse n'iserukiramuco rizwi nka """" Tropicalia """" bazerekaniramo umushinga wabo rizafasha abantu kwibaza ariko bakanabona amahirwe yo kwiga uko uyu mushinga uzakomeza gufasha mu kubungabunga urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Biteganyijwe iyi nzu izaba irimo ibimera by'ubwoko butandukanye , ikaba ubuturo bw'inyoni zitandukanye n'ubwoko bw'amafi asanzwe aboneka mu mugezi wa Amazon .
Izaba ari ndende kandi ku buryo itazabuza ibiti birebire bizaba bihinzemo gukura .
Coldefy mu gishushanyo mbonera cyayo yateganyije ibiraro birebire abantu bahasura bazajya bacaho , inateganya ko habamo restaurant umuntu yakwiciramo isari n'inyota mu gihe yakenera kwikora ku munwa .
Binateganyijwe kandi ko hazaba harimo icyumba kinini gishobora kuberamo inama ndetse hakanagira laboratwari y'ubushakashatsi ku mirimo izaba ikorerwa muri iyo nyubako .
Ivumburamatsiko kuri Matene , inyoni nto ivugwaho udushya twinshi .
Ubusanzwe imiterere y'inyoni usanga ijya gutandukana n'iy'abantu kuko mu nyoni usanga ikigabo aricyo kiba ari cyiza cyane kandi gifite imiterere ikurura ikigore .
Iyo miterere yo guhinduka ngo ikigabo gikurure ikigore hari inyoni ziyihorana buri gihe cyose , ariko kandi hari n'izigira iyo miterere mu gihe cyo kororoka .
Imwe muri izo nyoni zibasha guhindura imiterere yayo ngo ibashe gukurura ikigore ni inyoni yitwa Matene .
Matene by'umwihariko ingabo ni inyoni ishobora guhindura imiterere yayo bitewe n'ibihe runaka .
Matene y'ingabo iyo iri mu gihe cyo kubangurira ingore ifata indi miterere n'ishusho itari isanganywe .
Muri icyo gihe usanga ifite amabara y'umukara n'umweru ndetse n'imirizo miremire cyane kandi ikagira ibara ry'umukara ku mutwe .
Imirizo yayo muri icyo gihe cyo kubangurira iba igizwe n'amababa ane maremare afite uburebure bwa santimetero 20 - 22 .
Ku nda haba ari ibara ry'umweru kandi umunwa wayo uba ari umutuku .
Amaso yayo aba ari ikigina ndetse amaguru n'amajanga biba bijya gusa n'umukara w'ivu .
Iyo miterere tuvuze haruguru iboneka kuri Matene y'ingabo mu gihe cyo kubangurira ingore .
Iyo Matene y'ingabo iri mu bihe bisanzwe iba ijya gusa n'ingore bigatandukanira n'utubara twinshi turi ku mababa kandi ikaba ari nini kuruta ingore .
Ibyo bivuze ko iba ifite imirizo migufi kandi amababa yayo aba ajya gusa n'ikigina . Ku nda hayo haba hasa n'umukara n'ikigina kandi hari n'utuntu tw'udusharagure .
Matene zishobora kuboneka mu busitani , umukenke , mu byatsi , mu mirima n'ahandi .
Uburebure bwa Matene bubarirwa kuri santimetero 12 , ikagira uburemere bwa garama 14 - 19 .
Matene kandi ishobora kubaho kugera ku myaka irindwi .
Iyi nyoni yitwa Matene itungwa n'imbuto ikura mu byatsi ndetse n'udusimba duto .
Utwo dusimba ibasha kudufata mu gihe tuba turimo kuguruka .
Imyororokere ya Matene
Matene kimwe n'izindi nyoni zimwe na zimwe zigira imico idasanzwe yo kutubaka ibyari ahubwo zikajya gutera amagi mu bindi byari by'izindi nyoni kugira ngo zizifashe kurarira , guturaga no kuzirerera imishwi .
Matene y'ingabo iyo iri mu gihe cyo kubangurira ingore iba ifite umubare munini w'ingore ziyigaragiye kandi iba ifite amahane menshi ku buryo yirukana izindi nyoni kugira ngo yisanzure yo n'ingore zayo .
Ingore iyo zimaze kubangurirwa hari utunyoni duto two mu bwoko bw'amafundi Matene iba izi igihe duterera amagi nayo ikagenda igateramo amagi .
Amagi ya Matene aba ari umweru .
Iyo Matene ije gutera amagi mu cyari cy'izindi nyoni ntacyo itwara amagi isanzemo ahubwo yongeramo ayayo gusa .
Iteramo amagi ari hagati y'abiri n'ane .
Izo nyoni zirarira amagi yose kandi zikayaturaga .
Amagi ya Matene aturagwa nyuma y'iminsi 11 - 12 .
Nyuma y'ibyumweru bitatu imishwi iba imaze gukura bihagije .
Imishwi ya Matene iba ishobora kwigana amajwi y'imishwi ya ya nyoni itari nyina .
Gusa , nubwo iyo imishwi iyo ikiri mito iba ijya gusa n'iy'inyoni yaraririye amagi iyo mishwi yaturutsemo , imishwi ya Matene iba ari minini kandi uko igenda ikura igenda ihirikira hasi iyo mishwi yindi , ibyo bigatuma imishwi ya ya nyoni yaraririye amagi ya Matene ipfa .
Mu Rwanda akenshi abantu b'igitsina - gabo bakunda guhiga Matene y'ingabo by'umwihariko igihe iri mu gihe cyo kubangurira .
Akenshi bayihiga bagamije kuyica ngo babone imirizo yayo kuko bizeraga ko yifitemo ubushobozi bwo kubafasha kureshya igitsina gore kabone n'ubwo cyaba kitabakunda .
Mu bihugu bimwe na bimwe byo ku isi ahakorwa ubucuruzi bw'inyoni Matene iri mu nyoni zikundwa kugurishwa ikajya kororwa cyangwa gukoreshwa mu yindi mihango .
Ibyo bituma ziza mu nyoni zishobora gushira ku isi kuko zihigwa na benshi cyane .
Ivumburamatsiko ku bisiga by'ibigungumuka biboneka mu Rwanda bibasha kurama imyaka 70 .
Zimwe uzazibona zigusanze mu rugo , hari izindi uzabona ahantu bitewe n'ibihingwa cyangwa ibiti bihari .
Ku bantu bakunda gutembera cyangwa se bakunda ibyaremwe muri rusange bashobora kwibaza byinshi ku mibereho y'inyoni n'ibisiga dusanga mu Rwanda .
Wakwibaza uti """" Ziba ahantu hameze hate ?
Zitungwa n'iki ?
Zirama imyaka ingahe ?
N'ibindi bibazo .
Uyu munsi twabahitiyemo igisiga gitangaje cyitwa Ikigungumuka kandi uko bizadushobokera tuzakomeza kurebera hamwe amakuru y'ibanze kuri ibi biguruka twahawe n'uwahanze u Rwanda nta kiguzi .
Imiterere y'Ikigungumuka urebeye inyuma
Ikigungumuka cyitwa Southern ground hornbill nk'uko mu cyongereza izina ryacyo ribivuga .
Gifite ku munwa wacyo aho uhera ikintu kimeze nk'ihembe .
Iki gisiga kandi ni cyo kinini mu muryango w'ibindi bisiga bihuje ubwoko kuko kibasha kugira uburebure bwa santimetero 90 - 120 uvuye ku butaka .
Amababa yacyo ni umukara ariko ku mpera afite ibara ry'umweru .
Iki gisiga ikigabo n'ikigore ubasha kubitandukanya ubibonye n'amaso kuko ikigabo gifite ibara ry'umutuku ku maso no ku gikanu mu gihe ikigore gifite ibara ry'ubururu ku muhogo .
Iki gisiga kandi gitandukanye cyane n'ibindi byo mu muryango wacyo kuko cyo kigendagenda kandi kikibera hasi ku butaka kuruta kuba mu biti .
Iki gisiga iyo ari gito kiba gisa n'igisiga gikuze .
Ibigungumuka bikunda kuba ku butaka nubwo gacye cyane wabibona mu biti .
Ibigungumuka kandi bikunda kuba ahantu hari umukenke .
Mu Rwanda ushobora kubisanga muri Pariki y'Akagera .
Ku rwego rw'Isi ubu harabarirwa ibigungumuka 1500 .
Umuvuduko wacyo ubasha kuba ibilometero 30 ku isaha .
Uburemere bwacyo iyo kimaze gukura ni ibiro 2 - 6 .
Uburambe bw'ikigungumuka ni imyaka 50 - 70 .
Ikigungumuka gitungwa n'iki ?
Ikigungumuka ni indyanyama kuko gitungwa n'inyamaswa zigenda ku butaka harimo ibikururanda , ibigenda bisimbagurika , inyamabere ntoya n'ibindi .
Iki gisiga kandi gishobora kurya inyamaswa zapfuye iyo ibyo kurya byayo byibanze ari byo ibiburangoro byabuze .
Kuko iki gisiga gifite umunwa munini kiwukoresha gifata umuhigo kandi kigashobora kuwumira wose .
Iyo ari igihe kibasha kubona ibyo kurya bihagije kirabirundanya kandi kikajya kibirya gikurikije uko cyabibitse bikurikirana .
Uko ibigungumuka byororoka
Ibigungumuka ni ibisiga bikunda gusabana kuko ushobora kubisanga hamwe ari nka bibiri kugera ku munani .
No mu gihe cyo gutera amagi no kurera imishwi uko gukorera mu itsinda birakomeza .
Ikigungumuka kiba kimaze gukura ku buryo cyakororoka ku myaka itatu ariko gikora igisa no kuboneza urubyaro kuko nubwo kuri iyo myaka gishobora kubyara ariko kibikora ku myaka itandatu cyangwa irindwi ndetse gishobora no kugera mu myaka 10 kitarabyara .
Ibigungumuka bikora umuryango w'ingabo n'ingore bizabana igihe kirekire . Akenshi ikigabo kinini n'ikigore kinini mu muryango ni byo byororoka .
Buri muryango ugiye kororoka witabwaho nibura n'ibindi bisiga bibiri .
Ikigungumuka cy'ikigore gitera amagi mu mwobo w'igiti cyashaje cyangwa mu bitare .
Icyari kiba kimeze neza kuko kiba kirimo ibyatsi n'amababi .
Ikigore gitera amagi 1 - 3 y'umweru kandi akavamo imishwi itatu ariko umushwi umwe wabanje kuvuka ni wo ubasha gukura kuko indi mishwi yicwa no kubura ibyo kurya mu gihe ikiri mito .
Igihe cyo kurarira amagi kiri hagati y'iminsi 40 - 45 .
Muri iki gihe cyo kurarira ingore iba igaburirwa n'ibindi bisiga bigize umuryango .
Iyi ikigungumuka cyibyaye gishobora kongera kubyara nyuma y'imyaka itatu .
Imishwi ikomeza kubana n'ababyeyi bayo nibura kugera ku myaka icyenda ikabona kuba yajya aho ishaka .
Ibibangamira Ibigungumira
Kubera ko ibi bisiga biba hasi ku butaka ibyo bituma inyamaswa zihiga nk'ingwe n'ingona bibifata mu buryo bworoshye cyane cyane iyo bikiri bito .
Ikindi ntabwo ibi bisiga bifite uburyo buhagije bwo kwirwanaho keretse gusakuza cyane kugira ngo bikange ikije kubihiga .
Ikindi bishobora gukora ni ugusakuza cyane nibura kugira biburire ibindi bibashe kwihisha .
Ku bw'iyo mpamvu ndetse n'izindi zishingiye ku mihindagurikire y'ikirere , gutema amashyamba , kubyicisha uburozi , ubuhigi n'ubushimusi bituma ibi bisiga bishyirwa ku rutonde rw'ibisiga birimo gucika ku rwego rw'isi .
Mu bihugu bimwe na bimwe ibi bisiga bikunda kumenagura ibirahure byo ku nzu mu gihe birebyemo bikibonamo , bityo abantu bakabyitura kubyica kuko byabangirije .
Ivumburamatsiko kuri """" Vautour Fauve de Ruppell , """" igisiga gitangaje cyo mu bwoko bw'inkongoro .
Ibyo ni ukuri ; gusa ku rundi ruhande mu Rwanda dufite ibindi bisiga byo mu muryango w'inkongoro bidashingira ibyo kurya byabyo buri gihe ku ntumbi , kuko bimwe muri byo bibasha kwica umuhigo , ariko kandi hakaba n'ibindi bibeshwaho cyane n'imbuto .
Mu bwoko bugera kuri bune bw'ibisiga dusanga mu muryango w'inkongoro , uyu munsi turibanda ku cyitwa vautour fauve de Ruppell , igisiga gifite imiterere idasanzwe .
Izina Ruppell kirikomora ku Mudage wize ibijyanye n'inyamaswa kandi akaba umuvumbuzi wabayeho hagati ya 20 Ugushyingo 1794 na 10 Ukuboza 1884 witwaga Eduard Rüppell .
Mu Rwanda ibisiga byo muri ubu bwoko ushobora kubisanga muri Pariki y'Akagera ndetse muri Kigali ushobora kubisanga nko mu Murenge wa Kigali , Akagari ka Mwendo ahantu hari ikimoteri bajugunyamo ibisigazwa by'amatungo abagirwa mu ibagiro rya Nyabugogo , ushobora kandi kubisanga ku ibagiro rya Nyabugogo no ku kimoteri cy'i Nduba
ahamenwa imyanda iva mu ibagiro .
Imiterere ya Ruppell's Griffon Vulture
Ruppell's griffon vulture ni igisiga ubasha kubona ukagitandukanya n'ibindi .
Kigira amababa magari iyo kiyarambuye ariko kikagira amababa magufi ku mirizo .
Ijosi ryacyo hariho ubwoya bw'umweru kandi umunwa wacyo ni umuhondo .
Ku rwego rw'isi habarurwa ibisiga byo muri ubu bwoko bigera kuri 22 . 000 .
Iki gisiga gishobora kurama imyaka iri hagati ya 40 - 50 .
Iyo kigurutse cyihuta kigendera ku muvuduko wa kilometero 35 ku isaha .
Iyo gikuze gishobora gupima ibiro 6 , 4 - 9 .
Uburebure bwacyo buri hagati ya santimetero 85 - 103 .
Ibyo kurya bya Ruppell's Griffon Vulture
Ibi bisiga ni indyanyama kandi birya n'ibisigazwa biva ku nyamaswa zapfuye cyangwa zishwe .
Bivugwa ko bitajya byica ahubwo birya ibintu byapfuye .
Ibyo bintu bishobora kuba byishwe n'izindi nyamaswa nko mu mashyamba , bishobora kandi kuba byishwe n'indwara cyangwa byapfuye kuko bishaje .
Kuba ibi bisiga bitica ntabwo ari uko ari ubunebwe cyangwa intege nke .
Hari inyandiko zimwe na zimwe zivuga ko ari byo bisiga bishobora gutumbagira hejuru cyane mu kirere kuruta ibindi byose kandi bikabasha kureba hasi bikabona ibyo kurya .
Uko Ruppell's Griffon Vulture yororoka
Ibi bisiga bikora umuryango w'ingabo n'ingore imwe kandi bikabana mu buzima bwose .
Ibyo bivuze ko bidacana inyuma nk'uko bigenda ku bisiga n'inyoni zimwe na zimwe .
Ibi bisiga iyo bigeye gutera amagi byishyira hamwe mu matsinda atandukanye ku buryo ushobora gusanga imiryango hagati ya 15 na 20 yarateye amagi ahantu hamwe .
Iyo bishatse gutera amagi bishaka ahantu hatekanye ku buryo ikiremwamuntu bitacyorohera kuhagera ngo kibihungabanyirize umutekano .
Ingore itera igi rimwe ariko rikararirwa n'ababyeyi bombi mu gihe kiri hagati y'iminsi 52 - 60 .
Iyo igi rikimara guturagwa umushwi uba ufite intege nke kandi upima nibura amagarama 170 .
Iyo umushwi umaze iminsi 60 uba umaze kumera amababa kandi usa n'igisiga gikuru .
Nyuma y'amezi ane umushwi uba ushobora kuguruka neza ariko ntabwo uhita usiga ababyeyi bawo ahubwo bakomeza kuwitaho .
Ibi bisiga birasabana cyane kuko hari ubwo ushobora kubisanga ahantu hamwe ari nk'ibisiga birenga 100 .
Uruhare rwa Ruppell's Griffon Vulture mu kubungabunga ibidukikije
Ubusanzwe nko muri za pariki aho usanga hari inyamaswa zibeshwaho no kurya inyama haramutse hatabayeho uburyo bwo gukoramo isuku wasanga ahantu hose huzuye umwanda n'ibisigazwa bitari ngombwa .
Muri urwo rwego ni ho akamaro k'ibisiga byitwa Ruppell's griffon vulture kagaragarira kuko usanga bikora isuku binyuze mu kurya inyamaswa zipfushije kuko zishaje , amayezi n'ibindi bisigazwa by'inyamaswa zishwe n'izitunzwe n'inyama , bityo bigatuma aho hantu hadahora umwanda utari ngombwa .
Ku rundi ruhande , byakabye byiza abantu batunze inyamaswa zo mu rugo igihe zipfuye bitagateje ikibazo kubwo kujugunywa ahabonetse hose cyangwa ngo zijugunywe mu mazi abantu bazakoresha kandi hari ibisiga byazirya bikamererwa neza .
Ibibangamira Ruppell's Griffon Vulture
Muri iki gihe Isi ihanganye n'imihindagurikire y'ikirere ndetse ugasanga ibikorwa bya muntu bitita ku bidukikije ku rugero ruhagije , ingaruka zabyo zigera no ku bisiga .
Reba nawe ibikorwa byo gutema amashyamba bituma ibi bisiga bibura aho kuba byisanzuye , abantu barabihohotera mu buryo bumwe cyangwa ubundi kugeza n'ubwo babyicisha uburozi .
Mu gice cya Afurika y'uburengerazuba bivugwa ko ibi bisiga bikoreshwa cyane mu mihango yabo ya gakondo .
Abantu barindwi bamaze kwicwa n'ibiza , inzu 78 zarasenyutse muri Gicurasi .
Usibye abamaze kubura ubuzima , MINEMA yatangaje ko kuva tariki ya 1 kugera kuya 11 Gicurasi 2021 , inzu zigera kuri 78 zasenyutse , ubutaka bugera kuri hegitari 130 . 3 bumaze kwangirika mu gihe amatungo agera kuri abiri yapfuye naho imihanda itanu igasenyuka .
Umuyobozi w'Ishami Rishinzwe UbutabazI no gusana ibyangijwe muri Minisiteri ishinzwe ibikorwa by'Ubutabazi , MINEMA , Habinshuti Philippe , yabwiye IGIHE kuri ubu ikiri kwihutirwa ari ukurengera ubuzima bw'abahuye n'ibiza by'imvura .
Ati """" Ikiba kiri gukorwa ni ukureba ko abo bahuye n'ibibazo bari gukorerwa ubutabazi bw'ibanze noneho tugatangira gutegura ibyo gusana kuko ni ibintu bisaba gutegurwa , tukareba niba aho ari ahantu hakongera gutura cyangwa hakarebwa niba bashakirwa ahandi ho gutura . """"
Yakomeje ati """" Ingufu ziba zigomba gushyirwamo harebwa abo bagize ikibazo ngo bameze bate , bakeneye iki kugira ngo ubuzima bwabo bube bumeze neza . """"
Yavuze ko kuri ubu abamaze gusenyerwa inzu n'imvura hari abacumbikiwe n'abaturanyi abandi bakaba bacumbikiwe mu nsengero .
Habinshuti yasabye abaturage gukora ibishoboka byose kugira ngo birinde ibishobora kujyana ubuzima bwabo mu kaga .
Ati """" Turasaba abantu kugenzura niba aho batuye nta kibazo gihari , niba inzu zabo zitaratangiye gusaduka , bakareba cyane cyane ibibazo by'inkuba bakajya bugama mu nzu aho kujya hanze .
Turabashishikariza kugira ngo buri wese yumve ko iyo imvura iri kugwa haba hashobora kuza ibyago kandi buri wese aba agomba kuba akora ibyo akwiye kuba akora kugira ngo yirinde kandi agabanye ingaruka zo kuba yagerwaho n'ibiza . """"
Ikigo cy'Igihugu cy'Iteganyagihe , Meteo Rwanda , giherutse gutangaza ko mu minsi 10 iri imbere , ni ukuvuga kuva tariki ya 10 kugera kuri 20 Gicurasi , hateganyijwe imvura nyinshi mu gihugu iri kuri milimetero hagati ya 40 na 120 by'umwihariko mu gice cy'Amajyaruguru .
Loni yasabye ko hafatwa ingamba zo kugabanya Gaz Méthane mu maguru mashya
Iyo raporo yiswe Global Methane Assessment yamuritswe kuri uyu wa 6 Gicurasi 2021 , yerekana ko iyo gaz ihumanya ikirere ku gipimo cya 30 % nyuma ya dioxide de carbone , ariko bigatandukanywa n'uko Méthane yo imara mu kirere imyaka icumi gusa naho carbone ikaba yahamara imyaka isaga 100 .
Ni aho abashakashatsi bakoze iyo raporo bahereye bavuga ko kuyigabanya bishoboka kandi byagira akamaro kuko nko kugabanya 45 % by'iyo gaz bishoboka mu myaka 10 , ndetse mu gihe byaba bigenze gutyo nyuma y'imyaka 25 ubushyuhe bw'Isi bukaganukaho dogere Celisius 0 , 3 .
Umuyobozi Nshingwabikorwa wa UNEP , Inger Andersen , yavuze ko hakenewe ubufatanye bw'amahanga mu kugabanya iyo gaz mu maguru mashya .
Yagize ati """" Kugabanya Méthane ni cyo kintu gikomeye twakora mu koroshya imihindagurikire y'ikirere mu myaka 25 iri imbere , bikuzuzanya n'izindi mbaraga zikenewe mu kugabanya dioxyde de carbone .
Inyungu byagira kuri rubanda , ubukungu no ku bidukijije ni nyinshi kandi ntizabonerwa ikiguzi .
Dukeneye ubufatanye bw'amahanga mu kugabanya Méthane nyinshi ishoboka vuba na bwangu muri iyi myaka icumi . """"
Gaz Méthane ishobora kuva mu mu mazi cyangwa mu butaka nk'ibindi binyabutabire kamere no mu bintu biba bimaze igihe kinini byaraboze no mu bikorwa bya muntu bisanzwe .
Ibyo birimo ikoreshwa ry'ibicanwa ryongera 35 % , imyanda yongera 20 % ndetse n'ubuhinzi bwongera 40 % .
Ku rundi ruhande , iyo raporo yanagaragaje ko kugabanya iyo gaz bishoboka kuko nk'ibikorwa bya muntu biyongera ubu bishobora kwifashisha ikoranabuhanga rigezweho .
Ubuhinzi n'ubworozi byakorwa mu buryo bwa kijyambere , ibimoteri n'ahandi harundwa imyanda n'ibishingwe ku Isi hakagabanywa , ndetse ikoreshwa ry'ibicanwa nk'amakara , inkwi , ibikomoka kuri peteroli n'ibindi nka nyiramugengeri bikagabanywa himakazwa uburyo bujyanye n'igihe butanangiza ibidukikije .
Amasezerano ya Paris agamije kugabanya imyuka ihumanya ikirere yashyizweho umukono n'ibihugu 200 , agena ko buri gihugu cyayemeye cyakora iyo bwabaga kikagabanya imyuka cyohereza mu kirere ku buryo nibura mu 2050 ubushyuhe bw'Isi bwazaba buri kuri dogere Celisius 2 byaba byiza bukajya munsi ya dogere Celsius 1 , 5 .
Kuba gaz Méthane yatangira kugabanywa nk'uko iyo raporo yabisabye , ndetse n'uburyo bwo kugabanya dioxyde de carbone bugakomeza gushyirwamo ingufu hifashishwa amashanyarazi , bishobora kugeza kuri iyo nsinzi .
Abacuruzi basabye kubanza kwigishwa ibibi by'amashashi na pulastiki aho guhanwa .
Babitangaje ubwo kuwa 30 Mata 2021 , Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe kubungabunga ibidukikije ( REMA ) , cyongeraga gukora ubukangurambaga ku bacuruzi bagicuruza amashashi ndetse n'ibikozwe muri purasitiki bikoreshwa rimwe , ari nako basobanurirwa ububi bwayo mu kwangiza ibidukikije .
Batamuriza Chantal akorera ubucuruzi mu murenge wa Kanombe mu Kagari ka Kabaza , yavuze ko atumva uburyo hari amasashe amwe yemerewa kwinjira mu gihugu .
Ati """" Icyashyirwamo imbaraga ni ukubanza kudusobanurira ibyemewe n'ibitemewe .
Nk'ubu baramutse banciye amande bakavuga ngo fanta yo muri pulastiki ntiyemewe kandi nta kindi cyayisimbuye , urumva ko ari ikibazo gihari kandi umucuruzi adafitiye igisubizo cyacyo .
Hari ibintu bavuga ko bitemewe kandi byageze ku isoko , nka OMO ziri mu masashe kandi zifite inganda zizikora kandi zizwi , ntekereza ko ari ho bakabanje kubikemura . """"
Ngizwenayo Musa nawe yavuze ko kuba hari ibicuruzwa bimwe byemererwa kwinjira mu gihugu bipfunyitse mu masashi cyangwa pulastiki , biba bishobora gushyira mu gihombo umucuruzi .
Ati """" Ibyiza bakabanje guca iyo pulastiki mbere y'uko yinjira mu gihugu kuko iyo yinjiye imbere mu gihugu uri kuyicuruza niwe ubihomberamo kurusha . Ibyiza bayikumira mbere y'uko yinjira .
Bakadushakiye mbere ibyemewe ku buryo bitadushyira mu gihombo .
Umuyobozi Mukuru wungirije wa REMA , Munyazikwiye Faustin , yavuze ko iyo itegeko ryasohotse rireba buri umwe gusa ko hari abica mategeko nkana banyuza amasashe mu nzira zitemwe .
Yavuze ko ibicuruzwa byinjira bisa n'ibyemewe bipfunyitse mu masashe birimo inkweto , ibiribwa n'ibindi biterwa n'uko hari itegeko rigena amahoro y'ibidukikije , rigena ko agomba kuzajya acibwa ikintu icyo ari cyo cyose kivuye hanze gipfunyitse mu isashe kugira ngo ayo mahoro afashe mu gucunga neza uwo mwanda winjiye mu
gihugu .
Yavuze ko hakiri imbogamizi kuko iryo tegeko ritari ryemezwa n'inzego zibishinzwe gusa ko rizakemura byinshi .
Ati """" Nirisohoka rizafasha guhagarika bimwe mu bicuruzwa bipfunyitse mu masashi bitabuzwaga kwinjira mu gihugu kubera amasezerano igihugu kiba gifitanye n'ikindi mu bucuruzi .
Hakazajyaho amategeko ariko atabangamiye ubwo bucuruzi . """"
Munyazikwiye yavuze ko kandi hari ubwo abacuruzi bemererwa gutanga ibipfunnyitse mu masashi cyangwa pulastiki mu gihe hagaragaye ko nta kindi gihari kibisimbura .
Ati """" Itegeko ryateganyije ko mu gihe bigaragaye ko ikigiye gukorwa cyangwa ikigiye gupfunyikwa kidafite ikigisimbura REMA ishobora gutanga uburenganzira bwihariye ku muntu ufite ibyo ashaka gupfunyika . """"
Itegeko N ° 17 / 2019 ryo ku wa 10 / 08 / 2019 ribuza ikorwa , itumizwa mu mahanga , ikoreshwa n'icuruzwa ry'amasashe n'ibikoresho bikozwe muri pulasitiki bikoreshwa inshuro imwe .
Naho ingingo ya 10 ivuga ko umuntu utumiza mu mahanga amasashe n'ibikoresho bikozwe muri pulasitiki bikoreshwa inshuro imwe ahanishwa kwamburwa ayo masashe n'ibyo bikoresho no kwishyura ihazabu yo mu rwego rw'ubutegetsi ingana n'inshuro icumi ( 10 ) z'agaciro k'ayo masashe n'ibyo bikoresho bikozwe muri
pulasitiki bikoreshwa inshuro imwe .
Ni mu gihe umuntu uranguza amasashe n'ibikoresho bikozwe muri pulasitiki bikoreshwa inshuro imwe ahanishwa ihazabu yo mu rwego rw'ubutegetsi ingana n'amafaranga y'u Rwanda ibihumbi magana arindwi ( 700 . 000 FRW ) kandi ayo amasashe n """" ibyo bikoresho akabyamburwa , naho umuntu ucuruza mu buryo butaranguza amasashe
n'ibikoresho bikozwe muri pulasitiki bikoreshwa inshuro imwe agahanishwa ihazabu yo mu rwego rw'ubutegetsi ingana n'amafaranga y'u Rwanda ibihumbi magana atatu ( 300 . 000 FRW ) kandi ayo masashe n'ibyo bikoresho akabyamburwa nk'uko ingingo ya 11 n'iya 12 z'iryo tegeko zibivuga .
Malawi : Abaturage bagize ubwoba nyuma y'uko amazi y'ikiyaga ahindutse icyatsi .
Minisitiri ushinzwe amashyamba n'umutungo kamere muri ucyo gihugu , Nancy Tembo yatangaje ko guhindura ibara kw'amazi y'ikiyaga byatewe n'umwuka muke wa Oxygène nyuma y'imvura nyinshi imaze iminsi igwa .
Tembo yasabye abaturage kuba bitonze nibura mu gihe cy'ibyumweru bibiri amazi agasubira uko yahoze .
Inzobere zivuga ko guhinduka icyatsi kw'amazi y'ikiyaga biterwa n """" ibyatsi bito cyane bitaboneshwa amaso ( birebeshwa microscope ) byo mu bwoko bw'urubobi ( blue green algae ) byiswe """" Cynobacteria , """" byiyongera mu kiyaga , bigatuma amazi ahindura ibara agasa n'icyatsi cyererutse urebeye kure
, ibi bikaba bikunda kugaragara kenshi mu gihe cy'itumba .
Ibi byagaragaye no mu kiyaga cya Kivu mu mwaka wa 2016 .
Umwaka wa 2022 uzashira nta nyubako zigisakaje Fibrociment .
Hashize imyaka itanu Ikigo cy'Igihugu cy'imiturire , RHA gitangiye urugendo rwo kurandura burundu amabati ya fibrocement , azwiho kugira ikinyabutabire cya Asbestos kigira ingaruka mbi ku buzima bwa muntu .
Nyamara urwo rugendo rwakomeje gukomwa mu nkokora n'ingengo y'Imari nkeya .
Ikigo cy'Igihugu cy'imiturire cyivuga ko inzu zose zari zarasakajwe fibrociment hamaze gukurwaho izigera 70 . 1 % .
RHA igaragaza ko kugira ngo aya mabati akurweho , hakenewe agera kuri miliyari eshanu z'amafaranga y'u Rwanda .
Umuhuzabikorwa muri RHA ushinzwe gahunda yo gukuraho ayo mabati , Ntakirutimana Mathias , yabwiye IGIHE ko hari icyizere ko umwaka wa 2022 uzasiga ayo mabati yakuweho .
Mu mu turere dutandukanye tw'Igihugu twiganjemo itw'Intara y'Amajyepfo n'Uburasirazuba ku nzu za leta niho hakigaragara cyane amabati ya fibrociment .
Ibi bishimangirwa n'abaturage bo mu Karere ka Nyagatare bivuriza ku bitaro bya Karangazi aho basaba ko amabati ya Fibrociment asakaye ibyo bitaro yakurwaho kuko ashobora kugira ingaruka mbi ku buzima bw'umuntu .
Abavuganye na Flash Fm bavuze ko bafite amakuru ko aya mabati afite ingaruka mbi ku buzima bwa muntu bityo ko batumva ukuntu yaba agisakajwe ibitaro .
Umwe Ati """" Ariya mabati ya Fibro ciment ntekereza y'uko uretse hano Karangazi nta handi asigaye kandi ariya mabati afite ingaruka ku buzima bw'umuntu kuko ikintu abashakashatsi baba baratekerejeho , leta igafata icyemezo cyo kuyaca mu gihugu byanga bikunda ashobora gutera ubundi burwayi . """"
Aba baturage bavuze ko mu mwaka wa 2017 iki kibazo bari bakigejeje ku basenateri ubwo bari baje muri ako gace ariko kugeza ubu akaba atarakurwa kuri ibyo bitaro .
Ntakirutimana Mathias yavuze ko iki kibazo bakizi ndetse ko mu mwaka wa 2022 kizaba cyamaze gukemuka kuko ubu hagikorwa inyigo yabyo .
OMS ivuga ko abantu miliyoni 125 bakorera ahantu bashobora guhumeka umukungugu w'aya mabati bashobora kwandura kanseri y'ibihaha , ari nabyo bituma nibura ibihumbi 107 ku isi bipfa kubera ingaruka zo guhumeka uyu mukungugu .
Kugeza ubu mu Rwanda hari ibyobo 13 byo gushyinguramo amabati ya fibrocement .
RAB igeze kure umushinga uzagoboka abaturage bo ku Mayaga bajyaga bahura n'ikibazo cy'ubwatsi bw'amatungo .
Mu ukwakira 2020 Ikigo cy'Igihugu gishinzwe Iterambere ry'Ubuhinzi n'Ubworozi , RAB , cyatangiye gushaka igisubizo kirambye ku kibazo cy'ibura ry'ubwatsi gikunze kugaragara mu gice cy'Amayaga mu Rwanda kigatuma hari bamwe mu borozi bambuka bakajya kubushakira mu Burundi , bagahohoterwa cyangwa bagafatwa
bagafungirwayo .
RAB ibinyujije mu mushinga wayo ugamije guteza imbere ubworozi bw'inka zitanga umukamo witwa Rwanda Dairy Development Project ( RDDP ) yatangiye gutoza abaturage bo mu Karere ka Nyanza gutera ubwatsi ku bwinshi kugira ngo batazongera guhura n'ikibazo cy'ibura ryabwo .
Icyo gihe hahise haterwa ubwatsi ku buso bwa hegitari zigera kuri ebyiri mu Murenge wa Kibirizi kugira ngo abaturage bazabone imbuto yabwo ihagije .
Umukozi w'Umushinga RDDP , Nshokeyinka Joseph , yabwiye IGIHE ko kugeza ubu imbuto z'ubwatsi batubuye zamaze kuboneka ku buryo zigiye guhabwa abaturage bagatera mu mirima yabo .
Ati """" Muri gihembwe cy'ihinga cya 2021 A twari turi ku Mayaga muri Kibirizi aho twari twagiye gutangiza igihembwe cy'ihinga ry'ubwatsi ku rwego rw'igihugu .
Ni gahunda yakomereje no mu tundi turere . """"
"""" Ubu imbuto irahari imeze neza , twiteguye ko mu gihembwe cy'ihinga cya 2022 A izaba igeze ku gipimo cyo gutanga izindi mbuto zigahabwa bariya baturanyi bose bari hariya .
Tukaba tudashidikanya ko mu minsi iza abantu bose bambukaga bajya kwahira hakurya bitazongera kubaho . """"
Nshokeyinka akomeza avuga ko kugeza ubu imbuto yabonetse ari ibinyampeke birimo urubingo ruzwi nka Kakamega na Chloris Gayana ndetse na Panicum maximum na Panikum Chloratum .
Hari kandi ubwatsi bw'ibinyamisogwe aribwo Desmodium distrortum ; Desmodium incinatum ; Mucuna na Rabrab .
Ati """" Ibyo byose ni ibinyamisogwe usanga bijya kunganira bya binyampeke kuko iyo bigaburiwe inka iba ihawe ifunguro ryuzuye . """"
Bamwe mu bahinzi bo mu Karere ka Nyanza mu Murenge wa Kibirizi babwiye IGIHE ko biteguye kwakira imbuto y'ubwatsi kugira ngo babuhinge kuko babukeneye .
Mukakarera Immaculée ati """" Izi mbuto batuzaniye bigaragara ko ari nziza kandi zikura vuba .
Ubu rero dutegereje ko baziduha kugira ngo dutangire kuzihinga mu mirima yacu , turiteguye . """"
Undi mworozi witwa Nsigaye Paul na we yavuze ko nibamara kubaha imbuto , ikibazo cy'ibira ry'ubwatsi kizaba gikemutse .
Ati """" Hano ku Mayaga icyo kibazo cy'ibura ry'ubwatsi kimaze igihe kinini , ariko ziriya mbuto batuburiye inaha nibamara kuziduha tukazitera , kizaba gikemutse kandi nta muntu uzasubira kwahira mu Burundi . """"
Mu turere 14 umushinga RDDP ukoreramo mu gihembwe cy'ihinga cya 2021 A hatewe ubwatsi ku buso bushya bungana na hegitari 2000 .
Hagaragajwe ingaruka z'ifumbire mvaruganda ku mihindagurikire y'ikirere .
Politiki y'ubuhinzi yo muri 2018 ivuga ko """" Igihugu cyifuza kwihaza mu biribwa , imirire myiza n'iterambere rirambye , biyoboye ubuhinzi muri 2030 """" naho politiki y'ibidukikije n'imihindagurikire y'ikirere yo muri 2019 igira iti """" u Rwanda rukwiye kugira ibidukikije bisukuye , bishobora guhangana
n'imihindagurikire y'ikirere bitanga ubuzima bwiza kuri sosiyete . """"
Ubushakashatsi bwakozwe na Dr John Musemakweli buvuga ko nubwo izi politiki zombi zisa n'aho zuzuzanya ariko harimo byinshi bikenewe kunozwa kugira ngo hakomeze kwimakazwa kubungabunga ibidukikije no guhangana n'imihindagurikire y'ikirere .
Muri ibyo harimo ko gukoresha inyongeramusaruro mvaruganda ndetse n'imikoreshereze y'ibishanga bikigarara nk'ikibazo gikomeye ku kubungabunga ibidukikije .
Raporo ivuga ko guhinga mu bishanga ahanini bitera ibyago birimo kugabanuka kw'amazi no kuyanduza , bagasaba ko habaho gukoreshwa ibishanga mu buryo bunoze hatitawe gusa ku musaruro w'ibihingwa ahubwo hagamijwe no kubungabunga ibidukikije .
Ku kijyanye no gukoresha imvaruganda n'imiti imwe yica udukoko , raporo ivuga nubwo bigira umumaro ariko kubikoresha , cyane bituma ubutaka bwangirika , amazi akandura n'ibiribwa ndetse bikaba n'uburozi ku rusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
N'ubwo iyo raporo ivuga ibitagenda ariko inagaragaza ko hari inzira zishobora kwifashishwa hashakirwa umuti urambye bimwe mu bibazo bikigaragara .
Raporo isaba inzego bireba kurushaho gukora mu buryo bwo kugabanya imvaruganda hakongerwa ikoreshwa ry'ifumbire y'imborera , kugabanya no guhitamo neza imiti yica udukoko ikoreshwa mu rwego rwo kurinda abantu n'urusobe rw'ibinyabuzima .
Umukozi muri Minisiteri y'Ubuhinzi n'Ubworozi ushinzwe ibijyanye n'ihindagurika ry'ikirere André Gatete , yavuze ko ibyo abakoze ubushakashatsi basabye biri mu byo MINAGRI yiyemeje ariko agaragaza ko hari aho ubushakashatsi butagaragaza neza imikorere myiza y'ibishanga birimo kuba hakoreshwa na gahunda yo kuhira .
Yagize ati """" Ni raporo nziza kandi twishimiye ko n'ibyo musaba biri muri gahunda za Minisiteri , muri gahunda yo gukora ubuhinzi ariko bugendanye n'ihindagurika ry'ikirere [ . . . ] icyo nashakaga kuvuga ni uko bitoroshye kugabanya ikoreshwa ry'imvaruganda .
Turi gukora ubushakashatsi tureba ko hakoreshwa ifumbire n'imiti icyarimwe ariko tugamije kugabanya ibikorerwa mu nganda .
Biragoye kandi gukoresha imborera yonyine ni ibintu bizadusaba igihe kitari gito , ndatekereza ko dukwiye kwibanda ku nyungu zo kubikoresha byombi ducunganan'ihindagurika ry'ikirere . """"
Nsengimana Aimable wari witabiriye iki kiganiro yavuze ko hari n'igihe usanga inzego z'ibanze nazo zibigiramo intege nke mu ishyirwa mu bikorwa ku ngamba zinyuranye zigamije kubungabunga ibidukikije ndetse no kurinda ibyagezweho .
Umukozi ushinzwe porogaramu muri AFSA , Umuryango ushinzwe ubuziranenge bw'ibiribwa muri Afurika , Bridget Mugambe , usanzwe utera inkunga RCCDN yashimangiye ko bazakomeza gutera inkunga ku kijyanye no kwita ku ihindagurika ry'ikirere , mu bihugu bigera kuri 12 uyu muryango ukoreramo muri Afurika .
Umunyamabanga wa Leta muri Minisiteri y'ibidukikije Patrick Karera yavuze ko gushyira mu bikorwa ingamba zijyanye n'ihindagurika ry'ikirere Leta ikorana n'ibigo by'abikorera umunsi ku wundi ndetse anashimira abakoze iyo raporo no kugaragaza ingamba zagenderwaho kugeza kuri 2030 .
RCCDN ivuga hakwiye gushakishwa uburyo politiki y'ubuhinzi yavugururwa kugira ngo ingingo ziburamo zihuzwe neza na Politiki y'ibidukikije n'imihindagurikire y'ikirere , gushyiraho uburyo buhoraho bw'ibiganiro byatuma izi politiki zirushaho kuzuzanya aho kuvuguruzanya no guhanira gushyira mu bikorwa ibivugwa muri izo
politiki zombi aho guhera mu nyandiko .
Amashuri yashishikarijwe gutera ibiti nk'uburyo bw'isuku no kurwanya ibiza
Byatangarijwe mu gikorwa cyo gutera ibiti ku bigo by'amashuri mu Mujyi wa Kigali .
Ni igikorwa cyateguwe n'Umuryango w'Urubyiruko Ruhanira Kurengera Ibidukikije , The Green Fighter n'Ikigo Mpuzamahanga Cyita ku Bidukikije , Global Green Growth Institute ( GGGI ) , mu rwego rwo kwizihiza umunsi ngarukamwaka wahariwe kubungabunga Umubumbe w'Isi .
Ibi biti byatewe ku bigo by'amashuri bitatu mu Mujyi wa Kigali , birimo n'Urwunge rw'Amashuri rwa Cyahafi .
Umukozi Mukuru muri , GGGI , Michelle DeFreese , yavuze ko gutera ibiti ari uburyo bwizewe bwo guhangana n'ihindagurika ry'ibihe no kubungabunga ibidukikije muri rusange .
Michelle kandi yabwiye IGIHE ko kuba urubyiruko rwitanga mu bikorwa byo kurengera ibidukikije bizafasha u Rwanda guhangana n'imihindagurikire y'ibihe .
Ati """" Gutera ibiti ni imwe mu nzira zizewe zo guhangana n'imihindagurikire y'ibihe .
Ni iby'agacira gakomeye kuba biri kugirwamo uruhare n'urubyiruko .
Twizeye ko abanyeshuri bo kuri ibi bigo twateyemo ibiti bazabibungabunga . """"
Umukozi ushinzwe kwigisha ibidukikije n'imihindagurikire y'ibihe mu Kigo cy'Igihugu cyo kubungabunga ibidukikije , REMA , Rukwaya Jean Luc , yabwiye IGIHE ko ibiti byatewe birimo ibifite umumaro wo gufata ubutaka hirindwa inkangu n'isuri , mu gihe ibindi bigenewe kurimbisha aho byatewe , kuyungurura umwuka abantu bahumeka
, n'ibindi .
Icyakora kuko hari ahagiye haterwa ibiti nyuma ntibyitabweho bikaza kwangirika , Rukwaya yasabye abayobozi n'abanyeshuri b'aho ibi biti byatewe kubibungabunga .
Ati """" Hari aho byaterwaga nyuma tugasanga batarabyitayeho bikangirika .
Ni yo mpamvu twasabye ubuyobozi bw'ishuri n'abanyeshuri kubungabunga ibi biti twateye .
Tuzajya tugaruka kureba uko ibi biti bimeze . """"
Umubozi ushinzwe amasomo ku Rwunge rw'Amashuri rwa Cyahafi , Hategekimana Théogène , yabwiye IGIHE ko bishimiye guhabwa ibiti byera imbuto ziribwa , kandi babyitezeho kuzabafasha guhanga n'ikibazo cy'imirire mibi .
Ati """" Ni ikintu gikomeye kuri twebwe , kugira ubusitani burimbisha ikigo cyacu .
Akarusho ni uko harimo n'ibiti byera imbuto ziribwa .
Twiteguye kubibungabunga tukabirinda kwangirika . """"
Ibiti 49 byatewe ku bigo bitatu by'amashuri , birimo ibifata ubutaka , ibyera imbuto ziribwa , indabo n'ibindi bifite umumaro wo kurimbisha aho byatewe .
Ubwoko icumi bw'inyamaswa ziri gukendera mu Rwanda .
Abashakashatsi ku binyabuzima n'abarebera hafi iby'inyamaswa zo mu gasozi , bavuga ko kuba zimwe zarashizeho n'izindi zikaba ziri mu marembera bigirwamo uruhare n'ubuhigi bunyuranyije n'amategeko bukomeje kwiyongera , ba rushimusi , ndetse no kuziroga .
Zimwe zigenda zigabanyuka mu mibare n'aho zagaragaraga , naho izindi hashize imyaka myinshi zitakiboneka ahantu na hamwe mu Rwanda ku buryo bitekerezwa ko zishobora kuba zitakihaba .
Ubu ni ubwoko bw'igikeri kigira amabara avanze ku buryo ubona ameze nk'umutako cyashyizweho .
Amakuru aturuka mu Kigo gishinzwe Ubushakashatsi ku Rusobe rw'Ibinyabuzima n'Umutungo Kamere , Center of Excellence in Biodiversity and Natural Resource Management ( CoEB ) , avuga ko icyo gikeri giheruka kugaragara mu Rwanda mu 1950 .
Ubu bikekwa ko cyamaze gucika burundu mu Gihugu .
Amakuru IGIHE yahawe n'umwe mu barebera hafi inyamaswa zo muri Pariki ya Akagera , Karama Joseph , avuga ko inzobe zitakihaboneka , ndetse no mu bishanga bihegereye nta zihari .
Ati """" Ahubwo nta n'icyizere dufite ko zigihari .
Inzobe ziba mu bishanga kandi nitwe dufite ibishanga binini haba muri Afurika y'Iburasirazuba n'iyo Hagati , rero urumva ko zakabaye zihaboneka .
Abahigi barazigabije rwose ntiwapfa kuzibona . """"
